
Chapter 1 Major Operations


"Why were you fired?"

"I'll tell you a secret, didn't you offend Director Xiao? This is what Director Xiao instructed."

Jiang Tian remained calm.

Over a decade ago, his father was the deputy mayor and police chief, his mother a leader in the finance bureau, and he himself had just joined the anti-drug squad. Xiao Bo was just a guy from a remote mountain village, yet Jiang Tian treated him like a brother.

Due to an unexpected incident, Jiang Tian's mother was arrested, his father fell from grace, and Jiang Tian himself sank into despair.

In the end, Jiang Tian used his last remaining family connections to help Xiao Bo rise in rank.

Over a decade later, Jiang Tian himself was still struggling at the bottom, while the man he had desperately helped had been promoted, received a raise, married a beautiful and wealthy woman, and reached the pinnacle of life.

Over a decade ago, without his help, Xiao Bo would have been just one of the many at the bottom.

But Xiao Bo not only showed no gratitude, but instead found an opportunity to fire him from his last remaining position.

Jiang Tian, ​​dejected, took the bus home. Having been transferred to a remote rural area, he rarely had the chance to go home. Taking advantage of this trip back to the provincial capital, Jiang Tian planned to go home and visit.

Click!!!

He opened the door.

But what he saw was: "Adulterous couple."

Seeing Xiao Bo and a woman making out on the sofa, his mind went blank.

Bang!!!

Jiang Tian had just shouted in anger when a sharp pain shot through the back of his head. He collapsed to the floor, looking up in disbelief, only to see his son standing behind him with an iron rod. It was his son who had just done it.

Jiang Tian's wife, Wang Yifei, sneered: "Useless trash. Let me tell you, I've known Brother Xiao longer than you. It's just that Brother Xiao's family arranged this marriage, so I had to lower myself to your level, you piece of trash. Not only are you useless, your whole family is useless."

"Alright, don't corrupt Jiang Yu," Xiao Bo said mockingly.

“Dad, don’t call me Jiang Yu. That good-for-nothing isn’t my father. I don’t have such a useless father. We’ve done a paternity test; you’re my biological father. I should be called Xiao Yu. That old geezer should have died long ago; he doesn’t deserve a son,” Jiang Yu fawned.

“Yes, Brother Xiao, my son and I are all counting on you. That good-for-nothing, his family’s genes are all inferior genes of good-for-nothings. They don’t deserve to inherit. Every time I’m with him, I secretly take drugs. Brother Xiao, Yu’er is definitely your son.”

“Beast!!!” Jiang Tian roared in anger.

Bang!!!

A sharp pain struck, and Jiang Tian was plunged into darkness.

......

“Jiang Tian, ​​wake up! It’s an emergency meeting.”

Through a hazy vision, Jiang Tian vaguely heard someone calling his name. He opened his eyes and saw a face that was both strange and familiar.

“Don’t just stand there. This operation is extremely important. I heard that a high-ranking leader is personally overseeing it.” The voice sounded again.

Jiang Tian looked at the person who spoke.

This was his comrade-in-arms and roommate, Zhao Wei.

Reborn?

And, could this be the most important turning point in his life?

Jiang Tian's heart skipped a beat. Recalling his past life, Jiang Tian's eyes turned sinister.

"Didn't expect that, you bastard? I'm back." Jiang Tian clenched his fist.

At this moment, his father hadn't been placed under investigation yet, and his mother hadn't been arrested. It wasn't too late to avenge his family and exact revenge on his enemies.

Just then.

【There is always boundless evil in the world. The brighter the light, the more terrifying the evil. Do you have a heart for justice and are willing to uphold society?】

A voice rang out. Jiang Tian was overjoyed to find two options appearing before him: yes or no.

Sure enough.

With his rebirth, the system appeared.

“Yes.” Jiang Tian quickly chose.

Whoosh!!!

Instantly, a fluorescent light, visible only to him, appeared before Jiang Tian's eyes, like a control panel.

【Name: Jiang Tian】

[Entries: Marksmanship Novice (White), Martial Arts Average (White)]

[Marksmanship Novice (White): Your shooting talent is rather ordinary, nothing special.]

[Martial Arts Average (White): You have no talent for martial arts, and you will never achieve anything great in your life.]

Jiang Tian glanced at the panel, his face almost turning green. There were six categories of entries: black, white, green, blue, red, and gold.

He hadn't expected that not only did he not have a single green entry, but he was also so terrible.

[You have a newbie gift pack, do you want to claim it?]

"Claim." Jiang Tian took a deep breath.

[One of your random entries has been upgraded to the maximum level.]

[Marksmanship Novice (White) Upgraded to Unfailing Accuracy (Gold)]

Jiang Tian's heart skipped a beat. The next moment, he felt countless memories appear out of thin air in his mind.

These memories permeated even his muscles and every part of his body. His eyes were like a scope; at this moment, he possessed an overwhelming confidence that anything appearing in his sights would be a guaranteed hit.

"This is fucking awesome!" After a preliminary understanding, Jiang Tian realized just how terrifying the golden attribute truly was.

It was practically invincible.

In other words, no matter what kind of gun, even a bow and arrow, or even a dart—anything that could be thrown—if Jiang Tian wanted to, he could hit it with unerring accuracy, aiming precisely where he wanted.

The most incredible thing was that Jiang Tian was now even confident that he could fire an AK in rapid succession with the precision of a sniper rifle.

Wasn't this invincibility?

Jiang Tian's heart pounded with excitement.

"He's here! He's here! I heard it's a leader from Kyoto. This is a very, very important operation, and he's going to personally oversee the command." Zhao Wei said impatiently, his breathing rapid.

"Huh?"

Jiang Tian suddenly looked up.

Only then did he realize that he had unknowingly entered the operations room.

At this moment, a pre-mission meeting was underway.

The room was packed with people; a quick glance suggested at least several hundred.

All were members of this operation.

And not only were they narcotics officers in police uniforms, but more than half the people in the room were dressed as armed police.

The armed police and narcotics officers were operating together.

The next moment, a figure appeared on the platform at the front. Jiang Tian couldn't help but shudder when he saw that familiar face.

It was him.

On the platform, there was only one person, one seat, and only one name.

Gao Xiaolong.

The man who changed Jiang Tian's life.

Gao Xiaolong quickly reached the head of the platform, scanning the room. Jiang Tian could clearly sense that the other man's gaze was primarily searching for him.

And it lingered on him for a very long time.

"Now, let me announce the combat mission," Gao Xiaolong said in a deep voice.

Jiang Tian was deeply moved. Initially, everyone thought it was a small-scale conflict, a full-scale operation by the armed police and their anti-drug officers, and nothing unexpected would happen.

However, no one expected the conflict to be so brutal and terrifying.

It was during this mission that Gao Xiaolong met with misfortune, his father was implicated and placed under investigation, and his mother was arrested. In other words, if Gao Xiaolong survived, his life would be drastically different from his previous life.

"We've received intelligence that a major drug lord from abroad is planning to smuggle a massive amount of drugs into the country through our Yunhai border."



Chapter 2 Commander-in-Chief Oversees the Battle


"It really is a big fish! Jiang Tian, ​​let's seize this opportunity, brothers, and make a name for ourselves!" Zhao Wei said impatiently. "Look, isn't the leader looking at me?"

Jiang Tian's lips twitched.

"But..."

Gao Xiaolong removed his police cap, his face so dark it seemed it could drip water. He spoke with a fierce expression, "Today, a lady called my frontline anti-drug command center, asking me to look after her son. A black sheep got here through connections, but I like it. Why? Because what I love most is having these cowards fight drug dealers on the front lines, seeing them tremble with fear."

Whoosh!!!

With these words, the scene fell silent.

Everyone almost stopped breathing.

Heads darted around.

Seemingly searching for the person Gao Xiaolong mentioned who got in through connections.

Zhao Wei, sitting next to Jiang Tian, ​​gloated, "I wonder which unlucky bastard managed to get through Chief Gao's back door, hahaha..."

Jiang Tian glanced up at Zhao Wei, then at Gao Xiaolong, whose gaze was fixed intently on him.

Memories from his past life gradually overlapped.

Jiang Tian's mind raced.

In his past life, it was precisely because of this.

Speaking of which, Jiang Tian's family was well-off. His father was the police chief of Yunhai and the executive vice mayor.

His mother was a leader in the finance bureau.

In the eyes of ordinary people, they wielded immense power, and in reality, it was true. A position like Jiang Tian's father's could even allow one to control everything in Yunhai.

However, compared to Gao Xiaolong, Jiang Tian's father was nothing. Gao Xiaolong was from the capital, a man from the heavens.

Jiang Tian's mother was worried about his safety. She had originally arranged for him to come here to gain experience, but unexpectedly, he ended up on this major mission.

Jiang Tian vividly remembered the cause of this mission, or rather, the turning point of this event in his past life.

It began a few days prior with the arrest of Tucha's brother, a major drug lord in the Golden Triangle, at the border by Chinese police. Currently, Tucha's brother was not known to the Chinese authorities, being arrested as a regular drug trafficker.

However, Tucha deliberately leaked his drug trafficking trail.

As expected, the Chinese authorities took it extremely seriously and launched a large-scale operation.

But Tucha's objectives went far beyond that.

He dispatched a large number of drug traffickers, splitting into two groups: one group ambushed the police officers involved in the operation.

The other group secretly attempted to rescue Tucha's brother.

This was truly a turning point in fate.

In his past life, Gao Xiaolong, in a similar fit of rage, personally went to the front lines to oversee Jiang Tian's operations.

Ultimately, he fell into Tucha's trap and tragically sacrificed his life.

This caused a massive uproar throughout China, and amidst the immense commotion, the entire sequence of events was uncovered.

The issues surrounding Jiang Tian's mother's connections and other problems were magnified.

Ultimately, this led to Jiang Tian's parents being placed under investigation, and Jiang Tian being transferred to a small local police station as a clerk, where he lived a life of mediocrity and died in frustration.

The Jiang family, who had once enjoyed immense success and a promising future, were thus plunged into utter despair.

This was the turning point in Jiang Tian's fate.

"Dad didn't come. Was Gao Xiaolong deliberately sent him away?"

After the meeting, Jiang Tian glanced around. The deputy director of Yunhai, the anti-drug captain, the armed police leaders, and everyone else were present for this operation.

Logically, for such a large-scale operation, Jiang Tian's father, as the director, should definitely be here for the meeting, and might even give a speech.

In his previous life, Jiang Tian hadn't thought that much about it.

But now, Jiang Tian understood. Nine times out of ten, it was because Gao Xiaolong, in his rage, was deliberately targeting him.

This powerful figure, who hated evil, was targeting him.

He thought he was cowardly and that his family was corrupt.

But…

Jiang Tian's lips curled into a smile.

The scenes from his previous life wouldn't repeat themselves.

He subconsciously touched the pistol at his waist, a feeling of unspoken understanding welling up within him.

Next, everyone changed into their uniforms.

Donning a bulletproof vest and receiving his standard-issue weapon, the QBZ95, also known as the Type 95 automatic rifle, was a relatively new weapon widely adopted by hunting teams.

The moment he held the gun, all the specifications flooded Jiang Tian's mind.

The Type 95 automatic rifle uses 5.8mm ammunition, has an effective range of 400 meters, a firing rate of 40 rounds per minute (single shot), and a burst firing rate of 100 rounds per minute. It is equipped with five magazines, each holding 30 rounds.

"The Narcotics Enforcement Team is counting personnel."

Inside the transport convoy, Narcotics Enforcement Team Leader Song Liguo was counting personnel.

"Yunhai Narcotics Enforcement Team action group, 35 members expected, 35 members present, report complete." The deputy team leader quickly began the report.

Song Liguo nodded slightly, then glanced at Jiang Tian with a hint of worry.

In truth, he bore the main responsibility for this matter.

Because Jiang Tian's mother had originally called him, but Gao Xiaolong happened to be there and answered the call from an official landline number.

This instantly enraged Gao Xiaolong.

“Xiao Jiang, you’ll be working with me from now on,” Song Liguo said after a moment’s thought.

“Yes,” Jiang Tian replied, his lips twitching.

Having experienced his past life, he knew that their anti-drug squad was primarily responsible for supporting operations; the main fighting was handled by the armed police.

After all, their main tasks were investigations and small-scale arrests of drug dealers. Large-scale shootouts with drug traffickers were handled by the armed police; they were the ones providing support.

Jiang Tian also knew that Gao Xiaolong was only outwardly fierce and righteous; in reality, he was capable of saving him in crucial moments.

Although the misfortunes all started because of Gao Xiaolong, Jiang Tian never held a grudge.

Even though Gao Xiaolong said he wanted him to be part of the suicide squad, the main objective was still the armed police.

The anti-drug police were providing support from the sidelines.

No one expected that the entire main force of the Tucha (Tuchai) forces was concentrated on this narrow path, leading to horrific casualties.

It was even hailed as the most devastating and impactful case since the founding of the People's Republic of China.

In his previous life, Jiang Tian was terrified upon first encountering it.

But in this life...

Jiang Tian gripped the Type 95 rifle with burning passion in both hands, his gaze filled with unprecedented excitement and determination.

In his previous life, during a crucial moment in the fight against drug traffickers, Jiang Tian, ​​overwhelmed by fear, was preemptively shot by the drug traffickers. It was Gao Xiaolong who pushed him away at the critical moment.

Jiang Tian survived, but Gao Xiaolong died.

But this life will be rewritten.

Jiang Tian gazed out the window, his eyes filled with melancholy, taking deep breaths to compose himself.

The next moment.

Click!

The door of the armed police transport vehicle opened.

Gao Xiaolong boarded the vehicle with two heavily armed bodyguards.

"Commander."

Everyone instinctively stood up, their faces filled with astonishment and surprise.

Even the team leader, Song Liguo, felt his heart pounding.



Chapter 3 Changing Fate, Let's Begin Now


"Don't be nervous, everyone. I'll be traveling with you this time to make command easier," Gao Xiaolong said with a smile, gesturing with his hand.

His gaze, however, was subtly fixed on Jiang Tian.

His eyes were filled with coldness and anger.

"Commander, you can't come!" Song Liguo's face turned almost green.

Coming along with Commander Gao? Was he crazy? If anything went wrong, the entire Yunhai, from top to bottom, would be in serious trouble.

Song Liguo didn't even want to think about it.

In fact, that was indeed the case in his previous life, because it not only implicated Jiang Tian's parents but also Song Liguo.

Because it was later discovered that the phone call made through connections was to Song Liguo.

This led to Song Liguo being implicated and dismissed from his post.

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian breathed a sigh of relief. Fortunately, he still had a cheat system after transmigrating, so it wasn't too late.

At that moment, Gao Xiaolong, not far from Jiang Tian, ​​turned his gaze towards him.

His face was filled with a cold smile: "Why can't they come? If I hadn't come, I wouldn't have known there were such cowards in the team. If they're so afraid of death, why did they even join the anti-drug team, harming themselves and others?"

Gao Xiaolong was filled with rage at the sight of Jiang Tian.

Anti-drug police officers are on the front lines, the most dangerous frontline.

Entering the anti-drug team, especially in Yunhai, which is the frontline of the national anti-drug force, only to find such cowardice.

The ultimate result is not only harming themselves, but also potentially harming their comrades at crucial moments.

A cancer.

This is the cancer within the team.

Gao Xiaolong was burning with anger.

"Commander," Song Liguo tried to argue.

Gao Xiaolong interrupted, "You don't need to say anything. As the team leader, you're not immune to blame. Bringing in a good-for-nothing like him is incredibly harmful to the entire anti-drug team. Don't you know?"

In his eyes, Jiang Tian was a good-for-nothing, cowardly second-generation rich kid.

Song Liguo, his face covered in cold sweat, remained silent.

"His family wants someone to take care of him, fine, I'll take care of him myself. In this operation, I'll be his supervisor. If he dares to retreat during the fighting, I'll shoot him dead first. He can go somewhere else to get his resume. The anti-drug team isn't for good-for-nothings to gain experience."

Before, with more people, he had to be more considerate, but now that there were fewer people, Gao Xiaolong's words became increasingly harsh.

His voice grew louder and louder.

Inside the transport vehicle, everyone's expression changed.

Gazes darted between them, scanning their teammates.

Gao Xiaolong didn't name names, so no one knew who he was referring to.

Jiang Tian's identity, naturally, couldn't be publicized either.

However, those in the anti-drug team possessed incredibly sharp eyes. Seeing Gao Xiaolong's gaze lingering on Jiang Tian, ​​they had already gleaned some information.

"Does everyone understand?" Song Liguo shouted to everyone.

"Understood."

Everyone responded, including Jiang Tian.

He offered no rebuttal, nor did he say anything.

Because there was no need; the results would speak for themselves.

No matter how much he said now, it would only give the impression of impotent rage.

"This time, you'll finally look at me differently," Jiang Tian muttered to himself.

"Action!" Song Liguo ordered the driver with a bitter expression.

The Yunhai anti-drug task force consisted of thirty-five people in four or five cars. The car in the middle, including Jiang Tian and Gao Xiaolong's, was a large, twelve-seater official vehicle.

There were just enough seats for Gao Xiaolong.

"Sir, would you please sit?" Song Liguo, who was in the front seat, stood up to offer it to Gao Xiaolong.

But Gao Xiaolong shook his head and walked straight to Jiang Tian.

Next to Jiang Tian was Zhao Wei, who shuddered and stood up to salute when he saw Gao Xiaolong approaching.

"Gao..." Zhao Wei began to speak.

"Gao what? Go, find somewhere to sit. I'll sit here." Gao Xiaolong simply shoved Zhao Wei aside.

Zhao Wei didn't utter a word, dashing to the back and watching in shock as Gao Xiaolong sat down next to Jiang Tian.

Jiang Tian, ​​still shaken, kept his eyes downcast, but his mind was racing.

Zhao Wei's demeanor upon seeing Gao Xiaolong, and Gao Xiaolong's attitude towards Zhao Wei, were unusual.

Having experienced decades of ups and downs in his previous life, Jiang Tian keenly sensed that Zhao Wei's background was probably far from simple.

Thinking this,

Jiang Tian's whole body trembled.

Indeed.

The team was full of hidden talents. In his previous life, he had wasted his days in an administrative position, but he knew that many people in the team lived in anonymity.

They seemed unremarkable, but they often seemed to have divine assistance in their endeavors.

They practically handed credit to them. At first, Jiang Tian envied their luck, but later he realized that they truly had divine help.

It's connected to Gao Xiaolong... Hiss...

However, Jiang Tian didn't dwell on it. For him, the most important thing right now was how to deal with and resolve the situation with the drug lord, Tucha.

Undoubtedly.

While the main force of armed police ahead headed towards the intelligence route, their group of only thirty-five people took a different path.

The atmosphere in the car was somewhat oppressive, but there wasn't much psychological burden.

Because many people, including the branch captain and Gao Xiaolong, never considered that their roundabout route was Tucha's true intention.

The key was that Jiang Tian couldn't say anything.

Initially, Jiang Tian had considered whether to warn Song Liguo to be careful.

But now...

Because of Gao Xiaolong's misunderstanding, and even Gao Xiaolong's obvious dislike, Jiang Tian was now forced to remain silent.

Any rebuttal, any words, would be like a clown jumping around to Gao Xiaolong.

Besides being repulsive, it would serve no purpose whatsoever.

Throughout the journey, Jiang Tian's mind kept replaying scenes from his previous life.

Soon.

The convoy drove into a dense forest.

Jiang Tian's gaze swept over the scene. His memories of his past life, after all, were beginning to fade, decades had passed.

But, the moment they entered the forest.

A familiar feeling, a feeling as if it were yesterday, instantly washed over him.

It was this very forest.

Jiang Tian's entire body trembled.

It was here.

Zhao Wei died here.

Gao Xiaolong also died here.

Including...

There were thirty-five people in the team, plus Gao Xiaolong and his two companions, making a total of thirty-eight. Only eight survived.

Thinking of the scene from his past life...

Zhao Wei was shot, coughing up blood, and even after his death here, Jiang Tian never knew Zhao Wei's true identity.

And Gao Xiaolong.

Oh no.

The huge commotion in his past life probably wasn't just about Gao Xiaolong.

Even...

Jiang Tian glanced at Zhao Wei.

He took a deep breath.

I gripped my Type 95 rifle tightly. This life will be different; every shot will hit its mark.

Jiang Tian couldn't wait to test his marksmanship.

From this moment on, he would completely change his father's, his mother's, and even his own destiny.



Chapter 4 is a lie!


"Nervous?"

Beside Jiang Tian, ​​Gao Xiaolong glanced at him. His sharp eyes immediately noticed Jiang Tian's hands gripping the Type 95 pistol tightly.

In Gao Xiaolong's eyes, this was cowardice, a sign of nervousness.

Gao Xiaolong couldn't help but sneer inwardly. A good-for-nothing is a good-for-nothing.

This kind of good-for-nothing second-generation rich kid, it's one thing to slack off and gain experience elsewhere, but he actually brought his corrupt practices into the anti-drug team.

This made Gao Xiaolong increasingly angry.

Inside the transport truck, everyone was silent. Having heard Gao Xiaolong's voice, everyone's gaze, except for the driver, instinctively turned to Jiang Tian.

"Report, not nervous."

Jiang Tian answered subconsciously.

Actually, he had been thinking about things he hadn't noticed in his previous life.

In his previous life, the sacrifice of Gao Xiaolong and Zhao Wei caused a great stir.

Firstly, it was the faulty intelligence that led to this major loss, so Jiang Tian's family was just incidentally dealt with.

Even without the incident involving Jiang Tian, ​​Jiang Tian's father would still have been dismissed and investigated.

Because, the entire Yunhai, from top to bottom, seemed to have undergone a massive purge after this incident.

Even the top leader was almost entirely stripped down.

This caused a terrifying and enormous uproar throughout the country.

Originally, Jiang Tian was definitely going to be fired, but a beautiful girl came to mind, asking him to meet and inquire about Zhao Wei.

Later, Jiang Tian learned that she was Zhao Wei's sister, and very beautiful.

In his previous life, he didn't know so much, but now, Jiang Tian realized that his ability to transfer to an administrative position and stay there for so long was probably due to Zhao Wei's sister's influence.

Thinking this, Jiang Tian took a deep breath, his gaze gradually hardening.

He was determined to rewrite the ending of his past life.

Moreover, since he couldn't change the battle plan beforehand, and given his lowly status and lack of influence, he could only rely on the weapons in his hands.

He looked at the familiar yet unfamiliar faces inside the car.

These were police officers fighting on the front lines, earning only around three thousand a month, yet risking their lives.

He wouldn't complain if he lacked power.

But now that he had power, Jiang Tian felt he needed to do something.

“You're feeling insecure, but your mouth is tough. Good. Don't think that our support will prevent a battle. After the drug dealers and armed police finish their fight, they'll definitely retreat, ninety percent of the time taking this route. So, there's a high probability we'll have to fight the ruthless drug dealers. Bullets have no eyes; if you run away at the last minute, I'll shoot you first,” Gao Xiaolong said expressionlessly.

He was met with repeated contempt from Gao Xiaolong.

Jiang Tian's anger was also rising.

Yes, you are the leader from above.

You are someone who hates evil.

But, one after another, Jiang Tian's anger continued to rise, and he suddenly stood up.

This startled Gao Xiaolong so much that he couldn't help but lean back.

All eyes were now focused on Jiang Tian.

The next moment, Jiang Tian's confident voice rang out: "I'll take a step back. I don't need you; I'll shoot myself first."

Wow!!!

Good heavens.

Zhao Wei was stunned.

This was the first time he'd ever seen someone so assertive in front of Gao Xiaolong.

Even Gao Xiaolong was bewildered.

This guy...

doesn't seem like a loser!

He can actually speak so confidently in front of him—Gao Xiaolong just happens to like this kind of person.

But here's the problem: if he were really that assertive, would he have his family call his boss for special treatment?

Impossible, so this guy's faking it.

After confirming this, Gao Xiaolong sneered inwardly with a face full of disdain. This kid almost fooled him.

However, even a clay figure has some temper, let alone Jiang Tian, ​​who had been insulted time and time again.

Jiang Tian could endure it, but his golden "Infallible Shot" skill couldn't.

"Since that's how it is, I'll give you a big one," Jiang Tian thought to himself.

Before Gao Xiaolong could speak, Jiang Tian's voice continued, "I'm faster and deeper into the battlefield. For your safety, you'd better not follow. Otherwise, if anything happens to your precious body, we'll be in deep trouble and you'll be a burden."

BOOM!!!

What is a bomb?

This is a bomb!

Pfft!!!

Song Liguo coughed up his drink, staring at Jiang Tian in disbelief.

Zhao Wei stared blankly, as if he thought he was dreaming.

The colleagues present watched this scene with chills down their spines.

What started as Gao Xiaolong's insults to Jiang Tian—accusations of cowardice and a useless second-generation rich kid—had now...

Gao Xiaolong stared blankly, then abruptly stood up, his face also flushed red.

"This is outrageous!"

"This is a betrayal of Heaven!"

.....

Gao Xiaolong clenched his fists, repeating the same angry roar in his mind.

"You're talking nonsense," Gao Xiaolong gritted his teeth, enunciating each word clearly.

Jiang Tian sighed inwardly, glancing around in surprise, seemingly puzzled by Gao Xiaolong's intense reaction.

Jiang Tian knew his own fighting capabilities well. Moreover, with numerous drug dealers around, he would need to infiltrate deep behind enemy lines to minimize casualties.

If Gao Xiaolong were to supervise him like in his previous life, he definitely wouldn't be able to keep up, and even if he did, it would be extremely dangerous.

Gao Xiaolong absolutely couldn't afford to have anything happen to him.

When Gao Xiaolong looked at Jiang Tian with fury, he saw that Jiang Tian was genuinely concerned.

This made Gao Xiaolong want to vomit blood.

That bastard.

Gao Xiaolong's clenched fist trembled. The next moment, as if remembering something, he laughed, "You think saying this will stop me from watching you? Stop supervising you? Dream on. That kind of provocation won't work on me."

Jiang Tian was speechless, but said nothing.

It was pointless to say anything now. Gao Xiaolong had already decided he was a good-for-nothing second-generation rich kid; saying anything more would only cause misunderstandings.

Jiang Tian remained silent because the vehicle had arrived.

It was now two in the morning.

The mountain road was difficult to navigate at night, winding and twisting. After reaching a fork in the road,

"Everyone out of the vehicle, take cover." Song Liguo stood at the intersection of a small road.

Actually, in his previous life, there was another important reason why the battle ended so fiercely.

That was, the intelligence was wrong.

At first, only four or five drug dealers quietly approached, and after being apprehended, they weren't given much attention.

But then, a large number of drug dealers rushed in from all directions.

Jiang Tian got out of the car, put on his thermal imaging camera, and hid behind a tree by the roadside.

"Don't be too nervous. It's normal to be like this the first time. After all, you just graduated. You'll get used to it," Gao Xiaolong said, squatting not far from Jiang Tian.

After they got out of the car, the armed police vehicle had already driven away, and now the thirty-five men were hidden in the dense forest in great silence.

To be honest, Jiang Tian was somewhat surprised; he hadn't expected Gao Xiaolong's attitude.



Chapter 5 You were right, kid.


At this moment, Gao Xiaolong recalled Jiang Tian's stubborn words in the car and couldn't help but sigh.

After all, he was just a recent graduate, a young man in his early twenties!

Looking at the other sitting silently behind the dark tree, Gao Xiaolong smiled inwardly, telling himself, "Why argue with a kid?"

Although his behavior was somewhat reprehensible, he still had some character, just a bit of cowardice, but those could be changed.

Jiang Tian didn't answer Gao Xiaolong.

To be honest, Gao Xiaolong's status was indeed very high; he was a powerful figure, a true big shot.

But for Jiang Tian,

his most important task was to change the misfortune of his past life.

To reduce the casualties of the team.

Especially to ensure Gao Xiaolong's safety.

At that moment, Song Liguo, holding a walkie-talkie, addressed everyone: "Let's clarify the mission objective. We received intelligence that a major foreign drug lord, Tucha, is planning to smuggle a large quantity of drugs into the country tonight via a different route. Our mission is to prevent the drug traffickers from escaping."

"You'd better protect yourself," Jiang Tian said calmly in a low voice.

"Yeah, right."

Gao Xiaolong's eyes widened. What was this kid saying?

He, Gao Xiaolong, was actually being told to protect himself by this rookie, Jiang Tian.

Gao Xiaolong almost laughed in exasperation.

"They're here."

Just as Gao Xiaolong was about to say something, he heard Jiang Tian's voice.

"They're here?" Song Liguo was also full of surprise.

Because he hadn't received any news of a fight breaking out among the armed police!

"Five people."

Jiang Tian's eyes were sharp; through the thermal imaging camera, he spotted the figures in the distance.

To be honest,

wearing a thermal imaging camera on his head significantly affected his vision.

This is different from what the naked eye sees. Without very rigorous training, it's difficult to adapt to a thermal imager, especially when firing a gun while wearing one. Many people don't even know where they're aiming and just fire randomly.

"The fighting hasn't started over there yet, so why are people coming over here?" Gao Xiaolong's gaze sharpened slightly.

Song Liguo, standing not far from Gao Xiaolong, worried about him, said, "This drug lord seems very cunning. He might have split into two groups, and there are people staking out this area as well."

Gao Xiaolong thought for a moment and guessed, "Or maybe he's releasing a smokescreen. Even if you want to get through here, don't make a move yet."

Both Gao Xiaolong and Song Liguo are seasoned criminal investigators.

Based on their experience,

the biggest purpose of a major drug lord entering the country is to transport drugs; they're like rats, and would never engage in a direct confrontation with the police.

However, they overlooked a more important issue.

That is, the other party's main purpose this time wasn't drugs at all.

It was simply to rescue people and seek revenge.

Jiang Tian, ​​hidden behind a tree, listened to their discussion, his expression grave.

It appeared there were only five of them, but in reality, the other side had already arrived.

Based on the detailed intelligence Jiang Tian had gathered in his previous life,

at this point in time, an accomplice of the drug lord had already abducted Tucha's brother from the transport vehicle.

The other side deliberately created this opening to attract a large police force. They also knew that Tucha's brother would be transferred from the border detention center to Yunhai city that night.

However, tragically, Tucha's brother was killed by a stray bullet during the rescue.

In other words, Tucha's brother is dead.

So, they were actually facing not only Tucha, the drug dealer, but also a group of elite mercenaries.

Even more terrifying is that this will provoke Tucha's furious retaliation.

A frenzied retaliatory attack against them.

After shifting their mission objective from rescuing his brother… Jiang Tian's mood grew increasingly heavy.

The key is that Jiang Tian couldn't reveal these things.

Because even everyone in their anti-drug team didn't know these details.

Especially given that he was still being misunderstood by Gao Xiaolong.

"Is it possible that the drug lord deliberately created a smokescreen, with ulterior motives? For example, a group of people might suddenly appear behind us and attack us from both sides?" Jiang Tian asked calmly.

“Impossible. Our intelligence is flawless. Besides, he wouldn't be planning to enter the country unless it's for drug trafficking. You've only been in the anti-drug force for a short time; there are many things you don't know. You need to learn gradually,” Song Liguo patiently instructed.

Jiang Tian sighed but didn't say much.

“Young man, you still have a lot to learn. Seeing that you're not hopeless, I'll teach you. These people are probably sent by that big drug lord to scout ahead, planning to split up and transport drugs. You've just graduated; study hard, and you'll understand once you have experience.” Gao Xiaolong's impression of Jiang Tian had changed somewhat.

But ultimately, it depends on whether he'll be cowardly in a fight.

Thinking this, Gao Xiaolong, with his thermal imaging camera, observed and spoke to Jiang Tian.

Mainly, he was watching the journey, and Jiang Tian, ​​this young man, didn't seem as hopeless as he had imagined.

It's normal for young people to take the wrong path.

It's also normal to be a little naive.

They made a mistake, but as long as they acknowledge it and correct it, there's still a chance to redeem themselves.

After all, they've just joined the anti-drug team; it's normal to be a little cowardly. With proper guidance, they can correct their behavior.

Thinking this, Gao Xiaolong used the thermal imaging to scan the group and continued to instruct Jiang Tian.

“Young people just starting out on a mission often have these kinds of wild thoughts, like watching too many police dramas. Being attacked from both sides… um…” Gao Xiaolong suddenly paused.

He seemed to have just seen something.

He seemed to have seen the thermal imaging.

It was behind them.

Gao Xiaolong's face showed astonishment. Animals?

“Team Leader Song, do we have a second batch of support personnel behind us?” Gao Xiaolong asked in surprise.

Song Liguo waved his hand: “Sir, we're just assisting. Even if we're providing support, it's not for us. They've all gone over there.”

A jolt!

A bad premonition rose in Gao Xiaolong's heart.

He hurriedly looked up.

Whoa!!!

The next moment.

Gao Xiaolong's head exploded.

"Oh no, something's happened."

In Gao Xiaolong's line of sight as he looked into the jungle behind him, there were several figures displayed on the thermal imaging; at a rough glance, there were at least a dozen.

The next moment,

"Captain, there's a situation! Thermal imaging shows a large crowd gathering." Just then, the lookout suddenly spoke into the walkie-talkie.

Buzz!!!

Surrounded?

Gao Xiaolong was stunned.

Chapter 6 A Close Call


At this moment, Jiang Tian had no time to answer.

In both his past and present lives, for him, today's events had haunted his past life, etched in his dreams countless times, prompting him to devise a solution.

Initially, his only thought was to ensure Gao Xiaolong's safety. But now, Jiang Tian noticed, besides Zhao Wei, the faces of his teammates.

Drug enforcement officers.

Silently fighting on the front lines, protecting the people's interests and property with their own flesh and blood.

Reborn, Jiang Tian felt he needed to do something.

Since that's the case, then he should try to annihilate the enemy as much as possible.

"Let's try to retreat first and wipe out the drug dealers behind us," Song Liguo decisively ordered.

Because at this point, there wasn't much time for words.

The number of red dots representing drug dealers was increasing, and they were getting closer.

"Everyone, stop moving and prepare to retreat," Song Liguo said, cold sweat beading on his forehead.

Something was wrong today. Something was definitely wrong.

Jiang Tian, ​​however, quietly spoke up, "I feel that attacking from the rear is less effective than attacking from the front."

Huh???

Song Liguo and Gao Xiaolong were both stunned.

Gao Xiaolong, in particular, said gravely, "You know what you're saying. The thermal imager shows at least a hundred people ahead, and more are constantly arriving from behind."

"But didn't you see? The drug dealers in front are disorganized, but the dozen or so behind them, when moving through the thermal imager, are very disciplined and coordinate perfectly," Jiang Tian said.

Without his memories from his past life, Jiang Tian wouldn't have observed so closely and understood so clearly.

Because it was this group of mercenaries behind them who were instantly overwhelmed during their retreat.

Their anti-drug task force wasn't professional. Although they had training, there was still a difference between them and professional armed police or even special forces, in terms of combat effectiveness and teamwork.

Their skills were fine against drug dealers, but imagine how brutal it would be against professional mercenaries.

Jiang Tian knew that in his previous life, during the initial encounter, nine of his thirty-five men, plus Gao Xiaolong and his two companions—a total of thirty-eight—were instantly killed.

The enemy was professional.

Even Jiang Tian, ​​with his unerring aim, wasn't entirely confident against such well-coordinated, well-covered, and well-equipped mercenaries.

*Whoosh!*

Just as Jiang Tian finished speaking,

Gao Xiaolong and Song Liguo stared in disbelief.

"Kid, are you sure? You know, the consequences of a wrong judgment are unbearable for anyone."

"If that's the case, there's a high possibility of foreign interference!"

Both men spoke with cold sweat beading on their foreheads.

If even well-trained foreign personnel were involved, and coming from behind them, it meant the intelligence was flawed.

Both men had extensive criminal investigation experience, and in just a moment, they realized the danger they were in.

Gao Xiaolong only glanced at them briefly, but instantly broke out in a cold sweat, because it matched Jiang Tian's description perfectly.

A closer look revealed that, unlike the haphazard drug dealers in front, the dozen or so people behind them were positioned with strict discipline.

And if they really broke through from the rear and didn't discover the problem in front of them...

Hiss!!!

He didn't dare to think about the consequences.

Good lad.

Absolutely a good lad.

To be honest, Jiang Tian himself was completely surprised.

You have to understand the difference between ordinary drug dealers and a group of well-trained foreign forces.

Just then.

Bang bang bang!!!

A series of rapid gunshots rang out.

Everyone present turned pale.

The two roads were quite far apart, but in the silent night, the faint sound of gunfire could still be heard.

Jiang Tian glanced over and immediately understood that Song Liguo had probably just contacted the other side.

It seemed unlikely that reinforcements would arrive from the other side.

Both the armed police and anti-drug police had been deployed in full force; Yunhai had no spare manpower.

Even if reinforcements were mobilized, it would be difficult for them to arrive quickly.

By the time the army arrived, the battle would likely be over.

Gao Xiaolong's face was grave. In a short time, he had made a decision.

"Give the order: leave ten men to hold off the enemy in the rear with firepower; the rest, prioritize eliminating the drug traffickers in the front." Gao Xiaolong immediately slammed his hand on the table.

If it were just a matter of holding off the enemy with firepower, that wouldn't be difficult, even if the enemy was well-equipped and well-trained.

Song Liguo was cursing and swearing, "Has Tucha gone mad? What's gotten into him tonight?"

Song Liguo had dealt with Tucha, the Golden Triangle drug lord, quite a bit.

After all, the only route from the Golden Triangle into China was through Yunhai.

Anti-drug police are on the front lines of drug enforcement, and Yunhai's anti-drug police are the front lines among the front lines.

This resume and experience would be a huge help for future advancement, which is why Jiang Cai was arranged to gain experience here.

Generally speaking, drug traffickers' primary goal is always smuggling drugs and making money.

"No, something's not right. If Tucha is smuggling drugs, how come people have already entered the country? This is completely different from what the intelligence report said. Also, why didn't a large number of drug traffickers use the route indicated by the intelligence, but instead chose this route? In other words, Tucha's main purpose might not be smuggling drugs," Gao Xiaolong calmly analyzed.

After all, he was a big shot; he could still analyze things calmly at such a critical moment.

Sure enough.

Song Liguo, his face also covered in cold sweat, realized what had happened.

If their purpose was drug trafficking, they wouldn't be in any danger.

But if it was for some other purpose...

This time, their chances of survival were slim.

Cold sweat dripped from Song Liguo's chin. He wasn't afraid of himself, but rather of the narcotics officers who had fought alongside him in countless battles and rendered outstanding service, who might be killed.

He was even more afraid that something might happen to Gao Xiaolong beside him.

"Cover the commander's retreat first," Song Liguo decisively ordered.

"Nonsense! According to the battle plan, ignore me! That's an order!" Gao Xiaolong roared.

Song Liguo was about to say something.

But then, in the next moment...

He saw Jiang Tian standing behind Gao Xiaolong, his hands already raised, guns.

"Jiang Tian, ​​what are you doing?"

From Song Liguo's perspective, Jiang Tian was pointing his gun at Gao Xiaolong.

Is he crazy?

The next moment...

Bang!!!

A gunshot rang out.

At that moment, as Gao Xiaolong tried to turn his head, he clearly felt a bullet graze his ear.

He even felt a slight sensation in his ear.

Thud!!!



Chapter 7 entry upgrade, absolutely amazing!

Jiang Tian nodded firmly.

*Whoosh!*

Seeing this,

A person?

An enemy?

When?

Why didn't the thermal imager see them?

When did they get here?

Actually,

This person's disguise was excellent.

Because in his previous life, in the same location, in the same direction, no one had noticed this enemy.

Good heavens.

As soon as Jiang Tian finished speaking, Gao Xiaolong and Song Liguo were shocked. What kind of good person would use a thermal imager to look at their feet?!

Sure enough, after the group gathered around,

they saw a person lying in the bushes, completely covered in mud.

They were using the mud to avoid the thermal imager.

In other words, this person had been here for a long time.

They, the anti-drug squad members, had been exposed long ago.

His observation was meticulous.

But this meticulousness was too outrageous!

"If I remember correctly, this kid hasn't been officially a full-fledged officer yet, right?" Gao Xiaolong's mouth dropped open.

Song Liguo immediately replied, "To be precise, he's still a senior in college this year, currently a probationary police officer, having only joined the team a little over a month ago."

You're a fucking genius.

Gao Xiaolong gasped.

Think about it, from initially identifying and analyzing the drug dealers, to calmly firing his gun and directly killing a lurking drug dealer.

Indirectly averting two significant losses.

Without extraordinary observational skills, this would be absolutely impossible.

This means that this kid is wasting his talent in the anti-narcotics squad; he'd be better suited to the criminal investigation and major crimes unit!

"Good lad, what a genius! A bit scared, but I never expected him to have this trick up his sleeve. A true genius!" Gao Xiaolong's eyes lit up.

He'd just graduated; even these veteran detectives hadn't noticed.

Jiang Tian had spotted him twice in a row.

Of course, Gao Xiaolong didn't have much time to speak now.

With the sound of Jiang Tian's gunshot, they all knew their time was running out.

The drug dealers in the thermal imaging moved faster.

These people had gone mad.

"Xiao Jiang, what are you doing?" Song Liguo turned around and saw Jiang Tian squatting next to the drug dealer.

"Nothing," Jiang Tian replied, turning his head with a strange expression.

Then, he looked back at the mud-covered corpse on the ground.

He saw a green label floating above the corpse.

Level 5 label: white, green, blue, red, gold.

Jiang Tian himself, after four years of training at the police academy, only had two white labels.

Now, a green keyword had appeared.

Jiang Tian squinted.

Although the corpse was covered in mud, Jiang Tian could still tell that the person was wearing mercenary equipment—they were foreign mercenaries.

Then, Jiang Tian reached out and touched the keyword. The next moment, the keyword's information appeared in his mind:

【Insight into People's Hearts (Green): When criminals appear around you, you have a special sense.】

Hiss!!!

Wow.

Jiang Tian's eyes lit up.

If this upgraded to gold, wouldn't it become a scanning radar, able to sense the severity of everyone's crimes with a single glance?

Jiang Tian's heart pounded with excitement.

This is a huge win!

"If I want to upgrade an entry,"

[All entries can be upgraded in two ways. The first is by synthesizing entries of the same level. The second is by using the sin points gained from the host's capture and trial of criminals (the sin points gained are determined by the crimes committed by the criminals).]

[Current entries: Unfailing Accuracy (Gold), Insight into People's Hearts (Green), Martial Arts Average (White)]

[Current Sin Points: 352]

"Upgrading to Martial Arts Average." Jiang Tian's heart stirred.

The next moment, he saw the sin points decrease by one hundred.

That is to say, upgrading from the lowest level to green requires one hundred points.

The purchasing power of sin points is quite strong!

Jiang Tian's eyes lit up.

[Martial Arts Average (White) Upgrade to Martial Arts Minor Success (Green)]

The next moment.

Jiang Tian felt his whole body brimming with power, and some fighting techniques he couldn't remember before inexplicably appeared in his mind.

Very amazing.

But he could clearly feel a significant improvement in his physical abilities and the fighting techniques he learned at school.

Even just the green level had an immediate effect.

What if it were gold? Wouldn't he be a martial arts master, with unerring accuracy?

Hiss!!!

Jiang Tian abruptly turned to look at the group of drug dealers. At this moment, these dealers were no longer a source of danger, but rather tools for his leveling up.

If he were to eliminate all these drug dealers and leave them here,

how many sin points would he gain?

Besides sin points, how many other attributes would drop?

Hiss!!!

"We haven't even left the beginner's village, and we're practically becoming gods already!"

Normally, a newcomer like Jiang Tian would be assigned a senior mentor.

However, Jiang Tian is currently in his probationary period.

His time with the anti-drug team has been too short to be properly arranged, so for now, Jiang Tian has no choice but to follow him.

Gao Xiaolong's safety had to be guaranteed.

Chapter 8 You little rascal, are you a ghost?


Good luck, and a certain degree of keen observation.

Hiss!!!

Jiang Tian had killed three drug dealers today.

Even one of them was a mercenary infiltrator.

Bang!!!

The Type 95 automatic rifle, developed in 1995, wasn't widely adopted for hunting until 2000.

This rifle, although using small-caliber bullets, had obvious advantages: ease of carrying.

Low recoil.

Relatively simple calibration.

The disadvantage was its short effective range.

Only about 400 meters.

Normally, beyond 400 meters, the bullet's trajectory would be unknown, but don't forget, Jiang Tian was a crack shot.

The moment the opponent showed their face, Jiang Tian could instantly kill them.

It was as if they were telepathically connected.

How could there possibly be so many opportunities and such abundant resources under normal circumstances?

From initially analyzing the drug dealers' correct movements, then discovering and killing a dangerous enemy, indirectly saving him.

You're telling me, such a promising talent should be shot?

Is this some kind of sarcastic remark?

"Little Song, just kill him. Considering it's his first offense, it's unnecessary, completely unnecessary," Gao Xiaolong said in a muffled voice.

Bang bang bang!!!

Just then, even more intense gunfire erupted.

Gao Xiaolong quickly used the thermal imaging to look.

Jiang Tian had already charged towards the drug dealers.

He moved with exceptional agility through the jungle.

And thanks to the thermal imaging, it was practically a deadly weapon in Jiang Tian's hands.

He located the drug dealers' hiding places, quickly moved through the darkness, changed angles, and then shot them dead.

Then, anyone who showed their face was shot directly.

In a short time.

What Gao Xiaolong saw was that any drug dealer who showed their face, or was in Jiang Tian's line of sight, was instantly killed.

What? You're saying it's definitely Jiang Tian?

Because at this moment, both sides were still advancing step by step. The anti-narcotics team, hiding behind trees, were still using thermal imaging to maneuver and defend.

At this moment, only Jiang Tian charged towards the drug dealers.

He was incredibly fast.

In thermal imaging, unless you're covered in mud, using the mud to obstruct the image, any heat source would be easily detected.

"Holy crap."

Gao Xiaolong's eyes widened.

Insane.

This was utterly insane.

He had been in the public security department for so long, and had seen some elite soldiers from the armed police and the military, but even these people didn't seem to be as outrageous as Jiang Tian.

"Did this guy's bullets have eyes?" Song Liguo stammered, speechless.

Gao Xiaolong fell silent.

His face was burning.

It still hurts a little.

What happened?

Who slapped me in the face?

Meanwhile, Jiang Tian was cutting his way through, killing these drug dealers with a single shot.

A group of untrained people, lacking even the most basic military skills, just ordinary people carrying guns.

Some of them were even already physically exhausted from drug use.

Their combat effectiveness was appalling.

Plus, Jiang Tian was equipped with thermal imaging, moving like a machine gun in the dark, and his golden skill made him unerring.

Slaughter.

"Who's there? Don't come any closer!"

"Damn it, there's a sniper!"

"What the hell? Where did the sniper come from?"

These drug dealers weren't stupid.

As drug dealers fell dead one by one in the darkness within a short time,

they realized what was happening.

Firing would reveal their approximate location.

The drug dealers' gazes immediately shifted from the anti-narcotics team members to Jiang Tian's direction.

And Jiang Tian, ​​like a deathly ghost in the dense forest and the dead of night, silently reaped lives.

These were the culprits who deserved to be torn to pieces, the culprits who had tormented countless families.

They deserved to die.

Bang bang bang!!!

Just then, a dense hail of bullets swept in, and Jiang Tian hurriedly dodged behind a tree for cover.

"Thirty-four now."

Snap!!!

Jiang Tian hid behind a tree, mentally calculating his gains for the night, and casually swapped out his empty magazine.

He cocked his gun, opened fire in bursts, and quickly stood up and raised his weapon.

Bang bang bang!!!

Four more drug dealers met their end in the Northwest.

"Damn, that's too brutal."



Chapter 10 The Sea of ​​Clouds Trembles


A residential area with excellent greenery.

At this moment, bursts of arguing could be heard coming from inside.

"I just received news that Xiao Tian has been personally supervised by Chief Gao to the front lines. Luckily, he's not on the front lines, but rather flanking," Jiang Peng sighed deeply.

Looking at the woman sitting on the sofa with her head bowed, Jiang Peng sighed softly, his expression complex.

"I'm sorry, I really didn't know. The person who answered the phone was Chief Gao from Beijing," Jiang's mother admitted, bowing her head.

"Never mind, there's no point in saying all this now. Let's hope tonight's operation goes smoothly," Jiang Peng sighed again.

In the end, it was all for Jiang Tian.

It was just a bit of bad luck.

"But I'm still a little worried. Xiaotian is just an intern, not even a full-time employee yet. Am I wrong for doing all this? Now he's being supervised by Chief Gao. Xiaotian is a newbie, his first real combat experience... sob sob..." Jiang's mother clutched her chest, deeply uneasy, sensing something terrible was about to happen. She eventually broke down in tears.

"Chief Gao is a good person. He wouldn't take revenge on someone and deliberately send Jiang Tian to his death, so don't worry too much. Besides, over a hundred armed police officers and all the members of the Yunhai Anti-Drug Task Force are deployed tonight. There's no chance of anything unexpected happening," Jiang Peng reassured her.

Jiang's mother felt slightly relieved.

But the next moment, Jiang Peng's phone rang.

The next moment.

Buzz!!!

After fully understanding the contents of the call, Jiang Peng felt a wave of dizziness wash over him, almost fainting.

Jiang Peng's face grew increasingly pale.

Yunhai Police Station.

Brightly lit.

Jiang Peng, as the police chief of Yunhai and also the deputy mayor, looked extremely anxious.

"Contact the army, the armed police, and the resting criminal investigation teams—all go and provide support! Hurry, hurry!" Jiang Peng's blood was boiling with excitement.

So many major events had happened today.

Originally, Jiang Peng was supposed to be present for tonight's operation, even during the meeting, but because of that phone call from Jiang Tian's mother...

Jiang Peng was directly blocked and targeted by Gao Xiaolong.

In other words, he wasn't required to participate in tonight's operation.

He had been anxiously sitting at home, unable to sit still.

Then, the secretary called him directly, explaining the situation on the ground.

Jiang Peng's scalp tingled. He rushed to the police station, where Secretary Yunhai was already there.

His expression was extremely serious and urgent.

After making arrangements...

Secretary Yunhai patted Jiang Peng on the shoulder and said, "Don't worry, we've deployed quite a few people. We just investigated and confirmed that it was the younger brother of that drug lord in Tucha who was arrested. Those drug lords were there to rescue Tucha's brother. The initial reports were just a smokescreen. The army's special operations team has already gone there. Don't worry, there won't be any problems."

Actually, despite saying this,

Secretary Yunhai was also uneasy.

Danger.

Too dangerous.

Especially the safety of Commander Gao.

"How long until the army arrives?" Jiang Peng asked.

"Most of the troops went to the exercise next door today. The nearest reinforcements will arrive in about an hour," Secretary Yunhai said.

"An hour?"

Jiang Peng immediately stood up.

It's too late to say anything now. Whether it's recalling police officers, launching an emergency operation, or getting military support, it's simply too late.

"It's insane! Tucha's brother was killed by a stray bullet during the rescue, so Tucha is now retaliating," Secretary Yunhai said, leading Jiang Peng into the car.

The convoy quickly converged in front of the police station.

"This is all we can bring. The others are still on their way. Let's go check the situation first," Secretary Yunhai said.

Secretary Yunhai's real name is Zhou Zhao.

Normally, Zhou Zhao and Jiang Peng's relationship wasn't particularly good, but aside from work-related matters, they rarely contacted each other.

Tonight, however, was very unusual.

Zhou Zhao held Jiang Peng's hand, his face filled with urgency. Jiang Peng sensed something was amiss.

"Secretary Zhou, how many drug dealers are there?" Jiang Peng asked heavily.

Zhou Zhao sighed, then gave a number.

Buzz!!!

Jiang Peng was completely stunned.

At first, it was just said to be a drug trap, that the intelligence was wrong, but now, after hearing the number of people...

Jiang Peng's scalp tingled.

"The armed police have over a hundred drug dealers, and our Yunhai anti-drug squad has nearly two hundred, including a group of foreign forces, suspected mercenaries," Zhou Zhao said.

Wow!!!

Jiang Peng's face turned pale.

So, what about Jiang Tian?

A terrifying, ominous premonition rose in Jiang Peng's heart.

Besides Jiang Tian, ​​he instantly understood why Zhou Zhao had acted this way.

Because Gao Xiaolong was with the anti-drug squad, and if something happened to him...

Jiang Peng didn't even want to think about the consequences.

However, one thing was certain: if something happened to Gao Xiaolong, the entire Yunhai, from top to bottom, the officialdom would experience a terrifying earthquake.

Everyone, including Zhou Zhao, would be affected.

“There are no outsiders here; we're all in this together now,” Zhou Zhao said.

He went to the scene.

Zhou Zhao and Jiang Peng, along with the few combat-ready personnel from the police station, went to the scene.

The incident happened suddenly.

No one expected these drug traffickers to have set a trap.

In fact, neither Zhou Zhao nor Jiang Peng said anything, because they knew it was over.

Going to the scene now was merely a prelude.

By the time they arrived, the anti-narcotics team would likely be caught off guard.

More than three times the manpower, plus a team of professional foreign mercenaries.

Those people were ruthless killers, professionals in murder!

“Secretary, I’m sorry,” Jiang Peng apologized, his voice trembling.

Because he knew that his son Jiang Tian’s death meant little to others.

But Gao Xiaolong, because of a phone call from Jiang’s mother, had personally supervised Jiang Tian to the front lines.

This meant that if Gao Xiaolong was killed, he couldn’t escape responsibility.

As things stand, even if they arrived, all they could do was collect the bodies.

"It's too late to say anything now. Xiao Tian, ​​I've seen the file. After all, he's an intern who hasn't been promoted yet. It's normal to ask for leniency. It's not your fault. If Chief Gao knew about this, he wouldn't be so angry," Zhou Zhao sighed.

At this point, it's too late to say anything.

Gao Xiaolong, and the Narcotics Control Team.

Thinking of this,

Zhou Zhao was filled with worry about his bleak future.

Jiang Peng felt a pang of heartache thinking of his son, Jiang Tian.

He only had one son and one daughter in his life.

His daughter had just been admitted to a prestigious university.

Jiang Tian had also graduated from police academy. No one had expected this turn of events.

"Please accept my condolences," Zhou Zhao said, looking out the window.

Hearing these two words, Jiang Peng was shaken.

Because he knew that the anti-drug squad was probably finished.



Chapter 11: One Battle, One Hundred and Fifty Drug Dealers Annihilated, Shocking


They had prepared for the worst.

Based on the information and situation they had received, the situation at the front lines was dire.

Both Jiang Tian and Gao Xiaolong were likely in grave danger.

Whether they survived was entirely up to fate.

As for the thirty-five members of the anti-drug squad, they couldn't withstand them.

This was because the drug traffickers had targeted them from the beginning.

Thirty-five against nearly two hundred.

And that was under siege.

Zhou Zhao and Jiang Peng grew increasingly heavy-hearted. Something terrible had happened; this was a major disaster.

A disaster that would shake the heavens and earth.

If the casualties were severe, it was safe to say that even without Gao Xiaolong, they would bear enormous responsibility.

With Gao Xiaolong involved, the devastating impact would be arguably the most damaging and egregious case in recent decades.

When they finally arrived,

they saw a silent jungle in the distance.

This silent jungle instilled a deep sense of dread.

It felt like the gaping maw of a demon.

“Sir, it’s dangerous up ahead. Furthermore, our communication with the anti-narcotics team has been cut off. Those drug dealers are clearly prepared. We can’t just rush in,” said Sun Jianhua, the deputy director of the Public Security Bureau, sitting in the passenger seat, his voice heavy.

“Something’s not right,” Jiang Peng said, getting out of the car and looking ahead.

“How far are we from the ambush site?” Zhou Zhao asked.

The deputy director, standing beside them, knew the situation perfectly well: “About two li (approximately 1.5 kilometers).”

Two li?

A jolt ran through them!

Jiang Peng and Gao Xiaolong turned deathly pale upon hearing the deputy director’s words.

It’s over.

The sky has fallen.

That was the only thought in their minds.

Jiang Peng felt dizzy and almost collapsed to the ground.

Fortunately, the deputy director reached out to help him up.

“These damn drug dealers, they deserve to die! Aren’t they afraid we’ll provoke them and send the army across the border to wipe them out?” Zhou Zhao roared furiously.

The armed police wouldn’t be a problem for the time being, but the most dangerous situation was actually with the anti-narcotics squad.

Two miles away.

No matter what, they could hear gunfire.

But now.

“Damn it, these drug dealers deserve to die!” Jiang Peng clenched his fists, his eyes bloodshot.

The gunfire stopped. In their minds, the anti-narcotics squad was completely wiped out.

They were already annihilated.

As for wiping out more than two hundred drug dealers and a foreign mercenary group.

Thirty-five members of the anti-narcotics squad?

Don’t be ridiculous.

They hadn’t even dared to imagine it.

Even if the special forces came, they probably wouldn’t be able to defeat them tonight.

"Ask when the army reinforcements will arrive. I'll make them pay for their crimes in blood." Zhou Zhao gritted his teeth, then paused before continuing, "The anti-drug squad are all heroes. We can't let their sacrifices be in vain."

He knew.

Now everything was over.

The entire Yunhai province, from top to bottom, had been completely reshuffled. He, Zhou Zhao, as the Yunhai Party Secretary, was undeniably responsible.

This was the provincial capital, and he, as the top official, held a high-ranking position—a provincial party committee cadre.

But in this situation, he couldn't escape blame.

Forget about any future advancement; he was likely to be completely stripped of his position.

Because the situation was too dire; no one could escape it.

“Send the criminal investigation team to infiltrate and investigate,” Jiang Peng said through gritted teeth, almost enunciating each word.

The criminal investigation captain and his men were about to move when…

The next moment…

A series of footsteps approached.

They were especially loud in the darkness.

Almost everyone quickly found cover and prepared for battle.

“Damn it, these drug dealers came too fast,” Zhou Zhao thought, already assuming the drug dealers had arrived.

Everyone assumed the anti-narcotics squad had been wiped out.

The criminal investigation team members who had been brought along loaded their guns and aimed at the source of the sound.

Then they held their breath.

“I don’t care what methods you use, hold these drug dealers off until the army arrives,” Zhou Zhao ordered.

“Mission accomplished,” the criminal investigation captain promised solemnly.

Even though they only sent twenty men.

The next moment, Zhang, from the Criminal Investigation Detachment, said heavily, "Don't worry, leader. I won't let the Narcotics Control Detachment's sacrifice be in vain, nor will I let Captain Song's sacrifice be in vain. I'll hold them off even with my life."

"Good." Zhou Zhao nodded gently.

But before they finished speaking,

the indistinct figures on the distant path gradually became clearer.

When their outlines finally came into view,

"Wait, what's that?" Zhou Zhao's whole body trembled.

The moon was exceptionally round tonight.

Under the moonlight, the ground appeared unusually bright.

While not as bright as during the day, at least people within a ten-meter radius were clearly visible.

Even dozens of meters away, some outlines could be seen.

To be honest,

the moonlight tonight mirrored Gao Xiaolong's mood, from the initial dark clouds to the current moonlight bathing the earth.

The rain had stopped, the sky had cleared, and the feeling of surviving a disaster brought Gao Xiaolong no excitement.

Because even now, until it was all over, Gao Xiaolong still felt, in a daze, that he was dreaming.

Gao Xiaolong believed he was probably ill.

And very ill, trapped in a deep dream; otherwise, how could everything be so vivid?

In his dream.

He witnessed a drug enforcement officer, not even finished his probationary period, carrying a gun, getting headshots with every shot.

A CS:GO pro?

Even a pro couldn't do that.

Like a tiger among sheep, growing stronger with each battle.

He dreamt of that probationary officer, driving a fully automatic rifle—or perhaps semi-automatic, perhaps due to the rapid firing—who, even when drug dealers were pressing in,

wielded a single sweep, killing more than twenty people, every shot a headshot.

Gao Xiaolong frequently organized military exercises between the police and the army.

He had also witnessed many elite soldiers.

But none of those elite soldiers could compare to the guy in his dream.

He had seen elite soldiers of the entire army, the kind who could effortlessly switch targets with one hand and sweep through the entire force, but he felt they were far inferior to the person in his dream.

Because this person had single-handedly killed 130 drug dealers in a short period of time, and also killed two mercenaries. All the drug dealers fled for their lives, and he relentlessly pursued them, ultimately succeeding in his mission.

The total kill count stopped at 148, using 150 bullets. Even the two empty bullets hit their targets.

In short, he thought he was sick.

In a daze, he silently walked at the front, wondering when the dream would end.

Even after they emerged from the dense forest, his dream hadn't ended.

In a daze.

After walking out with his hands behind his back, he saw a group of police officers, led by Xiao Zhou, excitedly approaching him.

*Slap!*

Gao Xiaolong slapped him.

His hand hurt; he wasn't dreaming.

He was happy because he wasn't sick; it all seemed real.

The trainee policeman Jiang Tian, ​​whom he had deliberately targeted, was a sharpshooter.

A top-tier sharpshooter.

"It wasn't a dream. It was all real after all," Gao Xiaolong muttered to himself, looking at his hand.

"Old Gao, you're alive! I'm not dreaming." The slap jolted Zhou Zhao awake.

It brought Zhou Zhao back to his senses instantly, tears welling in his eyes.

Alive.

Old Gao was actually alive.

Thank God.

"Yes, I wasn't dreaming either," Gao Xiaolong said silently.

If he wasn't dreaming, then it was all real.

Thinking back to his own words cursing Jiang Tian as a black sheep,

Gao Xiaolong felt a pang of guilt.

This wasn't a black sheep; he was a police god!

"By the way, Old Gao, don't worry, the army will be here soon. They'll definitely take care of those drug dealers. You guys run first, we'll hold them off," Zhou Zhao quickly tried to salvage the situation.

The intelligence was wrong; it was their fault.

In Yunhai, the chaotic situation had already aroused dissatisfaction from above.

Especially with the increasing number of drug dealers, the more they were arrested, the more they found, and the drug dealers were resorting to any means necessary.

As the first line of defense in the fight against drugs, and also the first line of defense in the country.

Gao Xiaolong came all the way from Kyoto specifically to inspect the site.

Zhou Zhao, already displeased with his superiors, naturally wanted to make amends after this incident.

“Drug dealers?” Gao Xiaolong’s face showed a moment of confusion upon hearing these two words.

“Yes, drug dealers. Don’t worry, Mr. Gao, you’re safe now that we’re here,” Zhou Zhao quickly said.

“Where are the drug dealers?” Gao Xiaolong asked instinctively.

Hmm?

Zhou Zhao’s heart skipped a beat, his face paled. He was already wondering if Mr. Gao had been injured in the battle, suffered amnesia, or perhaps had a gunshot wound to the head; otherwise, how could he ask such a question?

As for the present moment.

Jiang Peng’s first thought was to find his beloved son.

A large group of people followed behind Gao Xiaolong; a rough glance revealed at least thirty people.

Some were injured, some were being carried.

There were casualties, about four or five people.

After all, bullets have no eyes on the battlefield. Even if Jiang Tian is a sharpshooter, it still takes time.

When the fighting started, facing attacks from both sides, it was inevitable that several people would be hit by bullets from all directions.

After all, this is the anti-drug police.

Beneath this peaceful exterior, in this tranquil world, there are always many, many lovely people silently bearing the burden.

In battle, there can be no deaths or injuries.

This was already a million times better than Jiang Peng had anticipated.

But among those who sacrificed their lives, was Jiang Tian among them?

Jiang Peng's heart was heavy, his legs felt like they weighed a ton, incredibly heavy.

He was also extremely uneasy.

"Good morning, Chief."

"Chief."

The anti-drug squad members greeted Jiang Peng.

Jiang Peng nodded with a smile, but deep down, his unease grew, each step heavy and trembling.

Finally.

In the next moment.

He saw him, he saw Jiang Tian.

From the very beginning, Jiang Tian hadn't told anyone he was the chief's son when he joined the anti-drug squad.

It was an unspoken rule; no matter how powerful your background, within the system, you had to keep a low profile.

Now, Jiang Tian saw his son, truly saw him, as if surrounded by stars, holding a gun, his face showing a newfound resilience.

Good.

Good, good, good.

Jiang Peng smiled. Having experienced the horrors of war, he clearly felt that his beloved son had completely changed; if he had to describe it, he had been tempered.

But why did everyone around him leave such a large space for Jiang Tian? What was the purpose? Isolation?

Jiang Peng frowned, his mood slightly heavy.

After today's events, Jiang Peng had come to a realization.

Perhaps some things couldn't be forced.

If you don't have the ability, don't force someone to help; otherwise, it's not helping him, it's harming him.

"Perhaps, letting this child settle down, get married, have children, work in an office, and live an ordinary life is a good choice," Jiang Peng thought.

He had already considered removing Jiang Tian from the front lines, relegating him to a lower-level position, making him a regular office worker, or even, if that didn't work out, a lowly police officer in the household registration office—that would be a decent option.

After today's events, Jiang Peng had come to a decision.

He decided to find Gao Xiaolong later to admit his mistake, take responsibility, and promise to transfer Jiang Tian to the household registration office as a junior police officer as punishment.

Turning his head, Jiang Peng caught a glimpse of Gao Xiaolong looking at his son.

His expression was complex.

Then, Jiang Peng looked at himself and sighed inwardly.

His son's future was completely ruined, and his own future was utterly destroyed.

Thinking this, Jiang Peng pulled Song Liguo to the roadside, offered him a cigarette, and took a deep drag, saying, "Old Song, I thank you for taking care of Xiao Jiang. I'll remember your kindness and repay you if I have the chance."

He knew that Jiang Tian was just a fresh graduate, barely an intern.

In such a dangerous situation, Jiang Tian's survival was undoubtedly due to Song Liguo's care.

Jiang Peng accepted this debt of gratitude.

However, Song Liguo lit a cigarette, but his hand, which was smoking, froze completely upon hearing this.

"Have you misunderstood something?"

"Chief, listen to me," Song Liguo tried to explain.

He wanted to explain the incredible feat he witnessed on the battlefield, Jiang Tian's legendary marksmanship.

He wanted to explain how he saw Jiang Tian single-handedly wipe out a hundred or eighty drug dealers.

Every shot was a headshot, every shot was fatal.

Their guns were just blind fire, but Jiang Tian's gun was alive; it could travel to the enemy's head and track the bullet.

Now, even if Jiang Tian claimed to know gunfighting techniques, able to make bullets curve with a flick of the wrist—a complete farce—Song Liguo would believe him.

But just as Song Liguo was about to explain,

Jiang Peng arrived beside Gao Xiaolong.

At that moment, Zhou Zhao was about to anxiously ask Gao Xiaolong if he had injured his head.

Jiang Peng's arrival interrupted him.

It also interrupted Gao Xiaolong, who was lost in thought, constantly regretting his actions.

"Commander Gao, I was wrong. I hope you can forgive me. I know my crimes are heinous, and I know how terrible this incident was, all because of my son, Jiang Tian. Commander Gao, I also know my son is a black sheep, a cancer in the force, ultimately cowardly and afraid of death."

"Therefore, I hope you will give Jiang Tian a chance to transfer to logistics. I've already decided to have him work in the household registration office as a junior officer. If you have any objections, I can have him leave the force."

Jiang Peng's words were extremely sincere.

They were filled with apology, regret, and remorse, seemingly regretting his impulsive decision to let his son join the police force.

Therefore, he was now deeply repentant, and if punishing Jiang Tian alone wasn't enough, he would punish him as well.

Anger.

Jiang Peng's heart sank.

He understood; being adept at reading people, his mood grew even heavier. He saw the burning flames of anger in Gao Xiaolong's eyes.

This made his hands and feet cold.



Chapter 12 The Hexagonal Warrior: Invincible Upon Emerging from the Mountain


The atmosphere was somewhat silent. Even Zhou Zhao, at this moment, looked at Gao Xiaolong with slightly tense eyes.

Gao Xiaolong held a very high position.

He was a true figure from heaven, a person whose word carried immense weight within the public security system!

Even Zhou Zhao, the municipal party secretary with a high-ranking official rank, dared not utter a single word at this moment.

After Jiang Peng finished speaking, he dared not say anything more.

But Gao Xiaolong felt as if the sky had fallen.

The sky had fallen.

They've rebelled.

They've all rebelled.

You, Handong, have utterly rebelled.

"Xiao Tian is a black sheep, I know. As his father, I didn't correct him in time. I'm also at fault. He's a cancer in the front-line team. But even as a cancer, I hope Chief Gao can give him a chance," Jiang Peng pleaded.

This request was perfectly reasonable.

Even Gao Xiaolong couldn't detect anything amiss. It was a perfectly reasonable request; did he have any reason to refuse?

Bullshit!!!

Gao Xiaolong awoke with a start.

The world had turned upside down.

This world was in chaos.

Because someone was actually trying to remove his war god from his police force.

"Insolence..."

Gao Xiaolong roared.

The entire room fell silent.

Jiang Peng trembled, his eyes flashing. Was Chief Gao really going to hold on tight, refusing even this small request?

Jiang Peng's heart grew heavier.

Just then, military reinforcements arrived, quickly passing by and heading towards the site of the recent battle.

And the military leader, who had appeared behind them at some point,

was frowning deeply.

Having arrived here to request backup, he felt a chill run down his spine upon learning the situation, and his heart ached for the Yunhai anti-drug police.

But upon arriving, he seemed to see a familiar face.

Although the military wasn't part of the official system, Gao Xiaolong was someone who frequently appeared on camera at national conferences.

Gao Xiaolong was alright?

A pleasant surprise.

The military leaders also felt a sense of relief.

But the next moment, Gao Xiaolong's voice rang out.

Instantly, the military leaders were jolted.

Gao Xiaolong's face was grim, like the calm before the storm.

The military leaders understood. They knew that even if Commander Gao survived tonight's events, the leaders of Yunhai would likely face repercussions.
