They didn't know the extent of the repercussions, and the military leaders silently prayed for the leaders and police force of Yunhai.

As expected.

Gao Xiaolong was enraged.

In a fit of anger, he suddenly became furious.

He questioned in an extremely angry tone, "You actually want Comrade Xiao Jiang to leave the front-line team? What are your intentions?"

Huh?

Jiang Peng, who was feeling down, looked up in astonishment.

Zhou Zhao, who had been silently grieving for Jiang Peng behind him and plotting how to sever ties with him, also changed his expression.

Initially, he thought that since Gao Xiaolong was in trouble, Zhou Zhao and Jiang Peng were no different—they were in the same boat—so he was very friendly towards Jiang Peng. Because if Gao Xiaolong was in trouble, it would be a devastating blow to everyone, and no one could avoid it.

But Gao Xiaolong survived and wanted to investigate. In his rage, he implicated Jiang Peng, so he needed to sever ties with Jiang Peng to ensure his own safety.

This was simply a basic human instinct to avoid harm.

He was already in the back, ready to watch the show, but Gao Xiaolong's tone was off, very off.

This didn't seem like he was settling scores.

The next moment, Gao Xiaolong's voice, filled with fury and anger, rang out: "Do you know how much contribution Xiao Jiang made?"

Contribution?

Jiang Peng looked confused. Jiang Tian? Had he performed exceptionally well?

Gao Xiaolong's angry questioning continued: "Do you know that without Jiang Tian, ​​we would all have perished there?"

Huh?

Jiang Peng's heart skipped a beat.

Zhou Zhao was even more horrified. What was Chief Gao saying?

"And do you know that in this battle, Comrade Jiang single-handedly faced over two hundred drug dealers, fired one hundred and fifty bullets, and killed one hundred and forty-eight drug dealers?" Gao Xiaolong said, enunciating each word clearly.

Buzz!!!

It exploded.

Hiss!!!

Zhou Zhao staggered, almost falling to the ground.

The military leader took two steps back, stunned by the words.

As for Jiang Peng, he was completely bewildered, his mind blank.

Completely blank.

What was Commander Gao saying?

Comrade Jiang, is that Jiang Tian?

One gun, perfect accuracy, single-handedly facing over two hundred drug dealers, including mercenaries, and killing one hundred and forty-eight drug dealers?

Buzz!!!

As the police chief, Jiang Peng knew the concept of gunfire.

During the War of Resistance Against Japan, many veterans of ten years of war probably didn't even have double-digit kill counts.

And now, what did he hear?

An automatic rifle, not a sniper rifle. An automatic rifle, that's a short-range submachine gun.

A sniper rifle could never do that, yet an automatic rifle accomplished it with a single shot?

Wait.

It seems Chief Gao meant more than just that.

Gao Xiaolong's gaze swept over him, his voice almost laced with sarcasm: "We were attacked from both sides by mercenaries and drug dealers. Comrade Xiao Jiang, alone, went deep behind enemy lines, and you... you actually said Comrade Xiao Jiang was a cancer, a black sheep? You slander our hero like this, you suppress our police god like this, what are your intentions?"

Staggering.

Jiang Peng took a step back.

Was this done by his own son?

Jiang Peng was somewhat bewildered.

Zhou Zhao's gaze turned to the distance; that dark figure seemed to be Jiang Tian.

He had seen him before.

During the operation, Chief Gao paid special attention, so he had specifically observed and learned about the individual: average police academy grades, average combat skills, average drill abilities.

A mediocre and ordinary person.

Such a miraculous feat, accomplished by a police academy intern?

No, this was a dream; Chief Gao was playing a joke on them.

At this moment, Song Liguo, the branch captain, could no longer hold back and stepped forward to rebuke, "Mayor Jiang, although we usually have a good relationship, I absolutely cannot tolerate you insulting our police hero, our savior. If it weren't for Comrade Jiang, we would all have been wiped out by the drug traffickers."

Hiss!!!

Another confirmation.

Everyone was processing this shocking news.

This left the arriving military leaders utterly bewildered.

If he hadn't recognized Gao Xiaolong, he would have thought the Yunhai police were putting on a show for him.

As a military leader, he understood all too well what this achievement meant; it was an impossible miracle.

The next moment.

A soldier jogged over, stood at attention, and saluted, reporting, "Report! We've just inspected the battle scene. A total of 167 drug dealers were apprehended. Five are still alive but have been shot; 14 died from gunshot wounds; and 148 were killed instantly by a single shot to the head."

Hiss!!!

It's true.

This is actually real.

Those seriously wounded and killed drug dealers must have been the ones Jiang Tian single-handedly wiped out after the remaining anti-drug squad rushed in.

At the same time, this incident will serve as a terrifying deterrent to all unscrupulous drug dealers.

Wait...

If all of this is true...

The military leader's eyes instantly blazed with fervor.

Just now, he seemed to have overheard someone say that Jiang Tian was a cancer within the unit.

A black sheep?

Such a formidable figure, your police force is too proud to accept him, but the military wants him.

"Commander Gao, I am the commander of the 346th Regiment stationed in Yunhai, I..." the military leader said excitedly, leaning forward.

"Shut up, get out." Gao Xiaolong didn't give him a chance to speak: "When I asked you for support, it was either windy or rainy. Now our police hero has finally shown us his mettle with a single shot, and you dare to come up here, harboring any improper thoughts."

A moment later, Gao Xiaolong's eyes seemed to devour him as he spoke: "If you dare to lay a hand on me, I dare to chop off your hand."

There was murderous intent.

The commander of the 346th Regiment was shaken, but such achievements, such a heroic figure, even the best soldiers in the entire army would have to give way.

He couldn't let him go.

Gao Xiaolong ignored him and instead looked at Jiang Peng, who was now cowering and timid.

Gao Xiaolong's heart sank. He never expected that his son, a police prodigy and a hero, would be such a coward.

However, considering Jiang Peng had nurtured such talent for the police force,

Gao Xiaolong decided, well, he would forgive him for now.

With Gao Xiaolong's declaration, Zhou Zhao strode forward, leading his men towards Jiang Tian.

It was confirmed.

If it were true.

Zhou Zhao could hardly contain his shock. He seemed to see a rising, dazzling police prodigy ascending.

Meanwhile,

Jiang Tian was still tallying up today's gains.

He made a fortune.

He truly made a killing.

Tonight, the entire Yunhai was in a frenzy.

Tonight, the incident sent shockwaves through Kyoto, prompting an immediate inquiry to Gao Xiaolong.

After confirming the details, they were even more stunned.

Upon returning, Jiang Tian went directly to the police station.

There, he worked with the narcotics squad and Chief Gao to prepare a combat report.

The only thing that left Jiang Tian slightly disappointed was that the damned Tu Cha hadn't shown up at all.

If he had eliminated Tu Cha, Jiang Tian couldn't even imagine how many crime points he would have gained.

But now, Jiang Tian was quite satisfied.

After all, greed knows no bounds.

Working late into the night, Jiang Peng didn't tell his mother about the day's events when he got home, only mentioning Jiang Tian's meritorious service.

Jiang Tian returned to his room and quickly tallied his gains.

A bountiful harvest.

"Open the panel," Jiang Tian exclaimed excitedly.

[Unfailing accuracy (Gold)]

[Insight into people's hearts (Green) - Scanning radar (Gold)]

[Martial arts minor achievement (Green) - Martial arts master (Red)]

[Strong physique (Green)] [Disguise minor achievement] [Superior memory (Green)] [Gambling skills minor achievement (Green)]...

[Sin value: 1200]

He glanced at his panel.

Two gold, one red, and numerous green stats.

Most of the stats, like "Theft prodigy," had been combined by Jiang Tian, ​​while the useless ones were only partially combined, so at a glance...

A sea of ​​green.

A huge profit.

After eliminating over a hundred drug dealers, this was Jiang Tian's entire haul.

Much of it was money, which Jiang Tian used to upgrade his equipment.

For example, the gold-tier scanning radar was dropped by the drug dealer Jiang Tian initially killed, and Jiang Tian prioritized upgrading it.

The scanning radar allows Jiang Tian to directly sense any criminal within a kilometer radius.

Or rather, with a thought, a kilometer-wide area becomes a map, and no criminal within that radius can escape his detection.

This is practically a divine skill; prioritizing its upgrade during combat was solely for Jiang Tian's convenience in eliminating drug dealers.

No disguise can escape Jiang Tian's notice.

Next, he upgraded to the red-tier Martial Arts Master, just one step away from gold.

Martial Arts Master—Jiang Tian can now say that almost all fighting skills and techniques existing in the world, such as eye-gouging and groin kicks, are lethal moves.

Combined with a strong physique...

Although it was green, it still placed him among the top-tier special forces.

This acquisition transformed Jiang Tian into an all-around invincible combat force.

He was a true all-rounder.

With a slight improvement in his physical attributes, surpassing human limits, Jiang Tian would be utterly invincible.

It felt great.

Of course, these things were secondary.

The most important thing was that it changed his destiny.

A significant destiny.

The next morning.

Jiang Tian opened his eyes and saw the ceiling.

It wasn't the despairing scene of his previous life. He realized then that he had truly been reborn, not dreaming.

"Xiao Tian, ​​dinner's ready," his mother's gentle voice rang out.

"Coming, Mom." Jiang Tian's eyes were slightly moist.

This was the voice he had longed to hear day and night, in his midnight dreams, in his previous life.

He sat down at the dining table.

Jiang Peng ate his morning breakfast while his mother poured millet porridge for Jiang Tian and peeled an egg, handing it to him.

At that moment, tears welled up in Jiang Tian's eyes.

In his past life, Gao Xiaolong had died in the battle the previous night.

Jiang Peng was immediately suspended from his duties and placed under investigation the following day.

Jiang Tian was even placed on leave at home to await the investigation.

Following this, Jiang Tian's mother was also placed under investigation and sentenced.

Yes, you read that right.

Sentenced to two years in prison.

Sentenced for abuse of power.

In his previous life, Jiang Tian's life was a complete disaster; fate had utterly plunged him into despair.

His mother, imprisoned and consumed by grief, fell seriously ill and died shortly after her release.

Jiang Peng, also devastated by his mother's death, succumbed to despair and passed away a few years later.

Jiang Tian was left a destitute ghost, wandering the world aimlessly.

Until he encountered that woman.

During Jiang Tian's years of depression and illness, that woman uttered these words:

"Useless trash. You don't deserve to have a child. This child belongs to Brother Xiao. I'm not afraid to tell you, the child I've raised for over ten years is Brother Xiao's. Since you're about to die, I'm not afraid to tell you either. Every time we did it, I secretly took medication. You're useless, your whole family is useless, you don't deserve to remain in this world."

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian clenched his fists, his eyes flashing with a chilling light: "Wang Yifei, are you ready for my revenge?"

And Xiao Bo.



Chapter 13 Beating Up the Enemy


"Xiao Tian, ​​you're riding high right now, but you need to be careful. Keep a low profile. Sometimes, being too flashy isn't a good thing," Jiang Peng advised Jiang Tian while eating breakfast.

These were lessons learned from experience.

Jiang Tian understood this all too well.

Being too flashy attracts too much jealousy.

This is true everywhere.

Especially in his past life.

Jiang Tian clenched his fist. In his past life, Jiang Tian treated Xiao Bo like a brother.

In fact, after his family fell from grace, Jiang Tian could have secured some connections thanks to his parents' influence.

However, he used all those connections to propel Xiao Bo to his position.

While some of the connections left by his parents were due to Wang Yifei's influence, the majority stemmed from the bond between Jiang Tian and Xiao Bo, whom he considered a brother.

He entrusted all of these connections to Xiao Bo without reservation.

And in the end, he was completely deceived.

But now, thank goodness.

"By the way, there's one more thing. Regarding your colleague Xiao Bo, I've already arranged his promotion. If all goes well, it should be resolved completely in a few days," Jiang Peng suddenly said while eating.

This speaks volumes about Xiao Bo's hypocrisy. Even a leader like Jiang Peng couldn't see through Xiao Bo's true character.

If Jiang Tian hadn't been reborn, he would never have dreamed that Xiao Bo could do such a thing.

"What's wrong, Xiao Tian? You're unhappy. Didn't you beg me about this several times?" Jiang Peng asked, puzzled.

Because he saw that Jiang Tian's expression wasn't very clear, and even the mention of Xiao Bo's name emanated a chilling aura.

That was killing intent.

After Jiang Tian slaughtered over a hundred drug dealers, his own aura, from the inside out, unconsciously carried a murderous intent, extremely intimidating.

"I begged you?" Jiang Tian was stunned.

As Jiang Tian pondered his memories, he finally realized what had happened.

In his past life, such an incident had indeed occurred. Although Xiao Bo had tried every means to obstruct it, that bitch Wang Yifei had been constantly whispering in his ear.

Therefore, Jiang Tian had repeatedly assured Xiao Bo that he could definitely help him resolve his promotion issue.

He had been truly foolish.

Jiang Tian wanted to slap himself a few times. If he weren't stupid, how could he have done something so idiotic? It was obvious that the two of them had conspired together—one whispering in his ear, the other pretending to be pure and noble, declining the promotion, and acting all innocent.

Not only had he not seen through it, but he had even valued Xiao Bo more.

He was truly foolish.

If it weren't for that incident before his rebirth.

If it weren't for…

Yes, and Jiang Yu.

“Wang Yifei was so aloof before, but suddenly she's all over me. She's probably already pregnant with that bastard Xiao Bo's child, and she's coming to me to be her dumping ground.” Jiang Tian’s forehead veins throbbed.

“Xiao Tian.” Jiang Peng frowned slightly.

Jiang Tian realized what was going on: “Dad, let’s forget about Xiao Bo’s promotion.”

“Why?” Jiang Peng asked.

“Dad, Xiao Bo told me before that he doesn’t like using connections. I thought about it, and I can’t force him, so let’s just leave it at that.” Jiang Tian lowered his head to eat, trying to hide his murderous intent.

“Alright, hurry up and eat. Xiao Bo is a good kid. Although he reminded me yesterday to call Captain Song to take care of you, it was a good intention that backfired, but Xiao Bo was only doing it for your own good.” Jiang’s mother said with a smile.

Swish!!!

Almost instantly.

Jiang Peng’s sharp gaze fell on Jiang’s mother.

Jiang Tian stared intently at his mother.

Because in his previous life, he had never heard his mother mention this matter. No, Jiang Tian suddenly remembered the way his mother looked at him hesitantly after she was released from prison and learned of his situation.

At that time, his mother probably wanted to tell him about this.

But at that time, he didn’t care at all, and was even bragging about his good brother Xiao Bo’s promotion.

Xiao Bo.

Jiang Tian clenched his fist.

Asking for leave, and even needing to pull strings to get his mother promoted.

If Xiao Bo didn't know something beforehand, nobody would believe it; there's only one truth.

Jiang Tian's eyes were low.

Second-generation children, under normal circumstances, enter the system by hiding their identities nine times out of ten. It's an unspoken rule. You can guess, and I know you can guess, but none of you can say it.

Jiang Tian was the same.

Jiang Peng casually mentioned that he would temporarily suspend Xiao Bo's exceptional promotion after returning, and then made no further comment.

But Jiang Tian felt that Jiang Peng must know something.

"Very good, very handsome."

Jiang Tian looked at himself in the mirror. Jiang Peng had already left for work, and Jiang Tian also concealed his identity at work. Basically, apart from Captain Song, his comrades didn't know Jiang Tian's identity.

The police uniform, which he hadn't worn for a long time, was on his body again.

He only saw the figure in the mirror: muscular limbs, upright posture, a fair face with resolute features.

Everyone who saw him would say, "What a handsome young man!"

A new life begins now.

After going downstairs, Jiang Tian got on his little motorcycle.

The millennium had just passed, and the national economy was still developing rapidly despite its relatively low starting point.

Civil servants' salaries weren't high.

While being a narcotics officer was a high-risk profession with good benefits, it was still relatively low. During a time when the whole country was tightening its belt, even frontline narcotics officers in this high-risk profession barely earned enough to support their families.

A typical narcotics officer, including bonuses, would earn around 1,000 yuan a month.

Jiang Tian was an intern, and his salary was only about 500 yuan.

Walking in the cold wind, Jiang Tian saw a Mercedes-Benz pass by, his eyes filled with envy.

Thinking about the drug dealers, all of them were incredibly wealthy, while the lives of narcotics officers were... well, let's just say they were miserable.

This situation presents a significant challenge for narcotics officers, who must constantly resist the temptation of bribes from drug dealers.

Jiang Tian arrived at the police station just in time.

Yesterday, before Jiang Tian left, Gao Xiaolong told him he would have a surprise for him today.

To be honest, Jiang Tian was very much looking forward to it.

A first-class merit award?

Jiang Tian was tempted.

Or, a direct promotion?

Jiang Tian was in a good mood.

“Little Jiang is here.”

“What Little Jiang? Call me brother.”

"Yes, yes, hahaha."

As soon as he entered, his teammates, who had returned yesterday, greeted Jiang Tian with an extremely high level of respect.

There was no way around it; Jiang Tian had, without exaggeration, saved the lives of everyone in the entire anti-drug squad.

Moreover, although their anti-drug department had made mistakes in yesterday's events, the elimination of so many drug dealers, even if not directly related to them, was still a collective achievement.

Therefore, everyone greeted Jiang Tian with almost universal smiles.

Just then, an unexpected voice rang out:

"Jiang Tian, ​​you're here! That's great! I thought you took the day off. I heard that Chief Gao scolded you yesterday, calling you a cancer and a black sheep. What happened?"

The voice was full of concern and care.

The entire anti-drug department fell silent, so quiet you could hear a pin drop.

Jiang Tian's face was full of sarcasm.

He turned to look at Xiao Bo, who sat at his workstation, looking at him with obvious concern.

That's right.

It was Xiao Bo.

This was the man he considered his best brother in his past life.

In reality, all signs pointed to this scoundrel as the root cause of almost everything.

He was outwardly hypocritical, but secretly, he had harmed his entire family.

Especially now, he outwardly showed concern, but what was he really doing?

Yesterday, Chief Gao didn't mention Jiang Tian's name explicitly, only referring to him as a "comrade." With so many people present, who knew it was Jiang Tian?

This also meant that Chief Gao had shown leniency yesterday, giving Jiang Tian a chance.

But today, Xiao Bo directly brought it all up, practically naming him by name in front of everyone.

In other words, if Jiang Tian hadn't performed a major service yesterday, even if Chief Gao returned safely,

the fact that Chief Gao had berated him at the meeting yesterday would still reach everyone's ears through Xiao Bo's mouth.

"That bastard, he probably never dreamed that last night I took down over a hundred drug dealers, and Chief Gao even hailed me as a police god."

Jiang Tian's eyes flashed, but inwardly he sneered at Xiao Bo.

Jiang Tian and Xiao Bo graduated from the same school, but Xiao Bo was two years older than Jiang Tian. They had always been good friends, and from the beginning, Xiao Bo even knew Jiang Tian's true identity.

Xiao Bo had been the one cultivating his relationship.

But in his past life, he was truly stupid and deserved to die; he hadn't seen through this man's disgusting face.

"Xiao Bo, what are you doing? Did you take the wrong medicine?" Zhao Wei frowned and stood up abruptly.

Xiao Bo quickly rubbed his mouth a couple of times, apologizing profusely, "My bad, my bad, I deserve a beating. I forgot, I let it slip. Xiao Tian, ​​how about this, I'll treat you to a meal tonight, and that'll be over. Um, Xiao Tian, ​​go get me a glass of water, I'm a little thirsty. I'll continue teaching you anti-drug techniques later."

These words were spoken.

Jiang Tian almost laughed.

He looked at Xiao Bo, who sat there calmly, showing no remorse whatsoever.

In his past life, back in school, Xiao Bo was an outstanding student and the vice president of the student council.

Jiang Tian's grades were average, so after joining the anti-drug squad, he always followed Xiao Bo around, learning from him.

This was also why Jiang Tian had been so open and honest with Xiao Bo.

But now...

He'd seen Xiao Bo's true colors.

Jiang Tian walked over expressionlessly.

"Xiao Tian, ​​I'm a little thirsty. Didn't you hear me ask you to get me a glass of water?" Xiao Bo said, his brow slightly furrowed.

He frowned deeply, sensing something was off about Jiang Tian today.

"What, you made a mistake, and you think you can cover it up with just a few words?" Jiang Tian sneered.

"Xiao Tian, ​​I've noticed a serious problem with your attitude. This needs to be corrected. How can you be a qualified narcotics officer with such a narrow mind?" Xiao Bo frowned, somewhat annoyed.

"Are you a narcotics officer?" Jiang Tian asked.

"Jiang Tian, ​​what do you want? This is working hours. This is the narcotics squad, not a place for you to vent your emotions." Xiao Bo slammed his hand on the table and shouted angrily.

After saying that...

Xiao Bo waited quietly for Jiang Tian to apologize.

This had happened many times before.

But every time he got even slightly angry, Jiang Tian would hurriedly apologize and treat him to dinner as an apology.

"Good bastard, daring to get angry at me today, tonight I'll kick Wang Yifei to the curb," Xiao Bo thought, a smirk creeping onto his face.

So what if Jiang Tian is a rich kid? The goddess he wouldn't even dare touch, he'd just kicked her to the curb.

She's still being played with by him.

But before he could finish his sentence...

*Slap!!!*

Still lost in his fantasy, Xiao Bo felt a sharp pain on his face.

A loud slap echoed throughout the room.

Xiao Bo covered his face in disbelief: "You fucking dare hit me, Jiang Tian, ​​you fucking black sheep, a cancer, you actually dared to hit me! Besides using connections, what else can a piece of trash like you do?"

The next moment...

*Pfft!!!*

A terrifying, excruciating pain shot through Xiao Bo's groin.

The pain shot straight to the top of his head.

Xiao Bo clutched his groin and collapsed to the ground, his entire body trembling with agony.

"That's right, I'm a cancer, a black sheep. What, you disagree?" Jiang Tian sneered.

Looking at the terrifying expression on Jiang Tian's face...

This was an expression Xiao Bo had never seen before, despite knowing Jiang Tian for years and having gained countless political resources from him.

This seemed completely unlike the Jiang Tian he knew.

Because it was too terrifying.

But at this moment, Xiao Bo's hypocritical side resurfaced: "What do you want, you black sheep? Do you want to be fired? We're good friends. Apologize to me now, and I might forgive you."

Xiao Bo endured the excruciating pain, lost in his own world.

Although Xiao Bo desperately wanted to get Jiang Tian fired right now,

he still didn't fully understand what had happened yesterday.

However, now that he'd made his move, Xiao Bo knew he was no match for Jiang Tian. After a moment's consideration, Xiao Bo changed his attitude.

After yesterday's events, Xiao Bo refused to believe Jiang Tian could remain in this team.

Second-generation rich kids were disliked by many.

Given yesterday's incident, he didn't believe Chief Gao would let it go so easily.

Jiang Tian, ​​however, wore a cold smile.

If it weren't for yesterday's events, this guy might indeed have succeeded. His hypocritical expression instantly revealed his inferiority.

But now...

"You little bastard, do you even know how powerful your savior is?

Do you know how much credit you've given everyone for bringing us this episode?

"Very good, keep it up." Jiang Tian squatted down, grabbed Xiao Bo's hair, and patted Xiao Bo's face.

Even as an enemy, Jiang Tian had to admire Xiao Bo's disguise.

It was just a pity that Jiang Tian could see through the hatred and malice in this guy's eyes at a glance.

His hands were almost digging into his flesh.

Yet he still had to act nonchalant. It was truly a pity.

One second he was angrily cursing him for being a black sheep, exposing his past, and after ruining his reputation, he immediately whitewashed his magnanimity.

This move directly trampled on him.

*Pfft!!!*

Jiang Tian stomped on Xiao Bo's face again.



Chapter 14 First-Class Merit and Award: My Mental State Collapses


Jiang Tian wanted to slap this person a few times for treating him like a brother. How could he be so despicable?

Vicious.

Moreover, Jiang Tian could roughly discern the other person's intentions: a resentment stemming from Jiang Tian's privileged background, leading to a vengeful mentality.

If only Jiang Tian hadn't acted so erratically yesterday.

Even if Jiang Tian and Gao Xiaolong had miraculously survived, Xiao Bo's direct exposure of Jiang Tian's connections and backdoor dealings left all his colleagues with the impression that he was a coward.

With the armed police, a couple hundred people, who knew who Gao Xiaolong was referring to? As long as Jiang Tian didn't come forward and admit it, no one would know that Gao Xiaolong was insulting Jiang Tian.

But Xiao Bo deliberately brought it up today, intentionally bringing it up casually after seeing Jiang Tian arrive at work unharmed.

Jiang Tian saw through this little scheme immediately.

He wanted to incite public outrage. Coupled with yesterday's events, if he performed poorly, he wouldn't be able to stay in this team today; if the consequences were worse, his family would be ruined.

Just like in his previous life.

In his previous life.

Jiang Tian used his parents' connections to push away that bastard Xiao Bo, blinded by Xiao Bo and Wang Yifei.

Jiang Tian himself lived a muddled life for over ten years, ending in a miserable state.

Xiao Bo, however, seemed to have opened the door to miracles after that, marrying a wealthy businessman's daughter.

His position rose rapidly, as if by magic, something Jiang Tian had envied in his previous life.

He fantasized countless times about whether he would be just as successful if that incident hadn't happened.

But…

Jiang Tian's eyes flashed.

He suddenly remembered that when Wang Yifei was whispering sweet nothings in his ear to him, she mentioned that Xiao Bo's current fiancée was that wealthy businessman's daughter, and that she looked down on Xiao Bo's circumstances.

Xiao Bo is two years ahead of Jiang Tian, ​​having graduated over two years ago and only recently becoming a Level 3 Police Superintendent.

Before a Superintendent, there are Level 2 and Level 1 Police Constables. However, due to conflicts within the civil service system, Police Constables are typically reserved for vocational school and high school graduates. Since the selection process for regular police officers requires at least a bachelor's degree, Level 2 Police Constables are rare. Aside from the probationary period as Level 2 Probationary Police Constables, they usually become Superintendents directly after their probationary period.

Normally, it would take Xiao Bo three years to reach Level 1.

He would need nearly two more years to potentially advance from Level 3 to Level 2 Superintendent, assuming everything goes smoothly.

But the system is a step-by-step climb; falling behind even slightly could mean waiting another three years. Like most people, he might remain a low-ranking officer his entire career—it's a one-size-fits-all situation.

The wealthy businessman's daughter's condition was that Xiao Bo prove his ability by being promoted to Level 2 Superintendent this year.

Despite the excruciating pain, Xiao Bo slowly stood up, gripping the table for support. His face was serious as he said, "Brother misspoke earlier. I know you have a bad temper and I shouldn't have provoked you. Those were just other people calling you a troublemaker and a cancer. Your brother Xiao was wrong; I didn't watch my mouth. Now we're even."

As he said this, the anger within Xiao Bo almost twisted him.

At that moment, he desperately wanted to crush Jiang Tian to the ground.

However, reason told him he couldn't do that.

Because of this, Jiang Tian's efforts to get a promotion through his father's connections were about to be ruined.

His attitude had softened.

Normally,

when he said this, Jiang Tian would worship him, thinking Xiao Bo was a true man, magnanimous.

Not only would they shake hands and make peace, but Jiang Tian would even apologize to him with a guilty conscience and invite him to dinner.

But now.

Before Jiang Tian even spoke, Zhao Wei angrily said, "Enough! Who are you calling a black sheep and a cancer?"

Interrupted from his spellcasting, Xiao Bo frowned slightly: "Yesterday, the big leader was furious at the meeting about someone using connections. Oh, Jiang Tian, ​​I wasn't talking about you. Don't be angry. We did make a mistake, and when you make a mistake, you have to endure it. You can't hide it forever, right? It's normal to be afraid of death, and everyone can understand, since we were on the front lines. It's good that we can correct our mistakes in the future."

He even smiled encouragingly at Jiang Tian.

He thought himself incredibly wise.

Click!!!

Just then.

Xiao Bo noticed the strange looks he was receiving from everyone in the office.

Before Xiao Bo could think further,

the office door behind him opened.

A heavy voice rang out.

"You said Jiang Tian is a coward, a black sheep and a cancer?"

The heavy, questioning voice rang out as Song Liguo walked out, his face grim.

Actually, he had heard the commotion outside earlier but hadn't come out, just listening to what was happening.

Upon hearing Xiao Bo's words, Song Liguo completely lost his composure.

Didn't he know that the big boss was furious yesterday for not understanding the situation, and he felt guilty and upset, even repenting?

This bastard, coming out today, even the big boss couldn't hide it anymore.

Not only did he jump out and spread it, but he also went to the person in question, acting like a green tea bitch to whom?

Originally, no one knew that the high-ranking leader had criticized Jiang Tian as a black sheep and a cancer before the operation last night, calling him a coward and afraid of death. They only assumed it was a member of the armed police or the anti-drug squad.

But now, everyone knows that the high-ranking leader's target last night was Jiang Tian.

This isn't just embarrassing Jiang Tian; it's embarrassing the high-ranking leader!

This might have fooled Jiang Tian in his past life, but it couldn't fool these seasoned veterans.

Before, they didn't care because they felt it was nothing and didn't want to get involved.

But now it's different.

Who is Jiang Tian?

He's a police god, their anti-drug squad's strategic weapon.

"Captain," Xiao Bo approached with a beaming smile, respectfully offering a cigarette, "Captain, it's my fault for letting this get out, but I think everyone would find out sooner or later. Teammates are meant to be close; hiding things won't last."

Song Liguo's face was grim, his anger building.

His fists clenched unconsciously, and he almost gritted his teeth as he said, "Xiao Bo, you've gone too far."

Xiao Bo, oblivious to the anomaly, continued with his righteous indignation, "No, Captain, we're fighting on the front lines. Who would entrust their back to a coward, right? I think it's necessary for everyone to know the truth; it's for everyone's sake."

Xiao Bo secretly glanced at Jiang Tian with venomous eyes.

Did they have a grudge?

Actually, no.

But Xiao Bo harbored nothing but jealousy and resentment towards Jiang Tian, ​​a second-generation rich kid.

Especially, Xiao Bo's deeper reason was political resources.

He understood perfectly well that Jiang Tian's political resources wouldn't only be out of his reach, but would even become obstacles to his success.

He was unwilling to accept this.

Bring Jiang Tian down, and then, based on his understanding of Jiang Tian, ​​a simple apology would likely be enough for this fool to be eternally grateful and forgive him, then unscrupulously use all his resources to help him.

Xiao Bo calculated in his mind.

*Slap!*

But the next moment.

A sharp pain shot through his face.

Xiao Bo was completely dumbfounded.

Turning his head, he saw Song Liguo's furious face, who said, word by word, "You said Comrade Jiang Tian is a black sheep?"

*Slap!*

After saying that, Song Liguo slapped him again: "You said Comrade Jiang Tian is a cancer?"

*Slap!*

"You said Comrade Jiang Tian is a coward?"

With each sentence, Song Liguo slapped him.

Previously, Song Liguo considered Xiao Bo a young man with some diligence and cleverness, someone worth nurturing.

But now, Song Liguo's anger was about to explode.

This bastard.

Song Liguo, seeing stars with rage, said, "Who gave you the courage to say that? Comrade Jiang Tian was fighting bravely on the battlefield last night, while you were lying at home sleeping. Comrade Jiang Tian faced over two hundred drug dealers alone, fighting to the death, while you were at home enjoying the air conditioning. And now you dare to say Comrade Jiang Tian is a coward? Who is the cancer in the team?"

"I..."

Xiao Bo's face was in excruciating pain, visibly swollen.

But the physical pain was nothing compared to the trembling in his heart.

Because when he turned around, he found that everyone was watching the spectacle.

Many people seemed to be surrounding Jiang Tian, ​​offering words of comfort and concern.

And him...

"I bet he got wind of it yesterday and ran away."

"I remember he hadn't taken a day off in over two years. I thought he was so conscientious, but it just so happened that he took leave right when there was a major mission."

"Yeah, maybe he knew the danger, but he's just a coward, and he even comes here to shamelessly slander Comrade Jiang Tian."

What a joke.

Do they know that yesterday, Jiang Tian saved the entire anti-drug squad?

Do they know that without Jiang Tian, ​​last night they even did tactical analysis and post-battle simulations.

They simulated it many times.

Their fate was only one: none of them would survive until rescue arrived.

They simulated it ten times, and ten times it was total annihilation. Even if one or two survived, it would be by sheer luck.

Knowing this outcome, who wouldn't be terrified? Who wouldn't be filled with fear?

But because of Jiang Tian...

They successfully preserved most of their strength at the cost of only a few teammates.

Jiang Tian gave them a second life.

They were universally condemned.

They had almost become public enemies.

Xiao Bo, who had done this many times before, had many people supporting him.

Even through his intentional or unintentional manipulation, Jiang Tian had almost incurred the dissatisfaction and even hatred of many.

He only had one friend, Zhao Wei.

And now.

It's his turn.

What happened?

What exactly happened?

Xiao Bo was nearly driven mad.

Before Song Liguo could speak again,

a group of people walked in from outside.

Many leaders arrived.

Director Jiang Peng and the deputy director, among others, and of course, leading the way was Gao Xiaolong, the high-ranking leader.

Drums and gongs were played.

The din of drums and gongs was deafening.

"A plaque for First-Class Merit, haha, just as expected."

"Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​please give him more guidance in the future."

"Yes!"

The people inside the room were all congratulating Jiang Tian.

"This good-for-nothing, impossible." Xiao Bo sneered coldly, his face grim. "Are you kidding me? This good-for-nothing wants a First-Class Merit?"

But the next moment...

Gao Xiaolong's expression was unusually solemn. He walked up to Jiang Tian, ​​and the crowd instinctively made way for him: "Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​last night we urgently reported to the capital. The higher-ups were extremely impressed by your miraculous performance and have specially approved a First-Class Merit for you."

This was a surprise Gao Xiaolong had prepared for Jiang Tian overnight.

It was handled as a special case, even expedited overnight, and approved with utmost speed.

First-Class Merit.

Jiang Tian looked at the medal on the plaque; at this moment, it shone so brightly and dazzlingly.

Jiang's father, following behind Gao Xiaolong, watched this scene and involuntarily wiped away tears from his face.

At this moment, how he wanted to shout, "This is my son!"

But he knew he couldn't say it now.

Jiang Tian took a deep breath.

He glanced up at his teammates who were defending him, and at Xiao Bo, who was being condemned by everyone, then looked at Gao Xiaolong, who was carrying the First-Class Merit medal and personally pinning it to Jiang Tian's chest.

Everything had changed.

At this moment, he finally believed that the gears of fate had shifted.

On this day in his past life, this very morning, he should have been suspended from his job and awaiting further notice.

Then a group of uninvited guests arrived and handcuffed Jiang's parents.

After a few days of dazed waiting, he saw Zhao Wei's sister, and a few days later, he was transferred to a sinecure department.

But now.

Everything had changed.

The situation of his parents being arrested had transformed into his parents being proud of him.

Bringing honor to the family.

This first-class merit was of great significance.

There's a saying: a third-class merit is received standing up, a second-class merit is received lying down, and a first-class merit is received by the family.

While not absolute, it illustrates how terrifyingly difficult it is to obtain a first-class merit in peacetime.

When the special-class merit medal hung on his chest.

Xiao Bo's head exploded.

How could this be?

How could he?

First-class merit?

A living first-class merit.

What does this represent?

A brilliant future. From now on, Jiang Tian will be officially on the honor roll.

Even disregarding his family background, Jiang Tian will be given priority for promotions.

But then, Gao Xiaolong added, "Comrade Xiao Tian, ​​I'm sorry you've been wronged."

What?

Xiao Bo's eyes widened.

A first-class merit, and he's been wronged?

What kind of outrageous words are these?

Xiao Bo trembled all over, looking around, only to find that everyone seemed completely unfazed by these words.

In fact, they all seemed to agree.

Aren't you shocked?

Shock made Xiao Bo completely forget his pain.

"Yes, the big leader is right, a first-class merit is indeed a waste."

"Given yesterday's situation, I feel it deserves even a Special Merit Award!"

"Commander, isn't this a Special Merit Award?"

"After 1955, everyone believed that Special Merits were impossible to award in peacetime, so they were abolished. What a pity."

No.

Insane.

Absolutely insane.

Is this world too crazy?

Xiao Bo staggered back, his face filled with shock, his pupils contracting.

Who knew, Gao Xiaolong also strongly agreed: "That's right, I originally applied for a Special Merit Award for you. The higher-ups considered that restarting the Special Merit Award would have too much impact, and you're still young; you'll have many opportunities in the future."

Saying this, he patted Jiang Tian's shoulder: "Your future depends on young people like you. Xiao Tian, ​​you haven't let me down, and you haven't let anyone down. I apologize for yesterday's events. I didn't investigate thoroughly and acted rashly, wronging you."

Last night, Gao Xiaolong carefully investigated the situation.

Finally, it was discovered that Jiang's mother had kept the backdoor admission a secret from Jiang's father and Jiang Tian.

After his investigation, he found that it was all Jiang's mother's doing; Jiang Tian was innocent.

Jiang's mother considered that Jiang Tian was an intern, newly joined the police force, and it was perfectly normal for her to ask someone she knew to help him.

In the end, it was all a misunderstanding.

However, he almost wronged a genius. Last night, Gao Xiaolong felt guilty and couldn't sleep, and tried his best to get Jiang Tian a special merit award.

But unfortunately.

"Furthermore, Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​in view of your outstanding performance last night, perfectly protecting the lives and property of the country and the people, making an outstanding contribution, you are hereby awarded a first-class merit medal, and your probation period is terminated early, and you are promoted to second-level police superintendent."

Skipping the second level directly.

Directly reaching the second-level police superintendent rank that Xiao Bo, who had been in the force for three years, had been desperately pursuing and plotting to achieve.

Sizzle!!!

Gao Xiaolong personally tore off Jiang Tian's probationary police officer rank and replaced it with a one-bar-two badge, equivalent to a second-level police superintendent.

A skipped rank.

This one rank saved Jiang Tian four years.

One year of probation, three years of promotion.

A full four years, all accomplished by Jiang Tian in one night.

......

Xiao Bo watched helplessly as Gao Xiaolong personally awarded Jiang Tian the first-class merit and then apologized.

This completely shattered Xiao Bo's composure.

For him, seeing Jiang Tian gain merit was worse than death.

At this moment, Xiao Bo, driven mad by the blow, stood up and angrily shouted, "Why? He's just an intern, why does he deserve a first-class merit? Why does he become a second-level police superintendent? He's a coward!"



Chapter 15: Promotion and Raise, Mental Breakdown, Insane Jealousy


Within the system, promotion is a gamble, a meteoric rise.

Starting as a Level 3 Superintendent after becoming a full-fledged officer, the basic requirement for promotion is at least three years of service.

You only get one opportunity every three years.

But this opportunity isn't available to everyone. With so many new officers joining each batch, the number of available positions is extremely limited. Why would you get promoted?

And if you miss one, the next opportunity comes after another three years, making it six years in total.

Jiang Tian, ​​however,

spent his first year of service and also skipped the previous three years.

This caused

Xiao Bo's mental state to explode.

First-class merit.

And he still felt wronged?

High-ranking leader Gao Xiaolong personally apologized.

Plus, he was promoted to Level 2 Superintendent in one fell swoop.

He went straight to Level 1, Level 2, from being his former subordinate who served him tea and water to becoming his superior overnight.

That mental breakdown caused Xiao Bo to lose all reason.

A cover-up.

There's a cover-up.

At this moment, Xiao Bo was absolutely certain that Jiang Tian was involved in something shady, acting lawlessly and without restraint.

"Damn it, damn it! These second-generation rich kids are utterly lawless! I thought Chief Gao was a champion of justice, but it turns out he's just in cahoots with him."

Xiao Bo trembled with rage.

He pointed at Jiang Tian and cursed, "He's a complete waste! Why did he get a first-class merit? Why was he promoted so blatantly? He's just a cowardly, back-door rich kid!"

Often, reality can drive someone mad, especially when there's a stark contrast. Watching Jiang Tian rise through the ranks, his future bright, while he struggled in the mud, his fiancée's demands already putting immense pressure on him, requiring painstaking planning.

In the end, the promotion he'd worked so hard for, so unattainable, was just a bonus for Jiang Tian, ​​a mere byproduct of his first-class merit.

"What did you say?"

Gao Xiaolong, who had just patted Jiang Tian on the shoulder with a happy expression, frowned slightly at the inappropriate voice.

He looked at the unfamiliar face.

The sharp, accusatory question rang out.

The unfamiliarity stemmed from the fact that Gao Xiaolong hadn't seen this person before. After yesterday's operation, he had scrutinized the faces of everyone in the Narcotics Control Team, including the few who had been killed.

He was certain he had no recollection of this person.

"The Narcotics Control Team is an important place. Strangers are strictly prohibited from entering. Who are you, and how did you get in?" Gao Xiaolong asked, his brow furrowed.

Xiao Bo quickly explained, "Sir, I'm also from the Narcotics Control Team."

"Why didn't I see you last night? Didn't I say that everyone in the Narcotics Control Team had to participate in the operation?" Gao Xiaolong pressed on.

"I...I...I'm feeling a little unwell," Xiao Bo said awkwardly, his face swollen.

"So, you don't acknowledge Comrade Jiang Tian's contributions, and you consider him a cancer and a black sheep?" Gao Xiaolong's face was expressionless.

Xiao Bo hurriedly nodded, "Chief Gao, he's a good-for-nothing. He was a good-for-nothing in police academy. Of course, I'm not insulting him, but just being responsible for him. Promoting someone with such mediocre talent and ability rashly is bad for his future. He needs time to hone his skills. Besides, how can a first-class merit be awarded to such a good-for-nothing? It's simply outrageous."

Jiang Tian's gaze, standing to the side, gradually turned mocking.

He didn't know who gave Xiao Bo the courage to question Gao Xiaolong, or to question his achievement in eliminating over a hundred drug dealers yesterday.

Jealousy had already driven him to the brink of madness.

However, Gao Xiaolong was known for his fiery temper and wouldn't tolerate this, especially after learning about Xiao Bo's situation. His anger flared even more.

*Slap!*

But what Xiao Bo faced was a slap from Gao Xiaolong.

His already swollen face bulged even more.

His eyes were almost slits.

"You ask for leave when your teammates are on duty, you sleep when your teammates are in danger, you question your teammates when they achieve merit, and you're jealous when your teammates get promoted."

*Slap!*

As he spoke, Gao Xiaolong raised his hand to strike again.

But the next moment, Gao Xiaolong took a deep breath, forcibly suppressing his inner rage.

He was truly furious.

Yesterday, Jiang Tian had created a miracle in a life-or-death situation, not only saving them from near death but also wiping out most of the drug dealers.

And someone who asked for leave turned around and questioned Jiang Tian's contribution?

"What's your name?" Gao Xiaolong's anger burned fiercely.

His voice was unusually cold and deep.

It was almost an angry growl.

Xiao Bo's heart skipped a beat.

"Boss, his name is Xiao Bo. He's from our Narcotics Control Detachment, Operations Team One, First Squad." A burly middle-aged man stepped out from the crowd.

The captain of a large squadron.

Also the captain of Jiang Tian's action squadron.

"Fine, Xiao Bo, right? From now on, you are suspended indefinitely and sent home to reflect on your actions," Gao Xiaolong said angrily.

Boom!!!

A bolt from the blue.

The sky collapsed.

Xiao Bo's face turned pale. The sky had collapsed, completely collapsed!

He came from a mountain village, the first college graduate from the surrounding area in recent years.

Especially after entering police academy, his family's doorstep was constantly being visited.

His family enjoyed immense prestige because of him.

Because of this, he desperately climbed the social ladder, and after entering university, he understood the vastness of the world.

He began to resent God for not being born into a powerful and influential family.

He resented those privileged children even more.

But now, thinking about his family's reaction after his suspension, Xiao Bo's mental state instantly crumbled.

"I'm not convinced! Why? Why did Jiang Tian, ​​that good-for-nothing, get a first-class merit? Why was he suspended just because someone said a few words? Has the darkness reached the police force? Yesterday you kept saying you were cleaning up the bad apples, but now, just because his family has power and influence, are ordinary people like us left with no way to survive? Just because someone didn't back down when facing drug dealers, he gets a first-class merit? Then why don't we all get first-class merits when we didn't back down when facing drug dealers?" Xiao Bo tried to evoke everyone's sympathy.

However, when Xiao Bo looked around, he found that no one spoke up for him.

Gao Xiaolong said coldly, "Fine, I'll tell you why Comrade Jiang Tian received a first-class merit: because he single-handedly wiped out 150 drug dealers yesterday."

Hiss!!!

Xiao Bo's pupils contracted.

150 drug dealers?

What a load of rubbish!

"Furthermore, your suspension isn't because of that. Yesterday, you were the one who instructed Comrade Jiang Tian's family to call the police station, and you timed it perfectly when I was in the office, weren't you? You also gave Comrade Jiang Tian's family that landline number, didn't you?" Gao Xiaolong said grimly.

He hadn't expected to be outmaneuvered by such a petty person so soon after arriving here.

He had almost wronged a police genius, a true hero.

"I was just concerned about Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​was it wrong for me to let his family know the situation?" Xiao Bo retorted stubbornly.

Fine, fine, fine...

Everyone present was almost laughing in anger.

Even now, they're still twisting the truth.

"You're utterly vicious, narrow-minded, and consumed by jealousy. You're the real scourge, the real cancer." Gao Xiaolong's face was icy. If he weren't still rational, he would have shot this bastard dead on the spot.

At this moment, Jiang Tian glanced at Xiao Bo, his face filled with disappointment.

Xiao Bo was now sitting on the ground, completely powerless. To be honest, his fighting ability was pathetic.

He had originally planned to keep him alive for slow revenge, to make him wish he were dead.

But who would have thought that before Jiang Tian even had a chance to do anything, Xiao Bo was already dead?

Indefinite suspension for reflection, but Gao Xiaolong's words were practically a blatant dismissal from his public office.

Xiao Bo was completely finished.

Jiang Tian sighed inwardly.

It has to be said, this is fate!

In his past life, Jiang Tian was the same way. Just like that, after being trampled on by Xiao Bo, he was utterly condemned to hell.

For over a decade, he lived a life worse than death, in a daze.

His family members died one after another in extreme torment.

Finally, even his son, whom he considered his most beloved, betrayed him.

His wife, who had stood by him through thick and thin, turned out to be his biggest accomplice in his schemes.

Unfortunately, he realized this too late in his past life.

But now, it's not too late.

All of this can be undone.

"I never expected it. Xiao Bo seemed so nice all along, but he turns out to be such a vicious person."

"Damn, I never thought Xiao Bo was so calculating. Knowing that Brother Jiang's family had some connections, he secretly went over and gave Chief Gao his phone number so he could get preferential treatment. He's so damn wicked."

"Ugh, absolutely disgusting."

Everyone was shocked.

Even Song Liguo hadn't expected such a thing to happen.

It was all orchestrated by this person.

He deserves to die!

As Xiao Bo left, Jiang Tian was surrounded by flattering voices.

Not only that.

Gao Xiaolong even brought a 50,000 yuan bonus.

And a collective second-class merit award.

A collective second-class merit award is already quite good, but the main reason is that Jiang Tian's contributions were so outstanding. Everyone else could say that this second-class merit award was actually earned through Jiang Tian.

“Originally, yesterday’s operation not only yielded no merit, but the intelligence error caused significant losses, and the entire Yunhai Anti-Drug Squad would be held responsible. However, considering the balance of merits and demerits, and given Comrade Jiang Tian’s annihilation of so many drug traffickers, we are awarding you all a collective second-class merit.” Gao Xiaolong then announced.

Wow!!!

This was an honor for everyone, a tremendous surprise.

Xiao Bo, who had reached the door, turned around upon hearing this, his eyes bloodshot.

He looked at Jiang Tian, ​​surrounded by the crowd, his first-class merit badge adorning his chest, his shoulder bar and two other badges shining brightly.

And him?

From now on, he was suspended from duty.

Xiao Bo’s eyes were bloodshot with jealousy; Jiang Tian was arguably the person he hated most.

Watching Jiang Tian get promoted, receive a raise, and reach the pinnacle of his life was more painful than death.

Ring ring ring!!!

Just as Xiao Bo was consumed by resentment, a cell phone rang.

Xiao Bo immediately bowed deeply: "Yoona, what brings you to call me?"

Yoona.

She was Xiao Bo's fiancée, but her condition for the engagement was a promotion this year.

"How's your promotion going? My dad said if you don't get promoted this year, our relationship is impossible. You know, our family doesn't want useless people." A cold voice came from the other end of the phone.

Xiao Bo said obsequiously, "I'm confident, Yoona, wait for me. We'll definitely be engaged by the end of the year."

Hanging up, Xiao Bo's fawning expression turned ferocious.

He gripped the phone as if he wanted to crush it.

In his mind, all of this should have been his.

It should all have been his.

Jiang Tian should have been the one condemned and left dejected.

Xiao Bo should have been the one receiving praise and adulation from thousands.

It was him, he had taken it all away.

Jiang Tian paid absolutely no attention to Xiao Bo's departure.

"Although everyone has made contributions, don't be too happy yet. Tucha's actions are a provocation against our country, and even more so, a provocation against our entire department. This is absolutely intolerable."

At this point, Gao Xiaolong paused slightly and continued, "Besides Tucha, the situation in Yunhai is also very serious. Drug traffickers are becoming increasingly rampant, which is deeply related to Yunhai's inadequate supervision. I don't care what you do, I have only one request: eradicate the drug traffickers in Yunhai."

"The higher-ups are taking this matter very seriously. According to statistics, 70% of the country's drugs enter the country through Yunhai. This is your dereliction of duty."

The drug trafficker problem in Yunhai is severe.

Because it borders the Golden Triangle, Yunhai has become the primary route for drug trafficking from the Golden Triangle.

In addition, Yunhai's environment is well-connected, and its transportation channels are extremely convenient.

It's practically a paradise for drug traffickers. Every day, massive numbers of drug traffickers smuggle drugs into Yunhai from the border using countless methods.

Some can be detected, while others cannot.

Because there are so many methods, it's practically impossible to prevent.

After Gao Xiaolong left, Song Liguo immediately canceled the celebration of credit, and with a gloomy face, called an emergency meeting, angrily reprimanding his subordinates.

"Now, everyone move out immediately. Each squad has a assigned task. From now on, everyone will conduct a widespread operation to apprehend the drug dealers."

"Also, Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​your squad leader was killed yesterday. You'll be leading your squad for now; manpower is tight. We'll make personnel adjustments later," Song Liguo concluded.

Wow.

A promotion and a raise?

Jiang Tian's eyes lit up.

Not only was his rank upgraded, but his position was also promoted.

"Damn, Brother Jiang is awesome!" Zhao Wei gave a thumbs up.

Jiang Tian was in a very good mood because, except for designated missions, the squad leader could basically conduct operations at will, in groups of three.

This allowed his scanning radar, with its kilometer-range scanning radar, to activate its map-wide attack.

Targeting exactly where he pointed.

Yesterday, the squad leader who led Jiang Tian and Zhao Wei was unexpectedly killed.

Jiang Tian filled that vacancy perfectly.

However, the team was actually missing one person.

Currently, only Jiang Tian and Zhao Wei were on the operation.

They got into the official car, fully armed.

"Just average," Jiang Tian said modestly.

Sitting in the passenger seat, Jiang Tian squinted at Zhao Wei, who was acting very unassuming as the driver.

If he hadn't been reborn, Jiang Tian would never have known that this guy had such powerful connections.

*Ring ring ring!!!*

"Brother Jiang, your phone is ringing," Zhao Wei reminded him.

Jiang Tian took out his phone and looked at the caller ID: Wang Yifei?

Seeing this name, Jiang Tian frowned deeply.

A nameless anger rose within him.

If she hadn't revealed it herself in his previous life, Jiang Tian would never have known that the child was Xiao Bo's.

What was even more infuriating was...

According to the circumstances of his previous life...

He was in a state of utter despair when Wang Yifei got him drunk and took advantage of him.

A month later, she told him she was pregnant.

In reality, Wang Yifei is now pregnant.



Chapter 16 Rescuing Jiang Xiaoyu, Yun the Drug Dealer


It was because Jiang Tian was so distraught that his mother was arrested and his father suspended from his job.

Overnight, the world collapsed for Jiang Tian in his past life.

He didn't even know the reason behind all this; Xiao Bo was behind it all, and Wang Yifei was definitely involved.

Jiang Tian unconsciously gripped his phone tightly.

The cold light in his eyes grew sharper and sharper. The hatred from his past life would be avenged in this one.

And the child in Wang Yifei's womb—Jiang Tian hadn't forgotten. The child he raised for over ten years in his past life turned out to be the culprit who killed him.

Especially with this call, Jiang Tian guessed that Wang Yifei had just found out she was pregnant and was desperately looking for a replacement.

Because Xiao Bo was pursuing that woman, Wang Yifei was just a backup plan.

And Jiang Tian? He was that woman's backup plan.

It's lamentable that Jiang Tian pursued this woman for so long in his past life, only to have her treat him as a backup plan from the very beginning, stringing him along.

In the end, she even made him the one left holding the bag.

In his past life, Jiang Tian was filled with countless regrets. His beautiful family and happy life—why did it all turn out like this overnight?

Jiang Tian slammed down the phone; he didn't answer.

Knowing the whole story, Jiang Tian's revenge plan would unfold slowly; there was plenty of time.

For now, he'd let him cool off.

Meanwhile,

As Jiang Tian's car drove away,

at the police station,

Jiang's father and Gao Xiaolong were still there, gathered in Jiang Peng's office.

Song Liguo was still somewhat worried: "Although Comrade Jiang Tian's individual combat abilities are very strong, he is, after all, a recent graduate with extremely limited criminal investigation experience. Letting him lead a small team is a bit like forcing a seedling."

Everyone present, including Jiang's father, nodded in agreement.

A marksman's marksmanship and agility on the battlefield don't guarantee the same level of skill in apprehending drug dealers.

"Young man, once you achieve something, you inevitably become arrogant. A little somersault when necessary is a good thing," Gao Xiaolong said shrewdly.

"Commander Gao, so this was all part of your plan," Jiang Peng said in surprise.

He felt a strange pang of sorrow for Jiang Tian.

"Hahaha, the drug dealers in Yunhai are a serious problem, with complex and intertwined relationships that aren't easy to uncover. Otherwise, despite years of crackdowns on drug trafficking in Yunhai, they wouldn't be so persistent. Without a veteran narcotics officer to guide you, you'd be like a headless fly," Gao Xiaolong said slowly.

As Gao Xiaolong said, the battlefield is different from searching for drug dealers.

Drug enforcement is ultimately about the ability to find the dealers. Once found, it's usually a direct confrontation.

Or a coordinated operation to wipe them out, etc.

Anyway, various methods are used.

Those who dare to confront narcotics police head-on, and fight like it's a battlefield, are a rare breed, perhaps appearing only once every few years.

...

"Wait, Brother Jiang, wait for me!"

Just then, a hurried voice came from behind Jiang Tian's car.

Screech!

Zhao Wei slammed on the brakes, and the woman quickly jumped into the car.

"Sister Li, what are you doing here?" Zhao Wei asked in surprise.

"Captain Song just assigned me to your team," Li Zijing quickly replied.

"What?! Holy crap!" Zhao Wei was completely dumbfounded.

He rolled his eyes, glancing at Brother Jiang, who had displayed incredible prowess on the battlefield, sweeping away all opposition, and had just been promoted after completing his probationary period.

Then he looked at his own shoulder insignia; he was still a probationary officer, not yet officially a full-fledged officer.

Then he looked at Li Zijing's delicate appearance.

He was speechless.

"What kind of look is that? I've been in the anti-drug squad for three years. You two are both newbies, and you don't even know as much as I do," Li Zijing said proudly.

Jiang Tian glanced at Li Zijing's proudest chest without showing any emotion, and nodded imperceptibly. She certainly had reason to be proud.

Jiang Tian didn't feel any aversion to Li Zijing joining the team, mainly because, in both his past and present lives, he had a considerable fondness for her.

In his previous life, when Li Zijing was subtly and overtly belittled by Xiao Bo because of her naive personality, she had mentioned this more than once.

Unfortunately, Jiang Tian didn't take it to heart at the time.

And Li Zijing, in her previous life, also died in the drug dealers' encirclement last night.

Before she died, Li Zijing told Jiang Tian that Xiao Bo had a gloomy personality.

Li Zijing would often bring Jiang Tian food and take care of him.

“Brother Jiang, where are we going now?” Zhao Wei asked.

“Patrolling the streets first.” Jiang Tian, ​​fully armed, sat in the back seat.

Two thousand years ago, their police force, apart from the official vehicles used for calls, usually patrolled in Santanas.

The windows were completely blacked out.

“We got a mission from above, to find the drug dealers' trail. Running around like this won't get us anywhere,” Li Zijing complained.

“Who said that?”

Jiang Tian grinned.

Scanning radar.

This is a gold-level attribute! With this attribute, appearing within a kilometer of Jiang Tian means no drug dealer can escape his keen eye.

Before Jiang Tian's eyes appeared, his scanning radar activated, displaying various small dots.

Ordinary people were white.

However, those with a crime value would have a slight red tinge, proving they had definitely committed some illegal act.

Jiang Tian simply ignored those with only a slight red tinge.

The rest...

Jiang Tian carefully observed the pedestrians passing by.

"Stop the car."

Just as the car reached the entrance of a school, Jiang Tian suddenly straightened up.

At this moment, the scanning radar in Jiang Tian's mind clearly saw several bright red dots.

"Huh, what's this?"

Jiang Tian got out of the car, his face full of surprise.

"Brother Jiang, this is Yunda University," Zhao Wei explained.

Yunda University.

Jiang Tian frowned, thought for a moment, and finally realized.

Yunda University, wasn't that where his sister went to school?

Yunnan University is the only Double First-Class University in Yunnan Province. Jiang Tian's younger sister was an excellent student and gained admission through her own hard work.

However, in his previous life...

Jiang Tian's relationship with his sister was damaged because of Wang Yifei.

After their parents passed away, his sister, who was still in school at the time, returned home, only to be targeted by Wang Yifei.

Jiang Tian was immersed in grief and didn't intervene.

After Wang Yifei kicked Jiang Tian's sister out, Jiang Xiaoyu, homeless, had no choice but to return to live at the university.

The next time Jiang Tian learned of this was that his sister had jumped to her death due to hallucinations caused by drug overdose.

At that time, Jiang Tian was heartbroken and filled with grief. He hated himself countless times, feeling as if he had given up.

His heart was almost dead.

Later, Jiang Tian's sister's best friend found Jiang Tian and told him the truth: that day, Jiang Tian's sister had been forcibly given drugs by several people at school.

Unable to bear the humiliation, Jiang Xiaoyu jumped from the school rooftop.

*Snap!*

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian unconsciously clenched his fists.

Wang Yifei and Xiao Bo had completely ruined his life!

And that wasn't all.

There were also the drug dealers—no, the drug addicts—at the school.

Later, Jiang Tian specifically investigated and found out that the person who drove Jiang Xiaoyu to her death was the leader of a group that had pursued Jiang Xiaoyu, but she had consistently ignored and rejected him.

Finally, he went completely mad, wanting to control Jiang Xiaoyu with drugs.

Or rather, to get Jiang Xiaoyu.

“Brother Jiang, school’s out.” Zhao Wei, standing to the side with his police dog, said expectantly.

“It’s a holiday.” Li Zijing didn’t know what Jiang Tian was doing here.

“Oh, right, today is Saturday.” Zhao Wei belatedly realized, scratching his head: “Our holiday this week is gone again.”

Jiang Tian raised his hand and slapped him: “As a qualified narcotics officer, millions of people in Yunhai live in dire straits, living under the threat of drugs. You still want a holiday? Joining the narcotics team means being prepared to be away from your family at any time, understand?”

Mainly, Jiang Tian thought of Zhao Wei’s sister. Her eyes were terrifying, as if she could see through people’s hearts. To be honest, Jiang Tian never wanted to see that woman again.

It was a bit scary.

Zhao Wei trembled, his eyes glistening with tears: “Brother Jiang, I’m guilty. As a narcotics officer, my understanding was inadequate.”

Jiang Tian smiled with satisfaction.

"Brother."

"Brother, over here."

Just then, a joyful voice rang out.

Jiang Tian turned his head and saw Jiang Xiaoyu transform into a gust of wind, rushing into his arms.

A fragrant scent filled the air as Jiang Xiaoyu's head nestled against Jiang Tian's chest.

A long-lost fragrance.

A long-lost feeling.

Jiang Tian's lips were chapped; that familiar voice, that familiar scent, made him think he was dreaming.

In his past life, for over ten years, countless times in the dead of night, he had dreamt of this scene.

Dreaming that his sister was still alive.

"Damn it, Brother Jiang, I misjudged you." Zhao Wei's eyes widened, almost spitting blood.

Damn it, just a moment ago he was saying that narcotics officers had to be free from worldly desires, not only without holidays but also having to keep their distance from their families.

They had to voluntarily work overtime.

And the next moment, his sister was in his arms.

"Stop nagging, you're on holiday, right?" Jiang Tian patted Jiang Xiaoyu's head, his guilt suddenly becoming tangible.

Besides, she was such a sensible and clingy little sister.

"Waaah, brother, I'm hungry," Jiang Xiaoyu pouted.

"Brother will take you out for a big meal," Jiang Tian waved his hand. After all, who wouldn't love their little sister?

"Um, Captain, we're still on a mission. The higher-ups are very strict; failing to meet the targets will result in punishment," Li Zijing said, desperately wanting to avoid interrupting.

However, considering the urgency from above...

The rampant drug trafficking in Yunhai forced him to interrupt this heartwarming scene.

“Nothing matters more than having dinner with my sister,” Jiang Tian said with a wave of his hand.

“Brother, brother, what about me?”

Just then, the little girl following behind Jiang Tian asked, her eyes lighting up.

Jiang Tian then turned to look at the little girl behind Jiang Xiaoyu.

He had been so busy catching up with Jiang Xiaoyu that he had forgotten something important.

Looking at this little girl, Jiang Tian’s eyes gleamed with admiration.

Lian Xin.

In his past life, it was Lian Xin, Jiang Xiaoyu’s best friend, who told Jiang Tian the whole truth.

Later, Lian Xin even went so far as to avenge Jiang Xiaoyu after graduating from law school, joining forces with Jiang Tian to find evidence of the drug traffickers’ crimes and hand it over to Xiao Bo. Although this solved the drug trafficking case, it also gave Xiao Bo another reason for his promotion.

But now, everything had been rewritten.

"Together, together!" Jiang Tian waved his hand.

Having just received a 50,000 yuan bonus, Jiang Tian was quite generous.

"Long live the boss!" Jiang Xiaoyu exclaimed excitedly.

However, Jiang Tian ignored Jiang Xiaoyu. Instead, his gaze swept across the room and instantly spotted a evasive figure.

At that moment, a red light flashed in Jiang Tian's eyes, a murderous aura crossing his face.

But he quickly suppressed it.

Then, calmly, he said, "That classmate, I saw you following Xiaoyu earlier, so you must be Xiaoyu's friend. Let's eat together, don't rush off."

"That's not a friend, boss, you've mistaken me for someone else," Jiang Xiaoyu said hastily, his face changing.

"How can you not be? Xiaoyu, I'm about to say something to you. How can you leave your friend behind to eat? I just saw that classmate following behind you, talking to you." Jiang Tian said gently.

“I…” Jiang Xiaoyu was furious, pounding her little fist on Jiang Tian’s chest. “Brother, you’re driving me crazy! I’m not talking to you anymore!”

“Brother, hello, my name is Gao Fei, I’m Xiaoyu’s classmate.”

The male classmate following behind Jiang Xiaoyu walked up and shook hands with Jiang Tian. Jiang Tian smiled slightly, “We’re all friends, all friends. Let’s eat together, no need to be polite.”

“Thank you, brother.” Gao Fei glanced at Jiang Xiaoyu, nodding repeatedly with delight.

Since one car wasn’t enough, Jiang Tian took everyone directly to the large hotel across from Yun University.

On the way, Jiang Xiaoyu stared at Jiang Tian’s police rank insignia, her little eyes darting around, then at the two trainee police officers following behind him.

“Brother, aren’t you a trainee police officer? Where did you steal that rank from?” Jiang Xiaoyu whispered.

“Don’t talk nonsense. Do you think your brother needs to steal his rank?” Jiang Tian was exasperated.

"Brother Jiang, you didn't really get promoted, did you? I remember you just graduated!"

Lian Xin looked surprised after ordering food at the restaurant.

"I was lucky enough to get promoted, so I did it out of the ordinary," Jiang Tian said modestly.

"But brother, isn't it a bit too much to ask for a private room just for us?" Jiang Xiaoyu hesitated.

"It's on the company tab, what's the big deal?" Jiang Tian said, glancing at Gao Fei out of the corner of his eye.

That's right.

It's not expensive at all. After all, compared to Gao Fei, any expense would be worthwhile.

Sure enough.

Gao Fei's eyes lit up at that moment.

His eyes darted around; this trip had unexpectedly given him such a big surprise.

Flies don't land on eggs without cracks.

Gao Fei was madly pursuing Jiang Xiaoyu. Besides her beauty, he had also inadvertently witnessed Jiang Peng picking her up.

Coincidentally, Gao Fei knew Jiang Peng was the director of the Yunhai Public Security Bureau.

If he could get rid of Jiang Tian,

wouldn't Jiang Peng be able to easily deal with him, and perhaps even use Jiang Tian to win Jiang Xiaoyu's heart?

As for the methods...

Gao Fei had a plan in mind.

Li Zijing and Zhao Wei remained silent.

Their attitude had changed.

Their Captain Jiang wasn't a police god. Xiao Bo and yesterday's Chief Gao weren't wrong; they were truly black sheep!

Using public funds for smuggling—was it really okay to do it so blatantly?

"Ahem, Captain, our team's funds are a bit tight," Li Zijing whispered from the side.

Unfortunately, Jiang Tian seemed not to hear her.

"It's my treat, Brother Jiang, please do me the honor," Gao Fei said generously, standing up.

Jiang Tian grinned.

He'd been waiting for this moment.

Many people who hadn't lived through this era simply didn't know how arrogant the drug dealers in Yunhai were.



Chapter 17 I just wanted to cut a watermelon, how did it become a crime?


For example, when Jiang Tian brought his men to a nicer hotel for dinner, it startled Zhao Wei and Li Zijing.

As a narcotics officer,

their average monthly salary is only a few hundred yuan, even with substantial subsidies within the civil service system.

A normal civil servant might only earn three or four thousand yuan a year.

And if someone dies—Jiang Tian specifically inquired about it today—his teammate who died last night received an 80,000 yuan compensation.

That's a human life!

Only 80,000 yuan in compensation for death.

Even if the children of martyrs receive preferential treatment, what good is that?

The breadwinner of a family is gone.

However, this very situation further emboldens drug traffickers.

While narcotics officers earn only six or seven hundred yuan a month to support their families, they face bribes of hundreds of thousands or even millions of yuan from drug traffickers.

The most terrifying thing is that many drug traffickers have even infiltrated the anti-narcotics team.

They even knew the family situations of the members of the anti-drug team.

As far as Jiang Tian knew, this wasn't the first time his teammates' families had run into trouble.

The ruthlessness of drug dealers was unimaginable.

“Captain Jiang, I fell in love with Jiang Xiaoyu at first sight. Could you give me a chance to pursue her? I swear, I will treat Xiaoyu well,” Gao Fei said, holding his wine glass.

Jiang Xiaoyu, sitting next to Jiang Tian, ​​looked furious upon hearing this, her hands sweating as she gripped Jiang Tian's hand tightly.

Jiang Tian reached out and patted his sister's hand.

Then, without revealing any emotion, Jiang Tian said, “My sister is so beautiful, she has many suitors. Who do you think you are?”

Gao Fei wasn't angry. He looked around, his eyes flickering, and finally smiled at Jiang Tian, ​​“Captain Jiang, could we go outside and talk alone?”

“Oh, sure!” Jiang Tian nodded readily.

“Brother,” Jiang Xiaoyu said anxiously.

"Xiaoyu, wait here patiently," Jiang Tian instructed, then turned to see Jiang Xiaoyu's best friend, Lian Xin, puffing out her cheeks and talking about how delicious the food was.

Jiang Tian hadn't been frugal today; he'd ordered expensive things like sea cucumber and abalone.

"Damn it, Captain, where are you going?" Li Zijing asked anxiously.

She was eager to earn merit.

However, Li Zijing was now seriously doubting whether following Jiang Tian was the right decision.

She couldn't help but wonder if this guy was actually a black sheep.

A black sheep with a decent shot?

"Captain, we have police laws and official regulations. Accepting bribes is illegal," Zhao Wei said, swallowing hard.

He noticed something was amiss.

Why was Jiang Tian acting more and more like a corrupt official?

A mere squad leader was already being treated to meals; what was next? Was it a bribe?

Zhao Wei was timid.

Even the most foolish person would sense something was wrong when they saw Gao Fei's expression.

"We are great public servants. What's wrong with the people inviting us to a meal? What's wrong with reasonably listening to the people's demands?" Jiang Tian said righteously.

Gao Fei, standing to the side, brightened his eyes even more.

His smile grew even brighter.

Li Zijing and Zhao Wei opened their mouths.

"I...!!!" Zhao Wei angrily tried to stand up.

"Hmm?"

The next moment, facing Jiang Tian's righteous yet utterly shameless face, Zhao Wei instantly cowered and sat back down: "Captain, I didn't see anything."

The wariness in Gao Fei's eyes lessened slightly.

"I have a few brothers who have long admired Captain Jiang. They've already booked a private room upstairs, just waiting for you." Gao Fei led the way.

Jiang Tian straightened his collar, a slight smile playing on his lips as he followed behind.

How could he forget?

In his previous life, when these people were arrested, Jiang Tian asked Gao Fei why he had driven his sister to suicide.

Gao Fei's words then.

"A shameless woman. If she had that deputy mayor father, it wouldn't matter. That old bastard's already gone. What's killing her? Too bad, he'd already taken his pants off, but before he could even enjoy her, she jumped."

Gao Fei's words still echoed vividly in Jiang Tian's ears.

And what was Gao Fei?

A social scumbag.

A piece of trash.

A drug dealer.

Even in his past life, Jiang Tian would have looked down on such trash.

It was then that Jiang Tian understood that in this society, without power or influence, even trash could trample you underfoot.

Fortunately, all of that changed.

He had just stepped out the door.

Jiang Tian paused slightly.

He stopped and turned to look at a woman.

Wang Yifei.

They were eating in a private room on the first floor; there were accommodations on the top floor.

At this moment, Wang Yifei was holding Xiao Bo's arm, waiting at the elevator.

Seeing Wang Yifei, hatred flashed in Jiang Tian's eyes.

In his past life.

Jiang Tian should have lived a glorious life, but because of this despicable couple, Xiao Bo and Wang Yifei, they not only ruined him...

Even Jiang Tian's father was implicated.

The whole family was betrayed by these two scoundrels.
