Thinking of this, Jiang Tian took out a hidden camera from his pocket and filmed Wang Yifei and Xiao Bo.

During this time period.

Jiang Tian and Wang Yifei had a very close relationship; they had even confirmed their relationship as boyfriend and girlfriend.

However, before this, Wang Yifei had always refused, citing her conservative nature and insisting that she could not be open before marriage.

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian suddenly paused.

Because he suddenly remembered.

On this day in his previous life, heartbroken and drunk, he woke up the next morning.

Wang Yifei was lying naked on the bed, with a pool of blood on it.

Besides the blood, there was indeed a certain smell on the bed and in the room.

At the time, Jiang Tian genuinely thought he had... you know... with Wang Yifei.

But that's not right.

Jiang Tian suddenly remembered that when he helped Wang Yifei out of the hotel, that bastard Xiao Bo was sitting in the lobby, claiming he was worried about him.

In other words, from beginning to end, Jiang Tian might never have touched Wang Yifei in his previous life.

Xiao Bo might even have taken advantage of him while he was drunk, right in front of him.

Then... after they established their relationship, for the next year, Jiang Tian never touched her.

He claimed she was pregnant and couldn't have sex.

"What bullshit about chastity and loyalty? It's all bullshit. She's just a slut."

Jiang Tian sneered.

Killing this pair of scoundrels would be too lenient.

No, that's not right.

Jiang Tian suddenly remembered something: Zhao Wei's sister, that mysterious woman, had found him in the hotel.

When the door opened, Jiang Tian and Wang Yifei were both naked.

At that moment, Jiang Tian clearly saw the heavy disappointment in the woman's eyes.

And her forlorn tone as she said, "I thought you were pretty good, but after that incident, you're still doing this kind of thing in a hotel."

In other words, even if he fell, he still had a chance, all because of this pair of scoundrels.

"Captain Jiang?" Gao Fei was startled when he saw the hidden camera being pulled out, his face instantly turning wary.

Jiang Tian explained, "Hahaha, Brother Gao, that woman is my girlfriend."

Huh?

The wariness in Gao Fei's eyes turned to confusion.

He glanced at the couple embracing intimately at the elevator entrance.

Then he looked at Captain Jiang, standing around the corner in his narcotics officer uniform, wielding the rank insignia of a narcotics officer.

He looked incredibly handsome.

He just couldn't understand what kind of woman that was.

Jiang Tian smiled, took out his phone, and dialed a number.

Sure enough, Wang Yifei, who was waiting for the elevator, made a move, taking out her phone as well.

I just agreed to your pursuit, and you do this? Have you fallen for someone else? You men are all the same! All I wanted was for you to buy me a birthday present, you poor wretch, if you didn't have the money, you should have said so earlier! Why did you have to do this?"

Even from that distance, Gao Fei could hear the woman's voice clearly.

"Captain Jiang, my condolences." Gao Fei remained silent for a moment, then offered a silent word of comfort.

He could remain calm even like this.

"Sigh, even a hero can be brought down by a penny." After recording, Jiang Tian turned off the hidden camera.

Gao Fei completely relaxed his guard, his face beaming. He had only been halfway there, but now, Gao Fei was ninety percent certain.

A few minutes later.

Jiang Tian and Gao Fei arrived at the private room upstairs.

Four people.

Jiang Tian's brow furrowed.

Something was wrong.

Because in his previous life, when this group was arrested, there were six people in total.

That meant one person was missing.

"Let me introduce you all, Captain Jiang, the son of the Vice Mayor of Yunhai, and currently the head of the anti-drug squad. Please give him a warm welcome," Gao Fei introduced solemnly.

"Hello, Captain Jiang."

"The Vice Mayor's son, you've met such an important person."

Welcoming voices rang out.

Jiang Tian remained noncommittal.

After the warm welcome, Gao Fei felt the atmosphere was just right and couldn't help but ask, "Captain Jiang, how much does an anti-drug officer earn a month?"

Jiang Tian glanced sideways and said calmly, "Six hundred yuan."

"Only six hundred? Captain Jiang, you risk your lives, and you only get six hundred a month?" The people at the table scoffed.

Jiang Tian's gaze swept over their faces.

These people were unforgettable to him; every single one of them was the culprit who, in his past life, forced their sisters into drugging and driving them to their deaths.

"After all, it's for protecting the lives and property of the country and its people," Jiang Tian said, feigning slight resentment.

This excited Gao Fei even more; he secretly thought he had a chance.

"Captain Jiang, this is a small token of our appreciation."

Gao Fei pulled a box from under the table.

Then he laboriously brought it to the table.

"What are you doing?" Jiang Tian asked, feigning surprise.

"Captain Jiang, this is a token of our brotherly affection," Gao Fei explained.

Jiang Tian lowered his eyes, opened the small box, glanced inside, and after a moment's thought, prepared to play along.

"Captain Jiang, there's a million here. If you worked, could you earn that much in your lifetime?" Gao Fei asked.

Six hundred a month, seven thousand a year—indeed, it would take at least 130 years to earn a million.

"What do you want to do with it?" Jiang Tian asked calmly, a cold smile playing on his lips.

"We have a shipment we want to bring in. Captain Jiang, when are you on duty at the border? Could you do us a favor?" Gao Fei said.

As he spoke, Jiang Tian subtly glanced around and noticed everyone at the table staring at him nervously and warily. If anything seemed amiss, they would instantly act.

"You're all the cream of the crop from Yunnan University. How did you end up on this path?" Jiang Tian asked knowingly.

"How much can the cream of the crop earn? Take Captain Jiang, for example. You graduated from police academy with great difficulty, and your father is the director of the Public Security Bureau and the deputy mayor. But what good is it? You're still empty-handed. We make astronomical sums on a single shipment—more than we could earn in a lifetime," Gao Fei continued.

Jiang Tian shook his head righteously, "Sigh, you guys, the risk is a bit too high. You'll have to figure it out yourselves."

"Captain Jiang." Everyone present paled.

Jiang Tian shook his head and sighed, "You make so much profit on each shipment, yet you're only willing to offer such a small return. The risk and the effort are disproportionate!"

Gao Fei visibly relaxed, "Captain Jiang, name your price."

Jiang Tian held out his hand.

"What?" Gao Fei sat up abruptly.

Returning to this era, Jiang Tian couldn't help but marvel at the extent to which drug traffickers were rampant.

Blatant bribery.

And the narcotics officers, while enduring the danger their families faced, had to resist this temptation and also eradicate drug traffickers.

One can imagine the terrifying price the narcotics officers paid in this era.

Every ray of peace was hard-won.

"Captain Jiang, I'm going to make a call." Gao Fei's face was grim; he hadn't expected Jiang Tian to have such a huge appetite, and he seemed unable to make the decision.

Upon hearing this, Jiang Tian's hands unconsciously clenched.

His expression remained unchanged, but Jiang Tian was deeply shaken, because this meant that this wasn't just Gao Fei on his own.

In other words, there was someone else behind Gao Fei.

Unexpectedly, Jiang Tian hadn't anticipated such a sudden and delightful surprise.

He originally intended to save his sister and, incidentally, take down a small-time drug dealer.

But he never dreamed that this drug dealer had an entire drug trafficking ring behind him.

The credit just fell into his lap!

After Gao Fei left, he disappeared for a while, but an hour later, he returned with several boxes.

Five boxes in total, neatly arranged with five million yuan.

Rampant.

This is rampant; this is how terrifying the rampant drug trafficking is in this era.

Jiang Tian was also certain that the other party was so generous because they wanted to drag him and his father into this mess.

Once the money was received,

they would be completely bound together.

But they probably never imagined this.

"Captain Jiang, the money's all here." Gao Fei's teeth ached.

He secretly hated Jiang Tian for being so greedy, but the thought of controlling Jiang Tian's family from now on made Gao Fei's heart tremble.

He thought of Jiang Xiaoyu.

Gao Fei sneered inwardly. He'd take back whatever he got now, with interest, and not only that, he'd take Jiang Xiaoyu too…

Thinking this, Gao Fei felt a little less pain and picked up a fruit knife to cut the watermelon.

“Captain Jiang, this watermelon is good.” Gao Fei was in high spirits.

“What are you trying to do with that knife?” Jiang Tian suddenly stood up, furious.

Me?

Gao Fei was completely dumbfounded.

He then noticed that the hidden camera was somehow attached to Jiang Tian's chest. Jiang Tian, ​​his face filled with shock, said, “You drug dealers are not only audacious, but you even dare to openly threaten the police with knives?”

Gao Fei's head was buzzing, even more confused.

But then he saw Jiang Tian pull out a gun.

“No, I'm just cutting the watermelon.”

Jiang Tian… Bang!!!

…

Meanwhile, at the entrance to the private room.

Li Zijing stood at the door with Jiang Xiaoyu and three others.

They had heard every word spoken inside the room.

“Brother…?” Jiang Xiaoyu covered her mouth in disbelief.

Zhao Wei and Li Zijing were even more terrified.

They hadn't expected Jiang Tian to be so audacious.

They certainly hadn't expected Jiang Tian to actually become a black sheep.

But the next moment…

Bang!!!

While they were still reeling from the shock,

a gunshot suddenly rang out from the private room.

The sound was deafening.

The next moment…

When they rushed inside…

What they saw…

Jiang Tian held up his gun, as if calling roll.

Those sitting at the table seemed completely oblivious.

Bang! Bang! Bang!!!

Jiang Tian fired, headbutt after headshot, expressionless.

Gao Fei sat next to Jiang Tian, ​​holding a fruit knife, his face blank.

“Zhao Wei, make the following record: Just now, five drug dealers openly tried to bribe me, a public servant, to help them transport drugs. I refused to yield, and the dealers attempted to attack me with knives. I was forced to retaliate with my gun, successfully killing four, arresting one, and seizing five million yuan in drug money.”

Gao Fei: “???”

I just wanted to cut a watermelon, why did it turn out like this?



Chapter 18 Collapse: You're not a cop, you're a madman.


Rewind three minutes to when Gao Fei entered the private room.

Downstairs, Li Zijing and Zhao Wei, worried, brought their men down.

Li Zijing, a veteran of the police force for two or three years, had a keen sense of things and immediately suspected Gao Fei was involved.

Furthermore, Jiang Tian's actions hinted at corruption.

Jiang Xiaoyu was also extremely anxious.

"Don't worry, Xiaoyu, Brother Jiang loves you so much, he would never agree to Gao Fei pursuing you," Lian Xin comforted Jiang Xiaoyu.

The four of them reached the door of the private room, and through the not-so-secured door, the sounds of conversation coming from inside could be clearly heard.

Inside the private room.

Gao Fei's four accomplices were eating and chatting happily.

Who was Jiang Tian? A young, high-ranking anti-drug squad leader.

Most terrifying was Jiang Tian's background—his father was the director of the Yunhai Public Security Bureau!

In this situation,

Jiang Tian was dragged into it, and through him, his father was also implicated.

Throughout Yunhai,

they will be able to act without restraint from now on.

What does this represent? It represents enormous profits.

Five million.

That's terrifying.

Especially in this era, five million is terrifying.

For those within the system, it's an astronomical figure, considering Jiang Tian's monthly salary is only seven hundred yuan, and that's his current income after becoming a full-fledged employee.

Before becoming a full-fledged employee, during his probationary period, Jiang Tian earned two hundred and thirty yuan a month.

And that's with high standards and high benefits.

Even now, Jiang Tian's monthly salary is higher than that of Jiang Peng, the police chief.

After all, the police chief's monthly salary is only five hundred yuan.

Yes, you read that right, that's his monthly take-home pay.

Five million—that's indeed a terrifying number.

However, for Jiang Tian, ​​this was no less than a provocation from drug dealers.

A provocation against the judicial authorities.

“Brother Gao’s watermelon-cutting skills are pretty good, straight and even, hahaha, Captain Jiang, don’t worry, no one can guess our delivery route.”

In short, four words:

Absolutely audacious.

To what extent?

They used Yunnan University as their drug den.

They rented a classroom in the university’s entrepreneurship park.

They conducted drug trafficking activities there.

It could be said that they took the darkness under their noses to the extreme; probably no one would have imagined that their drug den would be located inside a top-tier university.

Turning some of the brightest minds directly into drug addicts.

The case is huge, terrifying.

Bang!

A drug dealer stood up angrily.

But the next moment...

The three drug dealers who had stood up were each shot in the head.

Wasn't Jiang Tian a good-for-nothing second-generation rich kid?

Wasn't he bribed by them?

"What are you doing with those fruit knives? Are you trying to coerce me, to coerce the police?" Jiang Tian sneered.

What a joke.

Threatening him was one thing, but threatening his family was another.

In his past life, these people killed his sister.

Jiang Tian had no interest in playing this game of cat and mouse with them.

Bang!!!

A gunshot rang out, and the drug dealer instantly fell to the ground.

Gao Fei couldn't be killed yet, because Jiang Tian keenly sensed that there were probably bigger fish behind Gao Fei.

Indeed, killing Gao Fei, the mastermind, would be too easy for him.

When Li Zijing and Zhao Wei entered,

"Zhao Wei, take the following record: Just now, five drug dealers openly tried to bribe me, a public servant, to help them transport drugs. I refused to yield, and the dealers attempted to attack me with knives. I was forced to fight back, successfully killing four, arresting one, and seizing five million yuan in drug money."

Then he calmly placed it on his waist.

Gulp!!!

Zhao Wei swallowed hard.

She was stunned.

He was afraid.

A madman.

This is a madman.

Gao Fei stared at Jiang Tian in horror, momentarily stunned. He thought back to how he had initially treated Jiang Tian like a lamb, a good-for-nothing rich kid who was just waiting to die.

He thought he could easily drag him into this mess and then let these drug dealers control him.

Don't underestimate this private room; it was the place where they paid, and it was under the most concealed surveillance cameras.

Once Jiang Tian accepted the money, Jiang Tian and his father would be trapped in their control for life.

This was a common trick used by drug dealers.

A school leader was easily manipulated by this method, with just 100,000 yuan, allowing them to place drugs in the school's entrepreneurship park with almost no restraint.

Then they discovered something.

This guy is no lamb to the slaughter.

This guy is a madman!

A complete and utter madman.

Just because he was cutting a watermelon with a watermelon knife, he turned around and shot his accomplices dead, firing shots in a flurry.

Slap!!!

A madman who kills without blinking an eye.

“What are you standing there for? Did you remember it?”

Having just killed several people, Jiang Tian was seething with killing intent, his eyes seemingly bloodshot, and his every word exuded a palpable murderous aura.

Zhao Wei jolted, his hands trembling, and quickly pulled out his notebook and pen, scribbling furiously: "I've got it, I've got it, don't kill me."

Hey!!!

Jiang Tian was speechless. Was he really that scary?

If these drug dealers hadn't threatened Jiang Tian and his sister, it would have been one thing, but these drug dealers dared to openly threaten his sister and family. How could Jiang Tian tolerate that?

Besides, it was the police's duty to crack down on drug dealers.

Moreover, the anti-narcotics police were strictly regulated by the police law, allowing them to use unlimited self-defense against drug dealers if they perceived any danger.

This level of self-defense was quite significant.

Jiang Tian looked at Li Zijing, who was stunned, and sighed inwardly. No wonder the drug dealers were so arrogant with this kind of attitude.

For Jiang Tian, ​​to eradicate drug dealers, he had to be even more arrogant than them.

More ruthless, more brutal.

Jiang Tian pulled out handcuffs from his lower back.

*Click!*

He handcuffed Gao Fei's hands behind her back.

"I'm bleeding! I'm bleeding! I need to go to the hospital!" Gao Fei cried out in despair.

As time passed and the adrenaline subsided, she felt a piercing pain.

Her face turned deathly pale almost instantly.

*Slap!*

Jiang Tian slapped her hard. "Shut up! Can't you see I'm performing official duties? Obstructing official business is an aggravated offense, don't you know?"

As he spoke, Jiang Tian looked at the bright red mark next to Gao Fei on his radar.

He was already impatiently waiting to know how many trial points Gao Fei would bring him.

"I'm going to sue you! I'm going to sue you! You heartless bastard! You're not a cop, you're an executioner! You're a madman! You're a complete lunatic!" Gao Fei was nearly insane.

He felt Jiang Tian was absolutely insane.

A complete and utter madman.

A policeman, yet he was countless times more ruthless than drug dealers like them! They were drug dealers, yet the policeman had shot several of them dead without a word.

Don't you need a trial for executions?

Don't you need evidence for executions?

Just because he took a fruit knife to cut a watermelon, he accused me of kidnapping him.

...

"Ugh!!!"

Just then, a sound of vomiting suddenly rang out.

Jiang Tian turned around and saw Jiang Xiaoyu and Lian Xin vomiting violently outside the door.

Two young girls.

These were young girls still in school.

Heaven knows what they had gone through.

Gao Fei was their classmate.

Although he had always been chasing after Jiang Xiaoyu, his lack of boundaries was annoying and disgusting.

But they never even considered killing them!

Or shooting them!

Gao Fei's accomplices, while not in their class, were in the same department and often saw each other during large lectures.

These were all their classmates.

Now, they watched helplessly as these vibrant lives lay dead in pools of blood, their faces unrecognizable, pierced by bullets, blood everywhere.

When had these young girls ever experienced such trauma?

They were terrified.

Lian Xin collapsed to the ground, vomiting violently.

Jiang Xiaoyu, besides vomiting, was so pale she could barely stand.

Lian Xin only felt fear and disgust at seeing dead bodies, but Jiang Xiaoyu had much more to worry about.

"Just a few scoundrels, how come they were all shot dead?"

"Brother, you killed someone!" Jiang Xiaoyu's face was filled with terror.

At this moment, Jiang Xiaoyu's biggest worry was Jiang Tian. Murder is a crime, and murderers must pay with their lives—that's the education she'd received since childhood.

"Brother, you won't be shot, will you?"

Jiang Xiaoyu was terrified.

Jiang Tian comforted her from the side.

Meanwhile, inside the private room.

Li Zijing's hands were trembling as she dialed Captain Song's number on her phone.

Captain Song saw Li Zijing's call, a smirk playing on his lips, seemingly expecting it.

After all, drug dealers aren't so easy to find clues about.

Especially searching like headless flies is even less likely.

Searching for drug dealers would require technology, subtle clues, and reporting to the police, but these technologies were far beyond the capabilities of Jiang Tian and his two companions.

"It's a good thing to deflate Xiao Jiang's ego," Captain Song thought gleefully.

Nonsense.

The entire team received a first-class merit award, and he had a super-cop under his command—how could he not feel good?

Even the higher-ups specifically praised him.

Captain Song asked with a smile, "Xiao Li, are you running out of leads? If not, you can take your police dogs to the border to assist the border police in searching for people passing through. Maybe you'll run into them."

"Captain Song, something terrible has happened! We're at the Shengxiang Hotel across from Yunnan University. Captain Jiang killed four or five people!" Li Zijing said, her voice trembling.

Silence fell on the other end of the phone.

After an unknown amount of time, Captain Song's trembling voice finally came through: "Jiang Tian shot four or five?"

"Yes, four were shot in the head, and one was shot in the thigh," Li Zijing confirmed accurately.

He forgot.

Captain Song suddenly forgot something.

Because the mission was urgent, Jiang Tian went home to rest early last night, and he forgot to give Jiang Tian psychological counseling.

Thinking of this, Song Liguo's heart skipped a beat.

"I just saw them seemingly preparing several million to bribe Captain Jiang, but Captain Jiang shot them all."



Chapter 19 Uncovers a Tremendous Case, the Sky Is Falling Down


For police and military personnel, psychological counseling is essential in any operation resulting in death or injury.

However, Jiang Tian's psychological counseling was slightly delayed due to his meritorious service yesterday and the urgent award ceremony today.

It wasn't done immediately.

The psychological impact on an individual, especially after murder, is terrifying, something Song Liguo, having experienced it himself, fully understands.

Song Liguo's heart sank.

An ominous premonition grew stronger.

Damn it.

They finally have a war god and police god in Yunhai. If, due to inadequate psychological counseling, he commits a mistake or indiscriminately kills innocent people,

even with Jiang Tian's great achievements, he won't be able to get past this hurdle.

Half an hour later.

Song Liguo arrived at the scene.

As far as the eye could see, four bodies lay scattered in the private room, and another was injured and bound.

"Jiang Tian," Song Liguo said, his face extremely serious.

Four lives lost.

This is an accident.

A massive accident.

Three or more lives lost at once, regardless of location, is a catastrophic event.

Even an accident with three or more deaths is terrifying; it can cause a major upheaval.

Let alone four already dead.

“Chief Song, these five people at the scene are all students from Yunnan University,” Jiang Tian saluted.

Hiss!!!

Song Liguo's face turned deathly pale.

Damn it, top students from Yunnan University?

Song Liguo's head was about to explode. This is terrible, this is going to blow up.

It's a disaster.

The sky has fallen!

Song Liguo had been in the anti-drug team for so many years, and he hadn't encountered many truly devastating events, but in two days, the sky had fallen twice.

Song Liguo wasn't sure if it was his age or the immense shock he'd experienced, but his heart was starting to ache.

"You managed to kill four of Yunnan University's top students?" Song Liguo's mind went blank.

"Chief Song, they weren't just top students from Yunnan University, students from top-tier universities, they were a group of ruthless and audacious drug dealers." Jiang Tian's eyes flashed.

Huh?

Drug dealers?

Song Liguo tilted his head back and took a deep breath.

Good heavens.

He thought to himself, "Good heavens."

Four of Yunnan University's top students, all drug dealers?

Song Liguo's face paled even more. Was this a good thing?

No, no, no.

This wasn't a good thing!

Damn it, university students, top-tier university students, all turned to drug trafficking in Yunhai.

This just goes to show how rampant drug trafficking is.

The higher-ups were already extremely dissatisfied with Yunhai, and now, good heavens, even a top university has a drug trafficking gang! Song Liguo didn't even want to think about it.

Because if even a top university has drug dealers, how rampant must drug trafficking be throughout Yunhai?

Jiang Tian also sighed.

To be honest.

In his previous life, his father Jiang Peng and Song Liguo were both placed under investigation.

To be honest, in the month since joining the team, Song Liguo had taken good care of Jiang Tian in every way.

Especially in many matters, Song Liguo basically prioritized Jiang Tian's needs. Besides their official relationship, their private relationship was also quite good.

Song Liguo had been Jiang Tian's neighbor since childhood, and the two families had always had a good relationship. The investigation of both Song Liguo and his father into the "double regulation" (a form of internal party discipline) had two contributing factors.

This is the truth Song Liguo revealed after being placed under "double regulation," witnessing Jiang Tian's decline and downfall.

The truth was that the drug trafficking network in Yunhai was rampant.

Two months before Jiang Tian joined the team, a major drug lord gang was busted domestically, with over 100 kilograms of methamphetamine, commonly known as crystal meth, seized in a single operation.

This successful case should have been a cause for celebration.

However, besides the credit for those who solved the case, it also exposed the inadequacy of domestic drug control efforts, which drew serious attention from higher authorities.

The dangers of drugs are well-known; 300 kilograms can destroy countless families.

Fifty grams is enough for a death sentence; 300 kilograms is utterly catastrophic.

Finally, the investigation revealed that the drugs originated from Yunhai.

This incident completely ignited the dissatisfaction of higher authorities.

Furthermore, of all the drugs seized domestically, tracing their source reveals that while 70% might be a bit high, at least 50% spread nationwide through Yunhai.

The higher-ups are extremely dissatisfied with the overall anti-drug efforts in Yunhai.

From top to bottom, Gao Xiaolong was merely a catalyst.

What ignited all of this was the inadequacy of Yunhai's anti-drug efforts.

The higher-ups are already considering replacing him.

In other words, if no results are achieved, Jiang Tian understands that both his father and Song Liguo will likely be moved.

To be replaced by someone more capable of managing the situation.

While the drug traffickers Jiang Tian eliminated yesterday may have slowed the trend, it's not a fundamental solution. Essentially, drug trafficking in Yunhai remains rampant.

Even a narcotics officer like him dares to openly accept bribes.

Jiang Tian can't even imagine just how terrifying and rampant the drug traffickers in Yunhai truly are.

No…

Jiang Tian suddenly thought of his past life. After his father stepped down, the newly appointed bureau chief only lasted three months before dying in an accident. Not only him, but his family members were also involved in a car accident.

Afterwards, it seemed to be because of the investigation of a drug dealer.

Jiang Tian took a deep breath. Overall, the fight against drugs in Yunhai was a long and arduous task.

Jiang Tian clenched his fists. He absolutely could not let the tragedy of his past life repeat itself.

If he didn't have the ability, so be it. But looking at his terrifying stats, Jiang Tian believed that with the ability, he absolutely had to eradicate the entire Yunhai.

“Drug dealers, even Yunda University has drug dealers.” Song Liguo's eyelids twitched.

Damn it.

How could a little investigation reveal such a terrifying situation?

There's a saying that goes, when you see a cockroach, there are already countless cockroaches in the corners you can't see.

"Yunnan University's pride and joy! A bright future after graduation, how did they end up on this path? What kind of education does Yunnan University provide?" Song Liguo clutched his agitated heart.

Jiang Tian didn't hide anything either: "Not only that, they also used Yunnan University's entrepreneurship park as their drug trafficking hub. It's blind under the lamp. To be honest, if they hadn't told me, I wouldn't have even imagined they could be so audacious."

Buzz!

It exploded.

Song Liguo completely exploded, his eyes widening as he stared at Jiang Tian.

His chest felt like it was about to burst.

His head felt like it was about to explode too.

"Jiang Tian, ​​can you take responsibility for every word you've said?" Song Liguo's voice trembled low.

This has blown the sky.

This is another bombshell.

It can't be contained, it's simply impossible to contain.

Song Liguo couldn't believe these people dared to be so crazy.

Yes, even Jiang Tian hadn't expected them to be so crazy, so audacious.

Because, without them, who would have thought that a top-tier university would become a drug den?

The narcotics police would never have imagined a drug den could exist in such a place.

They've gone mad.

Completely mad, Song Liguo knew this was about to explode.

This is a bombshell.

“I’m 100% sure. They just tried to bribe me with five million, and that guy even had a fruit knife and seemed about to attack me. To protect myself, I had to strike first and take care of the drug dealers. This one was the leader; I risked my life to stay behind. Is that alright?” Jiang Tian explained softly.

No matter what, four lives are no small matter.

“If what you’re saying is true, none of this is a big deal. Not only is it not a big deal, it’s a monumental achievement,” Song Liguo said through gritted teeth.

Jiang Tian exposed this achievement, and while he got the credit, the Yunhai anti-drug team might not fare so well.

The higher-ups would hold them accountable from top to bottom.

Fortunately, he blew the snot himself, making amends.

If an outsider had discovered it… ugh, Song Liguo didn’t even want to think about it.

“By the way, I suggest we interrogate Gao Fei quickly. He has connections, and there might be accomplices who have escaped capture,” Jiang Tian said quickly.

Song Liguo also knew the seriousness of the situation: “I know without you saying it. For a college student to come into contact with these criminal forces, there must be someone instructing or even guiding him.”

“Captain Guo, take your men and go to the school immediately to investigate. Once the evidence is confirmed, immediately seal off the entire school. Jiang Tian, ​​you come with me to report to Chief Gao,” Song Liguo said.

A top-tier university!

This matter could become a major incident if not handled properly. Song Liguo didn't dare to act on his own and left with Jiang Tian.

However, as Jiang Tian was leaving, he saw Xiao Bo watching the commotion at the elevator entrance in the lobby.

At this moment, a man with a sinister expression was staring at him, holding a phone in his hand: "Yes, Director Sun, I guarantee it's absolutely true. It's utterly audacious! They falsely accused college students of being drug dealers and shot several college students in a fit of anger! Don't worry, I would never lie to you. I guarantee it with my integrity."

Xiao Bo's integrity seemed to be quite effective; the other party hung up and did something else.

Jiang Tian and Song Liguo, along with Jiang Xiaoyu and Lian Xin, two junior high school girls acting as witnesses, sat in the back of the police car. Both girls' faces were pale.

They watched as the wailing sirens of police cars pierced the streets.

In this urgent situation, there was no time to hide their whereabouts.

The matter had escalated significantly.

Before they even arrived at the police station, Secretary Zhou Zhao of the Municipal Party Committee, Director Jiang Peng, and the deputy director were already waiting at the station entrance.

Gao Xiaolong took the lead, his face grave and serious.

If Jiang Tian's words were true...

Gao Xiaolong could hardly imagine the extent of drug trafficking in Yunhai, how rampant the drug dealers were.

A top university used as a drug den.

Top university students becoming drug dealers.

This was nothing short of a blatant provocation against the authorities.

"Report, report, this is Action Team Two. We have found twenty kilograms of methamphetamine in the Entrepreneurship Park."

When they arrived at the police station, Yunhai University, the closest university to the hotel, had already been raided by Captain Guo's team, who had indeed found evidence of drugs.

At that moment, a voice crackled from the walkie-talkie.

Jiang Peng, his face grim, watched the anti-drug convoy enter the police station.

The atmosphere was heavy; no one spoke.

Who dared to speak?

At this moment, Gao Xiaolong's face was so dark it could drip water.

"Who just said Jiang Tian was a black sheep, a cancer?"

Gao Xiaolong turned to look behind him, his face grim.

The shooting of four college students was a serious matter.

Gao Xiaolong and Zhou Zhao had come to the police station immediately to confront him.

Of course, most importantly, to find the person who had delivered the message to them.

"Who said Jiang Tian was unruly, a black sheep, a cancer in the police force, arrogant and spoiled, and that because of a petty squabble, as a narcotics officer, he shot and killed four college students and should be executed?" Gao Xiaolong raised his voice even higher.

He was furious.

Gao Xiaolong was completely enraged.

Heaven knows, when he went to the municipal party committee to learn about the overall drug control situation in Yunhai, suddenly, people from the municipal party committee rushed into his and Zhou Zhao's office and started berating him.

They were startled; the shooting of four college students was a matter of utmost importance.

When they arrived and learned what had happened, they discovered that things weren't quite as they seemed.

Four college students shot dead?

Good riddance.

Absolutely good riddance.

But it also indirectly revealed the rampant drug trafficking.

"Drug police officers already face immense pressure and terrifying danger when dealing with drug traffickers, with the constant threat of death. And to have our own people drag us down at a time like this," Gao Xiaolong said, suppressing his anger, glancing at the person next to Jiang Peng.

Sun Haibo, the deputy director of Yunhai.

It was he who made the call to the municipal party committee.

He made the call without fully understanding the situation.

And these matters...

were not even discussed with Jiang Peng.

Jiang Peng glanced at Sun Haibo. It wasn't that the two were usually at odds; it was just that Sun Haibo had a history of underhanded tactics and sabotage.

Jiang Peng usually ignored such matters, but this time things had gone too far.

The news reached the police station, but instead of being relayed to him immediately, it was reported to a higher level, even with added embellishments.

Gao Xiaolong felt like killing someone.

With leaders like this, it's no wonder the drug dealers in Yunhai are so rampant.

With leaders acting like this, how can the narcotics officers below them perform their duties? Who would dare entrust their life to someone who betrays them like this?

At this moment, the one whose mentality was most shattered was undoubtedly Sun Haibo.

Sun Haibo knew Xiao Bo's character well.

In the past, he had greatly valued Xiao Bo.

He greatly admired Xiao Bo, considering him a capable and principled leader.

Xiao Bo handled both professional knowledge and interpersonal relationships exceptionally well.

If trained well, he could take over the anti-drug squad in the future, putting it under his control.

This time, Sun Haibo decided to trust Xiao Bo. If successful, he could bring down the currently powerful Jiang Peng and his son, freeing up a position for himself.

But who knew?

Damn it, Xiao Bo had completely screwed him over.

Looking at his powerful backer in the municipal party committee, looking at him with murderous intent,

and seeing the disdain of his superiors,

Sun Haibo felt utterly dejected.

"I admired and trusted you so much, and you've ruined me like this?"

"Xiao Bo, you've ruined me!" Sun Haibo's eyes were filled with resentment.

However, Gao Xiaolong didn't seem to pursue the matter further at this point, because the most important thing right now was the Yunda drug trafficking case.

"Comrades, this is a disgrace, a colossal disgrace! The higher-ups sent me here prepared for rampant drug trafficking in Yunhai, but we never expected it to reach such a terrifying level. A top university has become a drug den, and top university students are involved in drug trafficking gangs! What is this? This is dereliction of duty in drug control! This is your dereliction of duty! This is the dereliction of duty by the entire Yunhai!" Gao Xiaolong roared in fury.



Chapter 20 I'm doing a good deed, Xiao Bo, what are you doing?


"At this critical juncture, we must seize the time to interrogate Gao Fei, whom we've arrested. He's the only survivor," Jiang Peng said, forced to speak at this point.

As the police chief, frankly, he couldn't escape responsibility for such a massive and horrific oversight in his area of ​​responsibility.

As for Liu Haibo, who was secretly reporting on him, Jiang Peng couldn't worry about that now.

However, one thing was certain: Sun Haibo's political career was essentially over.

Good heavens! Not only did the report bypass the proper channels and reach the municipal party committee, but it also resulted in this ridiculous blunder.

It gave everyone a real shock.

You have to understand, the wanton shooting of several university students, especially those from Yunhai, all because of a heated argument, meant that practically no one could protect Jiang Tian.

Even Gao Xiaolong was no exception, because this was something that could truly shake the heavens.

Don't you see, even when one student in a university jumps off a building due to excessive pressure, the entire school is on high alert, sweating profusely in the process; let alone when several people die directly.

But if these people are drug dealers, the impact is no less significant.

Because this represents an even more terrifying influence.

Jiang Tian got out of the car. At that moment, an ambulance was already rushing to Gao Fei's aid.

It wasn't exactly aid; he had just been shot in the thigh, receiving some basic emergency treatment, but it didn't interfere with their interrogation.

As soon as he got out of the car, he turned around and heard the shouting and discussions from the entrance of the police station.

Jiang Tian's hearing was terrifying. With numerous affinities, he was practically an invincible all-rounder.

His marksmanship was unparalleled, his hand-to-hand combat was also unparalleled, unbeatable at both close and long range.

Adding to this was a physical ability beyond its limits—though not yet at the gold level, it far surpassed that of ordinary people, and his hearing was terrifying, able to hear clearly even from such a distance.

“Sun Haibo.”

Jiang Tian narrowed his eyes, suddenly thinking of Sun Haibo.

If there was anyone who kicked his family while they were down after their family's downfall in his previous life, without a doubt, it was Sun Haibo. He was the most active and the most vocal in suppressing them.

He accused Jiang Peng of running a one-man show, blaming Jiang Peng entirely for the loss of control over the Yunhai drug cartel.

Besides all that, Sun Haibo could also be considered Xiao Bo's mentor.

Xiao Bo's rise to power was also inseparable from Sun Haibo's behind-the-scenes support.

But…

Jiang Tian's eyes flickered. If he remembered correctly, a few years later, Sun Haibo's case came to light.

After Jiang Peng's downfall, the newly appointed bureau chief met with an accident, and after Sun Haibo's case came to light, it was confirmed that Sun Haibo was responsible for the incident. Behind this, an even more terrifying and major case was involved.

And the person who exposed him in his previous life, barring any unforeseen circumstances, was Xiao Bo, whom he had personally promoted.

Xiao Bo, leveraging this achievement, rose even higher, surpassing Jiang Peng in rank before Jiang Tian's transmigration in his previous life, at less than forty years old.

At that time, he was truly at the height of his fame.

However, fate had other plans in his previous life.

In this life, Jiang Tian desperately wanted to know what path Xiao Bo would take.

“But now, I've seen your true colors. It seems you were the one who lied and caused such a huge misunderstanding for Sun Haibo. Xiao Bo, what do you have left to rely on in this life?” Jiang Tian thought to himself.

He still felt somewhat uneasy.

He felt he could find an opportunity to give the photos he had taken to Sun Haibo's fiancée.

“Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​you've done a great job. This case you solved is crucial. Time is of the essence. Immediately take your men and assist Branch Chief Song in investigating all the drug trafficking forces behind Gao Fei.”

After Jiang Tian walked over, Gao Xiaolong spoke to him immediately.

To be honest.

Right at the municipal party committee, Gao Xiaolong and Zhou Zhao lamented that Jiang Tian's personal abilities were sufficient, but anti-drug police were different from the military.

It's not enough to just have good marksmanship and agility to be perfectly competent.

Extremely rich experience in drug enforcement and criminal investigation is also required.

Drug enforcement officers are arguably the most dangerous and challenging branch of the police force.

The required professional knowledge and skills are comprehensive.

Based solely on yesterday's performance, Gao Xiaolong acknowledged Jiang Tian's combat capabilities, but regarding his experience in criminal investigation and drug enforcement, he remained somewhat skeptical.

His main motivation was to hone Jiang Tian's skills, hence the exceptional promotion.

Administratively, a squad leader is roughly equivalent to a deputy section chief, while a battalion commander is equivalent to a section chief.

Promoting Jiang Tian after only one month on the job was also part of Gao Xiaolong's strategy of giving him valuable experience.

Unexpectedly, on his very first day, he solved such a major case.

Especially his ruthless and decisive actions.

Drug enforcement officers desperately need elites like him.

Thinking this, Gao Xiaolong's admiration for Jiang Tian grew stronger.

One night.

Last night, he was still in a meeting berating Jiang Tian for being a black sheep.

He even asked around and found that many people were calling Jiang Tian a cancer, a black sheep, and someone who got in through connections.

Just yesterday, he had felt extreme disgust for Jiang Tian.

But now, Gao Xiaolong only wanted to know: Who was spreading rumors?

Who was targeting the police genius?

"Yes, sir!!!" Jiang Tian saluted.

Watching Jiang Tian lead his men into the interrogation room.

Gao Xiaolong's eyes filled with hatred. Such a genius—who was it?

Slandering a genius.

Spreading rumors about this police genius?

Police station conference room.

The conference room was large, easily four or five hundred square meters, enough to accommodate dozens or even hundreds of people.

Many things couldn't be determined solely by Jiang Tian's testimony.

Although the evidence was conclusive, the rules and regulations were in place.

Next, Jiang Tian gave another statement about the day's events, along with Jiang Xiaoyu who was with him.

The statements were largely consistent.

Jiang Tian didn't intend to hide anything, basically revealing everything in the conference room in front of all the leaders.

Including the five million yuan bribe, etc.

"Wait, how can we be sure this wasn't you initially soliciting a bribe, and then suddenly killing someone because you discovered someone eavesdropping outside?" Sun Haibo asked impatiently, as if he had discovered something.

The Jiang father and son grew increasingly arrogant.

For Sun Haibo, it was as unbearable as eating shit.

As a deputy director, he had no voice or presence in the police station; what use was this deputy director to him?

Especially with Jiang Tian's rapid rise to prominence and bright future,

Sun Haibo felt utterly miserable.

If Jiang Peng didn't fall, wouldn't he be stuck with no advancement even until retirement?

Now that he had finally found leverage over Jiang Tian, ​​how could Sun Haibo possibly let it go?

After all, Jiang Tian's achievements yesterday had already caused a sensation. With another such significant accomplishment today, who could possibly suppress the momentum of Jiang Tian and his son?

"Sun Haibo, now we're investigating the case," Jiang Peng said, tapping the table with a grim expression.

Sun Haibo's words carried a strong hint of leading and inducing.

A poor answer would imply that Jiang Tian had solicited bribes, accepted bribes, and so on. In that case, forget about any merit; they might even receive a demerit or a punishment that cancels out their achievements.

“We’re now investigating the case,” Sun Haibo said, his eyes fixed intently on Jiang Tian. “Could it be that you initially intended to accept bribes, and according to the surveillance footage, Gao Fei smuggled an additional four million afterward? Did you ultimately intend to kill him to cover your tracks, but unexpectedly, Li Zijing and her group suddenly stormed in, allowing you only enough time to fire a single shot that missed, failing to kill him?”

As Sun Haibo finished speaking, all eyes turned to Jiang Tian.

This was no small matter.

In fact, Sun Haibo’s suspicions had always existed within the police force, and the supervision of narcotics officers was particularly strict.

Drug dealers were willing to go to any lengths to tempt narcotics officers—money, sex, anything.

Some even used family members to coerce officers into coercing them.

Behind every bloody crime and every regulation in the past lay a tragic lesson.

The interrogation of Gao Fei is still ongoing. Jiang Tian was not involved in this matter. The police station naturally has interrogation experts. Jiang Tian was originally assisting with the case, but he was unexpectedly called over halfway through.

After Sun Haibo's analysis, everyone felt a sense of clarity.

He had analyzed almost everything, from cause to effect.

His analysis made perfect sense.

Everyone found it reasonable as well.

Criminal investigation is supposed to be about analyzing facts, right? But everyone present sensed something was amiss.

Jiang Tian looked at this person who, in his past life, had been the most eager to kick someone when they were down.

Then, recalling the major cases behind him, no one had imagined how terrifying the connections behind Deputy Director Sun Haibo were.

Terrifying enough to pave the way for Xiao Bo's future political career.

But now…

Jiang Tian's lips curled into a sneer, his face full of disdain. "Missed the shot? How about a bet, Deputy Director Sun? I'll let you run three thousand meters, and with a sniper rifle, I can kill you with a single shot?"

Huh?

Everyone suddenly remembered Jiang Tian's terrifying record from last night.

A record of kills with every shot.

"Deputy Director Sun, don't you know that if I didn't solicit bribes, how would the drug dealers trust me? How would I know their hideout was at Yunnan University?" Jiang Tian said, his expression unchanged.

But Sun Haibo's face was already purple with rage, yet he still forced himself to continue: "You're such a good shot, why didn't you stop them so we could set up the arrest? Why did you act without consulting your superiors?"

At this point, Sun Haibo could only grit his teeth and keep going.

Indeed, with proper planning, they might have gained even more.

But…

If they hadn't threatened Jiang Tian's family, Jiang Tian might have helped them find even more evidence.

“I faced five drug dealers alone. Are you blind? Didn't you see they were armed?” Jiang Tian slammed his fist on the table, pointing at Sun Haibo's face and unleashing a torrent of abuse.

Now that Jiang Tian was on the front lines, to be honest, even if Sun Haibo was the deputy director, he wouldn't back down.

His father, Jiang Peng, wasn't exactly weak-willed, but he wasn't particularly tough either.

His prestige within the police station was average, and Sun Haibo, relying on his seniority, had caused Jiang's father no shortage of trouble in the past.

And now…

He still dared to cause trouble. Jiang Tian wouldn't tolerate it.

“You dare to insult me? I'm the deputy director. What's wrong with asking you a couple of questions? They were just cutting a watermelon.” Sun Haibo's face darkened completely.

He had lost face in front of most of the anti-drug squad members.

“You say it’s like cutting a watermelon, and they cut a watermelon. Drug dealers are ruthless; our frontline officers are constantly in danger. What if it’s a sudden attack to kill? The first priority for narcotics officers is protecting their own safety. That’s stipulated in the Police Law. Or, Director Sun, why don’t you go talk to a few drug dealers? If they don’t make a move, can’t we narcotics officers make a move?” Jiang Tian retorted logically.

At this point, Jiang Tian sneered, “Besides, I’ve earned merit, while you haven’t earned any, yet you’re interrogating me, a meritorious officer, like a criminal. Sun Haibo, what are your intentions?”

Jiang Tian went straight for the kill.

Sun Haibo saw all the leaders staring at him with angry expressions, and his heart skipped a beat.

He’d angered everyone.

Then he looked at the narcotics officers’ eyes.

They were all burning with rage.

Hiss!!!

Jiang Tian had just directly put him on the opposite side.

Previously, Jiang's father didn't care, but Sun Haibo not only aggressively sought to establish his presence but also frantically consolidated his power and cultivated connections. The lower-level staff generally supported Sun Haibo.

That's why it's said they were in cahoots; Sun Haibo and Xiao Bo were exactly the same.

They were frantically recruiting people.

Many people were very protective of Sun Haibo, but now, Jiang Tian's words were practically saying, "You're sitting in a safe office, suppressing us frontline workers who have made contributions."

Very well.

Chapter 21 The arrogance of that adulterous couple deserves double the revenge.

Now, does this mean he even understands criminal investigation?

Police academy students begin their internships in their senior year, or at the very end of the second semester.

If the internship goes well, the police force will issue an internship certificate. If there are no problems, they will be officially hired by their original unit. However, there are exceptions, such as failing the internship or feeling it's unsuitable and wanting to transfer.

Jiang Tian essentially joined the narcotics unit directly in the second semester of his senior year.

Jiang Xiaoyu.

Every rule, every warning, comes from a bloody lesson.

The so-called radar warning means that if a criminal with murderous intent or a serious crime is found within a kilometer, an automatic alert will be issued.

That bitch!

Chapter 22 Political Legacy: Ultimately Leading to the Pinnacle of Power

Drug dealers are a bunch of ruthless thugs.

This administrator was a man in his thirties. He didn't hold any official position at the school, but he wielded considerable power.

The most crucial aspect of drug dealing is the distinction between suppliers and distributors. Gao Fei had revealed everything about his network.

His distributors consisted of two individuals from various walks of life, and all transactions took place in this very classroom at the university.

Wow, a prestigious university was being used as a drug trafficking location.

This is troublesome.

The distributors Gao Fei mentioned have been apprehended. As for the suppliers, they primarily maintained single-line contact.

That is, they only communicated directly when delivering goods.

The delivery location was here, but the recipient only contacted them upon arrival.

Jiang Tian repeatedly reviewed the details of cases from his previous life and compared them to this one.

There were many hidden secrets, especially regarding the sixth person.

Lian Ying?

According to the latest case information, your school's student council president, Wei Rong, whom you awarded one of the school's top ten outstanding students, is the leader and instigator of this gang. Good heavens.

Jiang Tian exclaimed in disbelief.

Jiang Tian hadn't considered this connection at all. He didn't have time to think about how Wei Rong, a rich second-generation, would be involved in drug trafficking.

When Branch Manager Song called, a large police force had already been deployed to investigate and apprehend Wei Rong.

Besides the school's police force, others had already gone to places Wei Rong might have been.

The year 2000 had only recently passed, and the nationwide surveillance network wasn't yet extensive, making solving cases and apprehending criminals far more difficult than in later generations.

The crime-solving rate in this era was extremely low.

"I know the place, I'll take you there," Lian Ying said hurriedly.

Good heavens.

How could he not know? Lian Ying had even visited Wei Rong's dormitory a few days ago, specifically chatting with this outstanding student and inquiring about his living conditions.

Now, damn it.

Lian Ying felt like killing Wei Rong.

Watching Lian Ying run off, Jiang Tian pursed his lips and remained silent.

At that moment, he suddenly understood why Xiao Bo, after he had fallen to rock bottom in his previous life, seemed to have taken off like a rocket.

there was also Lian Ying.

Because if this hadn't been caught and exposed, the problem would have been terrifying.

Throughout the days, they might have dragged in more and more students.

It was horrifying.

If things got out of control, Lian Ying might even face imprisonment.

And the principal of Yun University, a prestigious institution, possessed political connections and official positions.

This was something Jiang's father couldn't even imagine.

But now...

If it were just that, it wouldn't be so bad. The crucial point is that Xiao Bo showed absolutely no gratitude.

Instead, they suppressed him at every turn, ultimately cutting off all his means of survival. They not only forced him to resign, but even had the beast they'd raised for over ten years beat him to death.

But now…

Jiang Tian's eyes flickered; he was about to reach the pinnacle of power.

"Young comrade, Wei Rong's dormitory building is just ahead."

As Jiang Tian pondered this, Lian Ying, with a kind face, seemed to find Jiang Tian increasingly pleasing to the eye.



Chapter 23: Saving the University President, Drug Dealers Go Crazy


"He lives on the third floor, room 309. I don't know if Wei Rong is home right now. After all, it's Sunday, and his family lives in the city, so he might go home," Lian Ying said.

This guy, because of his family's donations to the school, and his own good grades, was not only the student council president but also selected as one of the top ten outstanding students.

Thinking about this, Lian Ying's face was more disgusting than if she had eaten shit.

However, Jiang Tian clearly understood that although Lian Ying's attitude was good now, Lian Ying was the president of a key university.

High position and great power.

This was true high position and great power, an administrative level that even Jiang's father couldn't match.

Compared to Jiang Tian, ​​he was practically a figure from heaven.

But now, the early discovery of this case, if its impact is minor, has undeniably saved Lian Ying's political career.

This political legacy.

Jiang Tian narrowed his eyes. In his previous life, he had sensed something was amiss, because after his family's downfall, Xiao Bo's promotions had been meteoric.

At the time, he hadn't thought much of it.

But now, Jiang Tian realized that it was probably because he had given Xiao Bo the clues to this case in his previous life, ultimately providing him with ample political resources and allowing him to pursue that second-generation rich kid.

And ultimately, he successfully rose higher and higher.

It could be said that he had given Xiao Bo a meteoric rise. All of this—the clues, etc.—was provided by Jiang Tian, ​​yet Xiao Bo showed him no gratitude whatsoever.

"This must be it. Damn, five million so easily, only a rich kid like him could pull that out. And what a waste of his good fortune, dealing drugs."

Jiang Tian thought to himself, clicking his tongue in amazement, then looked at Principal Lian and said, "Principal Lian, please wait here. We're not sure if the drug dealers have any dangerous weapons."

"Thank you for your trouble," Lian Ying said gratefully.

Jiang Tian turned to look at Captain Guo.

Jiang Tian hadn't intended to say much; Captain Guo could handle most things. However, Principal Lian had come straight to him.

Jiang Tian could only helplessly shrug.

"It's alright, you did a great job. You've saved Yunhai a huge loss this time. It's just that the drug dealers were too arrogant," Captain Guo said with a smile, not saying much more.

Because this case was big, no matter what, they would get a share of the profits, and maybe even some collective credit.

Following Jiang Tian around and reaping the collective credit, especially since he had just saved them, how could Captain Guo possibly be angry or overthink it?

His expression towards Jiang Tian was as amiable as could be.

However, just as Captain Guo and his team were about to go inside, Jiang Tian suddenly grabbed him: "Wait."

"What's wrong?" Captain Guo asked, puzzled.

At this point, they were very close to the dormitory building. Yunnan University, a key university, had a very large campus.

They hadn't noticed it at first upon entering the school, but as they got closer to the men's dormitory...

Jiang Tian's map alert appeared.

A scarlet map alert.

Jiang Tian frowned: "That Wei Rong might have a weapon."

He looked at the scarlet target. A drug dealer of this caliber might actually have firearms.

"Wei Rong is just a student, no matter what. We'll be careful, nothing will happen," Captain Guo reassured him.

Lian Ying also chimed in, "Comrade, Wei Rong shouldn't be here."

As he spoke, his gaze darted nervously towards the dormitory building.

As they arrived, students passing by the dormitory building looked at them with curiosity.

This was the men's dormitory.

Yunnan University, as a key university, had many students from all over the country. Even during holidays, most students spent their weekends on campus.

Lian Ying couldn't bear to think about it.

If that damn Wei Rong had a weapon and was openly using it in this dormitory building, the thought sent chills down Lian Ying's spine.

"Young comrades, thank you for your hard work," Lian Ying tried to comfort him.

But the next moment, before Lian Ying could even react, a sharp pain shot through his abdomen.

Lian Ying nearly vomited blood, exclaiming, "You kicked me?"

...

Meanwhile,

Inside the dormitory building, in a six-person room.

Because it was the weekend, only two students were in the room.

"Holy crap, so many police cars! What happened?" one of the students asked in surprise, peering out the window.

"President, do you think something happened in our dorm?" the student asked casually, still peering out the window.

Bang!!!

Before the student could finish speaking, a deafening sound rang in his ears, truly resounding throughout his entire head.

The sound was incredibly loud.

It was as if a huge firecracker had been set off right next to his ear; his entire head was buzzing.

The student's eyes widened, his peripheral vision shifting until he saw the student council president he'd spoken of, gun pointed downwards. A chill ran down his spine.

The gun, still wisps of smoke rising from the muzzle, testified that the man had just fired; the muzzle was still warm.

Just moments before the gunshot rang out.

Jiang Tian's mental alert reached its peak.

A sharp pain shot through his brow.

The police car pulled up right in front of the dormitory. After everyone got out, Jiang Tian stood with Lian Ying, preparing to leave the leaders outside while they rushed in.

That terrifying sense of crisis rose within him.

[Perfect Shot (Gold)]

[Scanning Radar (Gold)]

[Martial Arts Master (Red)]

[Strong Physique (Green)] [Minor Mastery of Disguise] [Exceptional Memory (Green)] [Minor Mastery of Gambling (Green)]...

[Sin Value: 2000]

Jiang Tian's stats are now practically explosive.

Especially his Scanning Radar; within a kilometer radius, it can instantly warn of any danger or enemy.

Especially in life-or-death situations, it can manifest a terrifying, spider-like sense of awareness.

Combined with his Martial Arts Master combat prowess and reflexes, Jiang Tian kicked him away almost without hesitation.

"You kicked me?"

Lian Ying, who had held such a high position for so long, had never been kicked before, but today he had.

As Jiang Tian kicked him away, his body tilted to the ground.

Bang!!!

At this critical moment, a gunshot rang out.

Lian Ying instinctively covered his ears.

His face was deathly pale.

"Quick, the second window on the third floor, fire!"

Captain Guo, without a second's hesitation, shouted.

After all, they were veteran narcotics officers, seasoned veterans, having fought countless battles with drug dealers. These were ruthless, inhuman individuals, truly capable of anything.

Captain Guo pinpointed the location of the gunshot in half a second and immediately gave the order.

Without giving the order, Jiang Tian grabbed the stunned Lian Ying and sprinted into the dormitory.

Hearing the gunshot outside, Lian Ying's face turned pale.

At that moment, he felt an itch in his ear, and instinctively touched it, only to see his hand covered in blood.

"Principal Lian, the situation was urgent just now." Jiang Tian, ​​holding his pistol, was also shaken.

It was a close call.

He stood next to Lian Ying. In that moment of extreme tension, Jiang Tian didn't even have time to react to whether the bullet was aimed at him or Lian Ying.

The situation was urgent; he had no other choice.

However, Jiang Tian glanced at the trajectory and was fairly certain that the bullet was aimed at Lian Ying.

But Jiang Tian thought about it and realized it made sense. Given Wei Rong's condition, it was impossible for the other party to recognize him in such a short time, nor would they have had the time, especially since he was fully armed and wearing a helmet.

An unfamiliar person wouldn't recognize him at all.

"Thank you, young comrade." Lian Ying's face was pale, his forehead was covered in cold sweat, and he was still shaken.

He looked at Jiang Tian. Lian Ying knew it was a close call.

"Was it Wei Rong who did it?" Lian Ying still couldn't believe it; after all, his impression of Lian Ying had always been positive.

Jiang Tian nodded, gun in hand. "That's why we crack down on drugs so severely. Once they're involved, they're capable of anything, whether it's trafficking or using drugs."

It's too ruthless.

To be honest, Jiang Tian also felt the immense danger.

That's why anti-narcotics police are one of the few departments that are constantly under fire even in peacetime.

Because drug dealers really are capable of anything.

"Young comrade, thank you so much," Lian Ying said repeatedly, still shaken.

"Everyone, get back to your dorms quickly, don't show yourselves," Jiang Tian said quickly when he saw some students peeking out of their dorms.

Fortunately, it was the weekend, so there weren't too many students.

Jiang Tian, ​​gun in hand, was about to go upstairs.

But then he glanced at the radar and noticed the red dot moving continuously.

Captain Guo, seeing Jiang Tian hadn't followed, said, "Where are you going? The drug dealers are upstairs."

"Forget it, this kid's still young. Let's go up first and teach him a lesson later."

Captain Guo hesitated, leaving the rest of his sentence unfinished.

Mainly, Jiang Tian's unauthorized action against the drug dealers had almost earned him a severe dressing-down from Captain Guo if it weren't for yesterday's events.

"I have God's-eye view, what can you do against me?" Jiang Tian, ​​leaving with a look of delight, didn't hear Captain Guo's words.

This God's-eye view was a true weapon of mass destruction.

He didn't go upstairs. Following the direction the red dot moved, he walked directly through the dormitory and stood against the wall at the corner of another stairwell.

Through this spot, he could see the stairs above.

Although there was no sound from upstairs, Jiang Tian, ​​with his omniscient perspective, knew that Wei Rong was up there.

Sure enough, two seconds later, a foot slowly descended the stairs.

Click!

Just then, the dormitory door next to Jiang Tian opened, and a head peeked out.

Jiang Tian frowned, retracted the foot, and gestured for the student to be quiet.

Damn it, if the situation weren't so bad, Jiang Tian would have slapped him.

He dared to watch any kind of commotion; he was truly courting death.

But thankfully, a few seconds later, the foot seemed impatient and hurried down.

The next moment, the entire figure came into Jiang Tian's view.

Face to face, the man visibly froze upon seeing Jiang Tian. When a gun was pointed at Jiang Tian, ​​he raised his hand and said, "I surrender."

Bang!!!

But before he could finish speaking, Jiang Tian shot him in the hand holding the gun.

The pistol fell to the ground. Wei Rong was completely stunned, even forgetting the excruciating pain in his arm: "I already said I surrender, why did you shoot me?"

"To surrender, you must first drop your gun. If you raise a gun, who knows if you're going to resist?" Jiang Tian said matter-of-factly.

As he spoke, Jiang Tian took out handcuffs and bound the man's hands.

Looking at Wei Rong's face.

To be honest, this was the first time Jiang Tian had seen the last enemy who killed his sister.

Even in his previous life, he knew there was a sixth person who killed his sister, but he had never seen them, nor did he know what they looked like.

"It's all over." Jiang Tian breathed a deep sigh of relief.

To be honest, Jiang Tian had actually intended to kill him with that shot.

In his past life, he killed his sister. Although it hadn't happened yet in this life, Jiang Tian hadn't forgotten the hatred from that past life.

However, Jiang Tian thought about it again. This guy's crime was basically punishable by death. Besides, drug dealers are generally best captured alive.

After joining the narcotics police, Jiang Tian also learned that many times, narcotics officers would risk their lives to capture someone alive.

Even at the risk of sacrifice, they would do it.

The main reason was that a living drug dealer had terrifying value. First, there were the suppliers, then the suppliers—both were of immense intelligence value.

Only by keeping Wei Rong alive could his value be maximized.

Thump thump thump!!

Just then.

Frantic sounds came from the stairwell.

Captain Guo and his men rushed down. When they saw Wei Rong crouching on the ground covered in blood, and a pistol lying nearby,

two men behind Captain Guo quickly rushed up and pinned Wei Rong down.

"We almost let him get away," Captain Guo said with relief.

It's unlikely he escaped, but the problem is he was carrying a pistol and had run into a crowded area; the consequences would have been terrifying.

As for the school and dormitories, that's the school's problem. With a little sealing off, the news won't get out.

Captain Guo went up to Jiang Tian and frantically patted him on the shoulder: "Damn, you even predicted the drug dealer's movements?"

That's amazing.

Damn it.

When Captain Guo rushed in, he saw Jiang Tian running towards the first floor and assumed the kid was trying to get credit, or perhaps he didn't know how to apprehend drug dealers.

His experience was rather limited.

But who would have thought the guy would arrest the drug dealer so easily, right on the first floor, having anticipated the dealer's movements?

Especially considering what happened at the stairwell, Captain Guo had initially thought Jiang Tian was hesitant to charge, perhaps afraid of death?

But this was a slap in the face, and Captain Guo seemed to be experiencing a bit of what it felt like to be slapped in the face.

Captain Guo touched his weathered face; it felt a little hot and red. Was this what it felt like to be slapped in the face?

"Usually, dormitory buildings have two staircases. I guessed it," Jiang Tian explained.

Captain Guo was filled with envy, but he couldn't be jealous. This talent was simply beyond his comprehension.

This kid.

Not only had he earned another merit, but Captain Guo clearly knew that Yunnan University would likely treat Jiang Tian like a VIP from now on, especially since Jiang Tian had just saved the university president.

That's a huge achievement!

Hiss!!!

Captain Guo couldn't even imagine Jiang Tian's future.

Two first-class merits upon joining the team, plus connections—who could stop him from getting promoted?

"You're a natural-born narcotics officer," Captain Guo commented.



Chapter 24 The Perfect Goddess Mu Ya, You, Xiao Bo, Are Not Worthy


"I want to report this policeman! He deliberately shot at me after I surrendered! He broke the law! I'm reporting him for breaking the law!"

He was being forcibly held down by two narcotics officers, but Wei Rong felt a burning pain in his arm.

The flames of anger burned even more fiercely within him.

Damn it.

He really deserved to die!

The excruciating pain made Wei Rong's emotions explode.

But at the same time, feeling the intense pain, he couldn't help but want to kill the policeman in front of him.

"What's going on?" Captain Guo frowned and asked Jiang Tian.

If he opened fire after surrendering, it would be a major incident.

Although narcotics officers have the highest right of self-defense among all departments and police units, after all, they deal with drug dealers every day. The level of danger is such that even criminal investigation police can only follow behind.

"I surrendered as soon as I saw him, but he still shot at me. This policeman has broken the law. I request that you arrest him as well; he's also suspected of intentional assault," Wei Rong said excitedly.

Hmm?

Everyone's eyes turned to Jiang Tian.

This was no small matter.

Especially since Wei Rong, although also a drug dealer, had an unusual status. If this incident involved violations, the follow-up would be very troublesome.

"Arrest him quickly! Arrest him too!" Wei Rong said impatiently.

Even if he died, he wanted to take someone down with him.

"He had a gun in his hand; who knows if he was surrendering or shooting?" Jiang Tian shrugged.

What a joke.

Was he wrong to shoot?

Indeed, he knew the other man was surrendering, but would surrendering make things easier?

This man, in his past life, had killed his own sister!

"Hmm, that's fine then," Captain Guo nodded knowingly.

"Huh?"

Wei Rong stared blankly at these people.

Jiang Tian walked up, looking at Wei Rong with an icy expression. Damn it, this guy was the mastermind behind his sister's death in his past life.

A wicked man.

Jiang Tian stared at the almost purplish-red dot on the scanning radar.

Now Jiang Tian had almost figured out all the functions of the scanning radar.

The lower the sin value, the less malice, the fewer crimes committed; conversely, the brighter and redder the dot, the more heinous the sin.

And clearly, Wei Rong was a heinous sinner.

"I'm going to sue you for covering for each other," Wei Rong said, his heart sinking.

Captain Guo was about to say something.

But at that moment, Jiang Tian stepped forward, raised his fist with a thud, and punched Wei Rong in the face.

This punch, however, Jiang Tian held back.

Otherwise, given Jiang Tian's current martial arts skills, he could kill him in countless ways within a second.

Even with his near-human limits, Jiang Tian's physique couldn't withstand that punch.

"Pfft!!!"

Wei Rong coughed up blood, and it seemed like a tooth was still lodged in.

The next moment.

A sharp pain shot through his head. He groggily opened his eyes and saw Jiang Tian's mocking smile. Jiang Tian was grabbing his hair with one hand: "I'm warning you, don't cause trouble here. You're a drug dealer now, you have no human rights. You heartless drug dealers, I'd be lenient by killing you."

"Waaah, I'm going to sue you, sue all of you!" Wei Rong mumbled incoherently.

As one of Yunhai's top rich second-generation heirs, he outwardly enjoyed boundless prestige.

Power.

Beauty.

Wealth.

These were practically within his grasp.

Through money, he had corrupted countless people, but this time was different.

"So fierce," Zhao Wei gasped.

To be honest, Zhao Wei and Jiang Tian joined the police force at the same time, but in Zhao Wei's memory, Jiang Tian had been unremarkable for the past month or so.

Until yesterday.

Bang!!!

The next moment.

Before Wei Rong could finish speaking, Jiang Tian punched him again.

At the same time, he grabbed Wei Rong's hair.

Jiang Tian still couldn't understand why drug dealers had the nerve to be so arrogant. Did they not know that drug dealers had no human rights?

"No, if I'm not mistaken, a month later in my previous life, due to the rampant drug trafficking, Kyoto even dispatched a patrol team to Yunhai to specifically investigate drug trafficking. Even the patrol team encountered threats from drug dealers."

Jiang Tian's eyes narrowed. This showed just how rampant and terrifying the drug traffickers were in Yunhai; they even dared to threaten the patrol team.

But at the same time, Jiang Tian also knew that Yunhai was too close to the border and was a developed city; it was practically a paradise for drug traffickers.

The drug traffickers in Yunhai were persistent despite repeated crackdowns.

"Xiao Jiang, Xiao Jiang, stop hitting him! Stop hitting him! If you keep hitting him, you'll kill him, and it'll be difficult to interrogate him later." Captain Guo was panicking.

Damn it.

Jiang Tian was too ruthless.

These slaps, left and right, were merciless; Wei Rong's face was almost mangled.

Now his speech was slurred.

"I couldn't help myself seeing how arrogant the drug dealers were," Jiang Tian explained.

The key point is, these arrogant drug dealers still want so-called human rights? Do these vicious thugs also want human rights?

"Captain Guo, I feel this person is definitely involved in more than just directing drug trafficking; there might be other cases," Jiang Tian reminded him, looking at the bright red marker.

"You're right," Captain Guo also remembered how this guy dared to fire a gun in public.

Right, where did that shot land?

The next moment.

Captain Guo saw Yun University President Lian Ying, clutching his bleeding ear, rushing over.

"President Lian, what brings you here? Didn't the ambulance come to take you to the hospital?" Jiang Tian asked.

"Young comrade, I was really worried and came to check on you. Thank you for saving me. If it weren't for you, your police forensic team came over and said that if you hadn't saved me, that shot would have blown my head off," Lian Ying said, still shaken.

I'm so embarrassed.

The operation was so rushed that Captain Guo overlooked a lot.

Now, hearing the principal's voice...

Captain Guo was envious.

Saving a principal from Yunnan University—what does that mean? It means connections, a huge network!

"It's what we should do," Jiang Tian said, feeling that the other party was being a little too enthusiastic.

But he forgot...

The feeling one has when facing a life-or-death crisis, facing their savior.

"Young comrade, I will definitely represent Yunnan University to present your police station with a banner of appreciation," Lian Ying said again, expressing his gratitude.

"This isn't solely my achievement," Jiang Tian replied.

Upon hearing this, Lian Ying's eyes flashed. He held a high position of power, and his connections throughout Yunhai were incredibly formidable. He had even just made a phone call to inquire whether this very person had solved the case.

He had uncovered the drug trafficking case at Yunnan University.

This first act had saved his political career.

And the second time, he had even saved him from the brink of death.

Twice in a row, and yet the other party could so readily decline credit, instantly making Lian Ying realize that the young man before him was definitely not an ordinary person.

"Yes, my mistake. Your police station does have a banner of appreciation too," Lian Ying corrected himself.

Jiang Tian nodded and left with the group.

After they left, in the dormitory behind them, a group of students peeked out. Many had been secretly observing them.

"Did you see that? That police officer was about your age, but he was armed, protecting our country, fighting drug dealers. And we, as students of a top university, have even committed crimes. Aren't you ashamed?" Lian Ying's smile vanished as she turned and angrily reprimanded them.

Unfortunately, Jiang Tian couldn't hear these words.

He sat in the beat-up Jeep in Kyoto, next to Wei Rong, with Captain Guo on Wei Rong's other side.

Although Wei Rong was bleeding profusely, the case was too important and complex to be investigated immediately.

The police car drove away.

In a hotel suite across from Yunnan University, the university's main gate was clearly visible from the window.

Xiao Bo stood at the window.

He watched the narcotics officers, dressed in neat uniforms, fully armed with newly issued Type 95 rifles and pistols.

"So many police cars! What happened at Yunda University?" Wang Yifei, naked, appeared behind Xiao Bo and hugged him.

"Those are our city's narcotics officers," Xiao Bo said through gritted teeth.

He should have been involved in the operation. The Yunda University case might be a major one, and solving it could even bring him great merit.

But now, he was suspended.

All of this was because of Jiang Tian.

"That damned Jiang Tian, ​​so heartless and ungrateful! I took such good care of you in the police force!" Xiao Bo's forehead veins throbbed.

As Xiao Bo spoke, he forgot how he had schemed against Jiang Tian in the police force.

In fact, if Jiang Tian hadn't displayed his prowess yesterday and given him advance notice, Jiang Tian's entire family would likely be facing a terrifying crisis today.

And all of this was because of his behind-the-scenes machinations.

“That bastard Jiang Tian actually suspended you! You took such good care of him, and he still tried to harm you. Today he even called me a bitch,” Wang Yifei said through gritted teeth.
