“After all, you did something good, and that bastard got all arrogant.” Xiao Bo grabbed Wang Yifei’s hair and vented his anger wildly, as if this was how he could get revenge on Jiang Tian.

“Brother Bo, didn’t you say he did something good and got noticed by the leaders? Tonight I’ll ask him out and treat him to dinner. Don’t worry, Brother Bo, as long as I give him a little something, he’ll be a real sycophant, pleading for you to get back into the police force.” Wang Yifei replied, pursing her lips.

Xiao Bo was even more satisfied.

But the next moment…

Xiao Bo’s phone rang. He glanced at it, quickly told Wang Yifei to shush him, then stealthily went to the window and cautiously answered the phone: “Xiao Ya, what’s wrong? Is something the matter?”

“Are you at the police station? I’m coming to your station.” Xiao Ya said on the other end of the line.

Hiss!!!

Xiao Bo’s expression changed drastically.

Mu Ya was the second-generation rich kid he had been pursuing.

A few years ago, the police force organized a selection of students for a study program at Yunnan University, and Xiao Bo was lucky enough to get one, allowing him to study more advanced drug enforcement knowledge at Yunnan University.

It was around that time that he inadvertently learned about Mu Ya's background. At the time, no one in the entire school knew about her background; rumors circulated that she was somewhat wealthy, but in reality, her father was just a businessman, and her grandfather had an even more terrifyingly powerful background. After he found out, he began a relentless pursuit.

Not only her background, but even her appearance was the most innocent and beautiful Xiao Bo had ever seen.

He was terrified of losing Mu Ya, and used every means possible to avoid any contact.

Mu Ya seemed to be constantly consulting her family, so she kept him hanging on, but he was content with this.

Until recently, when he had been pursuing her to take it a step further.

Mu Ya's family didn't try to curry favor with him; they only required him to demonstrate his abilities—the bare minimum: to be promoted this year based on his own abilities and merits.

This was a small test, but Mu Ya's father also demanded that he not touch Mu Ya with a single finger until he met this requirement.

Considering Mu Ya's background, he didn't dare harbor even the slightest thought. But promotions weren't easy, and it wasn't until Jiang Tian joined the police force that he began his frantic schemes to get Jiang Tian's family to promote him.

But now...

Not only had he not been promoted, he was even suspended from duty.

Furthermore, he had offended Chief Gao, a high-ranking official.

If Mu Ya's family found out, Xiao Bo was practically going crazy; he didn't even want to think about it.

"Xiao Ya, don't go over there," Xiao Bo said hurriedly.

"Why?" Xiao Ya asked curiously.

"I...I'm on a case outside, a very big one," Xiao Bo replied casually.

"Really?" Mu Ya's voice was full of surprise. Her father had said that the city's narcotics police had cracked a major case and received a collective second-class merit award.

Anticipating that everyone might be eligible for a promotion, she was specially allowed to visit Xiao Bo today. She was even somewhat moved, thinking about how Xiao Bo had worked so hard solving the case yesterday and was still busy with a major case today; it felt like she could choose him.

The next moment, Mu Ya said into the phone, "I've arrived."

*Whoosh!*

Xiao Bo's face turned deathly pale. He was terrified that Mu Ya would know the truth, because it meant Mu Ya would leave him.

Just then, a familiar male voice came from Mu Ya's phone.

"Comrade, you look familiar. Are you looking for Xiao Bo?"

*Buzz!*

Hearing this voice, Xiao Bo's mind went blank, and he nearly fainted.

Because he recognized the voice.

It was Jiang Tian's.

If Jiang Tian exposed his current situation, if Mu Ya knew he was suspended, if Mu Ya's family knew about this...

He would lose Mu Ya, lose his true love, and lose all his future prospects for advancement.

Mu Ya was more important than his life.

Beauty, power, wealth—Mu Ya's family had all three combined; she was practically Xiao Bo's dream girl.

"No, Xiao Ya, don't talk to him!" Xiao Bo cried frantically into the phone.

But unfortunately...

Mu Ya didn't seem to be listening to the phone; she was talking to the person on the other end: "Officer, hello, my name is Mu Ya. Can you tell me where Xiao Bo is?"

No.

Don't say.

Xiao Bo's hand trembled as he held the phone. He was afraid, terrified that the other person would reveal the truth.



Chapter 25 A Whip Kick Shatters the Drug Dealer's Arrogant Dream


At the police station entrance.

Jiang Tian was dragging Wei Rong off the police car, his movements simple and brutal.

Wei Rong's arm had been shot by Jiang Tian, ​​already in excruciating pain, and now Jiang Tian was subjecting him to a brutal beating.

The narcotics officers understood perfectly well; since this bastard dared to fire a gun, they were lucky Wei Rong hadn't died.

A bit rough, a bit strict enforcement of the law, what's wrong with that?

"Ouch! Ouch! Ouch!!!" Wei Rong cried out in pain.

Looking at Jiang Tian, ​​his eyes flashed with hatred and rage.

This policeman, Wei Rong would remember him, especially this grudge from today, he would definitely remember it.

"It hurts, it hurts, that's good, why would I slap you if it didn't hurt?"

*Slap!*

Looking around to make sure no one was watching, Jiang Tian casually slapped him across the face.

"My dad is Wei Youdao. You dare to use your position to settle personal scores and hit me? I'll remember you, kid!" Wei Rong's eyes were swollen shut as he glared viciously at Jiang Tian.

His mind was racing with thoughts of revenge.

Why was he so arrogant? It's simple: his father was Wei Youdao. That one name alone was enough.

In Yunhai, that was enough power and influence.

It also meant enough power and wealth.

"Wei Youdao?" Jiang Tian already knew about Wei Rong's family background when he arrived.

His father, Wei Youdao, rapidly amassed his fortune after Wei Rong was born in the 1980s. He only had one son, Wei Rong, whom he doted on immensely.

Initially, he made his fortune in transportation, controlling the market channels for Yunhai vegetables and other products. Later, he invested heavily in real estate, achieving phenomenal success.

Now, it's a dazzlingly successful and prominent company, a local icon of Yunhai.

So the question is, why would such a wealthy son of Wei Youdao be involved in drug trafficking?

Jiang Tian squinted, sensing something was amiss.

“Scared? Kneel down and beg me now, and maybe I'll forgive you,” Wei Rong said with a mocking smile.

A person's reputation precedes them. As the head of Yunhai's leading enterprise, Wei Youdao had a history of ruthless methods.

The more glamorous the facade, the darker the reality.

If Jiang Tian were an ordinary policeman, he definitely wouldn't be able to withstand Wei Rong's retaliation.

“Beg you?” Jiang Tian was a little confused.

“Kid, do you know how drug dealers retaliate? Don't you know what happened to the families of some of your seniors after joining the police force?” Wei Rong's smile was sinister.

Buzz!!!

A fire instantly ignited in Jiang Tian's mind.

Nothing else mattered.

But his family was the only obstacle in Jiang Tian's heart ever since his rebirth. In his previous life, until his death, Jiang Tian had finally seen through the world and the hearts of all people. Now, reborn, he had completely awakened to the truth.

And now, they were openly using his family to threaten him.

"You dog, kneel down and beg me, and I'll release your family, how about that?" Wei Rong continued his arrogant laughter.

"Our police files are all confidential. How could you know anything about my family?" Jiang Tian suppressed his anger.

"You little trash, we know your cop better than you do yourselves. Kneel down now, crawl between my legs, and maybe I'll spare your family." Wei Rong's arrogant face was contorted with a ferocious grin.

Arrogant.

This arrogance was so extreme that Jiang Tian felt both furious and horrified.

Especially, what shocked Jiang Tian the most was that the other squad leader, a veteran narcotics officer, Li Feng, who, like Jiang Tian, ​​was holding down Wei Rong, was now silently bowing his head.

Jiang Tian could see that, faced with the arrogant Wei Rong, Li Feng was silently suppressing him.

He was letting the drug dealer run rampant.

What did this represent? It represented the terrifying and rampant nature of drug trafficking!

Jiang Tian clenched his fists. This terrifying chaos, this shocking chaos, was undoubtedly a microcosm of the entire Yunhai region.

Wei Rong, pinned down by the two men, stopped in his tracks, even spreading his legs.

Jiang Tian looked up, and when he saw Li Feng, Li Feng even shook his head at him, meaning Jiang Tian should be patient and ignore him.

This made Jiang Tian's heart sink. Whether it was background or personal merit, Jiang Tian wasn't afraid.

But Li Feng, without any background, was facing such a ruthless drug dealer.

Thinking deeper, who had leaked their narcotics police information?

"Get over here," Wei Rong said viciously.

He could tolerate it in front of so many people at school, but in a secluded place, sorry, Wei Rong decided to teach this junior officer a small lesson.

...

Not far from the police station entrance, where the police cars were parked, Mu Ya was still on the phone with Xiao Bo, but her eyes had been fixed on them from the beginning.

Especially when this criminal arrogantly revealed his background and name, and even threatened the police to kneel.

This made the righteous Mu Ya clench her small fists tightly.

"How could they do this? These criminals are even threatening the families of police officers! How could they do this?" Mu Ya was stunned, her worldview, shattered by the sight of her childhood life in a rosy environment.

She couldn't believe what she was seeing; the drug dealers had become so brazen.

Would the threatened young police officer kneel down?

Kneeling on the ground wouldn't hurt if his family was threatened, would it?

Mu Ya bit her bright red lip.

Her heart ached with increasing resentment and heartache for the narcotics officers. These officers faced gunfire and danger while apprehending criminals, putting not only themselves in constant peril but also their families.

How noble they were.

In fact, it was precisely because of this that Mu Ya held an extraordinary admiration for police officers, especially those on the front lines, and that's why she hadn't directly rejected Xiao Bo but instead given him a test.

But now, she was witnessing the greatest darkness in the world.

So, what would this young narcotics officer do?

The next moment.

She saw it.

The criminal was standing with his legs apart, waiting for the young narcotics officer to crawl through.

And the young narcotics officer, slowly, bent his knees. Had he yielded? Faced with the drug dealer's threats, had he yielded? Mu Ya bit her lip until it bled, not because of the young narcotics officer's shame, but because of the humiliation of a dignified narcotics officer forced to kneel and compromise when his family was threatened. It broke her heart.

“Wei Youdao is the biggest businessman in Yunhai, and a representative to the conference. His son is threatening us. How could the junior police officers resist? If I hadn't seen it, I wouldn't have cared, but now that I have, I can't let this happen before my eyes.” Mu Ya gritted her teeth, ready to step forward.

But, just as she raised her leg…

Bang!!!

The junior narcotics officer, kneeling, made his move. He wasn't kneeling;

he was raising his leg.

In Mu Ya's eyes, the junior narcotics officer raised one leg, and the other, like a spring, leaped into the air, reaching great height, his entire body spinning.

Then, a powerful backflip kick, this kick landed directly on the criminal's face.

Crack!!!

Watching from ten or twenty meters away, Mu Ya subconsciously sniffed, feeling the pain in her nose as if she were witnessing it herself.

But compared to this brutal act, Mu Ya's eyes couldn't help but gleam brightly.

The dim light shone brightly.

Jiang Tian's backflip kick was swift, accurate, and ruthless.

Wei Rong's nose was almost shattered by Jiang Tian's kick.

Jiang Tian used slightly more force in this kick, and that slight extra force sent Wei Rong's entire body airborne for a moment before he crashed heavily to the ground a meter or two later.

At this moment.

Wei Rong's face was unrecognizable.

At this moment.

Wei Rong's eyes seemed unable to open, but the physical pain paled in comparison to the bewilderment in his mind.

"Why? How dare he? Why dare he? My dad is a delegate to the conference, my dad is a billionaire in Yunhai, how dare a mere policeman?"

Wei Rong's body convulsed with pain and fear.

This backflip kick shattered his arrogant dreams.

It was too brutal.

So brutal that Li Feng, the captain of another squad in the same action team, instinctively lunged forward to catch Jiang Tian, ​​who was about to advance even further.

"Xiao Jiang, Xiao Jiang, stop hitting him! If you keep going, something bad will happen!" Li Feng cried out in terror, clutching Jiang Tian's chest.

That kick had completely blew Li Feng away.

The style, the power—Li Feng knew he could never execute such a cool kick in his entire life.

Ugh!

Li Feng quickly banished those thoughts, dragging Jiang Tian away.

Meanwhile, Captain Guo, who had gotten out of the car first and was almost at the police station entrance, belatedly turned around.

His eyes nearly popped out of their sockets.

He had just gotten out of the car first, carrying documents, intending to quickly report to Chief Song, but in the blink of an eye, while jogging,

he turned and saw the style of Jiang Tian's kick. The move was too cool. Even though Captain Guo had undergone extensive training and considered himself a strong fighter, he could never execute a kick like that.

"Xiao Jiang, are you crazy? What are you doing? What are you doing?"

Captain Guo was practically exploding with rage, rushing towards the scene.

Good heavens, he had no choice but to charge. Jiang Tian pulled away from Li Feng, who was holding him, and followed closely behind, rushing towards Wei Rong, who was lying on the ground.

"Quick, help!"

Captain Guo rushed forward and grabbed Jiang Tian.

At that moment, Jiang Tian looked at himself being held by two men around his legs, Zhao Wei and Li Zijing holding his arms, and Li Feng and Captain Guo frantically trying to hold him back.

Although Jiang Tian's fighting skills would easily allow him to shake them off,

Jiang Tian thought for a moment and decided against it. Almost every move he used was a killing blow.

"Ugh, don't hit me, don't hit me!"

With both arms broken, face covered in blood, and nose shattered, Wei Rong could only tremble and struggle, retreating in a huddled position, watching with terrified eyes as the six men grabbed and dragged Jiang Tian. He was terrified.

This lash of the leg brought him back to his senses.

However, the anger in Jiang Tian's eyes subsided slightly as he pointed at Wei Rong and said, "See? Drug dealers are arrogant, so a couple of lashes will bring them to their senses. These harmful drug dealers can't be tolerated. One lash is enough to wake them up."

He could tolerate the arrogance of drug dealers, but his family was his bottom line.

The police officer holding Jiang Tian swallowed hard and nodded repeatedly.

An officer was already dragging Wei Rong, who was lying on the ground.

After the criminal left, Captain Guo, after understanding the situation, couldn't help but twitch his lips: "That bastard really deserved it."

Even Captain Guo was furious, let alone facing him.

"Alright, I understand. Xiao Jiang, calm down. Don't participate in the interrogation yet. We still need to get more information from him," Captain Guo quickly said.

Jiang Tian hesitated for a moment, then nodded slightly.

Jiang Tian hadn't gone all out. Actually, Jiang Tian was quite fierce, but he was controlling himself; otherwise, one move would have killed him. However, a drug dealer's life is sometimes a precious clue.

Kicking Wei Rong to death would easily kill that clue.

"You... awesome."

Li Feng was panting heavily. He had used all his strength to stop Jiang Tian, ​​only to find, to his horror, that Jiang Tian didn't budge an inch.

He felt like he was facing an elephant, terrifyingly powerful.

The most terrifying thing was that he had already chickened out. Not for himself, but for his family too, he was also driven by anger at the drug dealer's arrogance. Jiang Tian's actions undoubtedly filled him with exhilarating satisfaction and admiration.

A single whip kick shattered the drug dealer's arrogance.

That was truly deadly!

Li Feng swallowed hard. After spending the first month or so with him, he only now realized how truly terrifying Jiang Tian was!

"Don't be afraid of drug dealers. Only by being fiercer and more ruthless than them can you stop them," Jiang Tian said with a cold smile.

Kill his entire family.

Before that, Jiang Tian was going to chop up the entire drug dealer's family.

While violence is a bad thing, it's definitely the most effective.

"Captain, where do we go now?" Zhao Wei asked, bewildered, following behind Jiang Tian.

The two of them were in the back car.

They had heard him, but before they could get there, Jiang Tian had already made his move.

"Didn't you hear? Captain Guo told me to take a break for now, not to follow up on the interrogations, and to wait for the psychologist's treatment," Jiang Tian said irritably.

But before Jiang Tian could finish speaking,

out of the corner of his eye, he suddenly noticed a beautiful figure.

Oh no, it even seemed somewhat familiar.

The next moment.

Sure enough.

Memories from his past life overlapped.

Mu Ya.

In this life, Mu Ya doesn't know Jiang Tian, ​​but in his past life, Jiang Tian knew Mu Ya all too well.

In his past life, Jiang Tian was unaware of Xiao Bo's true nature, but Mu Ya seemed to gradually come to understand his repulsive and ugly side after their marriage.

Even so, Mu Ya didn't choose divorce, only separation from Xiao Bo. According to Mu Ya, she was someone who could be with someone for a lifetime—a woman Jiang Tian envied immensely, almost to the point of envy. How many women like that were there in this era?

In his previous life, Jiang Tian's home was constantly disrupted by Wang Yifei's disruptive behavior, with her frequently threatening divorce. Jiang Tian had endured it all for the sake of his beastly son. At that time, he had thought, even denied, that only someone like Xiao Bo was worthy of Mu Ya.

But now, thinking back, Jiang Tian wanted to slap himself repeatedly. He was truly pathetic.

Otherwise, why would he have had such thoughts?

Why hadn't he seen through his true colors sooner?

In her past life, Mu Ya had also taken great care of Jiang Tian. Perhaps having seen through Xiao Bo's character, Mu Ya had subtly hinted to Jiang Tian on more than one occasion that Xiao Bo was a despicable person, not as upright as he appeared. However, in his past life, Jiang Tian seemed bewitched, blindly accepting Xiao Bo as his team leader.

Perhaps, having been so thoroughly misled by Xiao Bo when he first joined the police force, he couldn't see through him.

After several warnings, Mu Ya was deeply disappointed that Jiang Tian wouldn't listen.

Especially since, in his past life, Jiang Tian often confided in Mu Ya after arguments with Wang Yifei, because in his heart, Mu Ya was like his dearest older sister.

But in her past life, whether out of guilt or something else, Mu Ya's attitude towards Jiang Tian was absolutely good.

Even when Jiang Tian was timidly brought home by Xiao Bo, and Xiao Bo mocked and ridiculed him in front of Mu Ya, Jiang Tian still tried his best to cooperate. Even though he was as weak as an ant, Mu Ya never looked down on him; in fact, she constantly encouraged him.

Thinking back to his past life, Jiang Tian's eyes momentarily lost their focus before he regained his senses.

It has to be said.

The Jiang Tian of his future life knew Mu Ya's true identity.

Because he knew, Jiang Tian knew just how outstanding a woman Mu Ya was. Not only was her family background excellent, but even her appearance, figure, and inner self seemed flawless.

"At this time, Xiao Bo still seems to be pursuing her, and Mu Ya hasn't even agreed yet, which means..."

What could Jiang Tian say?

Such a woman absolutely cannot be allowed to be with Xiao Bo!

"Young comrade, where did Xiao Bo go on his mission?"

Having heard about what had just happened—even the conference delegate, the son of Yunhai's wealthiest man, had been arrested—Mu Ya couldn't help but swallow hard, thinking to herself, Xiao Bo really hadn't lied to her.

It really was a big mission.

Was Xiao Bo absent because there was still a follow-up operation to apprehend him?

Drug enforcement officers, they are truly amazing.

Mu Ya's eyes shone with an increasingly brilliant light.



Chapter 26 The truth is revealed: Xiao Bo is actually a beast.


"I'm not called 'Little Comrade.' Let me introduce myself, my name is Jiang Tian."

Jiang Tian's eyes flickered. In his past life, he hadn't had a chance, but in this life, now that he had, how could he allow such a beautiful flower to be ruined by that beast, Xiao Bo?

Reborn, Jiang Tian only needed a moment's thought to understand how many times Xiao Bo had openly and secretly tried to harm him and tarnish his reputation.

Ordinary, mediocre, a second-generation rich kid coming to "gild his resume"—rumors had been circulating within their police force for some time, leading many to have a negative impression of Jiang Tian.

All of this was Xiao Bo's doing.

Murder for money.

The son he raised for over ten years was actually Xiao Bo's.

The destruction of his family was also Xiao Bo's doing.

In this life, Jiang Tian decided that this goddess—with her good personality and perfect looks—would be his to have.

"Jiang Tian?" Mu Ya exclaimed in surprise.

"You know me?" Jiang Tian was momentarily stunned.

"I..."

Mu Ya looked embarrassed and didn't know what to say.

Because Xiao Bo had told her, openly and subtly, more than once that a privileged son of a high-ranking official named Jiang Tian had joined their police force, and she, being fiercely opposed to evil, disliked him.

Especially because of the repeated sabotage he'd secretly put on his act, calling Jiang Tian a useless good-for-nothing, someone who just loafed around, a burden, and forced them to risk their lives to "gild" this good-for-nothing.

Furthermore, he was assigned to his subordinates, forcing him to take a huge risk for a privileged son of an official, which only fueled Mu Ya's resentment.

Perhaps, the credit should actually belong to Xiao Bo, but Jiang Tian had stolen it. Thinking of this, Mu Ya took two steps back, keeping her distance.

"Officer Jiang, I'm sorry, I accidentally called him that just now." Mu Ya's tone was distant, and she looked at Jiang Tian with disdain.

Jiang Tian instantly understood the difference in her attitude.

Damn it.

Jiang Tian instantly realized that Xiao Bo, that bastard, outwardly treated him with righteous indignation, but secretly his greatest hobby and emotion was to smear him everywhere.

He also used Jiang Tian's status to elevate his own fearlessness of power.

Jiang Tian was instantly enraged.

In his past life, Jiang Tian had suffered so much, but in this life, he was slowly rewriting his destiny.

Because he clearly understood that Mu Ya was definitely not the kind of person who would fickle.

Even after Xiao Bo's betrayal of Mu Ya, she never considered divorce, remaining steadfast in her commitment to him for life, silently helping Xiao Bo resolve the troubles he had caused.

She was a true virtuous wife.

And yet, she secretly smeared him like this, plus he had that despicable girlfriend, Wang Yifei.

Under normal circumstances, pursuing Mu Ya would be incredibly difficult.

But Jiang Tian wasn't angry.

Because he had a trump card.

Jiang Tian was eagerly anticipating what Mu Ya's reaction would be when she found out that while he was out there on a mission amidst gunfire, her teammate Xiao Bo was secretly having an affair with his girlfriend.

Jiang Tian was extremely curious to see Mu Ya's expression when she learned the whole truth, given her extraordinary admiration and respect for the police.

"Officer Jiang, I'm looking for your colleague Xiao Bo. He's right here, also a narcotics officer. Is he still out on a big mission?" Mu Ya asked coldly, looking at Jiang Tian with a hint of disgust.

Just now, when Jiang Tian kicked her, Mu Ya had unconsciously put away her phone, even forgetting to hang up.

"He's on a big mission?"

Jiang Tian's eyes flickered, but Zhao Wei and Li Zijing behind him almost choked.

Seemingly unsure how to answer, both of them looked at Jiang Tian.

Unconsciously, Jiang Tian had completely won over these two underlings.

Oh no, it should be a little sister.

But at this moment, Jiang Tian smiled.

On a big mission?

Looking at the expectant expression on Mu Ya's face, it was indeed a big mission, but this big mission involved playing with a woman in a hotel, and Jiang Tian's current publicly acknowledged girlfriend.

At this moment, Mu Ya immediately asked, "You just arrested the son of Wei Youdao, our city's top official. This must be a major case, right?"

What?

Xiao Bo, who was hurriedly dressing and listening on his phone at the hotel across from Yun University, was stunned.

The police had launched another major operation.

And judging from the looks of it, it involved the son of a wealthy man from Yunhai.

They'd even arrested him, proving the evidence was irrefutable.

And he hadn't participated in this mission.

Thinking about this, Xiao Bo's face turned green.

However, on the other hand, Xiao Bo felt a sense of fear, fear of the truth coming to light.

Xiao Bo's scalp tingled.

He absolutely couldn't lose Mu Ya; Mu Ya was his life!

"Brother Xiao, why are you in such a hurry? She's waiting for you. It's only been twice today, let's do it again," Wang Yifei tempted, hugging Xiao Bo's back on the bed.

If Jiang Tian were to witness this scene, he would undoubtedly mock this shameless woman for her hypocrisy.

In her past life, she not only became pregnant with Xiao Bo's child but also refused to let Jiang Tian touch her, ostensibly to protect the child.

In other words, Jiang Tian never touched Wang Yifei, yet she manipulated him into raising her child for over ten years.

But with Xiao Bo, she used every means at her disposal to seduce him.

“Get out! I don’t care what method you use, you must meet that good-for-nothing Jiang Tian today and make him believe this child is his.” Xiao Bo ruthlessly shoved Wang Yifei away.

But Wang Yifei showed no anger, only nodding repeatedly in agreement: “Brother Xiao, I’ve already planned everything, it’s absolutely foolproof.”

Xiao Bo said nothing and hurriedly left. Although he was suspended from his duties, he needed to go back and investigate.

He couldn’t afford to wallow in despair here.

"Jiang Tian, ​​you beast! Making you raise my son is already letting you off easy!" Xiao Bo, pushing open the door, thought to himself, as if he had bestowed upon Jiang Tian a tremendous favor.

The thought of a privileged son of an official raising the child of a country bumpkin like himself filled Xiao Bo with such excitement that he almost trembled with elation.

Before leaving, Xiao Bo turned back and gave Wang Yifei a disdainful look.

This shameless woman was indeed promiscuous, but compared to his goddess, Mu Ya, she was nothing but an ugly duckling, not even worthy to carry his shoes.

However, as Xiao Bo frantically rushed over, he listened to the voice on the phone.

His nerves were on edge, about to explode.

He didn't even know Jiang Tian had recorded them entering the hotel. If he did, this would be his darkest hour.

On the other end of the phone.

Mu Ya frowned slightly.

She sensed something was off. The two people behind Jiang Tian seemed to be holding back their emotions, their faces flushed.

They seemed to have something to say.

"What's wrong? Did you abandon him to carry out a dangerous mission?" Mu Ya continued to ask.

"Who told you Xiao Bo was on a mission?" Jiang Tian asked curiously.

Good grief.

He encountered this case today due to unexpected and special circumstances. He mainly hadn't expected the drug dealers to be so brazen.

Xiao Bo had already been suspended. What, was he going to steal the credit too?

Jiang Tian almost laughed.

"Xiao Bo said this task was something he led you through, right?" Although she wanted to keep her distance from Jiang Tian because of Xiao Bo, Mu Ya hesitated for a moment before asking.

She seemed to remember Xiao Bo saying that Jiang Tian, ​​this rich second-generation, often dragged him down.

However, the truth was that while Jiang Tian's abilities were mediocre, he was definitely Xiao Bo's loyal follower, doing everything from serving tea and water to being very hardworking.

In return, he received vicious slander and various schemes from Xiao Bo.

"Miss Mu, this case has had absolutely nothing to do with Xiao Bo from beginning to end," Jiang Tian said with a slight smile.

Ah?

Mu Ya blushed.

She wasn't an unreasonable person, nor was she making a fuss overtly or covertly. Her attitude towards Jiang Tian stemmed from Xiao Bo's subtle, almost brainwashing, slander.

It was very awkward.

Mu Ya felt her face burning; she fanned herself with her pale hand, trying to cool down.

"Jiang Tian, ​​you beast!" Xiao Bo slammed his fist on the taxi, his face burning with rage.

He hadn't expected Jiang Tian, ​​that beast, to actually dare to tell the truth.

Couldn't he have helped him keep it a secret?

Couldn't he have given him the credit in front of Mu Ya?

"Your brother Xiao has always been so good to you, why won't you help me with this little favor?"

"Ungrateful beast!" Xiao Bo seemed to have forgotten that he had never helped Jiang Tian at all; on the contrary, Jiang Tian was the one who served him tea and water.

However, hatred and fear clouded his judgment.

He knew that Mu Ya hated being lied to the most. He had just told her he was on a major mission. If Mu Ya found out the truth,

plus his suspension,

he was already sweating profusely with fear: "Jiang Tian, ​​you piece of trash, you damned piece of trash!"

But just then, a voice came from the other end of the phone.

It was Mu Ya's voice.

Xiao Bo listened nervously.

Mu Ya seemed embarrassed and tried to ease the tension: "Then he's probably on another important mission."

Xiao Bo's heart pounded: "Jiang Tian, ​​you good-for-nothing, you definitely won't tell the truth, will you?"

Because Xiao Bo remembered boasting to Jiang Tian more than once about his pursuit of Mu Ya, mentioning her family's wealth, hoping to use his emotional appeal to persuade Jiang Tian to use his connections to promote him.

Thinking this way, Xiao Bo relaxed for a moment.

Unfortunately.

The next moment.

"Oh, you mean Xiao Bo? He's been suspended." Jiang Tian seemed to have thought for a long time before remembering.

But his calm words, like a chilling wind, seeped into Xiao Bo's icy heart.

"Jiang Tian, ​​you piece of trash, you deserve to die!" Xiao Bo's eyes were bloodshot.

Sure enough, his words caused a stunned silence.

Mu Ya was truly stunned; she never expected this answer: "Are you mistaken? Xiao Bo is so outstanding, how could he be suspended?"

Zhao Wei then provided a crucial assist: "How could that be? It was Chief Gao from Beijing who personally ordered the suspension."

"Why?" Mu Ya asked incredulously.

Even more unbelievable was that Xiao Bo would lie to her?

She wasn't exactly heartbroken; after all, he was just a prospective employee, still evaluating her, and there were no real feelings involved. But being deceived was undeniably disheartening.

She hoped even more that Xiao Bo was innocent.

"Did you wrong him?" Mu Ya asked Jiang Tian.

Xiao Bo hung up the phone and frantically dialed again, trying to end Mu Ya's conversation.

Zhao Wei stepped forward from beside Jiang Tian, ​​his voice blazing with anger: "Yesterday, that bastard Xiao Bo went to Brother Jiang's house. Oh, and Brother Jiang's family has some connections. Seeing that Leader Gao was coming to the police station, he tricked Brother Jiang's mother into making a phone call to the police station to pull strings, causing Brother Jiang to be severely criticized by Leader Gao at the meeting. That beast framed his own colleague!"

*Buzz!*

Mu Ya's eyes widened, her breath catching in her throat: "He...did this?"

So vicious!

Vicious to the point of chilling her to the bone.

She didn't even care about being embarrassed, staring blankly at the faces of the three people in front of her. The two men behind Jiang Tian, ​​their faces contorted with rage, were clearly not lying.

But...

Mu Ya simply couldn't believe it; her worldview had been so utterly shattered.

Because Mu Ya clearly remembered how Xiao Bo had described Jiang Tian as a piece of trash, a beast, a burden to her, while she herself was portrayed as incredibly noble.

On the other hand, he had also shown off his own brilliance and greatness, his disdain for power.

But she never dreamed it would turn out like this.

The image Xiao Bo had constructed in her mind was crumbling. Just then, Mu Ya's phone rang.

Mu Ya took it out. It turned out she had forgotten to hang up. Xiao Bo, trying to interrupt them, had hung up himself and was frantically calling, but Mu Ya only glanced at it before putting it back in her pocket.

She began to deeply doubt Xiao Bo.

Not only because of Zhao Wei's words, but also because of Jiang Tian's demeanor and handling of the drug dealers.

That ferocious back kick, almost crippling the person with a single blow, was ruthless and sharp.

He acted decisively.

And when he needed to be calm, his face was completely composed, without any anger.

Mu Ya couldn't believe that this was the arrogant, good-for-nothing second-generation heir Xiao Bo had described.

"By the way, what's your relationship with Xiao Bo?" Zhao Wei asked belatedly after finishing his sentence.

"Friends, I guess." A fleeting awkwardness crossed Mu Ya's face.

"It's best to stay away from him. This guy is incredibly cunning. Brother Jiang used to treat him like dirt, but who knew he'd secretly sabotage Brother Jiang like this? He even asked Brother Jiang to use his family connections to get him a promotion, and Brother Jiang agreed. I never expected this guy to be so treacherous behind the scenes." Zhao Wei vented his anger with curses.

"To frame Brother Jiang is tantamount to killing him."

Zhao Wei wanted to kill that guy.

*Gulp!*

He did it?

Mu Ya's face showed confusion. She didn't know whether to believe him. Reason told her that the three narcotics officers and one female officer in front of her were all filled with righteous indignation and couldn't possibly be lying to her.

But emotionally, the only person she had ever shown even a slight liking for turned out to be such a beast.

She couldn't accept it.

"Alright, alright, don't scare Miss Mu. The captain has given us leave. Go do what you need to do." Jiang Tian clapped his hands and laughed loudly, "Wait for our credit."

Jiang Tian wanted to go back and spend time with his sister.

Even more, he wanted to talk to his sister.

In his past life, he felt guilty for over ten years and never saw his sister again. Now, he had finally made amends; all the criminals had been brought to justice.

His sister would never be in danger again.

As for Mu Ya, Jiang Tian wasn't in a hurry to produce the video recording that would determine her fate; it wasn't the right time.

Producing it now would eliminate any chance for Xiao Bo, but Jiang Tian wasn't very familiar with Mu Ya, making it too difficult to approach her.

He needed a catalyst.

If he remembered correctly, in his past life, Xiao Bo had been extremely arrogant, constantly boasting about his glorious history of pursuing Mu Ya.

It happened when Mu Ya went camping in the suburbs. At that time, a major drug dealer sentenced to life imprisonment seized a gun and a construction truck while a prison was under renovation, and fled to the mountains.

Then he kidnapped Mu Ya.

During the search of the mountains, Xiao Bo, by sheer luck, bravely rescued Mu Ya.

"Officer Jiang, could I have your contact information? I'd like to talk to you about anything later," Mu Ya asked almost cautiously.

Reason told her that she had accepted this heavy, difficult truth, and therefore felt some guilt for misunderstanding Jiang Tian.

Jiang Tian left his phone number.

Just then, Xiao Bo scrambled out of the taxi.

He ran frantically to Mu Ya.

"Mu Ya, I'm so sorry, it's an urgent mission, a big case, I'm late." Xiao Bo kept wiping his sweat, pretending to be very busy.

Then, in a low voice only the two of them could hear, Xiao Bo said, "Don't believe them. That good-for-nothing Jiang Tian is a rich second-generation. You know I come from a mountain village. Those two are his lackeys, deliberately slandering me. Mu Ya, believe me. I just worked hard on a dangerous drug trafficking case, and this good-for-nothing beast is secretly badmouthing me behind my back. He's worse than an animal."

Mu Ya hesitated, unsure who to believe, but then she suddenly saw a large bus approaching behind Xiao Bo.

The bus clearly displayed "Yunnan University School Bus."

"What's this?" Mu Ya asked, confused.

A moment later, a large group of people in suits and ties disembarked from the school bus, and most notably, they were carrying a banner.

Mu Ya's eyes flashed with hope as she looked at the banner.

"This...is it to give to Xiao Bo? Did I wrong him?" Mu Ya frowned slightly.

Her gaze shifted to Jiang Tian, ​​her teeth clenched slightly. If that were true, Jiang Tian deserved to die.

If that were the case, she would definitely go to his grandfather and explain the situation. Mu Ya had made up her mind.

But the next moment...

The leader holding the banner saw Jiang Tian as if he were his savior. He waved the banner loudly, saying, "Comrade Jiang, thank you! And thank you even more to your anti-drug police! This banner is presented to you on behalf of all the teachers and students of Yunnan University. Oh, and there's another one for your police team. As for this one, it's my personal thank you for saving me, Comrade Jiang. You saved the teachers and students of Yunnan University!"

Jiang Tian received two banners.

Xiao Bo's head was buzzing.

But it wasn't over yet.

The next moment...

*Slap!*

A loud slap rang out, and Xiao Bo felt a sharp pain on his face.



Chapter 27 Paving the Way: Yunnan University Graduate Students Begin Their Rapid Advancement


"Huh?"

A loud slap rang out. Lian Ying looked up, seemingly recognizing the girl who had struck him.

But Lian Ying had no time to dwell on it. For him, the most important thing right now was gratitude.

Thank you, Jiang Tian.

Thank you to the narcotics officers for everything they had done.

Without Jiang Tian, ​​without these narcotics officers, Yun University would have unknowingly become a drug den.

However, while Lian Ying didn't recognize Mu Ya, Mu Ya and Xiao Bo were extremely familiar with him.

Mu Ya was once a prominent figure at Yun University, the dream girl of countless people, a perfect goddess.

And Xiao Bo had even studied advanced narcotics techniques at Yun University.

Therefore, the two of them knew Lian Ying well and recognized him immediately.

It was precisely because they recognized him that they were shocked.

Lian Ying personally stepped forward, even presenting Jiang Tian with two banners of appreciation.

In the name of Yunnan University, a top-tier university, a banner was presented to Jiang Tian.

Then, another banner was presented to Jiang Tian in the personal name of the university's president.

Hiss!!!

What does this mean?

Damn it.

Xiao Bo even forgot the pain from the slap on his face; envy and jealousy made him unrecognizable.

Impossible.

This is impossible.

"This good-for-nothing, impossible, how could he? This good-for-nothing must have done it through his connections. These second-generation officials, they get promoted effortlessly just because of their family connections." Xiao Bo was almost driven mad by envy and jealousy.

Meanwhile, after a flash of shock, Mu Ya looked at Xiao Bo with slight disappointment.

To be honest.

Mu Ya had previously had some goodwill towards Xiao Bo, and after today's incident, she still had a sliver of trust in him, believing that he had truly been bullied by the powerful.

In that case, Mu Ya would definitely ask her grandfather for help.

But upon hearing this, Mu Ya was utterly disappointed.

"You mean, that Jiang Tian, ​​with only a bureau chief father, can make the president of Yun University bow and scrape? Do you know that's the president of a top-tier university, a full-fledged department-level official, with countless students? Would someone like that bow and scrape to a mere bureau chief's son?" Mu Ya said coldly, almost enunciating each word.

Lian Ying's rank was extremely high.

To put it bluntly, Jiang Tian's father was a level lower.

Because he was currently only a deputy department-level official, not even a standing committee member yet.

Would someone like that bow and scrape to a mere second-generation bureau chief like Jiang Tian?

It wasn't just jealousy and envy; it was short-sightedness.

"Impossible..." Xiao Bo's entire body trembled.

Then his face flushed even redder, his eyes burning with intense jealousy.

To have Jiang Tian achieve merit and receive such a high position was more unacceptable to him than death.

And just then...

Lian Ying's voice continued, "Comrade Xiao Jiang, I've already reported this to our superiors. Frankly speaking, you saved Yunnan University this time, and you saved countless teachers and students."

It seemed like just a few people dealing drugs, using Yunnan University as their base.

However, there were too many poor students in this era.

Starting with just five or six people, they were able to corrupt, even teachers and students, with money. Don't trust a person's inherent flaws and moral boundaries; it won't be long before...

The consequences would be terrifying.

Fortunately, everything is under control now.

Nothing has spread too horribly yet.

There's still a chance to salvage things. Jiang Tian has even indirectly saved all the leaders of Yun University.

Everyone looks at Jiang Tian with piercing eyes.

And Lian Ying's words...

made Xiao Bo tremble with jealousy.

Why?

This good-for-nothing, what makes him so special?

To this day, Xiao Bo still looks down on Jiang Tian, ​​he has always looked down on Jiang Tian.

In his mind, Jiang Tian is a good-for-nothing, only able to follow behind him like a fool, manipulated at his mercy, and even grateful to him—a useless second-generation rich kid.

He enjoys this feeling.

Because it gives him an unprecedented sense of accomplishment.

So what if he's a second-generation official? So what if his father is a bureau chief? He's still being manipulated like a shark's arm.

He despised and even scorned this good-for-nothing from the bottom of his heart.

But now...

he discovered that this good-for-nothing he looked down upon the most had somehow gotten incredibly lucky, achieving two major merits in two consecutive days.

The first time was one thing, but the second time was another stroke of luck.

Yes, that's right, pure luck.

"If I hadn't been suspended, Jiang Tian's job should have been mine, the merits should have been mine, and the credit should have been mine. This good-for-nothing stole my credit."

Thinking this, Xiao Bo was almost vomiting blood from jealousy.

He glared angrily at Jiang Tian, ​​as if Jiang Tian had truly stolen his credit.

But at this moment, Jiang Tian didn't care about Xiao Bo.

Because before he could respond, a man wearing glasses stepped out from behind Lian Ying.

Half his hair was white, but his eyes were bright as he looked at Jiang Tian and asked, "Comrade Jiang, may I ask where you went to university, and how long ago did you graduate?"

Jiang Tian scratched his head in confusion, but still honestly replied, "Well, I graduated from Yunhai Police Academy. I'm currently doing my internship in the second semester of my senior year, and I haven't graduated yet."

Hiss!!!

Not graduated yet?

The leaders of Yunhai University exchanged glances, and the one who spoke beamed with delight, saying, "That's perfect! Comrade Jiang, I'm the dean of the law department at Yunhai University. We cordially invite you to enroll in my graduate program."

Uh…

Jiang Tian blinked.

Yunhai University? A top-tier university!

To be honest, Jiang Tian's grades were barely enough for the police academy, and his academic performance was mediocre. He had never even considered getting into Yunhai University for graduate studies!

But then, Jiang Tian suddenly remembered his past life. That beast Xiao Bo—it seemed that after he gave him the case clues, Xiao Bo solved the case…

He then apparently went on to pursue a master's degree at Yunnan University, even becoming a renowned expert in criminal investigation and law.

So, this must be Yunnan University's way of expressing gratitude.

But in his previous life, Xiao Bo claimed he got in entirely due to his excellent grades.

Thinking this through, Jiang Tian felt a cold laugh. In his previous life, Xiao Bo had used the help and clues he provided to help him rise through the ranks.

But Xiao Bo had repeatedly framed him, ultimately conspiring with the bastard he'd raised for over ten years to kill him.

And now, all of this had simply returned to what was rightfully his.

“Comrade Jiang, don’t underestimate Dean Qin Gang. He’s not only a renowned legal expert in our country, but also possesses exceptional achievements in criminal investigation. He’s even sometimes invited to join the General Bureau’s criminal investigation team,” Lian Ying explained to Jiang Tian.

Buzz!!!

Standing not far away, Xiao Bo’s eyes widened.

Such a big shot was actually going to take Jiang Tian as his apprentice?

What did this represent?

Jiang Tian was even more surprised that Lian Ying’s reward came so quickly and so fiercely.

Xiao Bo was even more surprised that Jiang Tian had been directly invited. What did this mean? The postgraduate entrance exam was probably just a formality; whether he passed or not was another matter, but even if he didn’t, if Yunnan University invited him, they would find a way to get him in.

It was equivalent to being pre-selected as a student of Yunnan University’s renowned criminal investigation and legal expert.

What's most terrifying is that these powerful figures typically have a large number of students under their command and are bound to achieve great success. For Jiang Tian, ​​this represents a vast network of connections.

A teacher's network.

Jiang Tian clearly understood this as well, and quickly nodded. Did he have the right to refuse?

Absolutely not!

Moreover, Jiang Tian knew that the simplicity and limitations of his major meant that no matter how much merit he accumulated, his future would be limited.

But with a research certificate in law, his future path would be much wider!

"No wonder Xiao Bo, over the next ten years, even rose to the position of executive vice mayor, overseeing important work such as Yunhai's security."

From this, Jiang Tian completely understood the key reasons for Xiao Bo's rapid rise in his previous life: one was Mu Ya's help, and the other was this incident.

But Jiang Tian was very curious about what would become of Xiao Bo after losing these two—this cunning beast from the mountain village.

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian's vengeful desire instantly erupted.

"Thank you."

Lian Ying patted Jiang Tian on the shoulder, very pleased. "I should thank you."

Then Jiang Tian led Lian Ying and the others into the police station.

On behalf of Yun University, he expressed his deepest gratitude to the entire Yunhai Narcotics Control Detachment.

Finally, he presented a banner belonging to Yun University.

Clap clap clap!!!

Applause rang out.

Everyone present was extremely excited, as this was recognition of their work.

Of course, most importantly, all eyes were on Jiang Tian.

Outside the police station.

Xiao Bo was still pleading and begging, "Xiao Ya, believe me, I really didn't lie to you, Jiang Tian is truly a good-for-nothing."

"From now on, let's not see each other again." Mu Ya turned and left with a look of disgust.

After learning what had happened, and even the president of Yun University had come over.

Could it be that Jiang Tian, ​​just because he had a bureau chief father, could have all the leaders of Yun University come to thank him and stand by him?

Isn't this ridiculous?

Ultimately, it's because Jiang Tian made a significant contribution.

While Xiao Bo not only schemed against his colleagues behind their backs but also spread rumors about them.

While Jiang Tian was making a contribution, what were you doing?

Mu Ya was disappointed. She began to ponder whether her father was right, and whether Xiao Bo was a bad person.

Indeed, Mu Ya's family disapproved of Xiao Bo. They didn't even care about social status, but they placed great importance on character.

They could tell at a glance that Xiao Bo wasn't as upright as he appeared.

But Mu Ya persisted.

Now, Mu Ya realized with disappointment that perhaps her family was right.

This left Mu Ya even more confused, unsure of what to do, or whether she should forgive Xiao Bo.

"It's all mine."

Outside the police station, Xiao Bo listened to the enthusiastic applause inside.

He looked at Jiang Tian with envy, as if he were the center of attention, standing in the middle of the crowd.

He basked in the adulation around him.

This only fueled Xiao Bo's jealousy, making him tremble with envy.

But unfortunately, Jiang Tian didn't even consider him a threat.

Or rather, he hadn't yet made his move.

Jiang Tian, ​​surrounded by admirers, glanced sideways at the police station. Xiao Bo's eyes were bloodshot with jealousy; Mu Ya had already left.

Jiang Tian's lips curled slightly. Even so, he understood that completely disappointing Mu Ya wasn't enough.

Because he knew all too well how traditional Mu Ya's personality was; once she committed to someone, it was for life.

Although her relationship with Xiao Bo hadn't progressed, Mu Ya wasn't the kind of person to be so heartless as to completely sever ties.

Girls like that were truly hard to find.

If the two of them were to secretly pledge their lives to each other and get engaged, even if Jiang Tian used the video as his trump card, she probably wouldn't turn back.

Once she made up her mind, it was for life.

"Damn, Jiang Tian is too awesome."

"What Jiang Tian? Call him 'brother,' call him Brother Jiang."

"Damn, he went too far, but he was cool."

In this era, the underworld was rampant, and drug dealers were even more outrageously brazen.

Among them were various criminals with powerful backgrounds, and when they investigated cases, they were always restrained and cautious.

Because even if not for themselves, they had to protect their families.

Those people were truly ruthless.

One wrong move, and those heartless drug dealers could wipe out your entire family.

But Jiang Tian dared to be so brutally killed by a drug dealer with such a powerful background.

Many people couldn't help but secretly click their tongues in amazement, but they couldn't suppress the overwhelming satisfaction in their hearts.

This was how they, the anti-narcotics police, should be.

"Uncle, uncle, where's my dad? I can't find him!"

Just then, Jiang Tian felt his trouser leg being tugged. Looking down, he saw a little girl of about five or six years old.

She was looking at him with innocent and curious eyes.

Jiang Tian froze, squatted down, and asked, "Little girl, what's your father's name?"

"Brother Jiang, his father was Meng Yang. He died yesterday."

A fellow new recruit from the police station whispered beside Jiang Tian.

Yesterday, although Jiang Tian had fought fiercely, the intense gunfire and the brutal fighting in the dark made it difficult for him to penetrate deep behind enemy lines.

The drug dealers were not without their methods; their firepower was formidable. Jiang Tian couldn't penetrate deep behind enemy lines. It was Meng Yang and three others who launched a fierce attack from the other side, drawing fire and allowing Jiang Tian to successfully reposition himself. This allowed Jiang Tian to begin his frenzied flanking maneuver, catching the drug dealers off guard and securing victory.

But Meng Yang ultimately succumbed to three bullet wounds and died a heroic death.

This morning, after being reported, his posthumous First-Class Merit was approved overnight.

"Sigh, his family came to claim him today. Meng Yang had only been married for five or six years, had a three-year-old son, and his elderly father was almost seventy. I don't know how he'll manage in the future."

Those who knew the situation couldn't help but sigh.

Five or six years old, still unaware of death.

Jiang Tian's expression was also complex.

The celebratory sounds ceased; even the death of a comrade evoked a deep sense of sorrow. Seeing his comrade fall, seeing the families tragically claim their loved ones.

These were the pillars of their families.

With their pillars fallen, everyone's spirits were low.

In peacetime.

There are always those unseen people, silently moving forward.

Jiang Tian also felt heavy-hearted.

Meng Yang died drawing fire for him, leaving such a young child without a father.

Five people sacrificed their lives last night.

Of the thirty-eight who went, only thirty-three survived, and three others were wounded and hospitalized.

“Little girl, what’s your name?” Jiang Tian forced a smile.

At this moment, even Jiang Tian’s initial excitement at having performed a meritorious service vanished.

“Uncle, my name is Meng Tingting. Where’s my dad?” the little girl pressed.

“Tingting, come here. We should go.”

Just then, an elderly man with a hunched back and a full head of white hair walked unsteadily out of Song Zhi’s office.

His face was deeply wrinkled, and his eyes were dim, seemingly devoid of any light.

Jiang Tian knew this must be Meng Yang’s father. Behind him followed a middle-aged woman with red eyes, clearly having cried for a long time.

At this moment, Jiang Tian’s heart was heavy.

He felt he needed to do something for this era, to change something.

If he didn’t have the ability, so be it, but now…

Jiang Tian felt that he should climb higher and step by step reach the pinnacle of power to wipe out all the evil spirits.



Chapter 28 Chief Gao was stunned, the young man remained calm.


"Chief Song, was that Captain Meng's family member just now?" Jiang Tian walked into Song Liguo's office.

*Click!*

Song Liguo lit a cigarette. As a narcotics officer, the risks and psychological pressure of his missions were immense; usually, more than half of them were heavy smokers.

In his previous life, Jiang Tian didn't smoke or drink in college, but after a month in the police force, he became a heavy smoker.

However, after being reborn, Jiang Tian wasn't as addicted to cigarettes, but he didn't deliberately abstain either.

Given his physical condition, smoking wouldn't cause him much harm.

Through the swirling smoke, Jiang Tian vaguely saw Song Liguo's dejected face.

Jiang Tian had actually been working under Captain Meng during his internship at the police force. Unfortunately, Captain Meng had sacrificed his life. Although Jiang Tian had been promoted, seeing Captain Meng's family member completely extinguished any joy he felt for his promotion.

For the past month or so, Captain Meng had taken good care of Jiang Tian.

Finally, Meng Yang sacrificed himself while drawing fire for Jiang Tian. In fact, Jiang Tian clearly remembered that in his previous life, Meng Yang had survived.

In this life, because of him, Meng Yang had died.

“When you went to arrest Wei Rong today, the families of those who died yesterday came. Each family received a 100,000 yuan compensation,” Song Liguo said.

100,000 yuan was already an extremely high amount.

But Jiang Tian frowned: “Chief Song, Meng Yang’s family is huge. His parents can’t earn money, and he has two children to support. How can they survive on 100,000 yuan?”

100,000 yuan seemed like a huge sum.

But for a family’s expenses, it was a drop in the ocean.

“This is already a special favor. Normally, we wouldn’t get 100,000 yuan, you understand? Part of it is supplemented from our case-handling budget.” Chief Song knew exactly what Jiang Tian was thinking.

But there were some things even he couldn’t decide.

“Didn’t I seize five million yuan today?” Jiang Tian suddenly said.

"Hmm?" Song Liguo looked at Jiang Tian in surprise.

Jiang Tian remained calm: "Apply to the higher-ups, saying that our case-handling funds are severely insufficient, and the officers' welfare benefits are too poor. This is detrimental to eradicating drug traffickers. Furthermore, because of the difficult living conditions of anti-narcotics officers, drug traffickers dare to openly bribe them. Just apply to keep that money in our anti-narcotics unit to improve welfare."

That's right.

Jiang Tian was using that money, but it wasn't for his own spending.

Ultimately, Jiang Tian simply couldn't stand the treatment of their anti-narcotics officers. It wasn't that it was bad, but rather, they wanted to fight against the extremely wealthy and ruthless drug traffickers.

Necessary living conditions needed to be guaranteed. Jiang Tian always believed that one should receive commensurate rewards for their efforts.

Keeping five million for expenses was far more useful than handing it over.

"This is too difficult," Song Liguo thought of their recent achievements, but he felt the chances were slim.

"You write the application, I'll approve it."

Thump thump thump!!!

Just then, the office door opened.

Gao Xiaolong, leading the way, had an excited expression on his face.

Especially after seeing Jiang Tian, ​​Gao Xiaolong's face was filled with satisfaction.

Heaven knows how Gao Xiaolong felt knowing that drug dealers possessed firearms at Yunnan University and had nearly assassinated its president.

The sheer joy he felt upon learning that the university president himself had come to present a banner of gratitude was indescribable.

Because it was Jiang Tian who had orchestrated all of this!

Gao Xiaolong had thoroughly investigated the situation at Yunnan University and understood the perils involved.

Most importantly, this arrest involved a high-ranking drug dealer.

Rushing to the scene, Gao Xiaolong felt no disappointment despite the university president's departure. Reaching the office door, he heard Jiang Tian's voice.

At this time, only a short time had passed since the year 2000.

At least, to Jiang Tian, ​​who was familiar with the future, the police station seemed dilapidated and primitive.

Even the office door was just an iron door; there was no soundproofing whatsoever.

Gao Xiaolong heard Jiang Tian's voice.

"This suggestion is excellent. Only by improving the welfare and benefits of police officers can we ensure they fight on the front lines without hesitation or worries," Gao Xiaolong said immediately upon entering.

Jiang Peng, following behind Gao Xiaolong, seemed like a mere follower, invisible.

He had absolutely no presence.

No, it should be said that in the past few days, Jiang Peng had been shining brightly in the entire Yunhai officialdom.

Everyone knew that his son, Jiang Peng, had caught Gao Xiaolong's eye, and this high-ranking leader greatly admired Jiang Tian.

As the saying goes, fortune and misfortune are intertwined. Jiang Tian reversed the outcome yesterday, and similarly, completely rewrote Jiang Peng's fate.

Not only was he not suspended, but he was even subtly given important responsibilities by the Yunhai leadership.

Especially since Jiang Peng knew that before coming here, Secretary Zhou had a special conversation with him, subtly praising how he had raised Jiang Tian, ​​and implying that he should report to him more often in the future.

This was unprecedented; it meant Zhou Zhao had already considered him one of his own.

And all of this was thanks to his son, Jiang Tian!

Jiang Peng had never imagined that one day, the benefactor supporting him would be his own son. He hadn't given his son any resources, yet he was reaping the benefits from his son's success.

He felt a mixture of bittersweetness and secret delight.

After Gao Xiaolong finished speaking about approving the note, he went to Jiang Tian, ​​patted him on the shoulder, and said, "Xiao Jiang, nobody thought highly of you, including me at first, but you've proven them wrong."

Hiss!!!

After these words, the entire office fell silent.

What did this mean? This represented Gao Xiaolong's complete approval.

Gao Xiaolong ignored the shocked looks on the faces of the crowd and continued, "Whether it's luck or skill, merit is merit. You've twice saved the country and the people from enormous losses; your contributions are invaluable."

Jiang Tian was deeply shaken.

These words were the greatest recognition he could receive.

Jiang Tian clenched his fists. His fate had been rewritten, and so had his father's.

The man who had sacrificed himself to save him in his past life, ultimately dragging him and his entire family into the abyss, now held him in clear and full acceptance.

"And I can make the decision. If you have the ability, whatever you seize, keep as much as your anti-drug squad; don't hand it over. That's my promise to you. Originally, this kind of problem should be solved by the state, but right now our capabilities are very limited," Gao Xiaolong sighed as he said this.

To be honest, the police force's conditions were rudimentary, and the anti-drug officers' benefits were too low—these were immediate problems, and how could he not know them?

But knowing was one thing, knowing wasn't enough; there was no way to solve it. Funds were also lacking from above; the whole country was tightening its belt.

This also meant that every officer had to face ruthless drug dealers day and night, and even more so, the terrifying bribes offered with hundreds of thousands or even millions of dollars.

A single wrong decision could send them plummeting into hell.

"Thank you, Chief Gao, Branch Secretary Song. I hope some of this money can go to the families of those who sacrificed their lives yesterday. Without their breadwinner, they have no way to survive. Tens of thousands or even hundreds of thousands are just a drop in the bucket," Jiang Tian said.

Gao Xiaolong looked at Jiang Tian with even greater satisfaction.

He cared about his teammates.

He was incredibly capable.

How many people like him are there in the world?

This was a talent, a genius. Gao Xiaolong thought to himself that he must cultivate him carefully in the future.

It has to be said that Jiang Tian had unknowingly accumulated terrifying political resources.

With Gao Xiaolong in the past and Yun Da in the future.

In the future, as long as Jiang Tian doesn't get into trouble, he will naturally rise rapidly in rank.

"Sir, I'll be going now. I still need to do a psychological evaluation later."

After resolving these matters, Jiang Tian submitted a report. Conducting a post-murder evaluation is strictly regulated, and Jiang Tian couldn't avoid it.

“Stay here, don’t leave yet. This case is a bit complicated. I didn’t learn much on the way here, and you were the one who arrested the person and discovered the case. Don’t rush the diagnostic report; listen to it.” Gao Xiaolong made the final decision.

The case wasn’t exactly complicated, but it was also quite difficult.

“Wei Youdao started his business twenty years ago and eventually built it into a leading enterprise in Yunhai, affecting all aspects of people’s lives. Given the size of his business, it shouldn’t be related to him. During our recent drug raids, we’ve also found that many young people, from well-off families, are seeking thrills, yet they still choose to use and traffic drugs.” Song Liguo sighed.

He didn’t know how to describe this trend.

“This is an educational issue that needs improvement, but that’s precisely why drug prohibition is so urgent; we must resolutely eradicate this unhealthy trend.” Gao Xiaolong frowned.

The case had a significant impact, and Gao Xiaolong understood that it had already alarmed high-level leaders.

"How's the interrogation of Wei Rong going?" Jiang Peng asked hurriedly.

Song Liguo glanced at Jiang Tian with a slightly embarrassed expression.

Good heavens.

Song Liguo looked at him and almost didn't recognize him as a human.

"He's currently unconscious. A doctor is here providing basic treatment," Song Liguo explained.

"How can someone be unconscious after being shot in the arm? This is ridiculous! This case is very serious; the higher-ups are paying close attention. We must solve it by a deadline. How can we interrogate someone unconscious? Who is his supplier? How did he traffic drugs? We must find out as soon as possible." Jiang Peng sensed something was wrong. This kind of injury is easy to treat—remove the bullet, bandage it up, and interrogation can begin immediately.

Song Liguo stammered. He couldn't very well say that Jiang Tian had kicked him. He was capable of such things, but he couldn't openly admit it.

"At the police station entrance, this drug dealer was too arrogant, threatening to wipe out my whole family. I kicked him," Jiang Tian explained.

However, Jiang Tian stroked his chin.

He knew the force of that kick; it was controlled. Wei Rong couldn't possibly be unconscious.

"These damned drug dealers, let's go check on them." Gao Xiaolong's brow twitched.

Jiang Tian's flower reminded him of some unbearable memories.

No, or rather, the tragic fate of our anti-drug police predecessors.

Because these vicious criminals are no joke; there are numerous precedents.

Each incident is a shocking and heinous crime, but it cannot be publicized for fear of causing widespread panic.

Anti-drug police officers, after all, are human too.

"Fearless in the face of danger, resolute in character, unafraid of threats—what a good kid! Who said he's a black sheep?" Gao Xiaolong couldn't help but praise Jiang Tian in his heart.

What a good kid!

His actions in confronting drug dealers to the bitter end are even more admirable.

Soon, Jiang Tian followed them to the treatment room.

It was just a makeshift bed. Wei Rong's limbs were bound to the bed, and two doctors were constantly calling to him, but Wei Rong seemed dead, unresponsive.

"Sir, we used some anesthesia when treating his wounds, but he should wake up soon," the doctor explained.

Gao Xiaolong frowned deeply: "As soon as possible."

However, just as Gao Xiaolong spoke, Jiang Tian's gaze was fixed on Wei Rong, and he noticed that Wei Rong's eyebrows had twitched.

Damn it.

He was faking it.

It's no wonder Gao Xiaolong didn't notice; Wei Rong had been kicked so badly by Jiang Tian that his face was unrecognizable, and it was quite possible he was unconscious.

"Chief Gao, no need, I have a way, I can definitely wake him up immediately," Jiang Tian said, a sudden inspiration.

"He's unconscious, what way can you possibly have? Don't cause trouble," Song Liguo quickly stopped him.

"The doctor advised waking him up later, don't mess around," Jiang Peng also frowned slightly.

Mainly, he wanted to remind Jiang Tian not to get arrogant after making a contribution.

No matter how many contributions he made, in their eyes, yesterday proved Jiang Tian's ability, but today it only meant Jiang Tian was lucky, just happened to be bribed by drug dealers.

After all, Jiang Tian had only joined the anti-drug squad a month ago; he shouldn't get arrogant before making a contribution.

“Xiao Jiang, Wei Rong’s identity is unusual,” Gao Xiaolong added.

“I’m swearing an oath,” Jiang Tian insisted.

To be honest, Jiang Tian also wanted to solve the case as soon as possible. Was there anyone else behind Wei Rong?

If there was, they had to be caught.

And then there was Wei Youdao.

He had arrested Wei Youdao’s son.

Jiang Tian’s heart sank. For this Jiang Tian in this life, he dared not gamble.

So he couldn’t wait.

“Let’s give it a try.”

Before Song Zhi could say anything more, Gao Xiaolong made the final decision.

"Okay."

Jiang Tian pulled a black baton, about the size of a flashlight, from his waist.

The three men froze upon seeing what Jiang Tian held.

"Damn it, Jiang Tian, ​​what are you doing?" Song Zhi's forehead was dripping with cold sweat.

No wonder, Wei Rong was terrifying now, his face disfigured, and his arm shot.

Song Zhi was genuinely afraid he'd be interrogated to death.

"Damn it, young man, calm down." Gao Xiaolong gasped.

They might not know, but they knew.

Zzzzzzz!!!

Sure enough, the next moment, the stun gun in Jiang Tian's hand emitted a sizzling arc.

Gao Xiaolong felt his scalp tingle.

This young man was too ruthless, and this was a new recruit in the police force!

To be honest, Gao Xiaolong wanted to teach Jiang Tian a lesson.

But the next moment...

Jiang Tian, ​​holding the stun gun, pressed it directly against Wei Rong's crotch.

Before pressing it down,

Gao Xiaolong saw Wei Rong's face covered in cold sweat. Sure enough,

He was faking it.

He'd been taught a lesson.

He'd actually been taught a lesson by this young man.

Damn it.

Gao Xiaolong was completely dumbfounded.

The next moment, he watched in disbelief as Jiang Tian, ​​despite clearly seeing the man open his eyes,

still pressed the stun gun down.

"Ah!!!"

A hoarse, agonizing scream echoed for dozens of meters, until…

Even Wei Youdao, who had just been notified and entered the police station, vaguely heard this scream.

"Why does that scream sound a bit like my son's voice?"



Chapter 29 Revenge from a Drug Lord


At this very moment, Jiang Tian was conducting a thorough interrogation.

He had no chance in his past life, but in this life, now that he had a platform, Jiang Tian was unwilling to give up any opportunity.

The more than ten years of falling to the bottom in his past life had shown Jiang Tian far too much of the coldness and cruelty of human nature.

While Jiang Tian was conducting the interrogation intensively, Wei Youdao was on the phone at the door.

“Why did such a huge blunder occur?” Wei Youdao asked, his brows furrowed.

“This was purely because they found a narcotics officer named Jiang Tian and tried to bribe him. In the end, that narcotics officer Jiang Tian shot and killed several of them. Wei Rong was also shot at the school and arrested.”

The voice came from the other end of the phone.

This caused Wei Youdao's expression to change drastically: "Are they crazy?"

"No, it seems Wei Rong has taken a liking to Jiang Tian's sister and sent his subordinate Gao Fei to contact her, hoping to drag them down through Jiang Tian. According to their investigation, Jiang Tian is mediocre, but who knew he would actually dare to do this?"

"This is probably something you ordered," Wei Youdao said, suppressing his anger.

"Don't be angry. You have connections, right? You can use them. Besides, with your status, protecting your son is a piece of cake." The voice on the phone was relaxed.

But Wei Youdao angrily hung up the phone.

He turned to walk into the police station, but then, with a grim expression, he muttered Jiang Tian's name.

...

"Wei Youdao is here. Is it possible he's involved?"

Gao Xiaolong posed the hypothetical question.

Just now, Jiang Tian had shoved Wei Rong hard with a stun gun, causing Wei Rong to scream and wake up.

The actual interrogation will be conducted by professional interrogation experts.

Jiang Tian stood behind Gao Xiaolong and the others. In front of them was a one-way mirror, allowing them a clear view of the interrogation room.

Since arresting Wei Rong, although the trial hadn't yet taken place, Jiang Tian had already gained two thousand sin points.

That is to say, Jiang Tian now had a total of four thousand sin points. He hadn't added points randomly, mainly because he lacked suitable attributes.

The Martial Arts Master level was sufficient, and his physical attributes were currently adequate, so he hadn't added any points for the time being.

Wei Rong alone contributed a full two thousand points.

And the red dot appearing on Jiang Tian's scanning radar was now twice as bright as Wei Rong's.

Knock knock knock!!!

The next moment, a knock sounded on the door.

A moment later, Li Zijing opened the door and said, "Boss, Wei Youdao is here."

"Wei Youdao?"

Jiang Tian's eyes narrowed. At this moment, he realized why there hadn't been any follow-up to this case in his previous life.

As far as Jiang Tian knew from his previous life, only a few people, including Gao Fei, were involved; even Wei Rong was unaware.

Was it genuine ignorance, or did Xiao Bo fail to investigate further, or was further investigation too implicated?

Regardless of the reason, staring at the terrifying crimson dot on the scanning radar, Jiang Tian knew that Wei Youdao definitely had a huge problem.

“I’ll go talk to him,” Song Zhi stood up.

After Song Liguo left,

Jiang Peng tentatively analyzed, “He has a good reputation in Yunhai; it shouldn’t be possible.”

“Yes, without motive, with fame, wealth, and even power, it's unlikely he'd take such a risk and embark on this path,” Gao Xiaolong analyzed.

Indeed.

If Jiang Tian hadn't had the scanning radar, he wouldn't have known Wei Youdao had such a terrifying problem.

In fact, compared to Wei Youdao, based solely on the scanning radar, Wei Rong was practically insignificant.

“Maybe he's a major drug lord,” Jiang Tian licked his lips.

This is incredibly dangerous.

In his previous life, even a decade or two later, drug trafficking was difficult to eradicate, thanks to the complex geographical and cultural environment here.

The terrain itself is mountainous and interconnected, practically a paradise for drug traffickers.

Eradicating it would be an impossible task.

Jiang Tian pondered slowly. In his previous life, Wei Youdao hadn't been caught; he had even remained active for five years before his case finally came to light.

*Snap!*

The next moment, Song Zhi pushed open the door and walked in, saying, "I just chatted with Wei Youdao. Judging from his expression, he's completely unaware; it doesn't seem like he's acting."

Sure enough.

Jiang Tian breathed a sigh of relief. This Wei Youdao hadn't been discovered from beginning to end.

Then Jiang Tian became excited.

Because this Wei Youdao was a major drug lord!

Catching him would be a huge achievement.

"If I remember correctly, five years later, it was this achievement that helped Xiao Bo advance further in a key position," Jiang Tian pondered.

Suddenly, he understood why Xiao Bo had enjoyed harming him so much in his past life.

This feeling of revenge was indeed quite satisfying.

Of course, the most important thing was reciprocity.

What Xiao Bo owed him in his past life, he would make Xiao Bo repay tenfold in this life.

"Chief, the interrogation is over. His account is basically consistent with Gao Fei's," the interrogation expert walked in.

“Okay, I understand. Take him away for treatment.” Gao Xiaolong nodded.

“Xiao Tian, ​​the police station has made an appointment for you at the psychology department of Yunhai First Hospital. Go there later to get a psychological evaluation report,” Jiang Peng said to Jiang Tian.

Jiang Tian left the police station.

He changed out of his police uniform. Although he was now in civilian clothes, Jiang Tian still carried his pistol.

Those on the front lines like him usually have specially approved gun licenses.

After all, narcotics police officers can encounter various unexpected dangers or retaliation from drug dealers at any time.

Jiang Tian changed into his leather jacket.

He hadn't worn it for over ten years.

Since returning, Jiang Tian had always worn his police uniform. Suddenly switching back to the distinctive attire of this era felt a little strange.

Overall, it felt a bit odd, but Jiang Tian didn't think much of it.

“Young man, can we talk?”

Just then.

A Mercedes-Benz W14 stopped beside Jiang Tian, ​​and he stopped.

He watched as the blood-red mark approached.

He turned his head and looked out the open back window, where a kind, middle-aged face peered out.

Jiang Tian knew this was Wei Youdao.

To be honest, if it weren't for the terrifying, purplish-red mark in his mind reminding him, even he wouldn't have realized that this seemingly kind and honest man was actually a major criminal.

Or perhaps, even a major drug lord.

"My name is Wei Youdao. My son has caused you trouble," Wei Youdao began to explain.

"Oh, so you're that drug dealer's father. How could you, a seemingly honest man, raise such a heartless bastard? Boss Wei, your parenting is questionable! What, you've come to take revenge?" Jiang Tian seemed surprised.

Hiss!!!

A fierce glint flashed across Wei Youdao's face, but he disguised it well, smiling as he said, "My fault, young man. I heard you arrested him, and I wanted to thank you for bringing him to justice."

"That beast will be shot soon, no need to thank me," Jiang Tian waved his hand casually.

Hiss!!!

Wei Youdao felt a toothache.

Even with his exceptional patience, he felt an urge to kill Jiang Tian.

Toxic.

Wei Youdao felt this bastard was simply toxic, always bringing up the most sensitive topics.

“No, Officer Jiang, you rid the country and the people of a scourge; we must thank you.” Wei Youdao almost gritted his teeth, but still managed a forced smile.

“You’re such a weirdo. I was about to execute your son, and you still want to thank me.” Jiang Tian’s face showed a strange smile as he looked at the red, almost explosive dot on the scanning radar.

Now Jiang Tian understood almost everything: the redder the dot, the more evil it represented, and the brighter it was, the more hatred it represented.

Therefore, Wei Youdao now wished he could kill him.

Especially if he knew the situation.

But Jiang Tian also had his eye on him.

“Jiang Tian, ​​you bastard, why didn’t you answer my call?”

Just then.

A fierce voice rang out.

Jiang Tian turned his head and immediately saw a woman with barely above-average looks, but a vicious expression, walking towards him.

In a daze, Jiang Tian’s memories came flooding back.

Familiar.

Too familiar.

Wang Yifei.

That's right.

Wang Yifei is here.

Jiang Tian was unaware that while he was focused on solving the case...

Xiao Bo endured unimaginable torment.

Losing Mu Ya was like losing his life, and all of this was because of Jiang Tian.

Xiao Bo desperately wanted Jiang Tian to lose everything, but he was even more terrified of actually being fired; to him, it felt like the sky was falling.
