Back home, Xiao Bo brutally beat Wang Yifei, completely disregarding the child in her womb.

He vented all his hatred for Jiang Tian on Wang Yifei.

Then…

Wang Yifei, her legs weak and her face still flushed, went to find Jiang Tian.

Enemies meeting are always filled with hatred.

Jiang Tian squinted, looking at Wang Yifei's appearance, which clearly showed she had just finished exercising, and his fists clenched so tightly they cracked.

It wasn't that Jiang Tian still harbored feelings for Wang Yifei; it was purely because this bitch was so hateful.

But then Jiang Tian had a change of heart.

"That beast Xiao Bo likes this woman so much, I wish them well. As for Mu Ya, I'll accept her."

This bitch, who had wronged him so badly, Jiang Tian knew she was heartless.

In his past life, when Xiao Bo was powerful and influential, this woman might have been devoted to him.

But now that Xiao Bo had lost everything, Jiang Tian wondered if he would follow in his footsteps.

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian suddenly felt a surge of intense interest.

With their positions reversed in this life, Jiang Tian's lips curled into a smile. Those two beasts—even killing them would be too lenient for them.

"Oh, I just blocked you. You definitely won't answer my calls." Jiang Tian was disgusted by the two harassments and blocked Wang Yifei.

"You piece of trash, you dare block me?" Wang Yifei's face was filled with disbelief and shock. She seemed to have never expected that her former simp would dare block her.

Wang Yifei and Jiang Tian were classmates in college.

Back then, Jiang Tian didn't know what possessed him, but he became Wang Yifei's simp.

And Wang Yifei kept him as a backup for four years. Finally, after graduation, Jiang Tian's background was exposed, and this woman finally softened her stance.

A month ago, Jiang Tian took an instant liking to Xiao Bo and introduced him to Wang Yifei.

Jiang Tian guessed that the two of them had secretly started a relationship back then, and even that Xiao Bo was pregnant.

It just goes to show that birds of a feather flock together.

This woman's chastity was only in front of him; to everyone else, she was a whore.

"I don't know where you got your confidence, you slut, trying to act tough in front of me." Jiang Tian turned and left.

Actually, Jiang Tian planned to act today, to investigate Wei Youdao. A barking dog doesn't bite, and this Wei Youdao posed a significant threat to Jiang Tian.

Before that, he had no interest in playing games with this slut.

"Officer Jiang, so that's why you haven't had time for me. Turns out you had a fight with your girlfriend." Wei Youdao joked from the car.

As if nothing had just happened.

Jiang Tian glanced at him but ignored him, driving away directly. He couldn't alert him yet, but he was determined to take this guy down tonight, no matter what.

With a sharp weapon in hand, the killing intent naturally arises.

"So, you're afraid of my revenge, so you deliberately quarreled with your girlfriend? But you didn't expect that, did you? I saw right through you. Heh, losing a loved one must be very painful. You're nothing compared to me."

Watching Jiang Tian leave, Wei Youdao's gaze instantly turned icy cold.

He had already taken everything that had just happened as an act by Jiang Tian, ​​a pretense to protect the woman's safety.



Chapter 30 A Ruthless Attack, The Vanishing Jiang Yu


"What should I do with Xiao Bo? He saw us entering the hotel today, and he seems very disappointed in me now. He's ignoring me. What should I do?"

Watching Jiang Tian ride away on his bicycle, Wang Yifei, unsurprisingly, called Xiao Bo on her phone.

Meanwhile, Xiao Bo was racking his brains trying to figure out how to explain things to Mu Ya, or even how to take things further.

"He's ignoring you? Can't you give him a little something in return?" Xiao Bo snapped angrily.

"But you said you wouldn't let him touch me," Wang Yifei said, sounding a little aggrieved.

That's right.

They met when Wang Yifei came to the police station to see Jiang Tian, ​​who was then pursuing her intensely.

Wang Yifei had relented at the time, and their relationship was developing.

Xiao Bo happened to see this.

Upon seeing Wang Yifei, Xiao Bo had ulterior motives. He could tell at a glance that Wang Yifei was no good.

Sure enough, with just a few tricks, Wang Yifei became incredibly grateful and devoted to him, clinging to him like glue.

A thought struck Xiao Bo: he wanted Jiang Tian to raise his child. The two conspired together.

So, they never used protection, and Wang Yifei, incredibly lucky, became pregnant in just a few days.

Xiao Bo even demanded that Wang Yifei maintain a relationship with Jiang Tian, ​​but that Jiang Tian not touch her.

Wang Yifei was completely obedient to him.

“Even though that good-for-nothing Jiang Tian is brainless, you can’t leave him completely without any benefits. Keep him hanging on, at least give him some sweetness, make a sacrifice,” Xiao Bo continued.

“But he won’t see me,” Wang Yifei said, distressed.

“Alright, come back first. We’ll think of something. This afternoon, go to Jiang Tian’s house and talk to his family. Jiang Tian’s mother is just as simple-minded as this good-for-nothing; she’s easy to fool,” Xiao Bo said.

To this day…

Xiao Bo still didn't think Jiang Tian had changed; he still thought Jiang Tian was the same good-for-nothing he remembered.

This good-for-nothing only got lucky and stole his credit.

"Okay, I'll head over then." Wang Yifei hung up the phone.

Watching Jiang Tian's retreating figure, Wang Yifei bit her lip, a hint of disdain flashing in her fox-like eyes: "This good-for-nothing got off easy. Looks like I'll have to make a small sacrifice. I'll sleep in the same bed with this good-for-nothing tonight. He'll definitely be grateful then, and I can slowly manipulate him. Just thinking about letting this kind of good-for-nothing touch me is disgusting."

Wang Yifei also thought that Jiang Tian was disappointed because he couldn't get what he wanted; giving him a little sweetness might make this sycophant come back.

Meanwhile.

Jiang Tian leisurely rode his bicycle.

Today was his administrative leave, a paid leave, but he didn't plan to rest. He planned to thoroughly investigate Wei Youdao today.

"If I find out, fine. If I don't, I can't let this bastard live." Jiang Tian's brows furrowed.

At the same time, his gaze subtly shifted in one direction.

That's right.

At the distant intersection, a dilapidated Santana was waiting at the traffic light.

Normally, there would be nothing wrong with it, and Jiang Tian didn't sense anything unusual. However, if it weren't for the glaringly bright warning in his mind,

Jiang Tian wouldn't have realized that this might be his death sentence.

"Damn it."

Jiang Tian gasped.

It's easy to dodge a spear in the open, but hard to guard against a hidden arrow. Jiang Tian was thankful that he had leveled up during the drug bust.

He had directly created a scanning radar.

Otherwise, dealing with these vicious, organized, and premeditated criminal gangs would have been extremely difficult.

At that moment, Jiang Tian's hair stood on end.

He appeared to be casually looking around, but in reality, his eyes were fixed on the Santana across the intersection.

The next moment.

The green light turned on.

The Santana suddenly roared to life.

Jiang Tian was preparing to swerve.

But the next moment.

Jiang Tian blinked and suddenly realized that the car wasn't facing him.

"Not me?" Jiang Tian was genuinely surprised, but the malice was unmistakable, and the scanning radar warning was definitely not fake.

A moment later, the vehicle roared violently, hurtling straight towards the person behind Jiang Tian.

At that moment, Jiang Tian saw the man's face.

A man in his forties, seemingly intoxicated. Jiang Tian had heard of such accidental murders before.

Now he witnessed it firsthand.

The next moment.

Bang!!!

A crash rang out.

The distance was considerable, about four or five hundred meters.

The vehicle, after hitting the person, slammed into a utility pole.

The car didn't even stop; it immediately reversed rapidly, clearly intending to flee the scene.

No, if it weren't for the scanning radar in Jiang Tian's mind, this would be considered a hit-and-run. And now, with the scanning radar, it further confirmed one thing: this wasn't a simple drunk driving accident; it was intentional.

"Stop!"

Jiang Tian ran frantically behind.

But the car continued like a madman, without stopping at all.

...

On a rooftop two blocks from Jiang Tian.

At this moment, Wei Youdao, who had already left, was watching this scene with a mocking expression, binoculars in hand.

A satisfied look graced his face.

“Let me let you taste the pain of losing a loved one first. Some things are not for a lowly narcotics officer like you to touch. You don’t have the right to be arrogant in front of me.” Wei Youdao sneered.

“Tonight, arrange for Lao Liu to cross the border and leave the country. Let him hide in a neighboring country for a while.”

A moment later, Wei Youdao said to his secretary behind him.

“Understood, boss.”

Wei Youdao nodded without speaking, his gaze fixed on the distance. The so-called Lao Liu was the man driving.

But at that moment, Wei Youdao's expression faltered slightly, then a sneer appeared on his face: "This kid, is he a little out of his mind? Oh no, he's probably gone mad from losing the woman he loved most, taking a broken pistol with an effective range of fifty meters and shooting at someone driving a car three hundred meters away."

He paused slightly at this point.

His smile widened.

He could have targeted Jiang Tian, ​​so why didn't he?

Was it because he was afraid of the consequences?

No, no, no, simply killing Jiang Tian wasn't enough for Wei Youdao to vent his anger; his face gradually turned cold.

Having survived decades of hardship, he knew that a kind person could never do this; he wanted to make Jiang Tian despair.

"Thinking he can act all high and mighty here in Yunhai just because he has a policeman father? Call this naive young man and tell him today is just a lesson, give him some money, see if he takes it. First, find a way to rescue Ah Rong, hopefully he won't be ungrateful..." Wei Youdao's expression was indifferent.

But the next moment.

A gunshot rang out. Wei Youdao didn't take it seriously; even a sharpshooter couldn't hit him.

"Boss, the car isn't moving?" the secretary asked in alarm.

"Old Six still wants to play around?" Wei Youdao felt he needed to teach Old Six a lesson; he couldn't be so arrogant.

"Boss, look! Old Six has been dragged out of the car, looks like he's been shot?" the secretary continued.

"What did you say?" Wei Youdao's eyes instantly turned red.

Sixth Brother was one of his old comrades, having followed him from the very beginning!

He wasn't just his skilled bodyguard;

he was also a brother who had helped him rise from humble beginnings.

Most importantly, Sixth Brother knew a great deal about his criminal activities.

Hiss!!!

"Quick, go check! We absolutely can't let Sixth Brother live!" Wei Youdao's composure vanished; his scalp tingled with fear.

Has he gone mad?

How could he hit that accurately?

"Oh no, we can't let Lao Liu live!"

Wei Youdao was terrified. He absolutely couldn't let him live, because once Lao Liu confessed, he would have no chance of survival.

...

Jiang Tian, ​​who was dragging the driver, immediately observed the situation and was surprised because the crime value wasn't low, at least not lower than Wei Rong's.

But he didn't have time to think further. Jiang Tian wanted to check on the injured person, but the next moment, he heard a voice beside him.

"My child, my child..."

Jiang Tian turned around and froze. Wang Yifei was lying in a pool of blood, clutching her stomach.

So...

"So Jiang Yu was gone before he was even born?" Jiang Tian was completely stunned.

This rebellious son, or rather, this bastard, who had killed him with a single blow in his past life.

...gone in such an unexpected way?

The butterfly effect?

Jiang Tian's eyes were thoughtful as he looked at the driver who committed the crime. He was certain it was premeditated.

Then what was the killer's motive?

Jiang Tian pondered, feeling that he was about to make a great contribution. No matter who was behind him, he was going to expose them this time.



Chapter 31 Don't let him get cocky. What? He's done it again?


"Who sent you?"

Jiang Tian, ​​dragging the driver, sensed something was amiss.

Something was wrong.

Although Jiang Tian hadn't been a narcotics officer long, he frequently encountered drug dealers and drug users while investigating cases in this unit.

At first, Jiang Tian thought this man was drunk, but he wasn't; he was on drugs.

Jiang Tian's shot hadn't killed him; it had grazed the man's side of the skull.

This speaks volumes about Jiang Tian's freakish marksmanship.

The shot to the side of the skull caused temporary disorientation and unconsciousness; with timely treatment, it wouldn't be life-threatening.

But that was contingent on possessing Jiang Tian's incredible marksmanship.

"I...I..." The driver shook his head, seemingly disoriented, his face covered in blood.

Click!!!

Jiang Tian didn't say anything. He pulled out handcuffs from behind his back and quickly slipped them over the man's arms.

After doing all this, Jiang Tian turned around.

At this moment, Wang Yifei was clutching her stomach; blood was flowing continuously from her legs, though the rest of her body was unknown.

Jiang Tian himself hadn't expected this scene.

An unexpected turn of events had caused the rebellious son who would kill him in the future to miscarry.

How unpredictable!

Jiang Tian had been feeling lost and dejected. That rebellious son from his past life had inherited the genes of both Xiao Bo and Wang Yifei, those two beasts; he was definitely not a good person in the future. Moreover, he had killed him in his past life, and Jiang Tian was thinking about when he should take revenge.

But unexpectedly, before he could even act, the little bastard was gone.

"I'll call an ambulance for you," Jiang Tian said, dialing the ambulance number on his phone.

However, based on Jiang Tian's experience, the situation was serious.

Wang Yifei's legs hadn't moved from the ground; she might be paralyzed from the waist down.

"Thank you for saving me just now." Wang Yifei clutched her stomach, her face contorted in pain, but her gratitude towards Jiang Tian was undeniable.

It must be said that the perpetrator, seeing that he hadn't killed her head-on, still tried to run her over.

Jiang Tian's shooting, ironically, gave her a chance to live.

Especially since Jiang Tian fired at the crucial moment, it had a tremendous impact on Wang Yifei. As the saying goes,

Wang Yifei was a woman who admired strength, and this admiration bordered on the obsessive.

At this moment, looking at Jiang Tian's profile, Wang Yifei suddenly thought that if things could just end like this, completely reconciling with Jiang Tian and living happily ever after, it might not be such a bad thing.

It was Xiao Bo's little scheme that had driven her to such a frenzied pursuit, even actively seeking him out.

In the end, she was essentially a despicable person.

"This is the first time I've heard you say thank you," Jiang Tian said with a mocking smile.

These words stunned Wang Yifei instantly: "Jiang Tian, ​​I'm already like this, and you don't even think about caring about me. Instead, you're fussing over such trivial things. I thought you'd matured a bit, but it turns out you're still the same."

Jiang Tian almost burst out laughing.

He really wanted to slap this bitch. Why should I care about you? I saved you, do I owe you something?

Jiang Tian checked the drug dealer's injuries, not caring about the blood on his hands.

Mainly, he was afraid the drug dealer was dead.

"Dying here would be quite troublesome."

He didn't answer Wang Yifei's words, only pondering.

What Wang Yifei? That's clearly impossible.

In his previous life, Wang Yifei hadn't been attacked, but now she had. This proves the problem isn't with Wang Yifei, but with himself.

The only people who know his identity and have a grudge against him have acted in the last two days.

"So, it's highly likely that Wei Youdao misunderstood something, and this is revenge and a warning to me?"

Jiang Tian thought of Wei Youdao's sinister face as he left, and he was basically 80% certain.

But it was precisely because of this guess that Jiang Tian's heart skipped a beat.

No other reason than...

The arrogance of the drug dealers made even Jiang Tian gasp.

When he saw cases before, he didn't feel anything, but only when he experienced it firsthand could he truly feel it.

Jiang Tian didn't even dare to imagine how he would feel if it wasn't Wang Yifei lying here, but Jiang Xiaoyu.

“Wei Youdao.” Jiang Tian let out a deep breath.

The danger for narcotics officers isn't just their own, but also the danger to their families. However, the arrogance and terror of drug traffickers in this era are beyond imagination.

Jiang Tian had identified his target and decided that the sooner the better; he had to eliminate Wei Youdao by today at the latest.

He was now completely confident in his abilities.

So, Jiang Tian took out his phone, preparing to call Song Liguo to report the situation.

Song Liguo squinted. The office was unusually quiet at this moment, but Song Liguo was in a pretty good mood.

Yesterday, he turned the tide, and today Jiang Tian had achieved such a great result.

And he had done it all in front of Gao Xiaolong.

In just two days, Song Liguo's impression of Jiang Tian had completely changed.

“How did this kid do that?” Song Liguo took a sip of water, thinking silently.

The reason was simple: Jiang Tian's past performance had been far too mediocre. It wasn't that he was useless or anything, but rather that while he was good-looking, his academic performance was mediocre; he barely passed the police academy entrance exam.

Even after entering the academy, he failed his courses every year, whether due to a lack of learning ability or other reasons.

In fact, Song Liguo had even advised Jiang Peng against letting Jiang Tian join the police force.

The most significant reason was Jiang Tian's past timid and cowardly nature.

To put it bluntly, he was weak and easily bullied.

His timid and hesitant demeanor made Song Liguo wonder if he had misremembered.

After all, Jiang Tian was practically a neighbor he had watched grow up.

"This kid was definitely hiding something before. Not to mention last night, just today's arrest of Wei Rong—his decisive actions were completely different from his timid and hesitant self," Captain Guo reported to Song Liguo in detail about today's operation.

Song Liguo nodded repeatedly. Jiang Tian's internship in the police force was with Meng Yang, one of Captain Guo's subordinates.

To be precise, Captain Guo of the First Brigade was Jiang Tian's direct superior.

"What you said isn't wrong, but this kid is young. After he comes back from the First Hospital, you'll need to take good care of him, especially by providing him with psychological support. Don't let him get carried away after making a contribution; young people are prone to getting arrogant." Song Liguo smiled contentedly as he sipped his tea.

"Don't worry, I feel that with that incredible marksmanship, this kid will be a pillar of our team within two years." Captain Guo stood up. "Chief Song, I'll be going now. Investigate the two drug dealers who are dealing with Gao Fei and Wei Rong."

Song Liguo stood up, about to speak, when the phone rang.

Song Liguo smiled slightly at Captain Guo, looked at the caller ID, and pressed the answer button.

The caller ID showed Jiang Tian's number.

As soon as he answered...

"Holy crap..."

"Really?"

"Okay."

"What did you say? This was a drug addict deliberately running someone over with his car, and even tried to run them over a second time. You saved the person. Okay, I understand."

"Comrade Jiang, well done! You did a great job!"

Swish!!!

After saying that, Song Liguo's face trembled with excitement, and his hands shook.

God knows the immense and terrifying pressure Song Liguo was under.

It's no exaggeration to say that Gao Xiaolong was sent by higher-ups specifically to monitor them.

Gao Xiaolong had been there for so many days, and Yunhai hadn't accomplished anything significant.

But the drug dealers and traffickers in Yunhai were utterly ruthless and showed no signs of restraint, yet they seemed impossible to catch. Gao Xiaolong had reached his breaking point.

Under these circumstances, the anti-narcotics team, eager for a breakthrough, finally obtained information from overseas intelligence.

They intended to pull off a big one, but instead, they stumbled upon a massive operation. If it weren't for Jiang Tian, ​​they would have been completely wiped out.

Before the day was even over, they arrested another group of drug dealers this morning, again from Yunhai.

On his way home on administrative leave,

he stumbled upon a murder plot involving drug addicts.

As a veteran anti-narcotics officer, Song Liguo instantly sensed something was amiss.

That's why Song Liguo was so agitated.

Before this, Gao Xiaolong had berated him countless times, and more than once stated that if he couldn't handle it, someone more capable should be promoted. Even Jiang Peng had been severely reprimanded by Gao Xiaolong for his poor performance in drug enforcement.

"Damn, Chief Song, is this guy going to get credit again?" Captain Guo was dumbfounded.

What?

These past two days haven't even passed, and this guy's got some serious motivation. He's been given a day off and can still grab some credit?

But Captain Guo wasn't really surprised; he was just pure shock and excitement.

Good grief, before, he couldn't even hold his head up when attending meetings at the provincial department.

He'd be criticized to his face, accused of "Yunhai's drug enforcement failures," and accused of "ruining their jurisdiction."

"Most of the drugs flow out of Yunhai; how are Yunhai's drug enforcement efforts even going?"

Such sarcastic remarks were countless.

"This kid's luck is just too good. He's still applying for a first-class merit at Yun University, is he going to get another one?" Captain Guo swallowed hard.

"Yeah, other people get first-class merits practically effortlessly, but this guy gets them wholesale. Let's go check it out. If nothing unexpected happens, he'll get at least a third-class merit." Branch Chief Song picked up his clothes.

After all, this was a life-saving operation.

Three merits in two days.

Wow, Branch Chief Song thought about himself. So many years as a police officer, so many years of diligent work in the anti-drug squad, and he's almost been surpassed by Jiang Tian in just two days—no, not in total, but in quality.

Because he doesn't even have a single first-class merit yet.



Chapter 32: Collecting Merits and Rewards with the Blessing of the God of Wealth


When Song Liguo and his team arrived,

the first thing they saw was Jiang Tian holding a prisoner in chains.

Not far away, there was a young woman, as the police station was the closest.

So, when Song Liguo and his team arrived, the ambulance hadn't arrived yet.

"How is the injured person?" Song Liguo's expression was serious.

Driving under the influence of drugs is far more serious than drunk driving.

"The situation is quite serious. She's bleeding from her genitals. We'll have to wait for the doctor to examine her. I haven't touched her," Jiang Tian explained briefly.

As a righteous narcotics officer, although Wang Yifei was a despicable woman, Jiang Tian still maintained a professional attitude in this situation.

When it came to official business, Jiang Tian wouldn't show any prejudice.

But to expect Jiang Tian to provide meticulous care, to actually fulfill his boyfriend duties, was just a load of nonsense.

"Hmm, that's good. Let's interrogate her properly." Song Liguo breathed a slight sigh of relief; at least no one had died.

Moreover, interrogating a drug user might lead to more connections.

"Wait a minute, Xiao Jiang, isn't that your girlfriend?"

Just then, Captain Guo, who was following behind, took a closer look. Good heavens, that one glance sent a shockwave through him, causing him to take a half-step back.

His face turned pale; clearly, this brought back a bad memory.

Having been in the police force for so long, especially as a narcotics officer, Captain Guo had witnessed drug dealers retaliating against their families.

And there were precedents for this.

Hearing Captain Guo's words, Song Liguo also turned around.

He had to admit, there was a regret from the past.

Song Liguo once had a wonderful daughter, a classmate of Jiang Tian, ​​and most importantly, they had grown up together.

Song Liguo had once thought his daughter and Jiang Tian would be lovers. Although Jiang Tian was a bit ordinary in the past, at least he was honest, and Song Liguo was quite at ease with him.

It was a pity that Jiang Tian didn't seem interested in his daughter, and Song Liguo didn't force it, so it was left at that.

His daughter later went abroad to study.

"No, she's not, don't talk nonsense," Jiang Tian quickly shook his head.

Damn it, thinking about it, Jiang Tian wanted to slap himself twice. How could he be so pathetic?

He found such a despicable woman, and to make matters worse, he brought her to the police station to show off.

"Broken up?" Song Zhi was slightly surprised.

Jiang Tian nodded decisively: "Broken up a long time ago."

Song Liguo patted Jiang Tian's shoulder: "Your sister Qiu Wan will be back the day after tomorrow. Let's get together then; you haven't seen each other for quite a while."

"Sister Qiu Wan is coming?" Jiang Tian's face lit up with joy.

To be honest, Song Qiu Wan's fate in her previous life was also tragic. In her previous life, Song Qiu Wan was abroad, and Song Liguo had already been suspended from his duties.

Later, Jiang Tian heard about it while drinking with Song Liguo. Something had happened; a drug addict had tried to assault him, and in a fit of rage, the addict shot and killed him.

However, in his previous life, Song Liguo hadn't extended an invitation. Back then, Jiang Tian was practically a sycophant to Wang Yifei, so Song Liguo probably didn't want the two of them to meet and cause any negative consequences.

"I understand," Jiang Tian nodded.

While they were talking, the ambulance arrived and took Wang Yifei away. Jiang Tian didn't even glance at her.

"That bitch! Jiang Tian just saved her; that was already within the bounds of police ethics."

Then, Jiang Tian went to the police station for the third time.

He gave a basic report on the mission.

A single shot from two or three hundred meters away pierced the side of the head, and crucially, it didn't kill the person driving under the influence of drugs.

This marksmanship.

Once again, it greatly shocked the police team.

"My god, that's incredible! A true marksman!" Zhao Wei stared at his Jiang brother in disbelief.

"This time, getting you a third-class merit award shouldn't be a problem," Song Liguo said to Jiang Tian.

Third-class merit award?

Jiang Tian considered it for a moment, feeling somewhat disdainful of a third-class merit award: "Just a third-class merit award?"

Song Liguo's face darkened instantly at Jiang Tian's disdainful look: "Get lost! Go to the hospital for a psychological evaluation right now. Is two days of paid leave enough?"

"Enough, enough."

Jiang Tian swayed and slowly left the police station.

The smile on his face gradually faded.

Before him, a light screen appeared that only he could see.

【Host has been found to have received multiple merits. The stamp collecting achievement task is now open.】

【1: Please collect three first-class merits. Reward: God of Wealth entry. After wearing, a certain amount of wealth will be generated every minute.】

【2: Please collect one first-class, one second-class, and one third-class merit. Reward: God of Body Shape entry. After wearing, the host will gain the most perfect body and coordination in the world.】

Damn.

Jiang Tian's eyes brightened: "At Yun University, the case itself isn't enough. You saved Principal Lian Ying, so you'll be given a first-class merit as an exception. That means you're one step short of two first-class merits. If you had killed Wei Youdao, that would have been at least a first-class merit."

As for the second entry, Jiang Tian was even more envious.

His physique had improved somewhat, but it was still only slightly muscular and looked disproportionate. At least, from Jiang Tian's perspective as a martial arts master, many parts of his body couldn't fully utilize their power or perform the corresponding movements.

Muscle groups and physique can only be developed through consistent, long-term training.

With this, Jiang Tian was instantly sculpted into the most perfect physique—how could he not be satisfied?

And the same applied to the wealth aspect.

Jiang's father owned a government car, but Jiang Tian couldn't use it for personal purposes, and the police's official vehicles were even more off-limits. He still commuted by bicycle.

Fifty thousand yuan wasn't enough to buy a car.

With the God of Wealth, Jiang Tian would never have to worry about money again.

Thinking this, Jiang Tian was full of energy and rode his bicycle directly towards the city center.

While at the police station, Jiang Tian had already researched Wei Youdao's information.

Jiang Tian, ​​in particular, retained fragments of his past life's memories. Five years later, Wei Youdao was discovered because a factory near the suburbs emitted a pungent, metallic chemical odor daily.

A report was filed, and an investigation revealed it to be a drug manufacturing plant.

And the owner was Wei Youdao.

Entering the drug trade is like entering a deep sea. Although Wei Youdao desperately tried to clear his name, the dark side is the dark side; once you're in this line of work, escape is impossible.

However, after the investigation, Wei Youdao did manage to flee.

An A-level arrest warrant was issued.

But even after Jiang Tian's rebirth, Wei Youdao hadn't been arrested.

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian immediately felt that solving this case would guarantee him a first-class merit.

Reborn, three first-class merits in hand.

Jiang Tian's heart raced involuntarily at this thought.

In a daze, he thought of his past life, at this time he was at his lowest point, his parents under investigation, and he suspended from his job.

The relatives who had once fawned over him scattered in an instant, fearing any connection to his family.

But in this life, his fate had been completely changed.

Evening.

The starry sky was dazzling.

Jiang Tian arrived at the outskirts of Yunhai.

Yunhai was actually surrounded by mountains on three sides, with various tunnels connecting to all parts of the country and overseas.

The well-connected mountainous environment provided fertile ground for crime.

Jiang Tian searched all afternoon.

Finally, at dusk, he found him hiding outside a factory.

“This is it.” Jiang Tian sniffed the air.

A strong, pungent metallic smell assaulted his senses.

Although he had only been with the anti-drug squad for a little over a month, Jiang Tian had learned about drugs back in school.

This was the process of making methamphetamine; after being subjected to high temperatures, it produced an extremely strong metallic smell.

It was incredibly pungent.

Jiang Tian surveyed the surroundings. The drug factory was located on the edge of Yunhai, very remote, only a few miles away from a small village, accessible only by a single mountain road.

On the surface, it appeared to be an ordinary small steel mill.

If it weren't for the dense red dots on Jiang Tian's scanning radar, he might not have even noticed it.

“So well hidden, no wonder the drug factory has remained undiscovered here for so many years.” Jiang Tian's eyes gleamed as he observed.

He didn't rush into action.

Based on his observation, there were about two lookouts on the outer perimeter, but facing Jiang Tian, ​​they easily infiltrated.

Inside the factory, Jiang Tian peered through the cracks in the windows and saw at least twenty people coming and going.

Undoubtedly, this was a massive drug manufacturing plant.

Jiang Tian then surveyed the yard.

A luxurious Mercedes-Benz was parked inside. "It's Wei Youdao."

Jiang Tian's eyes lit up, and he was about to call the police.

The next moment.

Wei Youdao led his men out of the factory, a large Tibetan Mastiff on a leash. "Old Ding, this is your job. Make sure it's safe. Be careful not to let word get out and attract the cops."

"Don't worry, boss, I know what to do," replied Old Ding, seemingly the factory manager.

"You know what's going on. Yunhai is cracking down on drugs lately. I heard a high-ranking official is personally overseeing the anti-drug operation. A major operation is likely imminent. But this shipment is crucial. Finish this batch, then stop for now. We'll talk again once things calm down," Wei Youdao said calmly.

“This batch of goods will be complete tomorrow,” Old Ding replied.

Wei Youdao nodded: “The sooner the better.”

After speaking, Wei Youdao turned to his secretary and said, “Be discreet for now. Don’t touch Jiang Tian’s other family members, but find an opportunity to take out that narcotics officer from Jiang Tian.”

When Wei Youdao said this, it seemed he wasn’t just asking for a life.

It was as if he were about to kill a cat or dog.

He had become indifferent to human life.

“Boss, we found out that Jiang Tian’s father is the director of the Yunhai police station. Is this the right thing to do?” The secretary hesitated.

“So what if he’s the director? If it weren’t for the higher-ups taking notice of Yunhai, I would have wiped out his entire family.” Wei Youdao’s expression was indifferent.

It seemed this wasn’t the first time he’d done something like this.

Human life, in the eyes of such a ruthless person, was probably less than that of a dog.

Hidden behind the wall, Jiang Tian’s eyes flashed with a vicious light.

“Luckily we acted early. If we had waited any longer, Wei Youdao would probably have gone berserk and attacked Xiaoyu and the others.” Jiang Tian’s face was also filled with murderous intent.

He was now completely clear-headed. Dealing with drug dealers was different from dealing with criminal police. Narcotics officers faced drug dealers who were organized and countless times more vicious criminals.

These people are ruthless and inhuman; driven to the brink, they'll use any means of revenge.

Moreover, most drug dealers have several lives on their hands.

Woof!!!

Woof woof!!!

Just then.

A dog barked.

In the quiet mountain area, in the quiet factory, the barking was especially jarring.

The Tibetan Mastiff, being led by Wei Youdao, glared fiercely in one direction, howling.

It even seemed to want to break free and pounce.

Wei Youdao turned his head curiously: "New recruits at the factory?"

Old Ding shook his head blankly: "Boss, you know, the cops are patrolling everywhere lately, investigating leads. How could we dare bring in new people? We haven't had any new recruits for over half a year."

Hmm?

The more Wei Youdao listened, the more serious his expression became.

Finally.

Wei Youdao suddenly looked at the wall, his scalp tingling, and shouted, "Who?"

He couldn't help but panic. If he hadn't been discovered, he was the tycoon of Yunhai, the conference representative, the renowned philanthropist of Yunhai, who had donated to over a dozen primary schools.

But if he'd been discovered, he was a drug dealer.

More than fifty grams is punishable by death. His drug production and trafficking had been going on for so many years; the amount was unknown.

He could probably be executed tens of thousands of times.

How could he not panic?

This was a matter of life and death.

Without evidence and without being discovered, he could do anything.

Now that he'd been discovered, facing the state apparatus, Wei Youdao remained rational.

"Go."

A moment later, hearing no movement around him.

Wei Youdao, leading his Tibetan Mastiff and his men, hid behind the car, then gave a look to the security guards at the factory.

The four guards exchanged glances, then cautiously moved out of the vehicle's reach and approached the area behind the wall.

Ten meters.

Five meters...

The next moment...

A flash of silver light.



Chapter 33 Upgrade, Triple Limit, This is Crushing Victory


The provincial government's conference room was brightly lit despite the darkness of the night.

Gao Xiaolong sat at the head of the table.

Below him sat the provincial government director, Jiang Peng, the director of Yunhai County's anti-drug bureau, and below them were Song Liguo and other heads of the anti-drug teams, as well as the head of the provincial anti-drug brigade.

Sun Haibo was also seated to Jiang Peng's left.

Everyone's expression was serious, their brows furrowed, their eyes lowered as they waited for Gao Xiaolong to speak.

Gao Xiaolong did not disappoint, giving a brief, indifferent glance to the provincial government director, Shen Han.

Shen Han glanced at the time before speaking with a grave expression, "This afternoon, the Narcotics Control Team apprehended a group of drug dealers at the bus station, but unexpectedly, they were carrying a large quantity of firearms, resulting in the unexpected deaths of six provincial narcotics officers."

Gao Xiaolong didn't give anyone a chance to react, banging on the table with a serious expression, "Comrades, our provincial capital has become a drug den. Drug crimes in Yunhai have reached a point where there's no time to lose."

It's very serious.

The most terrifying thing is that not only is the problem rampant in Yunhai, but it's actually escalating despite crackdowns.

Jiang Peng and Song Liguo, representing the Yunhai Municipal Public Security Bureau, were both sweating profusely.

Especially their hands, which were clenched tightly, their palms unconsciously damp with sweat.

They couldn't help but be nervous. They hadn't realized it before, but now they finally understood why Gao Xiaolong had come from Beijing—he was clearly there to investigate them!

Or rather, it was all about taking them down, but because of Jiang Tian's heroic performance in the previous battle against drug dealers, Gao Xiaolong gave them a chance.

"Chief Gao, let us explain," Jiang Peng tried to explain.

Gao Xiaolong immediately raised his hand to interrupt: "I don't want to hear any explanations. I want to see results, I want to see your determination to crack down on drug dealers, and even more importantly, I want to see you solve major cases."

Shen Han's eyelids twitched.

Major cases are never that simple.

Having fought drug dealers for many years, Shen Han knew very well that these drug dealers were not only ruthless but also used unimaginable methods to conceal drugs.

Many methods were simply impossible to detect, and impossible to uncover.

However, at this moment, Shen Han angrily accused Jiang Peng: "The provincial anti-drug brigade oversees the entire province, so it's understandable that they can't be everywhere at once, but what's wrong with your municipal anti-drug team? How are you handling cases?"

Jiang Peng wanted to argue, but he couldn't.

Which drug trafficking organization isn't experienced, with extensive experience in battling narcotics police?

Especially in some cases, in the past, if the investigation went too deep, it even led to problems for the families of the investigators.

Of course, this situation has serious historical roots; it didn't develop in just three or two years.

Even the provincial department can't change this situation.

Upon hearing that the provincial department had directly sacrificed six narcotics officers in a major case, almost everyone instinctively gasped for breath.

This isn't a small problem; it's a huge problem that has alarmed the entire capital.

"This also fully demonstrates the incompetence of your municipal bureau. In all these years, have you had a single major case to show for yourself? Narcotics control is practically non-existent, and drug traffickers run rampant," Shen Han continued.

“Um, Director, excuse me for interrupting, but yesterday one of our sharpshooters killed 150 drug dealers on the spot,” Song Liguo said, somewhat unconvinced.

“I know, do you need to remind me? Besides that…” Shen Han’s brow twitched. As the director, how could he not know about such a major incident?

He had even personally gone to the scene afterward and vividly remembered that sharpshooter named Jiang Tian.

“Well, today we cracked another drug trafficking case at Yunnan University, and that young comrade Jiang is about to receive his second first-class merit,” Song Liguo continued.

Although it was all Jiang Tian’s doing, he was one of their team members.

Song Liguo’s whole body seemed to harden as he spoke, his face radiating sternness.

He’d changed.

Shen Han’s eyelids twitched. He knew that this man, who used to be almost everyone’s punching bag and the object of everyone’s ridicule in the provincial department, had changed from today onward.

"Comrade Jiang is excellent, but he's still young and needs time to grow and develop. Now, I announce that today's case has alarmed the Kyoto authorities, who have requested the establishment of Task Force 512, a joint effort with the Narcotics Control Bureau, the Criminal Investigation Bureau, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau. The case must be solved within a specified timeframe. Shen Han, as the Director, you will be the head of this task force," Gao Xiaolong declared, slamming his hand on the table.

Gao Xiaolong didn't take Jiang Tian seriously. Ultimately, Jiang Tian was still young; he was just a good shot and had a bit of luck, but apprehending drug dealers wasn't so simple.

Because he was young and inexperienced, Gao Xiaolong didn't dwell on Jiang Tian, ​​let alone suggest he join the task force.

Ring ring ring!!!

Everyone stood up, about to answer,

A cell phone rang.

Everyone's gaze instantly turned towards the source of the sound: Song Liguo.

If Song Liguo had ever been stared at like this before, he would undoubtedly be sweating profusely.

But now.

Jiang Tian had handled two major cases so well in two days; he had the confidence.

“Commander Song, I’m on Gaoling Mountain. I’ve discovered a drug manufacturing plant here. Not only that, the owner is here too—it’s Wei Youdao. Requesting immediate backup.” Jiang Tian went straight to the point.

But Song Liguo’s face changed drastically: “What did you say? A drug manufacturing plant?”

Song Liguo was completely speechless.

Who was Wei Youdao?

A tycoon, a conference delegate, powerful, rich, and influential—he had everything he wanted.

So even if they couldn’t arrest Wei Rong, they never suspected Wei Youdao of anything.

But now…

They’d actually discovered a drug manufacturing plant.

He even witnessed Wei Youdao's actions firsthand.

Song Liguo's heart skipped a beat.

Pervert.

This pervert.

Oh no.

His precious treasure.

Their police force's precious treasure.

He was in a panic.

He was afraid something might happen to Jiang Tian.

Jiang Tian's status in Song Liguo's heart had risen immeasurably.

And now...

Before Song Liguo could think further, the next moment...

A loud bark came through the receiver.

Song Liguo's heart skipped a beat.

Jiang Tian's voice came through: "I've been discovered. A dog smelled me."

Song Liguo jumped up and exclaimed, "Hold on! I'm coming right now. Don't hang up!"

Looking up, he was surprised to find several faces in front of him.

Especially Jiang Peng, who was almost right in front of him, exclaimed, "What did you just say Jiang Tian did?"

A drug manufacturing plant?

The confirmation was received.

Everyone at the scene was shaken.

A drug manufacturing plant—what was this? This was an extremely large and terrifying criminal organization!

The ability to operate a drug manufacturing plant meant that there must be a terrifying scale of drug trafficking, and it also meant that the anti-drug operation would make a huge, successful start.

Just then!!!

A splattering sound came from the still-connected phone.

It was the sound of a sharp object piercing flesh.

A brief moment of silence.

Bang bang bang!!!

Intense gunfire erupted.

While everyone was in a frenzy, police cars sped out of the provincial government building, running red lights and rushing towards the location.

A fierce fight had already broken out in Jiang Tian.

The location was very remote.

Even at full speed, the provincial government, located in the city center, couldn't reach the mountainous area in the suburbs.

It would take at least half an hour to an hour, so Jiang Tian didn't plan to wait for reinforcements.

Of course.

Jiang Tian wanted to experience firsthand just how terrifying the combat power of such an awesome attribute was.

“Add some points…”

“Pshaw, System, upgrade the 'Strong Physique' attribute.” Jiang Tian said impatiently.

【Unfailing Accuracy (Gold)】

【Scanning Radar (Gold)】

【Martial Arts Master (Red)】

【Strong Physique (Green) Exceptional Talent (Blue)】(Your physical attributes have been greatly improved, approximately three times beyond human limits)

【Minor Achievement in Disguise (Green)】【Superior Memory (Green)】【Minor Achievement in Gambling (Green)】......

【Sin Value: 5000-4000】

These 5000 attributes were contributed by the arrest of Wei Rong and the drug-driving Lao Liu, as well as Gao Fei and his gang. However, Gao Fei and his gang contributed less; the majority came from Wei Rong and Lao Liu.

Jiang Tian lived frugally, saving for a rainy day.

Black, white, green, blue, red, gold—although these were level six attributes, Jiang Tian noticed that the starting attribute was white; black was practically unheard of.

White required 100 sin points to upgrade to green, 1000 sin points to upgrade to blue, 10,000 to upgrade to red, and a whopping 100,000 to upgrade to gold.

Jiang Tian had painstakingly eliminated over a hundred ruthless foreign drug dealers, and through countless low-level and useless attribute combinations, he had managed to synthesize one gold, one red, and several green attributes.

Now, fearing his physique wouldn't be strong enough, Jiang Tian upgraded his physique attributes ahead of time.

Sure enough, at this moment, Jiang Tian felt as if all the power in his body had exploded.

The green attribute pushed Jiang Tian almost to the limits of human capability.

The blue attribute directly exceeded human capability by three times.

This gave Jiang Tian complete confidence in his safety and combat power.

So, when faced with the approaching security drug dealers, Jiang Tian hid behind a wall, relying on his scanning radar without even looking.

Then, Jiang Tian casually picked up a tree branch from the ground.

A martial arts master, coupled with a body three times the limits of human capability.

Jiang Tian's close-combat killing ability could be said to be unparalleled in the world.

As expected.

One of the armed security drug dealers cautiously peeked behind the wall.

The next moment.

*Thud!*

Jiang Tian, ​​holding a tree branch, instantly pierced the man's eye and penetrated his brain.

The drug dealer didn't even have a chance to struggle; he died on the spot.

A martial arts master, Jiang Tian could see all the fatal weaknesses and flaws in his opponents, as well as countless martial arts techniques fused to their extremes.

His attacks were always deadly, always lethal.

"You..."

The nearest security guard, a drug dealer, was terrified and raised his gun to fire.

But the next moment.

*Snap!*

The two were very close.

Jiang Tian simply threw a punch, striking the man's throat, sending him sprawling to the ground, clearly beyond saving.

His attacks were always deadly.

Killing two people was as easy for Jiang Tian as waving a hand, leaving even himself astonished.

He seemed far more powerful than he had imagined; these drug dealers were in for a world of trouble.

Jiang Tian grinned.



Chapter 34 Are you crazy? One person overpowers twenty-eight drug dealers.


With the martial arts mastery combined with his exceptionally strong blue-tier physique, Jiang Tian felt an explosive surge of energy throughout his body—three times the human limit combined with his martial arts prowess.

However, Jiang Tian felt he was still lacking something. If he could upgrade his physical attributes to red, his combat power would likely increase several times over.

But Jiang Tian was only thinking about it. Upgrading his exceptionally strong physique to red would require at least 10,000 crime points, and he was currently 6,000 short.

Besides that, Jiang Tian actually wanted to upgrade his criminal investigation attribute. While it wasn't as necessary for narcotics officers as it was for criminal investigators, the criminal investigation attribute was crucial for tracking and solving cases.

A thought flashed through Jiang Tian's mind.

After smashing the throat of the second drug dealer, Jiang Tian casually grabbed the AK from his hand.

Jiang Tian wasn't out on a mission today. As a narcotics officer, he actually possessed a privilege: the privilege of carrying a gun. Many accidents had occurred when narcotics officers were unarmed.

Behind every system lies a bloody lesson, especially for narcotics police who face constant missions.

Their freedom regarding firearms is unmatched, even by criminal police.

But even with this freedom, Jiang Tian only had a regular pistol with a single magazine of bullets, which would be empty in a few shots.

There were so many people around.

Bang! Bang! Bang!

Just then.

The other two men opened fire.

But Jiang Tian's movements were always faster than theirs. He kicked the man he had just shot, sending him flying into the air to catch the bullets.

And Jiang Tian's AK instantly sprayed two streaks of fire, striking the two men in the head.

Four men.

In the blink of an eye, dead.

It took less than two seconds—from Jiang Tian's move to the deaths of four men—two seconds.

With his unerring aim, mastery of martial arts, and three times the physical limits of the human body, Jiang Tian is, without exaggeration, a walking strategic weapon.

Oh, and finally, with the scanning radar, Jiang Tian is practically fully armed.

Completely bewildered.

Completely dumbfounded.

Wei Youdao's face was blank as he stared at the four corpses lying haphazardly on the ground behind the wall at the intersection.

Not a single scream. Because it was outside the suburbs, the air quality was excellent, and the moonlight illuminated the scene; Wei Youdao could even clearly see the twig stuck in the eye of one of the corpses.

Hiss!!!

Wei Youdao's scalp tingled.

Ruthless.

Too ruthless.

The cops?

"Boss, the cops have arrived." Old Ding's forehead was also covered in cold sweat.

They'd only seen a dark shadow flash by; they didn't even know how many people were outside the wall.

His face was even a little pale.

The instantaneous deaths of four people had terrified him.

"Who goes there, looking for me?" Wei Youdao shouted.

He understood the cops, just as narcotics officers understood drug dealers.

In Wei Youdao's memory, narcotics officers posed no threat to them.

The past years had proven that.

If there were such formidable narcotics officers, would his drug factory have remained here for so many years?

Wei Youdao's forehead was dripping with cold sweat. He couldn't figure out who he had offended.

But unfortunately, the people outside the wall remained completely silent, as still as death itself, and an atmosphere of fear was spreading.

"Go and tell everyone inside to come out with their weapons," Wei Youdao ordered.

Old Ding crouched low.

He was already being very careful, but the car was still a distance from the factory, and he was covered in cold sweat.

He glanced at the road; it was about a few meters away, which relieved Old Ding.

He leaped forward, quickly running towards the factory to take charge.

While in the air,

Old Ding instinctively turned his head to look outside the wall.

"A flash of light?"

Old Ding was startled.

Where did the flash of light come from?

The next moment.

Bang!!!

A gunshot rang out.

Old Ding felt a jolt in his head. Then, his eyes lit up with understanding—a gun had been fired!

"Such a fast gun."

Old Ding's mind raced for a moment before he lost consciousness and became a corpse.

His left and right arms were gone.

Wei Youdao, hiding behind the car with his Tibetan Mastiff, was deathly pale.

It's no exaggeration to say that in the more than twenty years he'd been in Yunhai, Wei Youdao had gotten whatever he wanted.

He was high and mighty in Yunhai; everyone treated him with utmost respect.

He had enjoyed over twenty years of smooth sailing.

His life had been like a dream since he first made his fortune in the drug trade over twenty years ago.

But no matter how profitable other businesses were, they couldn't compare to drug production.

He had considered abandoning it completely and going legalistic, but the terrifying profits made him unwilling to give it up.

"Is it drugs? No, who did I offend?" Wei Youdao kept thinking, cold sweat pouring down his forehead.

"Da Hu, get in and drive." Wei Youdao looked at the bodyguard beside him.

This bodyguard, Da Hu, was Wei Youdao's nephew, a relative who had followed him for many years.

Because of his strength and slightly dim-witted nature, he had always been used as his personal bodyguard.

Da Hu didn't hesitate, quietly opening the car door and getting in.

"Boss, what's happening outside?"

"Why are there gunshots?"

Just then, a commotion erupted inside the factory, followed by more than twenty people rushing out with guns.

That's why it's said.

Drug enforcement officers are in great danger.

Because they almost always face large, organized drug trafficking organizations. Not only are they in danger themselves, but their families are also constantly at risk of retaliation.

Criminal investigators mostly deal with solving cases, handling conflicts and murders, or apprehending wanted criminals.

While there is a degree of danger involved, the individual risks are almost incomparable to those faced by narcotics officers.

"Perfect timing! An assassin's here. Over there by the wall. Kill him." Wei Youdao breathed a sigh of relief.

He was genuinely worried that the people inside the factory wouldn't have time to react before the assassin charged in.

The assassin might be dangerous, but Wei Youdao wasn't confident he could survive such a terrifying and professional killing.

"Brothers, let's go together." The factory workers exchanged glances, none of them backing down.

Although these people were all wearing white protective suits and masks, they shouldn't be mistaken for scholars or experts.

At least not.

Jiang Tian saw through the scanning radar that they were all a deep, purplish-red.

How many sin points did that take!

Jiang Tian took a deep breath, closed his eyes to regulate his breathing, but he didn't relax his guard at all. Even though he was powerful now, he was still just a mortal; a single bullet could still be fatal.

"Including Wei Youdao, twenty-eight," Jiang Tian calculated in his mind.

"Here."

Just then, two figures attacked from behind Jiang Tian.

Seeing Jiang Tian crouching in the shadows against the wall, the two men's faces lit up with joy.

He hadn't attacked yet, merely luring everyone else out of the factory.

This was a blatant first-class merit.

Jiang Tian could even receive a special blessing from the God of Wealth.

After confirming with the scanning radar that no one was inside the factory,

at least, no one with a crime score was in the criminal factory. The scanning radar had its limitations; it could only locate those with crime scores.

Jiang Tian instantly stood up, AK in hand, his body completely concealed.

He fired three shots in quick succession into the courtyard inside the wall, then leaped forward, rushing towards the bushes where the two drug dealers he had just killed were hiding.

The drug dealers, clad in white hazmat suits, swarmed out of the courtyard, unleashing a hail of bullets in the direction Jiang Tian had come from.

A second later, and Jiang Tian would have been riddled with bullets.

Boom!!!

Amidst the barrage of gunfire, an explosion even rang out.

It was a grenade exploding.

Jiang Tian's brow twitched.

These drug dealers were heavily armed.

But they were still a bit outmatched by him.

His gun peeked out, instantly exposing five drug dealers to his fire.

For Jiang Tian, ​​these were not only merits, but also a series of incredibly high crime points waiting to be harvested.



Chapter 35 generates another buzzword, it's awesome!


At this moment, Jiang Tian didn't even need to aim; he simply raised his hand and fired, based on what he could see.

The golden attribute "Never Misses a Shot" gave Jiang Tian the feeling that with every shot, he had an almost intuitive sense of where he would hit the target.

He just needed to fire to hit.

It was a very simple feeling.

Bang bang bang!!!

Jiang Tian didn't hesitate at all.

He drew his gun and started firing. AK bullets are relatively difficult to control.

Especially the AK; although it has many advantages, it also has its drawbacks, such as its relatively short range.

And ultimately, it's a relatively old firearm. Compared to the Type 95 automatic rifle that Jiang Tian frequently used in the police force and used for hunting, it felt much less satisfying.

However, for Jiang Tian, ​​the lack of feel for it was practically nonexistent.

"Nobody here?"

The drug dealers who rushed out exchanged glances.

The leader, in particular, was utterly bewildered. Jiang Tian had indeed been right there when he fired; they were only two or three meters from the edge of the wall, within sight of him.

It hadn't even taken a second or two before they opened fire, and now, their men were gone?

While he was still stunned,

Bang! Bang! Bang!

Has he gone mad?

The sounds of pistols and automatic weapons rang out incessantly.

But amidst this fierce gunfire, Jiang Tian found an opportunity.

Anyone with even a little training knows one thing: a sniper never fires a second shot from the same spot.

Jiang Tian was no exception.

He fired one shot and moved on.

Jiang Tian moved through the jungle like a cheetah.

The jungle provided Jiang Tian with excellent concealment. With his near-cheetah-like speed, he could quickly move after firing, almost undetectable to anyone, even when the two sides were very close.

"Including Wei Youdao, his bodyguard, and his secretary, there are fifteen more drug dealers in hazmat suits in these factories," Jiang Tian calculated in his mind.

At this moment, these drug dealers would never have imagined that Jiang Tian was perched atop a tree above them, looking down upon them.

It was like the gaze of death itself.

"Ten bullets left."

Jiang Tian checked the captured AK; it was low on ammunition, but he had a spare pistol.

"Nobody here."

The lead drug dealer in the hazmat suit went to the bushes, parted them, and found them empty.

Hiss!!!

The lead drug dealer's pupils contracted, and he exclaimed, "What is that?"

What horrified them most was that from the two lookouts to when they rushed out...

In just a few minutes, ten people had died without them even realizing it.

But the most terrifying thing was that they didn't even know who had done it.

"Including Lao Ding and the initial four, we've lost fifteen people in total. And you're saying we haven't even seen anyone, and each one died a gruesome death, blown off their head."

Wei Youdao, hiding behind the car, lit a cigarette with trembling hands. In his twenty-plus years in the underworld, he thought he'd seen it all.

But faced with such a horrific and bizarre scene,

it truly filled him with dread.

The unknown is always the most terrifying.

Even his secretary felt the same way; her lips moved as if she wanted to gag.

The scene was simply too bloody.

"Boss, let's run," the secretary pleaded, her heart pounding, beside Wei Youdao.

Wei Youdao nodded. "Run, but don't drive. That mysterious man is guarding the entrance. In this situation, he's still incredibly accurate. When did I offend such a sharpshooter?"

Wei Youdao had no idea that his appearance today would pose such a huge threat to Jiang Tian.

"The back door! The back door! Yes, the back door right now! Support me, we'll escape through the back door!" Wei Youdao immediately said.

What? You mean those factory drug dealers cautiously searching for the killer at the main entrance? Wei Youdao didn't care at all.

Even if they all died, it wouldn't affect Wei Youdao.

As long as this place wasn't exposed, or rather, as long as he left safely, the factory was gone, so be it.

As long as he severed ties with this place, even if all these people died, it wouldn't matter. On the surface, he would still be a powerful figure.

"Who is it? Who is it?" Wei Youdao thought fearfully.

The gunfire outside temporarily stopped, but Wei Youdao refused to believe the other party had left.

The ruthless methods, leaving almost no survivors, gave him a strong premonition that it was aimed at him.

“Boss, could it be that narcotics officer from this afternoon? He managed to hit Sixth Brother from hundreds of meters away?” The secretary suddenly realized something.

This stunned Wei Youdao.

Shot skills almost never seen before.

“Impossible. That shot this afternoon was just luck. The records say he's a good-for-nothing. His police academy grades were almost always at the bottom. Besides having a bureau chief as a father, he couldn't even get into the anti-narcotics team.” Wei Youdao shook his head decisively.

He had never thought highly of Jiang Tian.

Even arresting his son only showed that this guy was a reckless, fearless youth, like a hothead. He just bribed him, and he shot several people dead.

A somewhat reckless good-for-nothing.

After saying this, Wei Youdao hurriedly left with his secretary.

From another direction, this alley was planned from the beginning.

A small path leading to the back of the mountain was hidden behind the factory.

There wasn't a path here before, but after Wei Youdao built the factory, he specifically carved out a secret path behind it, just in case.

Now it had come in handy.

As they left along the mountain path, they were unaware that their every move was being monitored by Jiang Tian's radar.

Jiang Tian didn't hesitate at all. The moment they moved, he pretty much guessed their intentions.

If Wei Youdao escaped, Jiang Tian's first-class merit might be in jeopardy.

*Whoosh!*

Jiang Tian, ​​his feet gripping the branch, instantly hung upside down like a bat. At that moment, the two drug dealers, back to back, were still observing their surroundings.

The next moment.

*Snap!*

They barely struggled; Jiang Tian snapped their necks as easily as crushing chicks.

As their bodies slumped to the ground, no one was alerted.

"Not bad, these two have a good eight hundred crime points," Jiang Tian said with slight satisfaction.

Just then, Jiang Tian caught a glimpse of white descriptive words falling.

Two at once.



Chapter 36: Total Annihilation, Looting, and a Fierce Rally


[A somewhat pleasing melody (white)] Jiang Tian's expression was strange, but he still picked it up.

[A Novice in Traditional Chinese Medicine (white)]

Traditional Chinese Medicine.

Although they are novices in Traditional Chinese Medicine, it's not easy to have an entry for this subject. At least a considerable understanding of this field is required to generate an entry.

Especially Traditional Chinese Medicine, which is profound and complex. Truly skilled TCM practitioners can even bring the dead back to life and heal wounds, their methods are almost miraculous.

After killing over twenty drug dealers, Jiang Tian's crime points had doubled from four thousand after his "Exceptional Talent" upgrade to around eight thousand five.

Killing the last six would even give him enough points for a level upgrade from blue to red.

Especially considering the three times the human limit's physical attributes at blue, Jiang Tian couldn't imagine how terrifying the red attributes would be.

"No, don't kill me."

The person who initially led the drug dealers out was probably the head of this drug factory.

With Wei Youdao refusing to submit to the law, Jiang Tian felt unsafe.

The remaining six men, under Jiang Tian’s gaze, all placed their weapons at their feet.

And at that moment…

Jiang Tian slowly emerged from the shadows.

At this moment, the six tortured men finally saw Jiang Tian's face clearly.

A young face.

And a calm voice: "If you had been three seconds later, you would already be corpses."

Yes.

Jiang Tian was standing behind the bushes they had sprayed bullets at two minutes earlier.

And behind them.

"Are you human or a ghost?" The leader's pupils contracted.

For no other reason than that Jiang Tian looked far too harmless.

If he hadn't witnessed it with his own eyes, he would never have imagined that in just a few minutes, more than twenty of his comrades had died at the hands of this enemy, each one a gruesome sight.

The six men all lowered their heads and squatted on the ground.

Jiang Tian placed his gun on his waist.

Two drug dealers pounced on him instantly.

Their eyes were bloodshot and menacing.

For these people, surrendering and being caught by the police meant that, given their crimes, even the best behavior wouldn't save them from the death penalty.

But given even the slightest chance of survival, they would go berserk.

Crack!!

The sound of a skull shattering rang out.

Crack!!

At this moment, Jiang Tian truly unleashed his killing move to its fullest extent, holding nothing back.

To be touched meant certain death.

The other four had only just picked up their guns.

"Don't shoot, I..." the leader stammered, his voice trembling in the face of death.

"Don't be a drug dealer in your next life," Jiang Tian's eerie voice echoed.

Bang! Bang! Bang!!!

Three gunshots rang out, plunging the scene into utter silence, save for the corpses strewn across the ground.

Jiang Tian holstered his gun, not glancing at the scene.

He hastily looted the bag, glancing at it briefly, and found about two keywords.

All the entries were white, indicating Jiang Tian was quite adept at using the system. He almost laughed awkwardly, but thankfully, these entries would provide value for future synthesis.

Whoosh!!!

The next moment, Jiang Tian's shadow flashed, and he sprinted towards Wei Youdao's departing direction at full speed.

His speed became a phantom, completely demonstrating in the darkness what it meant to be faster than a cheetah.

With physical abilities three times the human limit, even a cheetah could be killed by Jiang Tian with a single slap; in a 100-meter race, even a cheetah couldn't catch him.

"Congratulations, host, for judging twenty-five drug dealers, gaining a total of 9,300 sin points."

"Current sin points: 13,300."

While running, Jiang Tian couldn't help but beam with joy upon hearing the voice in his mind.

He'd been so focused on killing and looting that he hadn't even had time to check how many sin points he had left.

Upon checking, Jiang Tian was overjoyed; it was exactly as the system had reported.

Jiang Tian's sin value had increased from 5,000 before the operation, and after a subsequent upgrade, the remaining 4,000 sin value became 13,300. This was enough for Jiang Tian to upgrade a blue attribute to red.

However, Jiang Tian wasn't in a hurry; he now had more than enough.

Compared to the physical improvements, Jiang Tian was currently most eager to acquire attributes related to criminal investigation and other areas. He planned to use these sin values ​​in case of emergencies.
