That is, why did Jiang Tian know that Wei Youdao had problems? Why was the drug manufacturing plant so remote that the entire police station didn't know about it, yet this intern discovered it? Was there something fishy going on?

And he killed more than twenty people—more than twenty people! Who knows if they were all criminals? Was it just Jiang Tian's side of the story?

Sun Haibo's words were utterly righteous.

Because the case was too serious, Sun Haibo stated righteously that Jiang Tian should be detained first, and all issues investigated thoroughly before being released.

As for whether it was a matter of personal revenge, to be honest, Wei Xun didn't know.

Well, Wei Xun certainly didn't agree with that explanation.

"I know you're definitely fine, and not only are you fine, this is a huge achievement. It's just that Director Sun Haibo asked me to keep an eye on you." Wei Xun handed Jiang Tian a cushion.

After all, a stool for a prisoner is definitely uncomfortable.

"Captain Wei, don't worry, I know," Jiang Tian smiled.

Wei Xun breathed a sigh of relief; he was genuinely afraid Jiang Tian would hold a grudge.

Everyone knew that Jiang Tian's success today was a huge achievement, and he had gained the high regard of the higher-ups.

And he had a director father.

What?

You're saying Jiang Tian is too young to be promoted?

Jiang Tian's father has been in this position for so many years; surely he can get a promotion soon?

In short, Jiang Tian's future is absolutely bright, and Wei Xun really doesn't want to offend him unless absolutely necessary.

"Sigh, I don't know how you offended Director Sun. Ever since you joined the police station, I've noticed he has some issues with you. I'll treat you to a meal later; we can talk things out then," Wei Xun said helplessly.

Jiang Tian chuckled.

With over ten years of experience from his previous life, how could Jiang Tian not understand Sun Haibo's intentions?

Especially after figuring out why Xiao Bo had so precisely targeted his home.

And, coincidentally, Gao Xiaolong was in Song Liguo's office.

If he remembered correctly,

Song Liguo seemed to have been called out by Director Sun at that time.

Therefore,

Jiang Tian is now almost 90% certain that this whole thing was orchestrated and coordinated by Sun Haibo, taking advantage of Gao Xiaolong's presence in Song Liguo's office.

Then he directly had Xiao Bo seduce Jiang Tian's mother.

This underhanded tactic had utterly ruined Jiang Tian's entire family in his previous life.

But in this life, Jiang Tian had weathered the storm unscathed, and his father had finally retained his position. How could Sun Haibo possibly accept this?

Moreover, Sun Haibo was afraid they would discover the truth and retaliate, so he would undoubtedly relentlessly try to make Jiang Tian commit a crime.

The conflict was already irreconcilable.

"What conflict could I possibly have with Director Sun? If he doesn't like me, there's nothing I can do. I can't expect him to apologize just because he doesn't like me," Jiang Tian sneered.

Wei Xun could only give a helpless bitter smile. It was a battle between titans; he, a mere administrative section chief, couldn't possibly participate.

Meanwhile, at this very moment, Sun Haibo

was in a terrible mood.

His mood was extremely low.

The autopsy report was out. They arrived here, stormed into the factory, and indeed discovered it was a massive drug manufacturing plant.

A drug manufacturing plant hidden beneath the steel mill.

At this moment, the drug manufacturing plant was deserted, containing various drug raw materials and manufacturing tools.

"The director has found it! There are 800 kilograms of drugs here, all pure! Damn, if this gets out, how many families will it ruin?"

Just then, a narcotics officer, beaming with excitement, ran out leading a police dog, shouting excitedly.

"What did you say?" Sun Haibo's head was about to explode.

Eight hundred kilograms! That's the kind of methamphetamine that carries a death sentence at fifty grams!

Sun Haibo clenched his fists. Sometimes, the entire detachment wouldn't be able to seize such a terrifying amount of methamphetamine in months. This level of seizure, combined with the drug manufacturing plant, was enough to earn two or three individuals two or three first-class merit awards.

But such a huge achievement seemed to have nothing to do with him; the harvesters had already reaped all the benefits.

The more drugs seized, the greater Jiang Tian's merit.

"Director Sun, we've now confirmed the problem here. It's indeed a large group of drug dealers. Wei Youdao's vehicle is parked outside, indicating that Wei Youdao is indeed the big drug lord behind it. This means Comrade Jiang is safe, right?" Song Liguo couldn't help but speak up.

Sun Haibo frowned, hands behind his back, and said calmly, "Xiao Song, we represent the interests of the country and the people. We must set aside personal feelings. The evidence confirms this is indeed a drug manufacturing plant, but do we understand the background? I admit Jiang Tian's discovery here is indeed good, but he acted without orders. Who gave him that authority? Who knows if there's something fishy going on? Believing his one-sided story and letting personal feelings cloud our judgment means betraying the people and the masses."

"You..." Song Liguo clenched his fists.

Looking at Sun Haibo's expression, he felt a surge of anger.

Jiang Tian had worked tirelessly to solve the case, fighting fiercely until midnight yesterday, and today he had cracked two major drug trafficking cases.

Especially tonight, this latest case was a direct result of the drug manufacturing plant's efforts.

Under these circumstances, instead of giving Comrade Jiang a medical check-up, Sun Haibo was suspicious of his comrade.

"Xiao Song, do you have any objections?" Sun Haibo, as the highest commander of this operation, asked unhappily, hands behind his back.

Someone actually disobeyed his orders.

Outrageous!

Thinking that his good relationship with Jiang Peng meant he could disregard him, a dark glint flashed in Sun Haibo's eyes.

But he didn't know...

At this very moment...

Gao Xiaolong and Shen Han, who had just arrived at the city police station, were now there. Shen Han was holding a phone, her face flushed with excitement.

"What's going on?" Gao Xiaolong asked, frowning.

"Old Gao, great news! We seized 800 kilograms of methamphetamine from the drug manufacturing plant!" Shen Han exclaimed excitedly.

This single seizure was unprecedented.

800 kilograms.

What does that mean?

If it were sold, how much money would it involve?

Even eight figures wouldn't be enough.

"That Wei Youdao is quite a figure, already very successful. If it weren't for Comrade Xiao Jiang, who would have thought this guy was actually a major drug lord in Yunhai?" Shen Han clicked his tongue in amazement.

After interrogating Wei Youdao, Shen Han couldn't even imagine how many people were involved, from upstream to downstream.

"Heh, in the end, profits drive people crazy. After making such terrifying profits, there's always a psychological gap between earning hard-earned money and doing it again. That's why many drug dealers get deeper and deeper into the mire and can't extricate themselves." Gao Xiaolong had long understood the criminal psychology of these people.

"However, you're right about one thing: Comrade Jiang is unexpectedly outstanding. Without him, with your abilities, it would indeed have been very difficult to solve this case."

Speaking of Jiang Tian, ​​Gao Xiaolong's expression softened.

Shen Han didn't know why, but Gao Xiaolong became so amiable when Jiang Tian was mentioned, even muttering, "Such a great achievement, a first-class merit isn't enough!"

"However, Jiang Tian is indeed a talent."

Shen Han was already thinking about finding an opportunity to promote him.

Such talent was being wasted at the grassroots level.

Unbeknownst to her,

Many people were actually standing behind Jiang Tian.

Because of Gao Xiaolong, Shen Han had long admired Jiang Tian, ​​even though they had never met, she felt a strong liking for him.

Jiang Tian had given her an explanation in front of Gao Xiaolong; although Jiang Tian was from the municipal bureau, it didn't matter whether he fell under the jurisdiction of the provincial department.

Seeing Gao Xiaolong's anger, Shen Han could only helplessly explain, "Don't worry, Mr. Gao, he's probably just back to inquire about the case."

"Comrade Jiang has been busy all day. Even if the mission is important, he should go to the hospital for a check-up. He can ask questions there. How can he act so recklessly?"



Chapter 40 Sun Haibo: The Leader's Favoritism Is Making Me Very Troubled


Gao Xiaolong walked expressionlessly towards the Municipal Public Security Bureau.

At this moment.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau wasn't particularly quiet in the evening.

Almost everyone who would have left work was back to work overtime.

Not just the narcotics officers, but even people from the criminal investigation departments were back working overtime.

In fact, narcotics officers and criminal investigators often work together on cases.

Sometimes, investigating even the smallest clues requires the cooperation of the criminal investigators.

But similarly, if the criminal investigators encounter a murder case related to drugs, they also need to transfer it to the narcotics officers for joint investigation.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau was brightly lit.

As Gao Xiaolong walked in expressionlessly, everyone working overtime paused.

Then they all stood up in unison.

What a joke.

Although Gao Xiaolong had only been there for two or three days, everyone in the Municipal Public Security Bureau knew him.

He was from headquarters.

Some even hoped to perform well, thinking that if Gao Xiaolong took a liking to them and promoted them, their future would be incredibly bright.

Unfortunately.

Gao Xiaolong didn't even look at them.

Instead, he glanced around.

He seemed to be searching for Jiang Tian.

"Hmm, where's Xiao Jiang?" Gao Xiaolong's brow twitched.

Looking up, Gao Xiaolong saw two people talking excitedly near the door of the interrogation room.

Gao Xiaolong nodded to the group and quickly approached.

"Let me in! Captain Jiang isn't a criminal. What are you doing keeping him here? Why don't you use that time to interrogate Wei Youdao? Why are you watching him?" Zhao Wei found it incomprehensible.

Zhao Wei considered himself Jiang Tian's top henchman.

Normally, he would have been there to provide support immediately, but Zhao Wei had gone to the airport to pick up his sister. It was only when he arrived that everyone else had already mobilized.

Before he could even react, he learned that Jiang Tian had been detained.

Instantly, Zhao Wei was furious.

Why was Captain Jiang being held as a prisoner?

“Don’t be ridiculous. Nobody said he’s a prisoner. It’s just that too many people have died; this is no small matter. We need to be careful now. Once the investigation is complete, he’ll be released, and it’ll be a major achievement,” Wei Xun explained helplessly.

Hmm?

Gao Xiaolong, who had just approached, was still thinking about how to reward Jiang Tian.

First-class hero?

A narcotics officer—too young, not ideal.

Easily targeted; if the news got out, it wouldn’t be good for Jiang Tian’s career.

A second-class hero would be just right, but if it were publicized, it would also be easy to target.

A first-class merit—this kind of award didn’t seem to reflect Jiang Tian’s contribution to this case. Gao Xiaolong was a little troubled.

But…

Now, that trouble disappeared.

What are these two talking about?

"Jiang is being held captive?"

A flicker of confusion crossed Gao Xiaolong's eyes. He seemed unsure if this Jiang was the person he was thinking of.

"Commander Gao."

As Gao Xiaolong approached,

Wei Xun and Zhao Wei quickly saluted.

"Who's inside?" Gao Xiaolong asked, squinting.

Wei Xun explained with a smile, "Commander Gao, it's Comrade Jiang Tian."

Buzz!!!

In that instant, Gao Xiaolong felt his mind go blank.

He looked behind him.

At this very moment, Wei Youdao, though handcuffed and shackled, was sitting openly on the sofa in the hall.

He glanced again at the tightly closed interrogation room.

The interrogation room wasn't used by the drug dealers first, but instead by the heroes who apprehended them.

Is this a joke?

No.

This is outrageous.

This is a complete reversal of the natural order.

This is a sign the sky has fallen.

Who?

Who is it?

When Shen Han and Gao Xiaolong came in and scanned the room, they specifically looked twice.

Wei Youdao, a well-known and powerful figure in Yunhai, how could they not know him? Especially after receiving the news, they investigated the intelligence immediately and recognized him at a glance.

They were just wondering why they hadn't seized the opportunity to conduct a surprise interrogation.

Good heavens.

An interrogation was indeed conducted.

But it turned out to be their own colleague.

"What's your name? What's your position?" Gao Xiaolong asked, suppressing his anger.

Wei Xun didn't think much of it; after all, although he didn't agree with what Sun Haiyang said, it did seem to make some sense.

"Report, my name is Wei Xun, captain of the Second Squad." Wei Xun reported honestly.

"Then tell me, why weren't the drug dealers interrogated, but your own colleagues were?" Gao Xiaolong's voice trembled slightly, a suppressed rage.

Shen Han could hear it best.

He understood that this was because Gao Xiaolong's anger had reached its breaking point.

Wei Xun scratched his head: "Well, Director Sun said that Wei Youdao's identity is special, so we need to investigate the situation first before conducting the interrogation. Besides, the case is complex, and this is also to be responsible to the people."

"Okay, okay..."

Gao Xiaolong laughed angrily, saying "okay, okay, okay" three times.

At this moment, even Wei Xun sensed that the atmosphere was off.

But he couldn't quite put his finger on what was wrong.

However, when he looked up at Gao Xiaolong, he saw a cold light flashing in Gao Xiaolong's eyes.

*Snap!*

And then...

Gao Xiaolong flung open the interrogation room door.

After entering, he glanced around.

Upon seeing Jiang Tian in the interrogation chair, Gao Xiaolong's anger erupted instantly.

"You, right now, call Sun Haibo and tell him to come over," Gao Xiaolong said to Wei Xun with a grim face.

He was determined to get to the bottom of this, to investigate thoroughly, regardless of who came.

He didn't lash out at Wei Xun.

Because Wei Xun's rank wasn't high enough.

However, don't mistake this for Gao Xiaolong not being angry; that would be a huge mistake.

Otherwise, he wouldn't have publicly berated Jiang Tian in the meeting.

This was a leader who truly couldn't tolerate any injustice.

"Yes, sir, right away," Wei Xun said, taking out his phone.

"Chief Gao, Director Shen," Jiang Tian hurriedly stood up at that moment.

"Well, it's good that everything's alright." Gao Xiaolong forced a smile. At this moment, in Gao Xiaolong's mind, Jiang Tian was already a precious gem in the anti-drug team.

"Sir, this is the recording from back then." Jiang Tian took out the video, which he had deliberately preserved.

Because he had a feeling that Sun Haibo would haunt him and cause trouble again, and sure enough, he was.

Meanwhile.

Sun Haibo, who had just come down from Gaoling Mountain, was in a rather sour mood.

He had made a wasted trip today, while Jiang Tian's reputation would only grow stronger.

This forced Sun Haibo to reconsider his next move.

Although Gaoling Mountain is relatively remote, the location is quite pleasant; from here, you can even see the brightly lit sea of ​​clouds.

Sun Haibo, dressed in his uniform, stood with his hands behind his back.

"The lives and property of millions of people in one city and five districts rest on my shoulders. I must pull myself together!" Sun Haibo muttered to himself, a mix of excitement and pride in his voice.

After a moment, there was no response.

Sun Haibo sighed. Usually at this time, Xiao Bo would have already rushed to his side. Without Xiao Bo, he felt like he was missing a crucial right-hand man. Sun Haibo took out his phone and sent Xiao Bo a text message: "Come back to work in the next couple of days. I've already made arrangements for you."

Just then, the phone rang.

Sun Haibo answered the phone casually, his gaze still fixed on the distant city. Without even looking at the caller ID, he said directly, "What is it? I'm busy, just get to the point."

"Oh, okay, I'll be right back."

Sun Haibo hung up the phone casually, shaking his head involuntarily. "Being in a high position, that's how it is. You're always not in control. The superiors' favor always makes me feel flattered."

After muttering to himself, Sun Haibo looked at the driver/auxiliary police officer: "Xiao Wang, have you heard of Chief Gao?"

Sun Haibo considered tonight's arrangements. Overall, he was quite satisfied. Although it might not be entirely fair to Xiao Jiang, he believed it would show the superiors his attitude towards cases: absolutely no favoritism, treating everyone equally.

"Chief, are you going to see Chief Gao? I've seen him on TV," Xiao Wang asked excitedly, somewhat surprised.

"Good job, young man. I have high hopes for you. Keep up the good work, and maybe you'll be promoted someday." Sun Haibo was quite pleased with this form of address.

And soon...

The Municipal Public Security Bureau was drawing ever closer.

"That's good. I may not have received any credit, but I'll at least get some recognition for my hard work."

Suppressing his excitement, Sun Haibo glanced at the bustling city center around him. At that moment, Sun Haibo strode confidently into the Municipal Public Security Bureau.

But what he saw...

Sun Haibo noticed something was amiss.

Why were the people who usually greeted him and saluted him now hurriedly bowing their heads, as if afraid of being implicated in something, avoiding his gaze altogether?



Chapter 41 With the attention of a big shot, we finally have a powerful backer.


Meanwhile, in the conference room, Jiang Tian, ​​along with Gao Xiaolong and others, were watching a video recording.

Gao Xiaolong had originally intended for Jiang Tian to go to the hospital for a checkup as soon as possible, and to be admitted for treatment, psychological evaluation, and therapy.

After all, the feeling of killing is completely different.

Let alone a person, even a dog, after being given raw meat once, will bite.

The same applies to killing. For someone with a weak mindset, their first murder can easily cause severe psychological trauma, perhaps even leading them down a path of crime.

How many people did Jiang Tian kill in a few days?

Over 180 people in two days. These are over 180 bloody lives, starkly recorded in Jiang Tian's file, sealed and kept safe.

However, Jiang Tian didn't leave: "Chief Gao, the case is far too important. My suggestion is to interrogate Wei Youdao first, and secondly, I can also provide a detailed account of the case through the video recording."

Jiang Tian's focused dedication to solving the case instantly contrasted sharply with Sun Haibo in the eyes of Gao Xiaolong and Shen Han.

One was single-mindedly focused on solving the case, while the other, in such a crucial department, was thinking about cultivating influence and building relationships.

Thinking of this, Gao Xiaolong couldn't help but gasp.

Especially when they watched the video recording next.

In the conference room, there were also criminal investigation experts watching.

From the beginning, Jiang Tian had been undercover.

Gao Xiaolong asked, "Jiang, how did you know Wei Youdao was involved?"

Jiang Tian grinned and replied, "Intuition. I can smell the criminal's scent."

Hiss!!!

These words surprised Gao Xiaolong, who looked at Jiang Tian with astonishment: "You smelled it?"

Jiang Tian thought for a moment about his scanning radar, then nodded confidently.

"Good lad." Gao Xiaolong was beaming, his eyes filled with admiration as he watched the scent emanating from Jiang Tian.

He truly hadn't expected Jiang Tian to possess this skill.

There was no doubt.

Because Jiang Tian had completely proven his abilities; otherwise, how could he have detected Wei Youdao's suspicious behavior and even followed him?

"However, although you've done a good job this time, never do this again. While you're skilled, drug dealers are ruthless; acting rashly is extremely dangerous. In the future, you must report any unusual activity immediately," Gao Xiaolong instructed.

That's right.

Jiang Tian's unauthorized actions were indeed problematic; otherwise, Sun Haibo wouldn't have seized the opportunity to target Jiang Tian, ​​who had just performed a meritorious service.

This also allowed Jiang Tian to finally breathe a sigh of relief.

Seeing Gao Xiaolong's admiration before him, Jiang Tian remembered how Gao Xiaolong had long since sacrificed himself in his past life, even causing a major earthquake.

Now, because of Gao Xiaolong's appearance, his own fate, his family's fate, and most importantly, Gao Xiaolong's fate, had changed.

Because this man was an elderly person who had made great contributions!

Furthermore, because of Gao Xiaolong's current high regard for him, Jiang Tian knew that his future was about to rise rapidly, embarking on a path completely different from his past life.

The video Jiang Tian had recorded was playing back, though slightly blurry due to the night.

However, the terrifying nature of it was still palpable.

As the barking of dogs rang out, Jiang Tian was spotted immediately.

Gao Xiaolong's gaze turned serious.

Seeing the four drug dealers rushing towards him, his heart skipped a beat.

Putting himself in their shoes, which narcotics officer could easily handle this situation?

And then, Jiang Tian's swift movements, almost deadly strikes...

Hiss!!!

Gao Xiaolong gasped.

Even Shen Han's face paled: "Xiao Jiang, interested in joining the provincial department?"

Tempted, Shen Han was completely tempted.

Damn it, who could resist such talent?

"You're trying to poach him?" Gao Xiaolong glanced at him.

And then, when more than twenty drug dealers rushed out of the factory, even the experienced Gao Xiaolong felt a chill run down his spine.

He was certain that anyone else would have been dead already.

Gao Xiaolong couldn't even fathom how he could escape from being surrounded by over twenty ruthless, armed drug dealers.

What they witnessed next was true terror.

Jiang Tian was incredibly fast, changing positions almost immediately after each shot. A second's delay in the original position meant being riddled with bullets.

Dangerous.

The assassinations that followed were utterly silent.

The entire operation lasted only a few tens of minutes, until the capture of Wei Youdao.

Only then, still shaken, did Gao Xiaolong realize he was drenched in cold sweat.

Dangerous.

Too dangerous. Anyone else would have been dead.

"Feeling wronged?"

Gao Xiaolong sighed, then turned to Jiang Tian and asked.

Having just survived such a dangerous fight, performed a great service by destroying the entire drug factory, he was now being locked up by his superiors.

Gao Xiaolong felt ashamed before such a heroic policeman.

“It’s not unfair, it’s serving the people,” Jiang Tian said with a smile, his eyes flashing.

“Good.”

Gao Xiaolong was even more gratified.

He had initially thought Jiang Tian, ​​being young, would be angry at being treated like this, but who knew Jiang Tian was so mature?

With Jiang Tian’s achievements and abilities, plus his background, even if he went head-to-head with Sun Haibo, Sun Haibo couldn’t do anything.

However, this also meant he was impulsive but lacked judgment, unsuitable for great responsibilities, only good for charging into battle.

Now, seeing Jiang Tian’s performance, Gao Xiaolong felt a strong sense of appreciation for his talent.

“This is my phone number. If you need anything, you can call me.”

Gao Xiaolong took out a business card with only five words: Headquarters Gao Xiaolong, followed by a phone number.

Hiss!!!

Shen Han stared at this scene in utter shock.

Shen Han knew perfectly well what this meant. Old Gao was a man who wouldn't tolerate any dissent, and he had never done anything like this before—openly protecting someone.

But now…

he had actually left his contact information. How could Shen Han not know that Jiang Tian had completely caught Gao Xiaolong's eye?

Jiang Tian quickly put away the business card. Even with his decadent nature from his past life, he was now barely able to contain his excitement.

This meant that from now on, besides having a bureau chief as his father, he, Jiang Tian, ​​also had a big shot from headquarters as his backer.

Perhaps it's impossible for this bigwig to pull strings for him, but given Jiang Tian's current abilities, if he needed connections, he might as well kill himself.

What Jiang Tian needs now is a fair and just environment, and Gao Xiaolong can provide that.

Just as Jiang Tian received the package, a glance out of the corner of his eye...

Huh!!!

He noticed someone standing at the conference room door.

Upon closer inspection, he exclaimed, "Good heavens, isn't that Sun Haibo?"

But why are his eyes a little red?

A little jealous?

He exploded.

Sun Haibo was indeed exploded.

He felt his chest was about to explode. Gao Xiaolong had actually given Jiang Tian his business card and contact information! This fair and just bigwig had actually made an exception for Jiang Tian!

His jealousy exploded even more! This meant Jiang Tian's future was bright!

Sun Haibo was indignant. Jiang Tian was just lucky and a little skilled, but what good were those if he just charged around recklessly?

Although Sun Haibo may not have made any great contributions, he has certainly worked hard. Why can't we give him a higher regard?



Chapter 42 Who gave you the right to target heroes?


"Chief Gao, you called me here, don't worry. We've properly resolved all the aftermath issues. After our city bureau's arduous investigation, and by treating every perpetrator equally and without discrimination, we've reached a detailed conclusion on this case," Sun Haibo quickly began, not seeking credit, but constantly trying to show off.

However, he didn't expect this.

When Gao Xiaolong heard this, he instantly flew into a rage and sneered, "Your so-called equal treatment means letting the drug lord sit on the sofa without arresting and interrogating him, while locking our greatest hero in capturing the drug lord and dismantling the drug factory in a small dark room?"

"Chief, it was mainly because of Wei Youdao's special status; he's a conference representative, and I reported it to higher authorities before taking action," Sun Haibo explained. Strictly speaking, his actions were reasonable, but he forgot.

Gao Xiaolong, a man who truly couldn't tolerate injustice, was even more enraged by this explanation: "So you can lock up a hero in a dark room, Sun Haibo? Who gave you the right to target heroes? Who gave you the right to use your privileges? Let me tell you, power comes from the people. Equality for all is not just a slogan, but a bottom line. Just because someone has a certain status, you can treat even a major drug lord differently. What wouldn't you dare to do?"

Boom!!!

A tremor ran through the room.

The entire conference room watched this scene in shock.

Especially after hearing Gao Xiaolong's words, the anti-drug police officers present were already furious, and even the assisting detectives had their eyes blazing with anger.

Because Gao Xiaolong's words resonated with them.

Putting themselves in his shoes, if they performed meritorious service and were locked up first just because the enemy had some status?

Who would dare to do it in the future?

Gao Xiaolong was also considering this problem.

Sun Haibo, awaiting praise, looked bewildered, sweat beading on his forehead as he stared blankly at the furious Gao Xiaolong.

He didn't think he had done anything wrong.

"Sun Haibo, you're in this position to solve cases, not for your personal connections. Black is black, white is white. There are no personal connections. You've locked up a comrade who's made a great contribution because of personal connections. What are you trying to do?"

Gao Xiaolong slammed his hand on the table, his face radiating oppressive force as he stared intently at Sun Haibo.

Sun Haibo, at this moment, was panicked, glancing furtively at Jiang Tian.

This bastard.

Sun Haibo's eyes were bloodshot as he watched Gao Xiaolong's merciless reprimand, then at the business card in Jiang Tian's hand.

Sun Haibo's eyes were filled with resentment.

Damn it.

He deserves to die!

“Sun Haibo, I will discuss this matter with headquarters. Is it appropriate to place you in such an important department? Furthermore, Director Shen has decided to issue a province-wide disciplinary notice against you.” Gao Xiaolong continued.

Buzz!

Sun Haibo’s face turned pale.

It’s over.

Sun Haibo knew he was finished; his political future was over.

But unfortunately, Jiang Tian didn’t have time to watch Sun Haibo’s performance before Zhao Wei pulled him out of the conference room and drove him to the hospital.

“Brother Jiang, why didn’t you call me for the operation?” Zhao Wei asked dejectedly.

“Didn’t you say you were picking up your sister from the airport tonight? I was just thinking of going over to check on things,” Jiang Tian explained calmly.

Jiang Tian remembered this very clearly. In his past life, when Zhao Wei sacrificed himself, Zhao Wei’s sister arrived tonight. He still had a chance to turn things around, but that bitch Wang Yifei ruined it.

“What about me?” Li Zijing sat next to Jiang Tian, ​​pulling him closer to examine him, seemingly trying to see if he had any injuries.

After seeing that Jiang Tian had no injuries except for some dirt on his clothes, Li Zijing breathed a sigh of relief.

It has to be said.

As a young man, being so close to a girl made Jiang Tian feel a little uncomfortable.

Of course, most importantly, Li Zijing was two or three years older than Jiang Tian, ​​and had a very pure and innocent look—the kind that gives the feeling of a classical beauty standing before you at first glance. Jiang Tian subtly increased the distance before finally letting out a sigh of relief.

"Didn't you say your blind date asked you out to dinner?" Jiang Tian replied.

Speaking of which, Jiang Tian suddenly remembered that in his past life, Li Zijing had died in yesterday's battle, and that blind date didn't seem like a good person either.

"He was supposedly filming porn, and got arrested later." Jiang Tian looked at Li Zijing and felt he should do something, after all, she had taken care of him since joining the police force, and now she was under his command.

Especially with written reports, case details, and police procedures, Li Zijing handled everything meticulously.

The clerical worker of the squad.

"Tch, no man is a good man. Your sister Li will never get married in this life, I'm a staunch non-marriage advocate," Li Zijing retorted.

"Fine, I was going to treat you guys to barbecue, but forget it then," Jiang Tian shrugged.

Li Zijing's face immediately fell. Jiang Tian had accurately grasped Li Zijing's fatal flaw: while she had a good figure, her gluttony was well-known.

"Fine, you're not a bad person," Li Zijing pouted, her face dark.

Jiang Tian didn't say anything. Wei Youdao's case was basically closed.

As for what would be uncovered later, that would be a tedious task, but Jiang Tian also knew that some things should be let go.

He had already secured the greatest credit.

Giving the remaining scraps to his colleagues was the proper way to handle things.

These small, minor credits wouldn't change anything for Jiang Tian, ​​but they would earn him the goodwill of everyone in the police force—a worthwhile trade.

"I wonder what Xiao Bo would think if he had the chance to come back and saw everyone showering me with praise and flattery," Jiang Tian thought, looking out the window.

Soon.

The car arrived at the hospital.

Although Jiang Tian was unharmed, the police still issued him a certificate and even ordered him to stay in the hospital overnight.

And it was at this very moment...

Wei Youdao's arrest, though late at night, immediately caused a huge uproar.

Who is Wei Youdao?

He has connections in both the legal and illegal worlds of Yunhai, especially with his immense reputation, and his businesses influence all sectors of Yunhai.

Provincial cadre residential area....

Mu Ya returned home, exhausted.

Her expression was somewhat haggard. The man she thought she could entrust her life to had turned out to be that kind of person—it was a huge shock to Mu Ya.

However, after returning home, Mu Ya was surprised to find that her father, who had previously been full of disgust for Xiao Bo, was now asking about him.

“Mu Ya, you don’t know, the city bureau’s anti-drug squad has been on fire these past few days. They’ve killed a couple hundred drug dealers overseas, cracked a drug trafficking case at Yunda University this morning, and then tonight they took down one of Yunhai’s biggest tigers, Wei Youdao. They say Wei Youdao is a major drug lord. The most astonishing thing is that all these cases were cracked by the city bureau. Xiao Bo is in the city bureau’s anti-drug team, right?” Mu Ya’s father exclaimed in amazement.

“Wei Youdao is a major drug lord?” Mu Ya was shocked. Even she had heard of Wei Youdao’s reputation.

“Yes, it’s said that the case was solved by a trainee narcotics officer. His name hasn’t been leaked, but I heard his surname is Jiang. I heard even Elder Gao treats him with special regard.” Mu Ya’s father was refined and approachable, exuding an undeniable air of authority befitting someone in a high position.

“It’s him.” Mu Ya’s mind instantly conjured up Jiang Tian.

It matched up.

At that moment, Mu Ya felt a surge of intense curiosity and a desire to explore Jiang Tian, ​​along with an unconscious admiration.

“Not bad, it seems Xiao Bo has passed the test. As far as I know, it requires at least two or three team contributions. If more effort had been put in, Xiao Bo might have received individual credit. It seems he’s passed the test.” Mu Ya’s father nodded with a smile.

“I…” Mu Ya bit her lip.

She wanted to completely sever ties with Xiao Bo, but she couldn’t bring herself to do it.

Her upbringing instilled in her the importance of fidelity. Although her relationship with Xiao Bo was uncertain and not yet confirmed, changing her mind easily would be fickle.

"I understand, but Dad, I want to go camping tomorrow. You can't let anyone follow me." Mu Ya wanted some peace and quiet to think about how to handle the situation.

She held her phone, looking at Xiao Bo's long post, filled with apologies and pleading, begging for his forgiveness.



Chapter 43 Endless Physical Strength, I am invincible, you can do whatever you want.


City Hospital.

The morning sun shone down.

But on a peculiar hospital bed.

Wang Yifei felt she couldn't accept it.

"I'm sorry, we've done our best, but unfortunately, the nerves in your left leg are severed. You'll probably need crutches to walk from now on."

These were the doctor's regretful words.

For Wang Yifei, it was like a bolt from the blue.

Because this meant she would become disabled?

Wang Yifei had once harbored a vicious contempt for disabled people, possessing a haughty, aloof attitude.

Especially after learning Jiang Tian's identity, the fact that a second-generation rich kid would fawn over her made her feel like she was on cloud nine.

And now.

They were telling this aloof girl that her leg was crippled?

"No, this isn't true! You did it on purpose! You doctors did it on purpose!" The aloof Wang Yifei was furious, almost losing her mind.

The anesthesia wore off.

The loss of all feeling in her left leg was driving Wang Yifei almost insane.

"I'm sorry, we've done our best," the doctor said coldly.

This was utterly unreasonable. If it weren't for the fact that she had lost a leg, she would have kicked her out of the hospital today.

"Also, your medical bills currently amount to 130,000 yuan. Please pay it off as soon as possible," the doctor coldly presented the bill.

They had initially wanted to give her some time to raise the money, but now, they couldn't blame the hospital for being ruthless.

If Jiang Tian were here, he would be very familiar with this situation. In his past life, Wang Yifei had acted the same way, but Jiang Tian was always the one who ended up cleaning up her messes.

"Oh God, what are we going to do!"

"Where would we get that much money?!"

The doctor frowned slightly, not wanting to argue: "If the fees aren't paid, we'll have to stop the medication. If an infection occurs, the patient may ultimately need amputation."

In the ward, as soon as the doctor left, Wang Yifei's parents, who had rushed over, felt like the sky had fallen.

After her tearful outburst, Wang's mother seemed to remember something. Her eyes lit up, and she immediately said, "Jiang Tian, ​​yes, daughter, didn't you say that good-for-nothing Jiang Tian is a rich kid? All officials have wealthy families. Quick, ask him for money!"

Wang Yifei's father also reacted: "Yes, that good-for-nothing definitely has money. He used to buy you phones, gifts, and designer bags; he must be rich."

Wang Yifei's parents were ordinary workers who had saved a little money through frugality. However, Wang Yifei had a younger brother who was getting married soon and needed financial support, so they were even less willing to give him any.

At this moment, Wang Yifei's expression froze. Hearing the name Jiang Tian made her hesitate, unsure how to explain.

Because Wang Yifei felt that Jiang Tian had changed. He used to obey her every word, but ever since she saw him with Xiao Bo in a hotel room, Jiang Tian had been different.

If she regretted anything, it was the emptiness she felt at losing Jiang Tian, ​​her cash cow.

But she didn't know that all the things Jiang Tian had bought for her before were bought with his hard-earned money from odd jobs.

"I...I can't contact him," Wang Yifei said hesitantly.

Wang Yifei's father, Wang Chang, flew into a rage: "Did he disappear because of your accident? That bastard! If he dares to abandon you, I'll report him, I'll report his whole family! Isn't his dad some kind of bureau chief? I'll go and report him! He bought you so many things, he must have embezzled them!"

If Jiang Tian were here, he would know all too well the ugly face of this family.

In his past life, this family had used up all the tens of thousands of yuan left by Jiang Tian's parents to buy a house for Wang Yifei's younger brother's wedding, and it still wasn't enough.

This family was utterly despicable.

While they were arguing heatedly,

they saw a large group of people in white shirts walk past outside the ward.

"Those are...high-ranking officials?" Wang Chang swallowed hard.

Even in his ignorance, he knew that people in white shirts with flowers on their shoulders were definitely important figures.

Most terrifyingly, there were also some people in suits following behind.

The doctor who had just been so arrogant towards them now stood with his hands respectfully placed in front of him, waiting for the group to pass.

He even greeted a smiling man at the door, calling him "Hospital Director."

The hospital director could only accompany them?

Wang Chang's heart skipped a beat; he immediately realized these were even more important figures.

"The elevators in your hospital are a bit inconvenient. You have to go around and change elevators after getting to the fourth floor," Gao Xiaolong commented, leading the way.

What? You say Gao Xiaolong isn't in the health system? Sorry, Gao Xiaolong's rank is high enough that he can handle all security issues; a few criticisms are perfectly acceptable.

It turns out that after learning about the case last night, Gao Xiaolong personally oversaw its resolution, resting only half the night, and was worried about his precious Jiang Tian early this morning.

Good heavens, the entire Yunhai had been stuck for so long without any breakthroughs.

Comrade Jiang solved two high-profile cases in just one day.

Highly influential.

After much deliberation, and following discussions with Director Shen, they jointly applied for an anti-drug vanguard honorary title for Jiang Tian.

However, considering Jiang Tian's young age, recent graduation, and already one exceptional promotion, further promotion would feel like forcing a seedling to grow too fast.

This honorary title would be a significant medal of honor, hence the early morning report to Jiang Tian of this good news.

"Old Gao, the first floor has direct access, and we can transfer on the fourth floor. It's not necessary to change elevators; we just happened to take this elevator on the first floor," the director explained.

Gao Xiaolong smiled slightly and said, "Comrade Jiang Tian is a good comrade and a young hero of our public security system. He must be examined with the best equipment and assessed and treated by the best psychological experts. This is of paramount importance."

It was undeniably a perfect fit.

Gao Xiaolong also had a mission: to rectify the anti-drug and security issues in Yunhai.

After several days of searching without finding a starting point, Jiang Tian's appearance was like a sharp knife in Gao Xiaolong's hand.

They severed the dense network of criminal organizations entrenched in Yunhai.

The group departed.

But their voices reached Wang Chang and the others in the hospital room without a sound.

"Great! That cold-hearted good-for-nothing Jiang Tian is actually in this hospital too! That's wonderful! All the leaders are here. If he refuses to pay, we'll make a scene, we'll report his family for embezzlement!" Wang Chang exclaimed, his face beaming with delight.

Wang Yifei swallowed back the words she was about to say. She didn't want an amputation; she still hoped for the best because the doctor said with proper rehabilitation, she might be able to walk normally again.

But this would require exorbitant medical expenses.

Now, Wang Yifei could only rely on Jiang Tian.

"With the leaders here, Jiang Tian must be under pressure," a spark of hope ignited in Wang Yifei's heart.

"Huang Mei, you silly woman, hurry up and follow them!" Wang Chang grabbed his mother and jogged after them.

The two were dressed rather simply.

Gao Xiaolong and the others glanced at them, assuming they were just family members of a patient and didn't think much of it.

Psychological rehabilitation was on the twelfth floor.

The elevator arrived quickly.

The hospital director personally led the way.

At this moment, Jiang Tian was idly looking at his attribute panel.

After last night's hard work, Jiang Tian has successfully upgraded one of his stats to red.

【Unfailing Accuracy (Gold)】

【Scanning Radar (Gold)】

【Martial Arts Master (Red)】

【Exceptional Talent (Blue)】【Traditional Chinese Medicine Novice (White)】【Minor Achievement in Disguise (Green)】【Exceptional Memory (Green)】【Minor Achievement in Gambling (Green)】【Slightly Appreciable Qin Music (White)】......

【Sin Value: 18300】

Special Missions: 【Blessing of the God of Wealth (Collect three First-Class Merits)】【God of Body Shape (Collect First, Second, and Third-Class Merits)】

Jiang Tian lay on his bed with his eyes closed, actually wondering if he would receive two First-Class Merits.

After all, the incident at Yun University was a major achievement—discovering the drug factory last night, especially what he did. Normally, two First-Class Merits shouldn't be a problem.

But he already had one First-Class Merit; would the higher-ups issue two more in quick succession?

Jiang Tian expressed his doubts.

However, looking at the 18,000 points he'd gained, the arrest of Wei Youdao was the biggest contributor, yielding a full 5,000 sin points. That's right, 5,000 from just one person! Jiang Tian had never encountered someone with such a terrifying amount of sin points.

Undoubtedly, the crimes he committed were countless.

"In terms of physique, my innate talent already gives me three times the human limit of strength. If it's red, isn't that at least ten times? What about gold?" Jiang Tian was somewhat tempted.

This, combined with a red Martial Arts Master, would unleash its most formidable power.

At that time, Jiang Tian felt he could truly walk sideways.

"Give it a shot?" Jiang Tian thought to himself.

He directly upgraded his innate talent.

The next moment.

Jiang Tian felt a flame suddenly ignite within his body.

His muscles trembled.

A strange feeling filled him.

[Exceptional Talent (Blue) - Limitless Energy (Red)] (At this moment, you have gained endless source power. As long as you have enough food, your strength will have no upper limit.)

Hiss!!!

That's awesome.

"Brother Jiang, you seem a little different," Zhao Wei, who was accompanying him, said in surprise.

Jiang Tian had asked them to leave yesterday, but the two refused, saying their superiors had ordered them to stay and provide overtime care, and since they were being paid, they couldn't leave.

Last night, Jiang Tian's mother came, and lo and behold, both beds for the caregivers were occupied by the two men, leaving her no choice but to leave.

Li Zijing nodded in agreement; for a moment, they both felt a chill run down their spines, as if they had encountered some monstrous beast.

But Jiang Tian hadn't had a chance to reply.

The next moment, a knock sounded at the door, and before Jiang Tian could turn around, Gao Xiaolong had already pushed the door open and entered.

Jiang Peng, however, didn't follow. Jiang Tian had learned from a phone call yesterday that his father had been working overtime at the city bureau last night, conducting a surprise interrogation of Wei Youdao.

Beside Gao Xiaolong, Jiang Tian noticed that Director Shen was also there.

And next to Shen Han was a woman in a white shirt—yes, a woman.

Around thirty-four or thirty-five years old.

She exuded an aloofness and a judgmental air about her.

“President Bai?” Jiang Tian squinted. He recognized her; this was Bai Qiu, the head of the provincial anti-drug task force.

In his past life, though he was from a lower-ranking position, he had seen her photo at a national awards ceremony for heroes and role models.

That award was for police officers who had sacrificed their lives for meritorious service.

And now, Bai Qiu was scrutinizing him with curious eyes.



Chapter 44 Honors Awarded: Anti-Drug Vanguard


Even the aloof Bai Qiu was shocked by Jiang Tian's achievements, having witnessed them firsthand yesterday. She had even gone to the scene last night to participate in the investigation.

The scene was so horrific that even she was stunned.

"Old Gao, we've conducted a detailed psychological assessment of this comrade to ensure there are no problems, and he's physically healthy with no injuries," the hospital director quickly interjected.

"Good," Gao Xiaolong said, his face beaming with joy.

"Chief Gao, what brings you here?" Jiang Tian asked, somewhat confused, mainly flattered. These were all big shots, truly big shots!

Chief Gao remained silent.

There was also Director Shen, and General Manager Bai.

He was just a lowly narcotics officer; what had he done to deserve this? In his previous life, he hadn't even had the hope of meeting these people.

Chief Gao smiled slightly: "Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​on behalf of the Ministry of Public Security, I'm here to present you with this award. Now, listen to my orders."

At that moment, Mr. and Mrs. Wang Chang carefully approached the ward door.

A deep, steady voice rang out.

"Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​fearless in the face of danger, eradicates evil and upholds the law, strictly enforcing the law against criminals. He always charges ahead when encountering crime, displaying unwavering courage and fully embodying the spirit of the people's police in the new era. His outstanding performance, especially in combating drug traffickers, is particularly noteworthy. To commend his advanced nature and promote righteousness, the Ministry of Public Security has decided to award Comrade Jiang Tian the honorary title of Anti-Drug Vanguard. It is hoped that Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​upon receiving this honor, will cherish this honor, continue his efforts, forge ahead with determination, and achieve even greater success."

*Buzz!*

Li Zijing and Zhao Wei, standing next to Jiang Tian, ​​stared wide-eyed.

From the moment these big shots entered, they had been trembling with fear, but after Gao Xiaolong finished speaking, they instantly erupted.

At that moment, they had only one thought:

What kind of amazing captain are they working for?

"My brother will always be my brother," Zhao Wei hissed.

Anti-Drug Vanguard.

Jiang Tian's eyes lit up.

Although it wasn't a nationally recognized heroic model title across all police systems.

However, the title of "Anti-Drug Vanguard" was definitely a significant affirmation for him.

Moreover, Jiang Tian wasn't in a hurry at all. He had only been back in the police force for two days since his rebirth, and had only been in the force for a month. Normally, he still had a year of internship left, yet he had already been promoted ahead of schedule.

Asking for too much would be counterproductive. Even though Jiang Tian wasn't afraid, a tall building starts from the ground up. In this life, besides wanting to eradicate crime, he also wanted to rise above others.

"Thank you, Chief."

Gao Xiaolong shook his head: "The Ministry of Public Security has been working overtime to process your certificate of honor. It will be delivered to you in a few days, along with your medal of merit."

Jiang Tian was somewhat disappointed.

He had thought he could collect all the blessings from the God of Wealth today.

Actually, besides Li Zijing and Zhao Wei, two people outside the door were also shocked.

"Old Wang, what's the 'Anti-Drug Vanguard' honorary title?" Huang Mei asked somewhat guiltily.

Because she saw that these leaders in white shirts were treating Jiang Tian rather well.

Wang Chang's eyes gleamed with excited delight. "An anti-drug pioneer? No need to ask! He's definitely made a contribution, and with so many leaders involved, it's a huge achievement. His future is incredibly bright. He loves Wang Yifei so much; not only can he use her money for medical treatment, but he might even be able to blackmail her for his bright future. These officials are loaded; we can take a tiny fraction of their wealth."

Not only that, Wang Chang was already thinking about how to quickly get his daughter, Wang Yifei, involved with Jiang Tian. Even if it meant being a liar, they'd stick to it. Then, using Jiang Tian's useless family connections, they could amass a fortune.

Wang Chang seemed to have discovered a path to riches.

"Who are you? What are you doing here?"

Just then, the guard at the door finally spoke up, reprimanding the two.

"We are the in-laws of the patient inside. What kind of attitude is this?" Wang Chang retorted defiantly.

Meanwhile,

Jiang Tian was actually talking to Bai Qiu.

“Comrade Jiang, our team has a case coming up. We’ve received information about a drug deal in the East District of Yunhai. We hope you can come and assist.” Bai Qiu asked calmly.

Actually, Bai Qiu wanted to test the waters to see if it was really as terrifying as the report described.

Mainly, Jiang Tian’s youthful face and the lingering air of youthful naiveté made Bai Qiu hesitate.

“East District?”

Jiang Tian’s expression changed slightly.

He was familiar with that name because a massive, unprecedented case had occurred in the East District before his transmigration, and Bai Qiu had died in that operation.

Due to insufficient preparation, he was captured by drug dealers.

The consequence was that he was ultimately tortured to death by those ruthless drug traffickers.

“No problem.” Jiang Tian nodded without hesitation.

“Good, then we’ll be going now. You can rest today; don’t remember to go back to work.” Gao Xiaolong patted Jiang Tian with satisfaction.

Standing outside the door, Huang Mei was still full of surprise: "Old Wang, why didn't we go in when the leaders were here?"

"Are you stupid? We'll threaten this good-for-nothing to pay Yifei's medical bills first. If he doesn't agree, we'll catch up with those leaders and expose this good-for-nothing's evil deeds." Wang Chang sneered.

So what if he's a second-generation rich kid? They'd experienced this good-for-nothing before; he's not worth mentioning. He believed this approach would work 100%.

So, just as Gao Xiaolong and the others left,

an untimely voice rang out: "Jiang Tian, ​​Yifei's treatment fees are already overdue. What are you doing? The medication has been stopped. If anything happens to Yifei, we won't let you off the hook."

Jiang Tian slowly turned his head. When he saw the two faces, his expression wasn't too surprised.

He thought that in his previous life, these two were even worse than they were now.

Jiang Tian had wanted a divorce many times because he couldn't bear the torment from Wang Yifei and her family.

But later, Wang Yifei used the child to keep them in check. Plus, her family was huge; Wang Yifei alone had three or four uncles and a large group of cousins.

"Hey, what if Xiao Bo married Wang Yifei?"

Jiang Tian looked at them, and suddenly a thought struck him, a vague inspiration striking him: what if he could simply pass on his tragic past life's misery to Xiao Bo?

Jiang Tian couldn't help but shudder at this thought, because he knew Wang Yifei, that despicable woman, all too well.

From what he knew, she and Xiao Bo initially got together for true love and excitement, but ultimately it was all for Xiao Bo's power.

Without Jiang Tian, ​​once the initial novelty wore off, Wang Yifei's wicked side would be fully revealed.

At that point, she would cause Xiao Bo's entire family a living hell, and Xiao Bo's family background was that of a child from a remote mountain village.

Marrying Wang Yifei would be an incredible stroke of good fortune for his entire family.

Thinking this, Jiang Tian feigned surprise and said, "Uncle Wang, we've already broken up, didn't you know?"

In his past life, Wang Chang had forced Jiang Tian to give money to Wang Yifei's younger brother to buy a house and pay a dowry.

But in this life, Jiang Tian really wanted to see how Xiao Bo would react to all of this.

"Break up? Jiang Tian, ​​you dare break up with our Yifei? You good-for-nothing! You used her and then went back on your word! There's no such thing as a free lunch! I'm going to report you! We're going to report you officials for bullying ordinary people like us!" Huang Mei jumped out, crying and making a scene.

Wang Chang frowned and said, "Jiang Tian, ​​you can't do something like this just because Yifei is injured and needs money. If that's the case, I'll go to your superiors. Think about it, your bright future will be ruined. Will your superiors still promote you?"

"With you guys, my bright future will be ruined," Jiang Tian thought coldly, but he shrugged and said, "Uncle Wang, you've got it wrong. Yifei has never let me touch her."

Wang Chang was stunned.

After learning Jiang Tian's identity, he and his wife forced their daughter to agree to his pursuit, assuming they already had a relationship.

"Even if she hasn't touched him, she can't shirk responsibility. Our daughter is too conservative; she wants to save her first time for her wedding night," Wang Chang said, playing the good cop.

Jiang Tian sneered inwardly, "That bitch is conservative? You think too highly of your daughter, don't you? You wouldn't let me touch her, but your daughter went to a hotel with that bastard's child. And the high medical bills weren't because of her leg, but because your daughter was badly injured during her pregnancy. Most of the money went to saving the pregnancy. It's that bastard's child."

After arriving at the hospital, Jiang Tian specifically checked Wang Yifei's medical records and found that the baby was still there. Jiang Tian couldn't help but marvel at how resilient that bastard was, surviving the accident.

"What did you say? I'll fight you, you piece of trash!" Huang Mei went berserk and tried to rush forward.

*Slap!*

Jiang Tian slapped her across the face, slightly raising his hand. The slap sent the fat Huang Mei flying backward, coughing up blood.

"You hit me! Murder! The police murdered me!" Huang Mei cried and screamed.

Even Wang Chang was sweating profusely, unsure how to handle the situation. They realized they had completely lost control of Jiang Tian.

What happened to this child?

"What a waste of money! This good-for-nothing!" Wang Chang felt like killing Wang Yifei.

“Instead of coming to me, you should go find that other man. He slept with Yifei, and he can just deny it. Besides, I have no relationship with Yifei, so asking me for money would be extortion. But asking the child's father is fine. If you don't believe me, I can do a DNA test,” Jiang Tian suggested.

Huang Mei stopped crying, forgetting about being beaten, and Wang Chang's eyes brightened.

As long as he could get something, money, he didn't care about Jiang Tian; he could find someone else. Besides, that good-for-nothing had abandoned Jiang Tian, ​​so he must have found someone better.

Better, right? That means more money?

Hiss!!!

“Who is that man? Tell me quickly!” Wang Chang's eyes were red.

“That other man is called Xiao Bo. He's also a local from Yunhai, but he's currently renting in Shengxiang Community. By the way, he and I are both narcotics officers, but we're suspended now. He's probably at home,” Jiang Tian kindly revealed.

Wang Chang and Huang Mei didn't even say a word; they practically ran out of the ward.

Jiang Tian felt relieved at that moment, but he could already foresee that Xiao Bo was going to suffer terribly.

Good heavens, tens or hundreds of thousands of yuan! He wondered if Xiao Bo's parents, with their land, could afford that.

Inside the room, only Jiang Tian, ​​who had been watching the spectacle, and the stunned Li Zijing and Zhao Wei remained.

They needed time to process this explosive news.

"That beast Xiao Bo, is he even human?" Zhao Wei's worldview was shaken. He already knew Xiao Bo was a beast, but he hadn't expected him to be this bad.

"Wang Yifei isn't any better. I used to envy how good you were to Yifei, Captain Jiang, but you wouldn't even let me touch her," Li Zijing chimed in, indignant.

"Sister Li, if I'm good to you, you'll let me touch you?" Jiang Tian asked in surprise.

"Ptooey, ptooey, ptooey..." Li Zijing rolled her eyes, pretending to be disgusted, but when she turned her head, no one noticed that Li Zijing's face was slightly red.



Chapter 45: Eating at a roadside stall, and credit comes knocking on your door?


Yunshan Prison...

It's arguably the most famous prison in the entire Yunhai Province.

Because those imprisoned here are either life-sentenced or near-execution criminals—basically, every one of them faces at least several decades of life imprisonment before they can be released.

Such an important prison naturally has extremely stringent security measures.

Under normal circumstances, it's absolutely impossible for the inmates here to escape, not even in their lifetime. But the worst thing can happen.

That day, a light drizzle was falling.

At dusk.

A deafening siren blared throughout Yunshan Prison, shattering all tranquility.

From the warden down to the lowest guard, everyone was in an uproar.

Because someone had escaped from Yunhai Prison.

Jiang Tian's memories from his previous life were correct.

During the day, after Jiang Tian was discharged from the hospital, he and two teammates tried their luck on the streets. Frankly, their luck wasn't great; after wandering around for a while, Jiang Tian didn't find any major criminals.

At most, they caught three or four petty thieves, which was insignificant to Jiang Tian.

But this completely thrilled Zhao Wei and Li Zijing.

In the evening, Jiang Tian was having barbecue with the two of them. Just now, they had handed over a petty thief who had stolen a mobile phone.

Jiang Tian was somewhat disheartened. What a joke! What kind of ability did he have? A perpetual motion machine? Did he want to be a drug dealer? After wandering the streets for most of the day, all he caught were a few petty thieves. Jiang Tian felt this was an insult to his scanning radar.

Jiang Tian fell into deep thought. He felt that his approach might be flawed.

"Captain Jiang, damn, this is so satisfying! We solved three cases today, saving people's property!" Zhao Wei exclaimed, his face beaming with satisfaction.

Jiang Tian sighed. This silly kid, so easily pleased.

"Delicious, delicious."

Hearing the sounds of chewing beside him, Jiang Tian turned to look at Li Zijing. Her mouth was greasy from eating. Honestly, if you hadn't seen it with your own eyes, you'd hardly believe that such a pure and beautiful girl could eat barbecue like this.

"Boss, another one! Waaah! Today, Brother Jiang is treating, we have to feast!" Li Zijing said, raising her small hand.

"You'll stuff yourself to death." Jiang Tian downed a bottle of beer in one gulp. For his physique, a bottle of beer was nothing.

But as soon as he put down his glass,

Jiang Tian felt his vision dim. Someone was standing behind him, seemingly out of nowhere.

Jiang Tian was about to put down the bottle when he felt a hand on his shoulder, accompanied by a voice slurred with alcohol: "Beautiful lady, what's the point of drinking with two thugs? Our table needs someone, come have a drink with us."

As he spoke, the arm tightened, as if trying to throw Jiang Tian aside.

Jiang Tian then looked up and saw the speaker. His arms were tattooed with dragons and tigers, and he was indeed quite large.

"From the underworld?" Jiang Tian asked, surprised.

"Within dozens of miles of Gangzi Ridge, you can ask around. My older brother is called Brother Dog. Brother Dog will treat the beautiful lady to a drink. As for you, you're not needed. Go wherever you want. My brother has no interest in drinking with two greyhounds," the tattooed man said arrogantly.

Jiang Tian slammed his glass down on the table.

Following his gaze, sure enough, a group of three or four people were sitting at the barbecue table nearby.

The leader was a young man in his early twenties. When he saw Jiang Tian looking over, he raised his glass and smiled slightly.

This attitude showed that he hadn't taken them seriously at all.

Forced a woman's abduction?

Jiang Tian hadn't noticed before, but he subconsciously glanced at the radar.

[Jianghu Name (Brother Dog) Sin Value 1900 points]

Jiang Tian's spirits lifted, because this sin value was no less than that of the drug dealer Wei Rong.

Good heavens.

Jiang Tian hadn't expected that after searching for so long without success, he'd found it.

The moment he finished a barbecue, it delivered itself right to his doorstep.

Of course, on the other hand, Jiang Tian wasn't surprised. This kind of situation was common, not just around the millennium, but even a decade or two later.

Where there is light in the world, there is darkness.

And this practiced manner, especially the way the people eating barbecue around him turned their heads, saw it was Brother Gou, and then all turned back as if they hadn't seen him, Jiang Tian knew this definitely wasn't the first time.

"Hmm?" At this moment, the tattooed man who had tried to forcefully throw Jiang Tian aside looked confused.

Because even with his strength, Jiang Tian's seemingly frail body hadn't budgeed an inch.

"Looks like 'Thin Dog' isn't me, it's you. Is that all the strength you've got?" Jiang Tian grabbed the tattooed man with one hand.

"You dare fight back?" The tattooed man was shocked. Having roamed dozens of miles of Gangzi Ridge, following the most famous boss, when had he ever encountered anyone who dared to defy him?

"This kid's in trouble."

"Being targeted by Brother Dog never ends well!"

"Yeah, in the end, he might even be tortured to the point of wishing he were dead. This kid's in trouble."

The people eating barbecue were even more shocked by this scene.

Such a scene also brought a heavy feeling to Jiang Tian, ​​because people had seen it all before, and had even become accustomed to it.

It also represented the crisis and chaos in society.

At this moment, Brother Dog, not far away, seemed somewhat surprised, a slight smirk playing on his lips as he said calmly, "Interesting."

"Damn, trying to show off in front of Captain Jiang?" Zhao Wei gasped.

Two hundred drug dealers had been killed by Brother Jiang, and a bunch of thugs and gangsters dared to be so arrogant?

"Given a chance, he didn't use it."

Jiang Tian glanced at the scanning radar.

[August 2001, assisted Brother Dog in forcing women, and even beat a man to death... Crime value 200]

Not the main culprit, mostly an accomplice.

But these are absolutely heinous crimes, punishable by death.

“Watch closely, we can’t show mercy to these social scum,” Jiang Tian said to the two men.

The next moment.

*Thud!*

Jiang Tian grabbed the man’s wrist, and as the tattooed man leaned forward, his knee slammed into the tattooed man’s groin.

Swift, accurate, and ruthless. While not a killing technique, it was absolutely capable of incapacitating the opponent with a single blow.

*Crack!!!*

The sound of bone cracking could even be heard from that knee strike, let alone in that vital area.

*Hiss!!!*

Zhao Wei gasped, instinctively clamping his legs together. He looked up at the previously arrogant tattooed man, now curled up like a shrimp, rolling on the ground, making hoarse noises, his eyes almost bulging out.

Too ruthless.

But then Zhao Wei remembered Jiang Tian's methods for taking down those drug dealers. Oh, then it's alright.

*Bang!!!*

"Kid, you've got guts. Do you know who I am?"

Brother Gou slammed his fist on the table, stood up, and grinned coldly as he looked up.

But the next moment, large beads of sweat dripped from Brother Gou's forehead.

A dark gun barrel was pointed at his head.

Dog Brother had only seen Li Zijing's beauty and harbored thoughts of getting close to her, but who knew he'd run into such a ruthless person?

A gun?

Dog Brother had a gun too, but he wouldn't dare show it so openly.

Jiang Tian smiled, looking at Dog Brother's wicked smile.

*Slap!*

Jiang Tian slapped him hard across the face. Blood shot from Dog Brother's mouth, and his previous calm and collected expression vanished instantly.

"Dog Brother, is it? Let's hear you bark," Jiang Tian said.

"Don't push your luck. Everyone here knows my name, Dog Brother," Dog Brother said viciously, determined to kill them when he got the chance.

But the next moment...

Bang!!!

It wasn't Jiang Tian who struck, but Li Zijing, who kicked Dog Brother in the groin: "What kind of bullshit Dog Brother is this? From now on, call me Sister Dog."

If it weren't for Li Zijing, and if Jiang Tian hadn't been there, any other woman without power or influence, Li Zijing couldn't even imagine what would have happened to her if she'd been targeted by someone like this.

Dog Brother doubled over, wracked with pain, feeling as if his body was shattered, yet also as if it could still be salvaged.

But before Dog Brother could even cover his groin with his hands, he heard a snapping sound.

Dog Brother was completely bewildered. My hands? Who tied my hands? Hey, why are there a pair of silver bracelets on my wrists?

When he looked up, Jiang Tian was holding identification. "We're from the Municipal Public Security Bureau. You're suspected of assaulting a police officer and obstructing official business. Come in."

"The Municipal Public Security Bureau, the police?" Dog Brother was dumbfounded.

Meanwhile, Jiang Tian stared at the bright red dot in his mind.

This belonged to Dog Brother.

Furthermore, Jiang Tian had also figured out a pattern: a crime value of 1,900 could never be achieved solely through organized crime and intimidation.

By extension, Jiang Tian had discovered a pattern among various types of crime: drug trafficking was the most prevalent.

Gambling, prostitution, drugs, and organized crime are inextricably linked, but drug trafficking, among all criminal activities, had the highest crime value and was also the most harmful.



Chapter 46 Locking the Mountain to Capture People: This is a Terrifying Being


"Run!"

Besides the tattooed man, three of Dog Brother's men turned to flee.

Especially when dealing with criminals, these damned beasts shouldn't be treated kindly.

Yesterday, I went to Yunnan University and didn't get any credit. If it weren't for Jiang Tian, ​​even Principal Ying might have been killed; that would have been a complete disaster.

Before transmigrating, he followed Xiao Bo. Back then, Xiao Bo taught him never to engage in any personal relationships within the police force, and especially not to associate with those people. He should focus on his own cases. Having just joined the police force, he believed him and actually did just that.

But that beast Xiao Bo secretly spread rumors and slander behind his back, using him as fodder for networking.

This made his career in the police force extremely difficult. Psychologically speaking, he trusted Xiao Bo, the only one who treated him well, even more.

Thinking back, there was a reason why Xiao Bo had been so rude before. Jiang Tian remembered that when he first joined the police force, Yu Hui greeted him, but Jiang Tian didn't even acknowledge her.

Thinking about this, Jiang Tian really wanted to slap himself.

Soon, Yu Hui started searching the public security system on the computer. What? No name?

The photo taken when he entered was directly uploaded to the computer for automatic comparison, with an accuracy rate of 99%.

“His registered residence is in Zhangjia Village, Dongcheng District. His name is Zhang Jiagou. He owns two nightclubs, both in Dongcheng District, one in the city center and the other in the south. At that moment, Jiang Tian seemed to realize that he had forgotten something important.

Yu Hui’s face was serious. After hanging up the phone, Yu Hui looked at Jiang Tian, ​​about to say something…

Jiang Tian's phone rang.

Taking out his phone, Jiang Tian realized it was Song Liguo calling. The call connected, and Song Liguo's voice immediately came through: "During the renovation work at Yunshan Prison today, a drug dealer who had been sentenced to death was supposed to be executed, but due to unresolved information, the execution was postponed. However, he managed to steal a guard's gun and escape during the renovation. You'll need to take a small team and patrol all areas near Yunshan. I'll send you photos later."

Hiss!!!

Jiang Tian's expression changed drastically. Only then did he remember something important he had forgotten.

That's right, it was Mu Ya.

To be honest, in the past two days, since his rebirth, Jiang Tian had been eager to take action and make a difference, but so much had happened that he had forgotten this crucial matter.

“According to my past life, if Xiao Bo had truly saved Mu Ya, even if everything were said to be utterly worthless, even if Xiao Bo were a complete scoundrel, it would absolutely not change Mu Ya's mind. She would be devoted to Xiao Bo for life, with no possibility of change. With Mu Ya's family and her father's help, Xiao Bo could definitely be brought back to life, and might even return to his former position of harming people.”

Jiang Tian's brow furrowed instantly at this thought. Damn it, if Xiao Bo really came back to life, and even had a powerful backer in the future, Jiang Tian would be furious enough to vomit blood.

“Damn it, how could I forget something so important?” Jiang Tian slapped his forehead.

“But we must be careful. That drug dealer is extremely skilled. He studied Krav Maga and is very powerful. He claimed to have stolen a gun and escaped, but in reality, he killed two prison guards instantly.” Song Liguo said seriously.

Jiang Tian frowned slightly. This incident was indeed not as simple as he had understood it in his past life.

In his past life, Jiang Tian only knew that, according to Xiao Bo's boasts, he had saved Mu Ya and apprehended the escaped drug dealer, which was why Mu Ya was so devoted to him.

But now it seems the matter is far more complex than that.

Because he remembered clearly that shortly after this operation in his previous life, the Ministry of Public Security commended several joint operation units, and this commendation felt more like a posthumous honor.

In other words, many people sacrificed their lives in this operation.

Therefore, Xiao Bo was definitely concealing the situation at the time, and it was probably not as he described.

"If that's the case, it means this operation was terrifying."

Even though Jiang Tian was mentally prepared, he still felt a sense of suffocation when he stepped out of the door fully armed in his police uniform.

Yunshan Prison was located in the suburbs.

But even though the city center was almost entirely under martial law, police had been deployed at every intersection.

Especially as Jiang Tian headed towards the mountain he remembered, the closer he got, the more checkpoints he found.

"Are they crazy? One drug dealer escaped, and they're making such a fuss?" Zhao Wei found it hard to understand.

Even when they passed by, they had to open the car doors and the passenger compartment for inspection.

"These are official police cars, and they're being checked!"

"This isn't your average drug dealer. Even if it were, an escape from prison would be a province-wide sensation," Li Zijing explained.

"Shawshank?"

Zhao Wei stared dumbfounded at Jiang Tian, ​​speechless, unable to refute him.

Jiang Tian shook his head, his gaze distant. In his previous life, he was already suspended at home reflecting on his actions at this point. The case hadn't had many flaws afterward, and Jiang Tian didn't even know exactly where the drug dealer was caught.

Jiang Tian wasn't particularly anxious, because the escaped drug dealers would inevitably leave clues; otherwise, Xiao Bo, in his previous life, wouldn't have had the opportunity to participate if he were in the police force at this time.

Given Mu Ya's conservative nature, she would absolutely not give Xiao Bo any further opportunities before giving her approval.

Sure enough.

A moment later, Jiang Tian's chest walkie-talkie crackled to life.

"Attention, everyone! Assemble! Three minutes ago, villagers reported seeing someone resembling a fugitive who had been to Baishan. Everyone, assemble at Baishan immediately! Seal off all exits and main roads of Baishan! Block off the entire mountain!"

Others didn't recognize the voice, but Jiang Tian, ​​who had switched to the mission intercom, recognized it: Shen Han.

It was Shen Han.

Shen Han personally taking command was enough to prove Jiang Tian's deduction was absolutely correct.

"City Anti-Drug Squad received this, providing support."



Chapter 47: Heavy Losses, a Series of Devastating News


"Brother Jiang, it's time to prove myself!" Zhao Wei said, his face flushed.

Especially the cases Jiang Tian had solved in the past two days—they had practically made Li Zijing and Zhao Wei idolize him. They would believe him even if he claimed to be omnipotent.

"What are you looking at? This case isn't that simple," Jiang Tian said irritably.

"A drug dealer? We've deployed over a thousand armed police officers and officers from the provincial and municipal bureaus. What trouble can he possibly cause?" Zhao Wei, holding his gun, showed no sign of tension.

Jiang Tian glanced at Zhao Wei but said nothing. If Jiang Tian hadn't experienced the hardships of his past life, he would have thought much like Zhao Wei, perhaps even more unrestrained.

But after more than a decade of struggling at the bottom of society, Jiang Tian had developed a maturity beyond his years.

"Attention all personnel! Emergency alert! Three armed police officers have encountered an accident in Baishan. The drug traffickers are ruthless and may even be disguising themselves as armed police. All personnel, conduct a thorough search in groups of two or more. If found, kill on sight. Warning: the perpetrator is extremely dangerous; be careful."

Just as Jiang Tian arrived at the foot of Baishan, an urgent voice came through the walkie-talkie.

This caused Zhao Wei and Li Zijing in the car to exchange pale glances.

This didn't seem like an ordinary drug trafficker.
