Having already possessed the "Martial Arts Master" entry, Jiang Tian knew the principles and power of this famous fighting style.

Of course, the Krav Maga that was actually practiced was far inferior to what Jiang Tian knew. The Krav Maga in Jiang Tian's mind, also known as Ancient Krav Maga, was even stronger and more terrifying than the censored version. However, Jiang Tian was too lazy to use it; his "Martial Arts Master" entry granted him a thorough understanding of almost all the world's fighting styles.

Jiang Tian didn't abandon them. In the current situation, going up the mountain alone meant he could be shot by friendly forces at any moment.

"Brother Jiang, the city police and even the provincial police must have all rushed here, and the entire Yunhai Armed Police must have been mobilized," Zhao Wei couldn't help but exclaim along the way.

Jiang Tian frowned deeply.

His mind was constantly processing the scanning radar.

Baishan was vast, a mountain range stretching for tens of kilometers, making the search for drug dealers incredibly difficult.

Furthermore, given the criminals' vigilance, even with a kilometer-long scanning radar, Jiang Tian didn't know how long it would take to scan alone.

Thinking of this, Jiang Tian felt anxious.

He feared that his presence might cause something to happen to Mu Ya, or that, like in his previous life, Xiao Bo might stage a stunning comeback.

Putting aside Mu Ya's beauty, and the reasons Jiang Tian hadn't taken a liking to her, Jiang Tian absolutely wouldn't allow Xiao Bo to successfully latch onto her.

Xiao Bo was only a perfect match for that bitch Wang Yifei.

"Does anyone know of a good spot with a view around here?" Jiang Tian asked.

"I know, a few kilometers ahead there's a path up a hill, halfway up the southern slope of Baishan Mountain, there's a cliff, from there you can see the continuous mountain range and half a sea of ​​clouds," Li Zijing immediately raised her hand.

Jiang Tian looked puzzled, seemingly not understanding how Li Zijing knew.

After a pause, Li Zijing explained, "I used to sometimes like to come here to climb the mountain and enjoy the scenery, and get some fresh air. Brother Jiang, what's up, you want to see the scenery?"

"Attention, two armed police officers have been killed in the eastern part of Baishan Mountain. Attention, everyone, everyone surround the eastern side!" Shen Ting's voice came through the walkie-talkie.

"The eastern side?"

Hiss!!!

Jiang Tian gasped, instantly realizing he had discovered his opponent.

Now Jiang Tian faced only two choices: the east, where the new trail had been discovered, or the southern mountainside.

Which place should he choose?

If he chose the east, it might be a diversionary tactic by the culprit, allowing them to escape from Baishan.

If such a culprit escaped, Jiang Tian's scalp tingled. With such skill, once they crossed the border, they would be impossible to catch.

This would be a disgrace to the entire Yunhai.

Choosing the southern mountainside, however, could result in Mu Ya's sacrifice due to the butterfly effect, because Mu Ya might not even be on the mountainside.

And getting to the southern mountainside would take at least an hour and a half of mountain climbing.

Bang...

Provincial Headquarters.

Brightly lit, but the atmosphere instantly exploded.

Such skill—this was an unprecedentedly dangerous individual.

Fighting evil inherently involves facing terrifying dangers at any moment.

No one knows what deadly weapon the criminal will pull out next.

No one knows when sacrifice will occur.

But they couldn't accept that this prison break had already resulted in seven deaths and injuries.

This is a major event.

Another major event.

Although Gao Xiaolong came here to do something, he's only slept a few hours in the past three days.

Don't be fooled by Jiang Tian's seemingly relaxed demeanor after solving the case; the cleanup work for those drug dealers he exposed is the most extensive and terrifying.

Check online/offline status.

And the investigation into the drug dealers and users involved along this route must all be found and dealt with.

"The handcuffs and leg irons don't have keys, but he found a large pair of steel-cutting shears from the construction team and cut the shackles to escape," said Chief Sun of the Criminal Investigation Department with a helpless bitter smile.

"The perpetrator is too ruthless and too capable. Nighttime is like a fish in water for him. No matter how many of us go in, it won't be enough for him to hunt down. The discovery of the body in the east could very well be a diversionary tactic. He's not only ruthless but also intelligent," Gao Xiaolong said through gritted teeth.

This was the only solution Gao Xiaolong could think of.

And that's not all. Among those who sacrificed their lives, some had lost their walkie-talkies, meaning the perpetrators could still receive their orders.

A moment later, General Gao, leaning on the table, added, "By the way, pass down the order: whoever catches the perpetrator will be awarded a first-class merit and a nationwide A-level reward of 300,000 yuan."

Soon, the order was issued to all parts of the province. The cover had been laid too big; it couldn't be kept hidden any longer.

Just as the order to seal off the mountain was being given,

at the foot of the mountain, Xiao Bo had already found his way there.

He couldn't contact her.

On his phone was the last message Mu Ya had sent him the previous night.

"Let me go out tomorrow and carefully examine our relationship. Don't look for me. I'll contact you again when I've thought it through."

This was the text message Mu Ya sent to Xiao Bo, and then she blocked him.

Xiao Bo was terrified. He immediately went to Mu Ya's house and learned from her family that Mu Ya had gone camping.

Of course, until now, Mu Ya's family's change of attitude towards Xiao Bo was due to their ignorance of the underlying problems and circumstances, which is why they revealed the true purpose to Mu Ya.

Xiao Bo's spirits lifted.

He clearly remembered that Mu Ya had once said she longed to visit Baishan and see its scenery.

If that were all, Xiao Bo wouldn't have been bothered.

The key was that this afternoon, Sun Haibo had called him, informing him of a major operation across the province.

A death row inmate from Yunshan Prison had escaped; he was a skilled criminal, and they hadn't caught him yet. It seemed he had fled to Baishan.

Of course, Sun Haibo wasn't telling Xiao Bo this hoping he would capture the criminal—that was impossible.

Chapter 48: Discovering Clues, Rewriting History


Even though Xiao Bo didn't want to admit it, he had to acknowledge that since the incident at the police station, the persona he had cultivated in front of Mu Ya had completely collapsed.

Pursuing Mu Ya, this wealthy and beautiful second-generation heiress, was becoming increasingly distant, and so was his chance to change his fate.

Especially with that good-for-nothing Jiang Tian now opposing him, Xiao Bo was desperate. He knew clearly that for someone from a mountain village like himself, climbing the social ladder was only possible through marriage.

Now, the opportunity had arrived.

Seizing this opportunity would make Mu Ya completely fall for him.

Then, with Mu Ya's family background, Xiao Bo could achieve a meteoric rise to power.

Moreover, he had a significant advantage over everyone else: no one knew Mu Ya was in Baishan, no one knew she was in danger, and no one knew better than him. Finding Mu Ya now and protecting her away from Baishan would ensure success.

Therefore, Xiao Bo dared not delay. If someone else found her first, it would be all over.

And just as Xiao Bo was heading up the mountain...

Jiang Tian didn't delay and ordered, "You two go check the trail of the heroes who sacrificed themselves in Dongshan."

"What about you, Brother Jiang?" Zhao Wei asked.

Jiang Tian frowned and said, "I'll go check the south. The south is near the border. I suspect he might be using a diversionary tactic, or maybe I'm overthinking it, but whatever you do, go check it out first and report back."

That was indeed the case.

Jiang Tian's main priority now was to find Mu Ya as quickly as possible.

"But if you're alone and encounter someone, you might be misunderstood," Li Zijing thoughtfully added.

Now everyone's in small groups, and acting alone could easily lead to being mistaken for a drug dealer and indiscriminately shot dead.

"The situation is urgent, and our city bureau's Chief Song has already led a team to the south. Go there and keep in touch via walkie-talkie," Jiang Tian explained.

He was also afraid of making a mistake.

However, unsure of the direction, he knew that with them around, he could quickly ascertain the situation to the east. The only problem was that Jiang Tian had too little useful information.

After the two left, Jiang Tian didn't waste any time, as every second could potentially endanger Mu Ya.

More importantly, every moment of delay increased the chances of these heroic police officers encountering danger.

Having honed his skills at the grassroots level for over a decade in his previous life, Jiang Tian understood all too well how difficult the work of a low-level police officer was.

Especially in this era, when investigating cases, anyone with even a little bit of organized crime was practically armed with a large megaphone.

“Stop! Move again or I’ll shoot!”

Jiang Tian was running through the dense forest when suddenly, a hurried voice rang out.

A powerful flashlight beam shone down, and although the reflection was blinding, Jiang Tian squinted and managed to make out the thermal image of the person's face.

“Don’t shoot, we’re on the same side.” Jiang Tian sighed helplessly.

He ran quickly through the dense forest, not taking Zhao Wei with him to save time. Normally, he wouldn't be detected, but with thermal imaging, he was too conspicuous in the darkness.

"Announce your badge number, and throw out your identification."

Jiang Tian reluctantly complied, and a series of bright lights flashed, causing him to squint.

Soon, one of the men stepped forward, bent down to examine Jiang Tian's identification, and then carefully scrutinized his face before turning back to say, "Captain, the identification is genuine."

The bright flashlights finally moved away from Jiang Tian's face, and everyone lowered their guns.

The group surrounding Jiang Tian, ​​who was leading the group, finally emerged.

A man in his thirties extended his hand and said, "I'm Song Han, the captain of the Narcotics Control Team from the Dongcheng Branch. Brother, why are you alone? Where are you from?"

"Jiang Tian, ​​from the Municipal Narcotics Control Detachment. My teammates are waiting for me up ahead," Jiang Tian replied casually.

"That criminal is extremely dangerous, brother. Be careful. Find your teammates and get back down quickly. We've been ordered to get down the mountain as soon as possible." Hearing that his teammates were there, Song Han waved goodbye with great enthusiasm.

That's why, although Jiang Tian's name had been revealed and he had done something significant these past few days, his subordinates didn't know.

And it was even less likely to spread widely, because this was a narcotics officer.

The officers at the branch office knew the city bureau had a hero, a hero who had repeatedly performed outstanding service, but they didn't know his name. Spreading his name would almost certainly result in retaliation against him, as a narcotics officer.

Unlike criminal investigators who don't harm family members, drug traffickers almost always commit organized and premeditated crimes.

The intricate web of relationships means there will always be those who slip through the net and seek revenge.

Behind every regulation lies a bloody lesson.

Jiang Tian ran swiftly, at a rapid pace.

A normal person would take at least one or two hours to jog, especially in the dark, but Jiang Tian reached his destination halfway up Nanshan Mountain in just half an hour.

"Mu Ya is indeed here."

Jiang Tian instantly breathed a sigh of relief, his face showing complete relief. He was truly afraid that his actions had created a butterfly effect, leading to an accident for Mu Ya.

Or that Xiao Bo would appear, making all his revenge a joke.

Fortunately, it wasn't too late.

As soon as he looked, Mu Ya was squatting outside the tent, starting a fire with a portable outdoor stove. But the amount of food inside made Jiang Tian's pupils contract—there was just too much.

Mu Ya was 1.7 meters tall but weighed only a little over 100 pounds; there was no way she could have prepared such a large pot of food.

Jiang Tian subconsciously glanced at the scanning radar and saw a bright, scarlet dot glowing intensely.

A scarlet, almost blackish red dot, inside the tent.

"Damn, I almost let my guard down."

Jiang Tian was startled. It was indeed here.

Then Jiang Tian looked more closely and, sure enough, below a gap in the tent, a dark gun barrel was pointed outwards.

He'd been taken hostage.

Jiang Tian's heart tightened, and his eagerness to obtain the criminal investigation terminology intensified.

His only weakness was the lack of criminal investigation skills. Luckily, he had the scanning radar; otherwise, walking out openly would likely have resulted in immediate execution.

Now, Jiang Tian was intently watching the drug dealers hidden in the tent, which likely meant they possessed criminal investigation skills.

Jiang Tian slowly drew his pistol from his waist, preparing to fire into the tent.

But just then…

Bang!!!

A muffled gunshot suddenly rang out.



Chapter 49 Instant Kill, is that all?


A deadly sense of crisis instantly surged into Jiang Tian's heart, causing him to instinctively dodge. A bullet hole instantly appeared in the tree beside him.

"I've been discovered?" Jiang Tian was startled, but not entirely certain, because he had arrived stealthily.

To be honest, this was the first time he had encountered a true expert, and without a doubt, this drug dealer was a master among masters.

Mu Ya was also frozen in place, her eyes struggling to turn towards the bushes.

"Don't hide, I see you. Look at your head!" a voice came from inside the tent.

Jiang Tian looked up and saw a colorful ribbon above him.

A trap, or perhaps counter-surveillance?

Jiang Tian had to admire her; ultimately, it came down to a lack of criminal investigation awareness.

Criminal investigation includes both reconnaissance and counter-surveillance.

"So strong, it'll probably reveal some investigative keywords, right?" Jiang Tian's eyes brightened.

After all, trying to extract criminal investigation information from a bunch of criminals is utter nonsense, and criminal investigators don't commit crimes, so they certainly can't.

"Kidnapping a woman is nothing. You can run away, why hurt an innocent woman?"

Jiang Tian's voice came calmly.

At that moment.

Mu Ya, who was cooking, froze instantly.

Because she recognized that voice.

She had heard it just yesterday, a voice she remembered clearly—Jiang Tian, ​​it was Jiang Tian.

Heaven knows how desperate Mu Ya felt.

She had only gone camping to calm herself down, but who knew she would encounter a death row inmate who had escaped and kidnapped her to cook? The despair, loneliness, and helplessness she felt were almost driving Mu Ya to the brink of madness.

And then, in this situation, a familiar person appeared.

It was like a ray of light.

Appearing before Mu Ya's eyes.

Seeing the situation before him, Jiang Tian instantly understood. In his past life, Xiao Bo had probably appeared before Mu Ya under similar circumstances.

How he survived was unknown, but he was definitely no match for this drug dealer.

Luck allowed Xiao Bo to survive, and he completely won Mu Ya's heart.

So what about him now?

Of course, Jiang Tian knew even more that with his intervention, Xiao Bo had no chance left.

Jiang Tian had completely extinguished Xiao Bo's hopes this time.

If that wasn't enough, sorry, Jiang Tian had a photograph in his pocket.

"I didn't want to kill anyone, you forced me. I didn't hurt this woman, I just wanted her to cook me a meal. You forced me to do this. If I don't kill her, I'll die," a voice continued from inside the tent.

The first ironclad rule of the police force: never believe a criminal's feigned helplessness.

"Come out now, don't report this. I won't hurt you. I'll leave after I eat. If you don't come out, I'll kill her," the drug dealer continued.

Hearing this, Jiang Tian understood that this drug dealer might still have a conscience.

In his past life, it was precisely because Xiao Bo did this that he ultimately won the heart of the beauty and survived.

However, Jiang Tian couldn't place his hopes on a drug dealer.

"You've already killed seven armed police officers, your crimes are heinous, won't you repent?" Jiang Tian rebuked.

Seven.

Mu Ya's face turned pale.

This drug dealer, who had slaughtered seven armed police officers, was far more terrifying than he had imagined.

“I’ll count to three, and you come out, or I’ll kill her,” the drug dealer shouted without response.

Jiang Tian emerged from the bushes.

He came out?

Mu Ya’s eyes trembled, and two streams of tears flowed from them: “You…you shouldn’t have come out.”

At that moment, seeing Jiang Tian emerge from the bushes was like a beam of light piercing her heart.

What trembled her even more was that Jiang Tian, ​​knowing full well that this man was a ruthless killer, had still stepped out of his safe hiding place for her safety.

“You cops are always so stupid. Don’t worry, I said I won’t kill you, and I won’t.” The drug dealer, seeing Jiang Tian emerge with his hands raised, breathed a sigh of relief and also stepped out of the tent.

Jiang Tian squinted, noticing a rock that had appeared inside the tent; he had just been hiding behind it.

Jiang Tian felt a surge of relief; thankfully, he hadn't acted rashly and fired, otherwise Mu Ya would likely be dead.

Although he wanted revenge on Xiao Bo,

Jiang Tian's feelings for Mu Ya were genuine. In his past life, Mu Ya had truly been a ray of light in his eyes.

A light completely opposite to the beast Xiao Bo.

In his past life, Mu Ya knew Xiao Bo was a beast, and despite enduring immense suffering, she remained bound to him for life.

Besides seeking revenge on Xiao Bo, he also wanted to help Mu Ya.

Jiang Tian avoided looking at Mu Ya to prevent the drug dealers from noticing anything amiss. Turning to the drug dealers, he carefully examined them, having seen their files.

Zhou Zicheng, twenty-eight years old.

He went abroad at sixteen, suspected of joining a secret organization and receiving special training. He had been caught in a trap while carrying drugs, resulting in the deaths of three anti-drug officers.

They hadn't executed him outright; they wanted to interrogate him to learn about the mysterious organization behind him.

At first glance, Jiang Tian exuded a powerful, muscular physique, the kind that seemed to walk with an air of authority.

Zhou Zicheng, looking at Jiang Tian's youthful face, breathed a sigh of relief: "Take the rope and tie yourself up."

As he spoke, Zhou Zicheng lowered his guard, and when he was three or four meters away from Jiang Tian, ​​he pointed a gun at him with one hand and threw the rope over with the other.

Three or four meters.

Even with Zhou Zicheng's relaxed guard, it was still a completely safe distance, at least for an ordinary person.

But for Jiang Tian...

Do you understand the concept of strength many times greater than the limits of the human body?

Jiang Tian narrowed his eyes, watching the moment his opponent made his move.

To be honest...

In that instant...

Mu Ya, who had been intently watching Jiang Tian, ​​didn't see clearly how he made his move.

She only saw Jiang Tian, ​​who had been standing still, disappear the next moment, until her retinas caught up with him.

At that moment, Jiang Tian had already raised the criminal's gun-wielding hand with one hand.

With the other hand, he punched Zhou Zicheng in the temple.

A normal person would have been instantly killed by this punch.

But not Zhou Zicheng. He tried to block with one hand, but the moment he made contact...

Boom!!!

Zhou Zicheng instantly crashed heavily to the ground.

He coughed up a mouthful of blood, and tried to get up.

But after several attempts, his arms still trembled.

He tried several times to turn his head, but couldn't. The fact that he hadn't lost consciousness was a testament to his terrifying physical abilities.

"You..." Zhou Zicheng's eyes widened.

But the next moment.

Boom!!!

Jiang Tian kicked Zhou Zicheng in the chest.

Crack!!!

The sound of his sternum breaking echoed as Zhou Zicheng flew more than ten meters through the air, crashing heavily to the ground with a thud. His body twitched slightly before finally falling silent.

Dead. Just like that, dead.

Jiang Tian cracked his knuckles. His consistent approach to these criminals was to eliminate them completely.

Otherwise, things would turn out like this, with endless trouble. Jiang Tian wouldn't leave himself any future problems. While he himself wasn't afraid, given Zhou Zicheng's skills, Jiang Tian didn't even want to think about what would happen if Zhou Zicheng attacked his family.

At that moment, a white light flashed on Zhou Zicheng's corpse.

"There's an entry." Jiang Tian's eyes lit up.

Jiang Tian rubbed his hands together and approached Zhou Zicheng. Upon seeing the entry, Jiang Tian was instantly overjoyed.

It was it.

【Agile Detection (White)】

After so long, Jiang Tian had finally obtained a criminal investigation-related entry.

Detection, also known as investigation, is a type of criminal investigation.

For example, detecting signs of crime, traces of crime, accurately reconstructing the scene and past events at the scene, etc.

This was Jiang Tian's biggest gain this time. Without further ado, Jiang Tian immediately clicked on the hunting gear.

"Are you...are you alright?"

But at this moment, Mu Ya was staring at Jiang Tian, ​​unconsciously lost in thought, until Jiang Tian's voice rang out, and Mu Ya finally snapped back to reality.

In her haste, Mu Ya hurriedly stood up, "Thank you, thank you."

Under the bright moonlight, Jiang Tian's face was clearly visible, his features sharp, exuding a dignified and upright air.

And just now, he had almost instantly killed the vicious drug dealer.

Mu Ya immediately thought of Xiao Bo.

Useless?

Trash?

A useless burden?

And a rich second-generation who posed a danger to her?

She laughed.

Mu Ya suddenly understood. Was he really useless?

"It must be because Xiao Bo saw Jiang Tian's excellence that he went to such lengths to slander him. Xiao Bo even said before that making Jiang Tian serve tea and water after he joined the police force was a way to force him out. Now that I think about it, it was all just harassment."

Thinking this, Mu Ya gritted her teeth.



Chapter 50: The Photos Are Fully Exposed, and Muya's Mental State Collapses


He had a natural admiration for the police, especially someone like Jiang Tian, ​​who perfectly embodied his ideal of a heroic police officer.

And he had witnessed Jiang Tian bravely step forward to face the gun in a crisis, his powerful and swift methods instantly killing the drug dealer before he could react.

Now, a deep sense of guilt appeared on Mu Ya's face—guilt for misunderstanding Jiang Tian. Such a heroic policeman, slandered by that beast Xiao Bo.

He had never hated anyone as much as he did now.

"I'm sorry. I actually believed Xiao Bo's slander, calling you a piece of trash, a black sheep, and a cancer in the police force. I never imagined he would do such a thing. He's the one who should be the black sheep," Mu Ya apologized solemnly.

Jiang Tian's brow twitched.

Because he hadn't heard any words of complete surrender from Mu Ya.

That's right.

Jiang Tian was secretly pleased. This was the perfect woman in his mind, the only woman he remembered as beautiful.

While seemingly condemning Xiao Bo, she actually made Jiang Tian feel that she was also representing Xiao Bo in apologizing to him.

Such a perfect goddess.

Even without Xiao Bo pursuing her, she remained so loyal. If he had actually won her over, for a man, having such a woman, such a virtuous wife, how could he not be riding high?

However, it was also clear that Mu Ya had completely lost hope in Xiao Bo, and now only one straw was needed to break her.

Therefore, at this moment, a pained expression appeared on Jiang Tian's face.

"What's wrong? Are you hurt?" Mu Ya asked anxiously.

Her fair face was covered in sweat from tension and fright, and the fine hairs at her temples clung to her face, making her pure and beautiful appearance breathtaking.

"Seeing you reminds me of my girlfriend, sigh," Jiang Tian shook his head sadly.

"What's wrong?"

Hearing that Jiang Tian had a girlfriend, a faint tension, imperceptible even to herself, appeared on Mu Ya's face, but Jiang Tian clearly sensed it.

There's hope.

Jiang Tian's lips curled into a smile.

At this moment, he was finally certain that he had completely cut off all of Xiao Bo's escape routes.

And the possibility of marrying a rich woman and rising to power was also completely eliminated.

"Yesterday, when Yun Da was on a mission over the Kairun Hotel, arresting drug dealers, he discovered that she actually... sigh." Jiang Tian sighed.

Mu Ya frowned, a deep disgust appearing on her face. She had a natural aversion to unfaithful women.

"That kind of woman doesn't deserve a police god like you. You'll definitely have someone better in the future." Mu Ya clenched her small fist in encouragement, but Jiang Tian looked at her with a hint of sadness.

This made Mu Ya's expression slightly startled.

Wait, why are you looking at me like that?

Before Mu Ya could react, Jiang Tian pulled a stack of photos from his pocket.

"Showing me these won't do any good!" Mu Ya smiled helplessly, realizing they were probably photos of him catching her cheating. She was frustrated; who shows someone something like this, especially under these circumstances?

She felt Jiang Tian was probably still too naive and immature.

Jiang Tian remained silent. Out of politeness, Mu Ya reluctantly took the photo. By the moonlight, it was clearer.

It showed a man and a woman embracing and kissing at an elevator entrance.

"That woman deserves to die! Her boyfriend is a heroic narcotics officer, on a dangerous mission against drug dealers, and she's cheating on him!" Mu Ya thought, seething with anger.

But...

Wait?

The man's profile looked familiar. Mu Ya looked up, confused, and gave Jiang Tian a blank stare.

"Look down," Jiang Tian pointed.

Mu Ya flipped the photo.

The next moment...

Boom!!!

Mu Ya's mind exploded.

The photo was very clear, taken by Jiang Tian with a high-definition lens using semi-professional techniques. The photo showed the adulterer being embraced by the woman, a frontal shot.

But this man...

It was... Xiao Bo.

Mu Ya's face turned pale.

She looked up at Jiang Tian, ​​finally understanding why he had shown it to her.

"You were on a mission, Xiao Bo, and he took your girlfriend to a hotel. So, that day, Xiao Bo claimed to be on an important mission, but he was actually just looking for this woman to go to a hotel with, and then he twisted the truth and told me about your achievements?" Mu Ya's face was deathly pale; her mind seemed to be exploding.

How could Xiao Bo do something like this?

And how unfair was this to Jiang Tian?

Jiang Tian was working tirelessly on his mission, while Xiao Bo was betraying and framing this heroic police officer behind his back.

Although it was Xiao Bo who did it, and she had no real relationship with him now.

He was merely a suitor, someone she had some mutual interest in, but a relationship that was better than friendship.

However, this was enough to make Mu Ya feel guilty towards Jiang Tian.

A petty, narrow-minded person would have watched with amusement, hoping for her safety, never risking their life to save her.

Knowing their close relationship, she was surprised that Xiao Bo would so selflessly rescue her.

This was the police god she admired most.

“Mu Ya, Mu Ya, you’re really here! That’s wonderful! Get out of here quickly! There’s a vicious criminal here. It’s dangerous. I’ll take you away.” Xiao Bo ran out from the side path, his face lighting up with immense joy when he saw Mu Ya.

Found her.

Finally, he had a chance to salvage their relationship. Xiao Bo was confident in his abilities; he was certain he could win Mu Ya back.

But at this moment, he didn’t know...

Mu Ya, standing before him, held a photograph in her hand, her fingers clenched so tightly they turned white.

Xiao Bo was about to say some heartfelt words to comfort Mu Ya when he turned and suddenly spotted a familiar figure.

Jiang Tian?

Xiao Bo instantly became wary, his face contorting with rage.

He knew all too well how perfect Mu Ya was, and he was terrified of being discovered and robbed. In fact, he had always pursued Mu Ya secretly, without telling anyone in the police force.

And now, in the dead of night, under the blazing moon, a lone man and woman.

However, Xiao Bo instantly remembered Mu Ya's personality, and his heart relaxed completely. Mu Ya was definitely not the kind of woman who would do such a thing.

"Jiang Tian, ​​what are you doing here? You good-for-nothing, instead of helping search the mountain, you're here trying to slack off? A good-for-nothing is a good-for-nothing. Alright, Mu Ya and I have something to talk about later, you can get lost." Xiao Bo said casually, almost instinctively.

"Remember this when you're on a mission: don't slack off. Honestly, without anyone watching, you good-for-nothing have absolutely no self-discipline."

Xiao Bo hadn't realized anything, or rather, having been beaten up, Xiao Bo seemed to have forgotten the pain.

Perhaps, the image of Jiang Tian as an honest but useless good-for-nothing in his mind was too deeply ingrained, and he habitually still referred to Jiang Tian as that same good-for-nothing.

"Shut up," Mu Ya said coldly, her face expressionless.

Looking into Xiao Bo's eyes, very cold and devoid of any emotion, she coldly questioned, "She's a good-for-nothing?"

Mu Ya almost laughed in anger. If Jiang Tian, ​​who had performed so many merits, and who had bravely saved her today, was a good-for-nothing, then what was Xiao Bo?

"Mu Ya, did that good-for-nothing use some sweet talk to say bad things about me?" Xiao Bo asked, shocked and angry. He had almost never seen Mu Ya before; her eyes were terrifyingly cold. He instinctively assumed Jiang Tian had spoken ill of him.

And this time, if Jiang Tian knew, he would definitely applaud. Xiao Bo seemed to be right.

But just then, a series of extremely rapid sounds rang out from the jungle, a chaotic clatter of footsteps.

A moment later, shadowy figures finally emerged from the dense forest onto the mountainside.

Jiang Tian showed no surprise.

Just after dealing with the dangerous drug dealer Zhou Zicheng, Jiang Tian immediately notified the police.

However, Jiang Tian hadn't expected such a large force.

Gao Xiaolong and Shen Ting almost came together.

They led their men out.

Gao Xiaolong's feelings were complicated!

The excitement of receiving the award for meritorious service that morning hadn't even cooled down when, that evening, good heavens, at the meritorious service ceremony, it was this guy again?

However, Gao Xiaolong was only joking in his mind; in reality, he was genuinely delighted!

Seven armed police officers—the entire police force was under terrifying pressure.

It was absolutely chilling, the impact terrifying. If it weren't for Jiang Tian, ​​who knows how many more people might have suffered.

The most terrifying thing was, if he escaped.

Gao Xiaolong didn't know how to face the people of Yunhai.

Gao Xiaolong solemnly stepped forward: "Comrade Jiang Tian, ​​we understand the details of your mission. You have once again successfully protected the lives and property of the people, fearlessly and tirelessly protecting our comrades."
